'oDolarer 
dam be^dhe deOyar ceShTa vul chilo' Dolarer biporIte Takar man kome zaOya niye deSer orrthonItibidoder motO orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhitoO udwign. tini bolocheno, Dolarer binimoy har 69 Takay be^dhe rakhar ceShTa vul chil. biDiniuj TOyenTifOr DoTokomoke orrthomontrI boleno, got kichudin dhore Takar biporIte Dolarer dam obyahotovabe baRoche. er fole amodani byyer paSapaSi rijarrver Opor cap poRoche. muhiter mote, got kichudine Dolarer binimoy har baRar ekoTi karoN hoj. zara hoje gecheno, tader Dolar niye zete hoyeche. ar cahida baRay damoO beReche. "oaroO ekoTi karoN holO- beS kichu din amora Dolarer dam 69 Takay be^dhe rakhar ceShTa korechilam. amader Oi siddhantoi 
vul chil. amora zodi tokhon Oi bybostha na nitamo, tahole ekhon Dolarer dam hoThat'' kore etO beSi baRotO na. aste aste baRotO. tokhon sohonIy mone hotO." ei poristhitite Dolarer dam komate sorokar ba bangladeS byangk kOnO hostokShep korobe ki na- janote caile biShoyoTi eRiye zan muhit. bideSi mudra lenodenokarI byangkogulOr songgoThon bangladeS foren eksoceNGj Dilarrs oyasOsiyeSon (obieefoiDie) got 10 okTObor joruri bOIThok kore Dolarer biporIte Takar mUly nirrdharoN kore dey. Oi bOIThoker por bieefoiDie-oer ceyaromyan O jonota byangker bybosthapona poricalok es em aminur rohoman sangbadikoder janano, amodani porryaye (oelosi ba rriNopotr khOla) proti Dolarer dor kOnO obosthatei 76 Takar beSi 
hobe na. ar remiTens O roptanir kShetre ta 75 Takar beSi hobe na. Dilaroder Oi podokSheper poroO Dolarer binimoy har baRotei thake. emonoki kOrobanir Id samone prabosI ay (oremiTenso) baRar poroO Dolarer dor komeni, ulTO beReche. bangladeS byangker OyebosaiTer tothy onuzayI, Ider age SeSh karrydibos brrihospotibar proti Dolarer bikroy har chil 76 Taka 29 poyosa. ar kroyomUly chil 76 Taka 24 poyosa. e din besorokari uttora byangk Dolar kineche 75 Taka 40 poyosay. ar bikri koreche 76 Taka 45 poyosay. ar bideSi byangk eicoesobisi 76 Taka 35 poyosay Dolar bikri kore kineche 75 Taka 35 poyosay. dor nirrdharoN kore deOyar 
poroO byangkogulO ken beSi dame Dolar kenabeca koroche janar jony brrihospotibar rate aminur rohomaner soNgge TelifOne zOgazOger ceShTa koreO take paOya zayoni. tobe bieefoiDier arek korrmokorrta nam prokaS na korar Sorrte biDiniuj TOyenTifOr DoTokomoke boleno, "oasole 10 okTOborer bOIThoke amora siddhant niyechilamo, Dolar kenabecar bybodhan zate ek Takar beSi na hoy. Dolarer dor bedhe deOyar kOnO siddhant neya hoyoni." Takar soNgge Dolarer binimoy har somonwyer jony 20o0o3 sale deSe vasoman mudra binimoy bybostha calu hoy. er age kendrIy byangkoi Dolar kenabecar dor Thik kore ditO. byangkogulO Oi dorei Dolar kenabeca korotO. kintu 20o0o9 O 20o10 sale Dolarer dam sthitiSIl rakhote 
olikhit hostokShep kore bangladeS byangk. Oi dui bochor Takar biporIte proti Dolar 69 theke 70 Takar modhye kenabeca hoy. eropor coloti bochorer januyari theke Dolarer dam abar baRote thake. 'omUlysfItir onytom karoNo' Takar biporIte Dolarer obyahot dorobrriddhii mUlysfIti baRar onytom karoN bole mone koren bangladeS unnoyon gobeShoNa protiShThaner (obiaiDieso) mohaporicalok mustofa ke mujerI. poristhitir unnoti na hole vobiShyte mUlysfIti arO baRobe bole sotorrk korechen bangladeS byangker sabek ei prodhan orrthonItibid. biDiniuj TOyenTifOr DoTokomoke tini boleno, "oTakar biporIte Dolarer dor brriddhi udwegojonok porryaye pOU^cheche. amader orrthonIti amodaninirrvor. Dolarer dor baRole amodani khorocoO beSi poRe. beRe zay poNymUly. baRe mUlysfItiO." kendrIy byangker 
tothy porryalOconay dekha zayo, rOjar Ider age (o29 ogasTo) proti Dolar bikri hoyeche 73 Taka 61 poyosay. ar brrihospotibar ta bikri hoyeche 76 Taka 29 poyosay. kendrIy byangker bOIdeSik mudra binimoy harer gotibidhi porryalOconay dekha zayo, got bochorer 5 okTObor proti Dolar bikri hoyechil 70 Taka 45 poyosay. ei hisabe ek bochore Dolarer biporIte Takar man komeche pray 8 SotangS. ke mujerI boleno, "oDolarer biporIte Takar man kome zaOyay amodani byy meTate beSi orrth byy hocche. ete bOIdeSik mudrar rijarrver OporoO cap poRoche. cap poRoche sorokarer bajeT bybosthaponateO." bangladeS porisongkhyan byurOr (obibieso) sorrwSeSh tothy onuzayI, got 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore goR mUlysfItir 
har chilO 8 doSomik 8 SotangS. ar poyenTo-oTu-opoyenT vittite sepTemwr mase mUlysfItir har chilO 11 doSomik 97 SotangSo, za got doS bochorer modhye sorrweacc. coloti 20o11-o12 orrthobochorer bajeTe goR mUlysfIti 7 doSomik 5 SotangSer modhye thakobe bole dhora holeO sorokarer ei lokShy pUroN kora koThin hobe bolei mone koren mujerI. "oe poristhitite Dolarer dor zodi beRei cole, tahole mUlysfIti SeSh porrynt kOthay giye da^Rabe, seTai ekhon cintar biShoy." biaiDies mohaporicalok boleno, Sudhu poNy amodanite noyo, Dolarer dor baRole Silp sthaponer jony proyOjonIy zontropati O Silper ka^camal amodanir khorocoO baRe. ar sob amodani biloi Dolare poriSOdh korote hoy. fole Dolarer dam 
baRole cap poRe bOIdeSik mudrar mojude. swavabikovabei sthanIy bajare poNyer dam beRe zay. orrthobochorer prothom tin mase orrthyat'' julai-osepTemwr somoye roptani aye 22 doSomik 56 SotangS probrriddhi holeO julai-osepTemwr somoye amodani byy ager bochorer ekoi somoyer ceye 24 doSomik 79 SotangS beReche. 20o11-o12 orrthobochorer prothom car mase (ojulai-ookTOboro) remiTens probahe probrriddhi hoyeche 10 doSomik 54 SotangS. Ider age probasIra tader poribaro-oporijoner kache beSi orrth paThanOy sepTemwr maser ceye okTObore remiTens beReche. sepTemwr mase 84 kOTi Dolarer remiTens esechil. ar okTObore probasIra paThiyechen 10o4 kOTi 18 lakh Dolar. brrihospotibar kendrIy byangker bOIdeSik mudrar rijarrver porimaN chil 10 doSomik 30 biliyon Dolar. 
sepTemwrer prothom dike ta 9 doSomik 8 biliyon Dolare neme asoleO pore abar 10 biliyoner ghor otikrom kore. tOIri pOSak khat 'oahladito' khato: orrthomontrI deSer roptani ayer prodhan khat tOIri pOSak Silp khatoke 'oahladit khato' bole ovihit korechen orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit. tini bolecheno, "oamader besorokari khater ekoTa coritr hocche khali naliS kora. biSeSh kore tOIri pOSak Silp malikora khub beSi naliS kore. sob somoy tara osubidhar (osomosya) kotha bole. sob somoy tara sorokarer kache subidha cay. amoraO (osorokaro) 'oahladit khato' bibecona kore tader khatir kori." "ozehetu ei khat soboceye beSi korrmosongsthan srriShTi koreche. 23 biliyon Dolar roptani ay 
deSe anoche, swavabikovabei sorokar tader du:kho-okoShT amole ney. ekoTu beSi khatir kori." bolen muhit. brrihospotibar dupure suiDener sTeT sekreTari hana helokuisTer soNgge bOIThok SeShe sangbadikoder soNgge alapokale orrthomontrI e sob kotha bolen. muhit boleno, "oetOdin suiDen SikSha O swasthy khate sohayota koreche. ekhon tara tader drriShTivoNggiO poriborrton korote cay. tara amader besorokari khate biniyOg korote cay. jwalani O zOgazOg khato, bondor bybosthapona emonoki TranojiT isyuteO tara biniyOg korote cay." "oami tader bolechi bangladeS bideSi biniyOger (oefoDiai) jony khuboi valO jayoga. kintu amader kichu somosyar (oamolatantrik joTilota, jwalani O zOgazOg khate ghaToti) karoNe kaksikShot efoDiai asoche na. ovizOg ache diner por 
din fail aToke thake. bideSi biniyOgokarIder jhamela pOhate hoy. amora e sob somosya somadhaner ceShTa korochi. biniyOg bOrrDoke Dhele sajanO hocche." sorokarer byangkorriN brriddhite udwign non orrthomontrI coloti orrthobochorer prothom tin mase (ojulai-osepTemwro) byangk bybostha theke sorokarer rriN grohoNer porimaN 11 hajar kOTi Taka chaRiye geche. za otIter ze kOnO somoyer ceye beSi. tobe e niye orrthomontrI udwign non bole abarO janalen brrihospotibar. sorokarer byangrriN prosoNgge ek proSner uttore orrthomontrI boleno, "oe kotha Thik ze orrthobochorer prothom prantike byangk theke sorokarer rriN beReche. tobe ami eTa niye mOTeO udwign noi." got maseO orrthomontrI bolechileno, sorokarer byangkorriN beRe zaOya niye tini 
udwign non. byangkorriN brriddhir karoN hisebe muhit boleno, "oorrthobochorer prothom dik hoOyay bideSi sahazyer probah kom. rajosw adaye probrriddhiO kichuTa kom. e karoNe byangk theke ekoTu beSi rriN nite hocche." "otobe agamI masogulOte ar e proboNota thakobe na." montoby kore tini boleno, "obideSi sahazyer goti baRole ar rajosw adayer probrriddhi baRole rriNer porimaN kome asobe." muhit boleno, "oami ageO bolechi, ekhonoO bolochi, bajeTe amora (osorokaro) byangking bybostha theke rriN neOyar ze lokShymatra dhorechilamo, ta kOnO obosthatei otikrom korobe na. bajeT ghaTotiO nirrdharit lokShymatrar (o5 SotangSo) modhyei thakobe." porisongkhyan diye orrthomontrI boleno, "obajeT ghaToti meTate ovyntorIN ut''s theke 27 hajar kOTi 
Taka ebong bideSi ut''s theke 18 hajar kOTi Taka rriN neOyar lokShymatra dhora ache. ami jOr diye bolochi, orrthobochor SeShe e lokShymatra otikrom korobe na." 'oamodani byy baRoleO rijarrv valO' bOIdeSik mudrar borrtomane rijarrv diye tin maser beSi amodani byy meTanO somvob bole janan orrthomontrI. tini boleno, "osaÂ¤oprotik somoye amodani byy beS beReche. taroporoO rijarrv sontOShojonok porryaye royeche. roptani ay baRoche. baRoche remiTens probah." agamIte rijarrv poristhiti arO valO hobe bole aSa prokaS koren tini. kendrIy byangker tothy onuzayI, brrihospotibar bangladeS byangker rijarrver porimaN chil 10 doSomik 20 biliyon Dolar. paikarite komoleO khucora bajare mosolar dam beSi Idul ajohar onytom

hajar 40o0 Taka ebong paikarir 620 Takar gOl moric khucoray 90o0 Taka. sokale nogorIr reyajuddin bajaro, kajir deuRi, cokobajaro, bohoddarohaTo, mOgoloTuli bajar ghure paikari bajar O khucoray bajare e tofat'' lokShy kora zay. paikari bybosayIra bolocheno, khucora bikretader karosajite paikari dam komoleO tar provab bajare poRoche na. onydike khucora bikretara bolocheno, ager kena poNy thakate paikarite dam komoleO beSi dame bikri korote hocche. tobe paikar O amodanikarokora janiyecheno, Idul fitoro'or por theke mosolar bajar swavabik royeche. onek poNyer dam komeche boleO dabi koren tara. deSer onytom paikari bajar khatunogoNGje Sukrobar sokale proti keji elac 1 hajar 120 Takay bikri holeO 
nogorIr kajir deuRi bajare 1 hajar 40o0 Takay bikri hocchilO. paikari-okhucoray parrthoky 30o0 Taka amodanikarok O khatunogoNGjer osIm enTaropraijer malik osIm kumar daS biDiniuj TOyenTifOr DoTokomoke janano, Sukrobar proti keji jira 355 Taka, miShTi jira 140 Taka, loboNgg 1 hajar 30o0 Taka, gOlomoric 620 Taka, darucini 170 Taka, pe^yaj man vede 22 theke 27 Taka, rosun 45 Takay bikri hoyeche. onydike nogorIr bajarogulOte khucora bikretara proti keji gOl moric 90o0 Taka, jira 450 theke 460 Taka, miShTi jira 220 Taka, loboNgg 1 hajar 60o0 Taka, darucini 240 Taka, pe^yaj 30 theke 32 Taka ebong rosun bikri hocche 65 theke 70 
Takay. bohoddarohaT bajarer khucora bikreta abdus samad biDiniuj TOyenTifOr DoTokomoke boleno, Idul ajohay sob dhoroner mosolar cahida ekoTu beSi thake. beSi dame ager kena poNy mojude thakay se hisebei bikri korote hocche. e ovizOgoke khucora bikretader karosaji dabi kore khatunogoNGjer rohoman TreDarrser malik joyonal abedIn biDiniuj TOyenTifOr DoTokomoke boleno, "odam baRole tokhon drut khucora bajoreO dam baRe, komole tar provab poRote deri hobe keno?o" dwiguN dame bikri hocche ada nogorIr khucora bajarogulOte pray dwiguN dame bikri hocche deSe ut''padit ada. khatunogoNGj bajare Sukrobar proti keji deSi ada 27 theke 28 Takay bikri holeO nogorIr cokobajare khucora bikretara 52 theke 55 
Takay bikri korochen. cokobajarer rohoman sTOrer bikreta abu taher biDiniuj TOyenTifOr DoTokomoke boleno, amodani kora adar soroborah kome zaOyay deSi adar cahida beReche. tai beReche dam. khatunogoNGj sotota baNijyaloyer bikroyokorrmI SamIm janano, proti keji deSi ada 27 theke 28 Taka ebong cIn theke amodani kora ada proti keji 52 Taka bikri kora hoyeche. khucoray cIn theke ana ada bikri hocche 70 Taka kejite. pe^yajer soroborah komoche pe^yajer soroborah komote thakay Sonibar theke pe^yajer dam baRote pare bole janiyechen amodanikarok O paikari bybosayIra. amodanikarokora janano, Ider karoNe sthol pothe amodani itOmodhyei komote Suru koreche. Ide benapOl bondh 5 din Id O saptahik chuTi miliye deSer sorrwbrrihot'' stholobondor benapOl bondore pa^c din amodani-oroptani bondh thakobe. benapOl kasTomos kliyaring oyanD forOyarrDing ejenT oyasOsiyeSoner netara janano, brrihospotibar dupurer por theke ekoTana pa^c din bondh thakoleO stholobondorer antorrjatik cekopOsT diye pasopOrrTodharI zatrIra colacol korobe. 4 O 5 novemwr Sukrobar O Sonibar bangladeSer saptahik chuTi, 6 novemwr theke 8

koren. e obostha mOkabelay sorokaroke ekoTi korrmoporikolpona Thik koroteO poramorrS diyechen tini. senTar for polisi Dayaloger (osipiDi) DisTingguiSoD felO debopriy brrihospotibar ek songbad sommelone boleno, vorrtuki babod sorokar e orrthobochore 47 hajar 40o0 kOTi Taka byy korobe bole avas paOya zacche. e orrther porimaN amader mOT rajosw ayer orrdhek. byangk rriNer dwiguNer beSi. coloti orrthobochore rajosw khat theke sorokarer ayer lokShymatra 92 hajar kOTi Taka. byangk rriN dhora hoyeche 180o0o0 kOTi Taka. coloti orrthobochorer bajeTe vorrtukir porimaN 22 hajar 50o0 kOTi Taka dhora hoyeche. tobe sipiDi mone koroche, e oNgk baRobe. debopriy boleno, "ovorrtukir porimaN komate oboSyi jwalanir mUly baRate 
hobe. emonoki jonorOSh dekha dileO sorokarer ta kora ucit." vorrtuki komanOr pokShe zukti dekhiye tini boleno, vorrtuki byy meTate sorokar byangk theke dhar koroche. kintu vorrtuki komale otirikt orrth ut''padonoSIl khate byy kora somvob. tate orrthonItir jony valO fol asobe. "osorokar doridroder sohayota vorrtuki dileO byangker kach theke dhar koray mUlysfIti abar baRoche. e duTi biShoy ekoTi arekoTir Opor provab rakhoche,o" bolen tini. 'obangladeSer orrthonItir borrtoman cyaleNGjo' SIrrShok e songbad sommelone sipiDir sabek nirrwahI poricalok boleno, coloman soNgkoTe sorokaroke monOzOg dite hobe. borrtoman poristhiti colote thakole e bochorer kaksikShot sat SotangS probrriddhi orrjon koThin boleO mone koren tini. e jony

raiT Seyar isyur bidhimala onumOdon koreche sikiuriTij enD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi). moNggolobar esoisi-oer bOIThoke ei siddhant hoyeche bole janiyechen songsthaTir mukhopatr saifur rohoman. sikiuriTij enD eksoceNGj raiTos isyu rulos 20o0o6 namer bidhimalaTi er age jonomot joripe paThanO hoyechil. kichu poriborrtoner pore ta onumOdon deOya hoyeche. saifur rohoman janano, bidhimalaTite koyekoTi biShoy notun songzOjon kora hoyeche. ekhon theke kOnO kOmpani primiyamosoh raiT Seyar isyu korote hole tar ager tin bochore laver rekorrD thakote hobe. primiyam nite hole protiShThanoTir oboSyi kreDiT reTing isyu thakote hobe. raiT ofarer ghOShoNa esoisi O dui sTok eksoceNGjer paSapaSi kOmpanir OyebosaiTe thakote hobe. esoisir onumOdoner tin korrmodiboser

dabisoh onyany dabi na mana hole 7 Disemwr mohasomabeS kora hobe bole janiyeche tara. doropotoner protibade rObobaroO bangladeS pu^jibajar biniyOgokarI OIky poriShoder byanare bikShOv korechil kShudr biniyOgokarIra. tara orrthomontrI, bangladeS byangker govorrnor O Diesoi korrtrripokSher biruddhe SlOgan dey. pu^jibajare byangkogulOr biniyOg baRanOr ghOShoNar por Diesoir sUcok baRar modhy diye Suru hoy got soptaher lenoden. kintu byangker biniyOg baRanOr biShoye biSw byangk O aiemoefer ekoTi protibedon duTi potrikay prokaSit hoOyar por budhobar O brrihospotibar bajare dhws name. pu^jibajar niye kotha bolote can na orrthomontrI pu^jibajar niye kotha bolote can na orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit. rObobar sondhyay socibaloye japaner raShTrodUt eic 
i SirO sadOSimar soNgge bOIThok SeShe pu^jibajare doropoton niye sangbatikoder proSner uttore tini boleno, "oeTa esoisir (opu^jibajar niyontrok songstha- sikiuriTij enD eksoceNGj komiSono) byapar. amar kache nei." rObobar deSer prodhan pu^jibajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGje (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok 231 poyenT kome 50o77 poyenTe neme eseche. got soptahe sUcok poRechil 235 poyenT. biniyOg O baNijy baRanOr tagid orrthomontrI boleno, japan amader boR unnoyon sohozOgI. kintu orrthonOItik somporrk byapok noy. baNijy O biniyOg khuboi kom. bangladeSe biniyOg O baNijy baRate japaner onek agroh ache. tobe seTar protifolon hocche na. muhit boleno, "oagamI bochor japaner prodhanomontrI ekoTi boR bybosayI protinidhidol niye bangladeS sofore asoben. 
aSa korochi se soforer modhy diye dudeSer modhye baNijy O biniyOg somporrke notun matra zOg hobe." podma setute jaikar orrthayon obyahot thakobe japane boR prakrritik durryeager poroO podma setute jaikar orrthayon obyahot thakobe janiye orrthomontrI boleno, "ojapaner raShTrodut janiyecheno, amader podma setute jaikar orrthayon niye kOnO somosya nei. tara ze protiSro"oti diyechilen se onuzayI orrthayon korobe." durrnItir ovizOg tule biSw byangk podma setute orrthayon sthogit koreche. 6 doSomik 15 kilOmiTar dIrrgh podma setu nirrmaNe byy dhora hoyeche 290 kOTi Dolar. er modhye 120 kOTi Dolar deOyar kotha biSw byangker. biSw byangk chaRa e setu nirrmaNer jony eDibir 61 kOTi, jaikar 
40 kOTi ebong isolamI unnoyon byangker 14 kOTi Dolar rriN deOyar kotha. pu^jibajare biniyOg baRanOr dabi pujibajare caNggavab firiye anote byangkogulOke sorrweacc biniyOge badhy korar dabi janiyeche bangladeS pu^jibajar biniyOgokarI OIky poriShod. 6 Disemwrer modhye e dabisoh onyany dabi na mana hole 7 Disemwr mohasomabeS kora hobe bole janiyeche tara. pu^jibajare obyahot doropotoner protibade motijhil baNijyik elakar ekoTi ofise sOmobar dupure songbad sommelon Suru kore kShudr biniyOgokarIra. bangladeS pu^jibajar biniyOgokarI OIky poriShoder sovapoti, e. ke. em mijanour roSid cOUdhurI boleno, byangkogulOke pu^jibajare sorrweacc biniyOge badhy korote hobe. procolit ain onuzayI 10 SotangS niyomosImay byangkogulOr 45 hajar kOTi Taka biniyOg moNggolobar 
thekei bastobayon korar dabi koren tini. likhit boktobye marrcenT byangko, arrthik protiShThano, ar bIma kOmpanigulOke deSer procolit aini sImar modhye sorrweacc biniyOge badhy koraroO dabi janan tini. biniyOgokarIder dabi, miucuyal fanDer mUlodhoner 80 SotangS badhytamUlokovabe pu^jibajare biniyOg korote hobe. kOmpani ain songSOdhon kore kOmpanir udyOkta poricalokoder komopokShe 40 SotangS theke 50 SotangS Seyar ebong byakti udyOktar komopokShe 30 SotangS Seyar sara bochor dhore rakhar niyom korar dabi janan OIky poriShod sovapoti. oprodorrSit orrth pu^jibajare biniyOger byapare enobiar O dudoker onapotti potr 72 ghonTar modhye jari korar dabi jananO hoy. echaRa bangladeS fanDosoh aisibir sob biniyOg fanD niye pu^jibajare drut Seyar 
kena ebong primiyam chaRa fesovyalute aipiO bajare anar dabi jananO hoy. songbad sommelone pu^jibajar biniyOgokarI OIky poriShoder neta-okorrmIder Opor hamola O mamola dayer bondh korar dabi jananO hoy. esob dabi moNggolobar thekei bastobayon kora Suru na korole 'odurrwar andOlono' korrmosUci deOya hobe bole huSiyari deOya hoy. 6 Disemwrer modhye dabigulO bastobayon O bajar sthitiSIl na hole 7 tarikhe sob biniyOgokarIke soNgge niye Dhaka Sohore moha somabeSer Dak deya hobe bole songbad sommelone bola hoy. sangbadikoder proSner uttore OIky poriShoder siniyor zugm sadharoN sompadok mOhammod jahaNggIr alom janano, bajar caNgga na hoOya porrynt protidin Diesoi-oer samone andOlon colobe. songbad sommelone dabi 
kora hoyo, pu^jibajarer byapare orrthomontrI, orrth upodeShTa, bangladeS byangk govorrnor netibacok montoby korochen. deSer ekoTi SIrrShosthanIy dOInik potrikateO netibacok O bivrantimUlok protibedon chapa hocche. pujibajar biniyOgokarI OIky poriShod er tIbr ninda janiyeche. songbad sommeloner por dupur 1Tar dike Diesoi-oer samone manobobondhonoO kore kShudr biniyOgokarIra. ciTagong vejiTebolosoke esoisir nOTis niyom bohirrvUtovabe mUly songbedonoSIl tothy prokaSer karoNe ciTagong vejiTebolos oyel inDasTrij limiTeDer ceyaromyanoke nOTis diyeche niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi). Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) OyebosaiTe moNggolobar e tothy prokaS kora hoy. esoisi boleche, sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (osubidhavOgI bybosa niShiddhokoroNo) bidhimala, 1995 er 3 (o1) dhara omany koray ciTagang vejiTeboler 
ceyaromyan samochul alom SamImoke karoN dorrSanO O Sunanir nOTis deOya hoyeche. 3 (o1) dharay bola hoyeche, "okOmpanir songghobidhi ebong kOmpanir kShetre prozOjy ony kOnO bidhibidhaner proyOjon bytit kOnO subidhavOgI kOnO mUly songbedonoSIl tothy ony kaharoO nikoT soroborah korite paribe na." got june SeSh hoOya orrthobochore SeyarohOlDaroder jony 25 SotangS sTok lovyangS got rObobar ghOShoNa kore ciTagong vejiTebolos. got ekobochore kOmpaniTir protiTi Seyarer mUly 6 hajar 699 Taka theke 1 hajar 841 Taka 75 poyosay OThanama kore. 20o10 sale kOmpaniTir Seyarer otirikt mUlybrriddhir karoN khotiye dekhote odhikotor todonter supariS kore pu^jibajarer osthirota todonte goThit komiTi. jiesopi fainyanser aipiO onumOdon jiesopi fainyans 
kOmpani bangladeS limiTeDer prathomik goNoprostab (oaipiO) onumOdon koreche niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi). moNggolobar esoisir niyomit sovay e siddhant neOya hoy. ekoi soNgge sovay iusibi inofrasTrakocar fanD name ekoTi miucuyal fanD goThoner prathomik onumOdon (oTrasT cukti) deOya hoyeche. sova SeShe esoisir mukhopatr saifur rohoman sangbadikoder janano, jiesopi fainyans bajare dui kOTi Seyar cheRe 50 kOTi Taka songgroh korobe. ekShetre 10 Taka ovihit mUlyer protiTi Seyarer dam nirrdharoN kora hoyeche 25 Taka. zar modhye 15 Taka primiyam neOya hobe. protiShThanoTir isyu bybosthapok aisibi kyapiTal myanejomenT limiTeD. sorrwSeSh 20o10 saler Disemwre prokaSit tothy onuzayI protiShThanoTir Seyaroproti mOT sompod mUly (oenoevi)

udwOdhonI onuShThane Suveccha boktoby den moDelo-oovinetrI Saromin lakI O munomun ebong koksobajarer prothom alOr nijosw protibedok abdul kuddus rana. akku cOUdhurI boleno, âobiSwer dIrrghotom somudrosOIkot koksobajare keefosir auToleT sthapon korote pere amora gorrwit. ei restOra^ calur fole koksobajarobasIr paSapaSi ekhane vromoNe asa deSi-obideSi porryTokeraO sulovomUlye biSwmaner khabar grohoNer suzOg paben.â akku cOUdhurI boleno, jonopriy fraNGcaij resTurenT keefosi nitynotun DiS O tar poribeSon kOUSol diye deSojuRe voktoder mon joy kore asoche. ei ovijNGotake keefosi aroO ekodhap egiye niye gel deSer porryTon praNokendr koksobajare notun auToleT udwOdhoner madhyme. onuShThane bola hoyo, keefosi sob somoy olp khoroce vinnotor swader khabar poribeSoner ceShTa kore,

sukOmol singh cOUdhurIr sovapotitwe onuShThane jonota byangker bybosthapona poricalok (oemoDi) es em aminur rohomano, siTi byangker emoDi ke mahomud sattaro, pUbalI byangker emoDi Sekh abodul ajijo, praim byangker emoDi ehosan khosoru, iunaiTeD komarrSiyal byangker emoDi Sahojahan vU^iya, nasiber sovapoti Sekh mO. abodus sObohano, krriShi byangk koksobajarer mukhy aNGcolik korrmokorrta mOtahar hOseno, Dhaka byangker koksobajar Sakhar bybosthapok sOIyod mofij uddin ahomod O koksobajar cemwarer sovapoti mO. abodus Sukkur promukh uposthit chilen. ï»¿ âoiurO oNGcoler songkoTe keu nirapod noyoâ krisotin lagarrde antorrjatik mudra tohobiler (oaiemoefo) prodhan krisotin lagarrde bolecheno, italir orrthonOItik songskarer udyOg iurO oNGcole songkoTer provab komate sohayota korobe. ar tai

DobliuTiOr sodor doptore arek dofa anuShThanik apotti janabe bangladeS. gotokal moNggolobar socibaloye onuShThit tOIri pOSak O bostr khater bybosayIder soNgge onuShThit ek bOIThok SeShe baNijysocib mO. gOlam hOsen esob kotha janiyechen. pororaShTrosocib mijarul kayeso, tOIri pOSak prostutokarok O roptanikarok somitir (obijiemoie) sovapoti Sofiul isolam mohiuddinosoh ony bybosayI netaraO e somoy uposthit chilen. baNijysocib bolecheno, bangladeSer obosthan holO sahazy O baNijyke ekosoNgge guliye fela zabe na. sahazy sahazyi ar baNijy baNijyi. ekoTir bodole arekoTi hote pare na. baNijysocib boleno, zodi pakistanoke ei subidha ditei hoyo, tobe ze 75Ti poNye subidha caOya hocche, segulO theke tOIri pOSak khater aToTi poNy bad dite 
hobe. gOlam hOsen boleno, ei obosthan khub drut jenevay biSw baNijy songsthar kache anuShThanivabe jananO hobe. bangladeSer obosthan otIteO ekoi chil ekhonO ache ebong vobiShyteO thakobe. er age baNijymontrI muhammod faruk khanoO sangbadikoder janiyechileno, âopakistane bonyasoh nana biporryy hoyeche Thik. e byapare bangladeS sohomorrmI. tobe unnot deSogulOr ucit e jony pakistaner proti sahazyer hat baRiye deOya.â iurOpIy iuniyoner bajare pakistaner tOIri pOSak dui bochorer jony 20 SotangS hare SulkochaRe probeSadhikarer ceShTa koroche. bonyay kShotigrost hoOyar fole sohayota hisebe onudaner bodole ei baNijy chaR pete itimodhye pakistan onek dUr ogrosor hoyeche. iurOpIy iuniyonoO ete sommot. kintu ei subidha pete hole DobliuTiOr 
onumOdon lagobe. kenona, unnoyonoSIl deS hisebe pakistan kOnOvabei bangladeSer motO swlpOnnot deSer somodhorrmI subidha paOyar zOgy noy. ar tai pray bochor khanek agei pakistaner jony zokhon iiu DobliuTiOte ei baNijy chaRer jony abedon kore, tokhon bangladeSo, varot O SrIloNgka apotti janay. biSeShoto, varoter apottiTa chil onek jOralO. varoter pokSh theke bola hoyo, eTa emon ekoTa drriShTant tOIri korobe, za onyderoO e rokom chaR pete ut''sahit korobe. othoc ta hobe DobliuTiOr nItibidhir poriponthI. varot oboSy ekhon tar apotti tule niyeche. borong pakistanoke somorrthon korote zacche. tobe jenevay got soptahe e songkrant ek bOIThoke bangladeSe abaroO apotti janale biShoyoTi ar ogrosor hote 
pareni. DobliuTiOr bidhan onusare kOnO ekoTi sodosy deS kOnO biShoye apotti janale, ta ar onumOdon kora zabe na. e biShoyer Opor baNijy montroNaloyer kora ek protibedone bola hoyeche, pakistan iiu theke jiesopi pele 80 kOTi marrkin Dolarer bajar harabe bangladeS. edike pakistanoke biSeSh SulkochaRer subidha prodane apotti protyahar korobe bangladeS antorrjatik barrta songstha royoTarrsoke e dhoroner kOnO boktoby deOya hoyoni bole janiyechen pororaShTrosocib. tini boleno, âoroyoTarrs e dhoroner songbad prokaSer age tar soNgge kOnO kotha boleni.â baNijysocib boleno, âogot jun mase DobliuTiOke amader ekoi obosthan janiye deOya hoy.â baNijysocib aroO janano, iiu pokistaner 13Ti poNye nirrdiShT porimaN roptanite SulkochaRer subidha 
diyeche, zar modhye bangladeSer dabi kora aToTi poNyer modhye choyoTi royeche. jana geche iiu âojiesopi plas 20o14â skimer aOtay pakistanoke SulkochaRer subidha dite caiche. ete bangladeSer paSapaSi SrIloNgkasoh beS koyekoTi deSer apotti ache. ullekhy, 20o0o9-o11 somoyokaler jony iurOpIy komiSon 16Ti unnoyonoSIl deSoke jiesopi skimer aOtay Sulkomukt subidha prodan kore. ei 16Ti deSer modhye ajarobaijano, boliviya, kolomwiya, kOsTarika, ikOyaDuro, el salovaDOro, jiyOrogiya, guyetomala, honDuraso, moNggOliya, nikaraguya, peraguye, peru, SrIloNgka O venijuyela. iiu agamI 20o14 sal porrynt jiesopi plas skim obyahot rakhobe. ete notun kore pakistanoke probeS koranOr ceShTa hocche. edike ol pakistan TeksoTail milos oyasOsiyeSon (oapoTa) iiute aToTi tOIri pOSakopoNye SulkochaR 
paOyar kShetre kOnO dhoroner apotti na janate bangladeSer proti ahwan janiyeche. pakistaner khyatonama dOInik Donoke apoTar ceyaromyan mohosin ajij bolecheno, pakistaner tOIri pOSak kokhonOi bangladeSer jony kOnO humoki chil na, hobeO na. tini dabi koreno, pakistan kokhonOi iiute bangladeSi poNyer probeSer kShetre kOnO badha tOIri koreni bolei sekhane bangladeSer roptani onek beReche. mohosin ajij aroO boleno, iiur aT hajar kOTi Dolarer tOIri pOSaker bajare ekhon bangladeSer roptani ek hajar 60o0 kOTi Dolar. othoc ei bajare pakistaner roptani matr 150 kOTi Dolar. ta^r mote, pakistani pOSakopoNyke dui bochorer jony e subidha deOya hobe, ar tai e somoyokale baRoti kOnO biniyOg hobe 
na. ar tai pakistani pOSak roptani bangladeSer jony humoki hobe na bole tini ullekh koren. SilpomontrIr soNgge udyOktader bOIThok varote emoes roD roptanite oSulk badha dUr korar dabi kOnO dhoroner oSulk badhar karoNe zen varoter bajare bangladeSi emoes roDer probeSadhikar badhagrost na hoyo, se jony proyOjonIy udyOg neOyar dabi janiyechen bangladeS oTO ri-orOling oyanD sTil milos oyasOsiyeSoner netara. aOtay dokShiN eSiyar swlpOnnot deSogulOr jony sporrSokator poNyer talika namiye eneche. er fole 25Ti bade bangladeSi sob poNy varote binaSulke roptanir suzOg tOIri hoyeche. sovay sTil mil malikera boleno, deSer sTil O ri-orOling milogulO emoes roDer deSIy cahida miTiye otirikt ut''padon koroche. deSe borrtomane roDer cahida royeche 30 lakh meTrik Ton. ar ut''padit hocche goRe pray 40 lakh meTrik Ton. ei Silp khate pray 20 hajar kOTi Takar sthanIy biniyOg royeche. somitir netara boleno, protibeSI deSogulOr soNgge protizOgitay Tike thakote hole emoes roDer ka^camal O rasayoniker amodaniSulk komanO proyOjon. lOUhojatIy Silp khater udyOktader jony byangk rriNer suder har ek oNgke 
(osiNggel DijiTo) nirrdharoNo, Silpokarokhanay gyas songzOg prodano, jahaj vaNga Silper melTing skrryap O pleTer dam komanO ebong piesoai protha protyaharer dabi janan somitir netara. mil malikoder boktobyer poriprekShite lOUhojat poNy Silpayoner vitti bole montoby koren SilpomontrI. tini boleno, emoes roDer Opor biesoTiai prodott maner sonod varote zen grohoNozOgy hoyo, se jony udyOg neOya hocche. dilIp boRuya boleno, jahaj vaNga Silp deSIy sTil O ri-orOling Silper ka^camaler ut''s hisebe vUmika rakhoche. sTil O ri-orOling milogulOr ut''padono-okShomotanuzayI proyOjonIy ka^camal jOgan dite poribeSobandhob jahaj vaNga O punorut''padon (orisaikling) Silp goRe tOla hocche. risaikling bidhimala cURant kora hobe. bOIThoke somitir ceyaromyan Sekh masadul alomo, sadharoN sompadok abul kasem mojumodaro, zugm sompadok mO. sirajul isolam mrridha, sanggoThonik poricalok muhammod SohIdoullaho, sodosy mO. sirajul isolamo, Obayodul hok promukh uposthit chilen. ï»¿ narI udyOktader jony sorokari udyOge bipoNonokendr sthapon deSer narI udyOktader ut''padit poNy bajarojatokoroN ekoTi boR dhoroner somosya. e somosya somadhane aj budhobar trriNomUl narI udyOktader ut''padit poNy bajarojat korar jony prothomobarer motO sorokari udyOge ekoTi swtontr bipoNonokendr calu kora hobe. prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina eTi anuShThanikovabe udwOdhon koroben. rajodhanIr dhanomonDir rapa plajar duTi flOre bipoNonokendroTi calu kora hocche. prodhanomontrI sokal 10oTay rajodhanIr rUposI bangla hOTeler

ekoi soNgge rijaroveSone pUrrNaNgg onolain pemenT sisTem calu koreche songsthaTi. coTTogramovittik bybosayI gOShThI habib gruper oNggoprotiShThan rijenT eyaroOyej kanaDar tOIri 50 siTer nijosw duTi DyaSo-o8-okiu 30o0 eyarokrafoT niye zatrIseba dicche. rijenT eyaroOyejer prodhan nirrwahI imoran asif gotokaloek songbad sommelone janano, prothom bochore rijenT eyaroOyej Dhaka theke coTTogramo, koksobajaro, zoSOr O sileTer ovyntorIN ruTe pray saRe pa^c hajar flaiT poricalona kore, zate dui lakh 20 hajar zatrI ana-oneOya kora hoyeche. songbad sommelone aroO uposthit chilen rijenT eyaroOyejer bybosthapona poricalok maSoruf habibo, bipoNon O bikroy bivager poricalok akhotar iu ahomed promukh. bijNGopti. ï»¿ byanDouiDother dam 40 SotangS komol Sudhu kolosenTar khate byboharer 
jony byanDouiDother dam komal sorokar. borrtomane byanDouiDother nirrdharit mUly theke 40 SotangS komiye sekenD proti megabaiTer (oemobipieso) dam choy hajar Taka kora hoyeche. ek emobipies byanDouiDother coloti dam 15 hajar Taka. e siddhant coloti bochor 1 novemwr theke karrykor bole janiyeche bangladeS TelizOgazOg niyontroN komiSon (obiTiarosi). biTiarosir ceyaromyan jiya ahomed prothom alOke boleno, kolosenTar Silp ba^ciye tOlar uddeSe e dam komanO holO. tini janano, kolosenTar Silp bikaSe sorokar O komiSon sob dhoroner suzOgo-osubidha debe. got moNggolobar komiSoner siddhant onuzayI biShoyoTi sorrwsadharoNer jony biTiarosir OyebosaiTe prokaS kora hoyeche. biTiarosi e porrynt pray saRe 30o0 kolosenTarer laisens dileO borrtomane sokriy ache 58Ti 
protiShThan. e chaRa bidhimala onuzayI laisens neOyar choy maser modhye calu korote byrrth hole kolosenTarer laisens batil korar ghOShoNa diyechil biTiarosi. se ghOShoNar poroi pray S duyek laisens batil ba biTiarosite ferot eseche. matr pa^c hajar Takar binimoye kolosenTarer laisens deOya holeO Sudhu dokSh jonoboler ovabe e ceShTa byrrth hoyeche bole swIkar koren TelizOgazOgomontrI rajiuddin ahomed. tini oboSy boleno, onytom bOIdeSik mudra orrjoner khat hisebe kolosenTar bikoSit korar porikolpona neOya hoyeche. e jony proyOjonIy sob bybosthai nebe sorokar. kolosenTarer madhyme ekoTi protiShThan tothy diye kretake seba O somosyar somadhan diye thake. bivinn protiShThaner kretader sohozOgita, TelimarrkeTing ebong protiShThaner bivinn seba, 
ofar O tothy jananOi kolosenTarer kaj. eTike bijones proses auTosOrrsing (obipiO) bola hoy. 20o0o8 sale biSwjuRe bipiOr bajar chil 382 doSomik 5 biliyon marrkin Dolar. 20o0o9 sale ta 641 doSomik 2 biliyon Dolare unnIt hoy. bipiOr modhye nolej proses auTosOrrsing (okepiO)o, ligyal proses auTosOrrsing (oelopiO)o, risarrs proses auTosOrrsing (oaropiO) O eDukeSon proses auTosOrrsing (oipiO) SIrrShe royeche. biTiarosir ceyaromyan janano, byanDouiDother dam komanOr paSapaSi deSojuRe kolosenTar proSikShoNer biShoye ekoTi porikolpona tOIrisoh proyOjonIy karrykrom grohoNe songSliShT korrmokorrtader nirrdeS deOya hoyeche. somproti varotIy kolosenTar proSikShoN protiShThan âohirO mainD mainoâ e biShoye proyOjonIy proSikShoN debe bole komiSoner soNgge bOIThokoO koreche. ï»¿ Dhakay aieji karrgOr 
poNy poribohon Suru Dhakay inTaronyaSonal eyarolainos grup (oaieji) karrgO ba poNybahI biman calate Suru koreche. hongkong theke got budhobar aieji karrgOr prothom baNijyik flaiT Dhakar Sahojalal antorrjatik bimanobondore ese pOU^cheche. eTi hocche ei oNGcole aieji (oinTaronyaSonal eyarolainos grupero) prothom karrgO flaiT. bOying 747-o8 freiTar diye eTi poricalona kora hocche. briTiS eyaroOyej OyarrlD karrgO brryanDer madhyme poricalit hocche ei flaiT. bangladeSo, pakistan O modhypracye aieji karrgOr aNGcolik baNijyik bybosthapok provin sing janano, âoDhakay zehetu 747-o8 freiTaroke swagot jananO hoyeche, sehetu Dhaka totha bangladeSer karrgO Silpe poNy poribohon seba dite ta^ra protiSrutiboddh. aieji karrgO borrtomane eSiyay sanghai, dilli, dubaisoh lonDono, SikagO, aTolanTa, 
hiusTon provrriti gontobye colacol koroche. bijNGopti. ï»¿ doropoton themeche, lenoden beReche pu^jibajarer sthitiSIlota ferate prodhanomontrIr nirrdeSonay sorokari udyOger khobore oboSeShe doropoton themeche. er biporIte deSer dui sTok eksoceNGjei gotokal brrihospotibar Seyarer mUlysUcok O lenoden ullekhozOgy hare beReche. deSer prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGje (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok 179 poyenT beRe abar pa^c hajar poyenTer mailofolok otikrom koreche. e niye got dui dine sTok eksoceNGjoTir sadharoN sUcok 517 poyenT baRol. er age Idul ajohar chuTir por tin dine sUcok kome chil 560 poyenT. ar Tana e doropotone oboSiShT pu^jiTuku haranOr atoNgker paSapaSi kShOv choRiye poRe sadharoN biniyOgokarIder modhye. e obosthay pu^jibajarer sthitiSIlota 
ferate ta^ra prodhanomontrI Sekh hasinar hostokShep dabi kore asochilen. oboSeShe got budhobar rate pu^jibajarer sthitiSIlota feranOr lokShye prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina songSliShT bivinn pokSher soNgge dIrrgh bOIThok koren. e bOIThoke bajarer sthitiSIlota feranO O sadharoN biniyOgokarIder lOkosan pOShate swlpo, modhy O dIrrghomeyadi podokShep neOyar siddhant hoyo, za agamI du-oek diner modhye jananO hobe. bOIThoke ekoi soNgge niScit kora hoy ze, pu^jibajarer oprodorrSit orrth ba kalOTaka biniyOg korole kOnO songstha theke proSn tOla hobe na. baNijyik byangkogulOr pu^jibajare biniyOg baRanOr byapareO ekomot pOShoN kora hoy. bajarosongSliShT byktira bolocheno, prodhanomontrIr bOIThoker por biniyOgokarIra abar aSabadI hoye uThechen. mUlot e karoNei bajare mUlysUcok O 
lenoden beReche. eTi bajarer jony valO khobor. tobe kOnO karoNe sorokarer sorrwOcc porryayer aSwasoO zodi sthitiSIlota ferate byrrth hoyo, tahole ta bajarer jony ager ceye voyaboh poriNoti Deke anote pare. se jony sorokarer otynt sotorrkotar soNgge podokShep neOya ucit bole ta^ra ovimot prokaS koren. bajarosongSliShT byktira ekoi soNgge biniyOgokarIder uddeSe boleno, pu^jibajar ekoTi jhu^kipUrrN biniyOger kShetr. ekhane biniyOg korole zemon uccohare munafa kora zayo, temoni lOkosaner porimaNoO hoy boR. tai sobar ucit jene-obujhe sotorrkotar soNgge e bajare biniyOg kora. karoNo, barobar sorokarer SIrrSh porryay proNOdona diye bajar Thik kore debeâoe aSa kora Thik hobe na. jana geche, prodhanomontrIr bOIThoker siddhant 
onuzayI poroborrtI bOIThok Thik korote aj Sukrobar orrth montroNaloyer sovakokShe orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhiter sovapotitwe bOIThok onuShThit hobe. e bOIThoke bangladeS byangko, jatIy rajosw bOrrD (oenobiaro)o, bima unnoyon O niyontroN korrtrripokSho, inovesTomenT koropOreSon ob bangladeS (oaisibi) ebong pu^jibajar niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSoner (oesoisi) SIrrShosthanIy korrmokorrtara uposthit thakoben. jana geche, e bOIThoke bajarer tarolyprobah baRanO O byangkogulOr biniyOgo-osokShomota baRate bidhiboddh nogod joma (osiaroaro) O bidhiboddh jomar (oesoeloaro) har komanO, pu^jibajare byangker aini biniyOg sIma (oeksopOjar limiTo) notunovabe songjNGayit kora, biniyOgokarIder rriNer sud moOkuf ba ekoTi nirrdiShT somoyer jony sthogit rakha, onadayI rriNer biporIte byangkogulOr nirapotta soNGciti rakhar badhybadhokota 
theke samoyik obyahoti prodano, jIbon bima tohobiler orrth pu^jibajare biniyOgosoh bivinn biShoye alOcona hobe. bOIThoke esob biShoye siddhant hole songSliShT korrtrripokSh projNGaponer madhyme jonogoNoke obohit korobe. bajar poristhiti: Diesoite gotokal lenodener prothom pa^c miniTer modhye sUcok 151 poyenT beRe zay. ekoporryaye ta sOya 20o0 poyenTer beSi beRe zay. tobe din SeShe sUcok 179 poyenT beRe pa^c hajar 166 poyenT otikrom kore. coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sUcok 234 poyenT beRe noy hajar 370 poyenTe da^Riyeche. sTok eksoceNGjoTite 174Ti Seyarer lenoden hoyeche. er modhye dam beReche 152Tiro, komeche 18Tir O oporiborrtit royeche caroTi protiShThaner Seyarer dam. siesoite edin 49 kOTi Takar Seyar 
lenoden hoyeche. ar Diesoite lenoden hoyeche 416 kOTi Takar Seyaro, za ager diner ceye 131 kOTi Taka beSi. Diesoi sUtre jana geche, gotokal sob SreNIr biniyOgokarIi lenodene sokriy chil. ï»¿oï»¿ barrShik ut''padon pray dui kOTi pis ï¬ ontot deR hajar kOTi Takar lenoden deSIy luNggi hocche brryanDo, zacche bideSeO sirajogoNGjer Sahojadopurer rUpopur elakay ekoTi TeksoTail milose zontrocalit ta^te luNggi tOIri korochen ta^tira zug zug dhore odhikangS baNgali puruSher nitydiner onytom pOSak luNggi. sompUrrN deSIy upokoroN O prozukti bybohar kore luNggir cahidar pray purOTai ekhon deSe tOIri hocche. deSer jonosongkhya baRar soNgge soNgge aramodayok e pOSaker bajar protibochoroi baRoche. luNggi ut''padon 
O bipoNoner soNgge songSliShT byktira janano, borrtomane luNggir deSIy cahida barrShik pray dui kOTi pis. tobe romojan mase Ider age Sudhu jakater jonyi er cahida ony masogulOr tulonay pray dwiguN hoy. probasI bangladeSider jony ekosomoy olpobistor O porOkShovabe luNggi roptani holeO koyek bochor dhore ta sorasori roptani koroche koyekoTi protiShThan. luNggi ut''padon O bybosar Opor sunirrdiShT tothy-oporisongkhyan nei bole janan bybosayI O ut''padokera. tobe ta^der prakkolon holO, luNggi bybosay bochore ontot deR hajar kOTi Taka hat bodol hoy. khO^j niye jana geche, swadhInotar por ekosomoy keranIgoNGjer ruhitopuro, dOharo, nobabogoNGj O SrInogorer hostocalit ta^ter (ohyanDolumo) tOIri luNggi prosiddh chil. kintu cahida 
baRar soNgge soNgge zontrocalit ta^te (opaOyarolumo) luNggi tOIri Suru hoy. ete ut''padon beRe zay koyek guN. borrtomane pabona, siragoNGjer belokuci, Sahojadopuro, enayetopur O kuShTiyar kumarokhalIr zontrocalit ta^tei cahidar odhikangS luNggi tOIri hocche. sutir cek O prinTer luNggir paSapaSi karukaj kora jyakeT luNggi tOIri hocche deSe. esob luNggi ut''padon O bipoNonokarI protiShThaner songkhya dui Sotadhik. er modhye onek protiShThan Sudhu sthanIyovabe, orrthat'' oNGcolovittik ut''padon O bikri kore thake. tobe beSir vag protiShThanoi ta^t malikoder kache karryadeS diye luNggi tOIri koriye ane. taropor ete nijeder protIk lagiye bajarojat kore. luNggir soboceye boR paikari bajar bose siragoNGjer Sahojadopuro, norosingdIr baburohaT O TaNggailer koroTiyay. 
ekhan thekei sara deSer paikari bybosayIra luuNggi kine sthanIy bajare bikri koren. deR zug ageO sthanIyovabe name-obename bikri hotO luNggi. ekhon beS kichu luNggi ut''padonokarI protiShThan eTake tader brryanD hisebe da^R koranOr ceShTa koroche. bola zayo, koyekoTi brryanD nam hoye geche. esob brryanDer luNggi deSer cahida miTiye modhypracy, dokShiN afrika, varoto, SrIloNgka, indOneSiya, sOUdi arobosoh bivinn deSe roptani hocche. brryanDogulOr modhye amanot Saho, sTyanDarrDo, eTiem O onusondhan luNggi onytom. ekadhik luNggi bybosayI dabi koreno, eSiyar modhye soboceye valO maner luNggi bangladeSei tOIri hoy. purOnO Dhakar OItihybahI sada luNggi ekosomoy varot theke amodani kora hotO. tobe ekhon obosthar poriborrton hoyeche. deSei 
e luNggi tOIri korochen ut''padokera, emonoki ta varoteO roptani kora hocche. nam prokaS na korar Sorrte ekadhik bybosayI janano, bivinn deSer sorokar luNggi roptanite vorrtuki dey. bangladeSeO got bienopi sorokarer somoy luNggi roptanite 10 SotangS vorrtuki deOya hotO. kintu tottwabodhayok sorokar ta bondh kore dey. borrtoman mohajOT sorokaroO seTi bondh rekheche. ta^ra oboSy e-oO janano, baNijy montroNaloy pa^c SotangS vorrtuki deOyar aSwas diyeche. eTi bastobayit hole roptani aroO baRanO somvob bole mone koren ta^ra. deSer bybosayIder soNgge kotha bole jana geche, probasI baNgali chaRaO filipaino, barrma, SrIloNgka, vuTano, nepalo, siNggapur O jorrdaner bohu manuSher nitydiner pOSak luNggi. tobe sesob deSer 
luNggi guNogot mano, dhoron O nokoSa bangladeSi luNggir ceye vinn. tar poroO vinodeSi luNggi tOIri O roptani kore safoly dekhacche ekadhik protiShThan. ut''padok O bybosayIra boleno, got koyek bochore suta, rong, rasayonik drobysoh onyany samogrIr dam beReche. ete luNggir ut''padon khoroc prokarovede 50 theke 10o0 Taka porrynt beReche. onek bybosayI ta^t bondh kore dite badhy hoyechen. kintu sorokar biShoyoTi niye itibacok podokShep nicche na. luNggir brryanDo: 1983 sal theke helal oyanD bradarrs amanot Sah luNggi tOIri koroche. tobe 1993 sale theke TreDomarrk laisens niye sTyanDarrD luNggir brryanDing Suru kore protiShThanoTi. prothome sthanIy bajare bybosa koroleO 20o0o1 sal theke roptanite name 
protiShThanoTi. borrtomane tara dubai, maloyeSiya, SrIloNgka, varoto, sOUdi arobo, dokShiN afrika O Omane luNggi roptani koroche. got orrthobochore pray dui lakh pis luNggi roptani kore pa^c lakh marrkin Dolar ay kore protiShThanoTi. protiShThanoTi swtwadhikarI mO. helal miya prothom alOke boleno, deS O bideSer cahida onuzayI bivinn dhoroner amanot Sah luNggi tOIri hoy. tini aroO boleno, sirajogoNGjer belokuci, narayoNogoNGjer aRaihajaro, norosingdIr rayopura, munsigoNGjer lOUhojongye sthanIy ta^t bybosayIder kache karryadeS diye luNggi ut''padon hoy. pore nijosw karokhanay chappor diye mORokojat kora hoy. protiShThanoTi borrtomane mase pray ek lakh pis luNggi tOIri koroche. ar ete kaj korochen pray pa^c Sotadhik korrmokorrta-okorrmocarI. amanot Sah 
luNggir pisoproti mUly 60 theke Suru kore dui hajar Taka porrynt hoy. helal miya aroO boleno, guNogot man O nokoSar karoNe bideSe bangladeSi luNggir cahida ache. sorokar zodi roptanite vorrtuki O ut''padone bybohUt kemikyal Sulkomukt amodanir subidha deyo, tobe aroO beSi rajosw aday somvob. luNggi bybosar bivinn dik niye ta^ra ekoTi somIkSha poricalonar udyOg niyechen boleO janan helal miya. eTi somponn hole e poNyer bajar somporrke kichu sunirrdiShT dharoNa paOya somvob hobe bole mone koren tini. deSer luNggi bybosay arek brryanD eTiem luNggi. manosommot luNggi ut''padon O bipoNon kore sthanIy bajarer biSal ekoTi ongS dokhole niyeche protiShThanoTi. SrIloNgka, modhypracy, indOneSiya, 
thailyanD O afrikay roptani hocche eTiem luNggi. protiShThanoTite kaj korochen sohosradhik korrmI. pray 40 bochor dhore bybosa koroche onusondhan luNggi. ekhon bochore pray saRe tin lakh pis luNggi tOIri koroche e protiShThan. onusondhan luNggi pisoproti 225 theke ek hajar 20o0 Taka porrynt hoye thake. mUlot deSIy manuSher cahidar meTate tOIri holeO deSer baireO zacche onusondhan luNggi. bohu kShetre sorasori na holeO probasI bangladeSi O ony protiShThaner madhyme onusondhan luNggi modhypracye roptani hoy. protiShThanoTir swtwadhikarI mO. faruk boleno, âoamora mUlot sthanIy bajarer cahida onuzayI luNggi tOIri kori. bideSer bajar purOpuri dhorote parini. hate gOna koyekoTi protiShThan bideSe luNggi roptanite safoly dekhacche.â 
sirajogoNGjer ta^to: sara deSer pray orrdhek ta^toi sirajogoNGje. jelar bivinn upojelay hostocalit ta^ter songkhya pray aRai lakh ebong zontrocalit ta^t ache deR lakh. sirajogoNGjer belokuci, Sahojadopuro, ullapaRa O cOUhalI upojelar enayetopur thana elakatei ta^ter songkhya beSi. sthanIy pray 50 lakh lOk SilpoTir soNgge protykSho-oporOkShovabe joRit. ekhan thekei brryanD O brryanDobihIn luNggi ut''padonokarI protiShThanogulO cahida onuzayI karryadeS diye luNggi tOIri koray. proti duTi hostocalit ta^t calate ekojon lOk proyOjon. ar protiTi ta^t diye soptahe pray 40oTi luNggi tOIri kora somvob. luNggiproti ta^tider 20 theke 25 Taka mojuri deOya hoy. belokucir ta^t bybosayI abodul mojid aroO boleno, âoage 45 hajar Takay paOyarolum 
kinechi. got koyek bochore meSiner dam pray tin guN beReche. fole kShudr O majhari bybosayIra iccha thaka sottweO ta^ter songkhya baRate parochen na.â abodul mojid janano, matr 20 vag bybosayI byangkorriN pan. e kShetre byangkorriNo-oprokriya sohoj kora proyOjon. eTa kora hole ut''padon aroO baRanO somvob. jelar ta^t malik somitir sovapoti hayodar alI janano, ta^t malikera sorokari kOnO subidha pacchen na. pa^c bochor age prantik O kShudr ta^tider jony rriNer subidha thakoleO borrtomane ta bondh. hayodar alI aroO boleno, mOUsume ta^tider bybosa kichuTa cololeO ony somoye kShudr ta^t malikoder dadoner SoroNaponn hote hoy. jIboner tagide bybosayIra dadon babod Taka niye bybosa 
korote badhy hon. ete lav tO dUrer kotha, lOkosaner dikei zete hoy. belokuci upojelar ekoTi gram tamai. ekhanei pray 40o0 bybosayIr 10 hajar ta^t ache, zar 95 SotangS ta^tei luNggi tOIri kora hoy. esob tothy diye gramoTir onytom bybosayI fojolur rohoman boleno, ta^t bOrrDosoh sorokarer songSliShT doptorer sunojor O boR udyOktara egiye ele ei khatoTir prosar somvob. ta^t gobeShoNa protiShThaner poricalok mO. mObarok hOsen prothom alOke boleno, tula theke tOIri sutar soNgge krritrim suta bybohar korote hobe. er soNgge paTer sutar bybohar baRate hobe. Sudhu tular sutay ut''padon khoroc dwiguN hoy. ta^t malikeraO lavoban hote paren na. DisenT luNggir swtwadhikarI

suporicit. tini protiShThalogn thekei Dibieicer poricalona porrShoder sodosy hisebe dayitw palon korochen. bijNGopti. be empOriyamer notun dOkan calu Dhakay dhanomonDir rapa plajay somproti âobe empOriyamoâ Su sTOr udwOdhon kora hoyeche. be gruper ceyaromyan Samosur rohoman ebong be empOriyam limiTeDer prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta em e kader Su sTOroTir udwOdhon koren. sTOroTite puruSho, mohila O SiSuder jony bivinn Dijainer juta paOya zacche. bijNGopti. rriNokhelapider soNgge sOIyodopure rakaber motobinimoy rajoSahI krriShi unnoyon byangk (orakabo) somproti khelapi rriNogrohItader soNgge motobinimoy koreche. byangker sOIyodopur Sohor Sakhay onuShThit ei motobinimoy sovay pray 15 lakh Takar khelapi rriN aday hoyeche bole rakaber songSliShT korrmokorrtara janan. motobinimoy sovay 
onyanyer modhye byangker jOnal bybosthapok mohidul hok O sOIyodopur Sohor Sakhar bybosthapok Ochimuddin uposthit chilen. sovay khelapi rriNogrohItara ta^der khelapi hoOyar karoN byakhya koren ebong sud moOkufer dabi janan. e somoy ta^der e dhoroner somosyar somadhane proyOjonIy bybostha neOya hobe bole aSwst kora hoy. brriddh mot''syjIbI bijoy kumar ray khelapi rriNer Taka poriSOdh kore boleno, âodu:somoye byangk amader paSe thekeche, rriN diye amader swabolomwI hoOyar suzOg kore diyeche. oboSyi somoyomotO rriN poriSOdh kora protiTi nagoriker korrtoby.â siOyan komiunikeSon O kanekT sevener soNgge siTiseler cukti somojhOta smarok swakShor onuShThane siTiselo, kanekT seven O siOyan komiunikeSonoOyaner Urrdhwton korrmokorrtara siTisel somproti kanekT seven 
ebong siOyan komiunikeSonoOyaner soNgge ekoTi parosporik somojhOta smaroke soi koreche. siTiseler prodhan bikroy O bitoroN korrmokorrta mO. tarikul hasano, kanekT sevener arooyanDoDi prodhan SahInur Ti ai em nobI ebong siOyan komiunikeSonoOyaner prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta galIb ahomed anosarI nij nij protiShThaner pokShe ei somojhOta smaroke soi koren. onuShThane aroO uposthit chilen siTiseler prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta mehobub cOUdhurI, kanekT sevener ceyaromyan Ti ai em nurun nobI ebong siTiseler mohabybosthapok gOlam anojumanarul isolamo, jiyaur rohomanosoh protiShThanogulOr Urrdhwton korrmokorrtara uposthit chilen. bijNGopti. aisiebir antorrjatik sommelon udwOdhonokale prodhanomontrI sotota lalone sieder aroO zotnoSIl hote hobe prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina bolecheno, ain O niyontroNer madhyme sotota srriShTi 
kora zay na. sotota hocche byktigot sompod. e sompod laloner byapare carrTarrD oyakaunTyanToder (osie) aroO zotnoSIl hoOyar biShoye tini aSabad bykt korechen. prodhanomontrI aroO boleno, arrthik proSason ebong orrthonOItik bybosthaponar kShetre suShThu, jobabodihi oporiharry ebong unnoyon korrmokaNDe arrthik SrriNgkhola bidhane sorokar boddhoporikor. sorokari orrther hisaber jobabodihi, SrriNgkhola O nirIkShar jony sorokarer dik theke sob dhoroner podokShep neOyar kotha ullekh kore prodhanomontrI boleno, âojonogoNer koShTarrjit orrther opocoy ami byktigotovabe kOnO somoy borodaSot korini ebong vobiShyteO korob na.â gotokal rObobar rajodhanIr ekoTi hOTele inosTiTiuT ob carrTarrD oyakaunTyanToso, bangladeS (oaisiebi) ayOjit carrTarrD oyakaunTyanToder antorrjatik sommelono, 20o11-oer udwOdhonI onuShThane prodhanomontrI esob kotha bolen. e 
somoy prodhan otithi hisebe sommeloner udwOdhon ghOShoNa koren prodhanomontrI. e sommeloner protipady âoTekosoi unnoyoner jony sorrwOcc corrca O protibedonoâ. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit O baNijymontrI muhammod faruk khan onuShThane biSeSh otithi chilen. ete mUl probondh uposthapon koren sauth eSiyan feDareSon ob oyakaunTyanToser (osafa) sovapoti e en roâyaman. aisiebir sovapoti parovIn mahomuder sovapotitwe onuShThane swagot boktoby den sommelon ayOjok komiTir sovapoti O aisiebir sabek sovapoti Sekh e hafij ebong dhonybad boktoby den aisiebir sohosovapoti Sahadot hOsen. theke alOr pothe ebong goNotantrik Sasonobybosthay fire esechi. kintu goNotontrer safolyer jony proyOjon boliShTh O gotiSIl orrthonIti.â e jony sob SreNI-opeSar manuShoke udyOgI hoye deS goRar kaje atmoniyOg korote hobe ullekh kore prodhanomontrI aroO boleno, âoami biSwas kori, byangko, kor proSasono, bideSi biniyOg O pu^jibajarer songskar korote parole jatIy probrriddhi aroO baRobe.â prodhanomontrI boleno, hisabobijNGan O nirIkSha peSar soNgge orrthonItir ghoniShTh zOgosUtr royeche. biSeSh kore, swcchota, jobabodihi O suShThu arrthik bybosthapona niScit korote ei peSajIbIder obodan onoswIkarry. tader protibedoner madhymei fuTe OThe ekoTi protiShThaner ayo-obyyo, day O sompoder khotiyan. carrTarrD oyakaunTyanToder uddeSe Sekh hasina boleno, âoaponader Opor zate manuSher asthar

Seyarobajare proNOdona gucch sufol pete kichu somoy lagobe Seyarobajare sthitiSIlota firiye anote ghOShit proNOdona bajare itibacok provab felobe bole mone koren bajar biSleShok O songSliShT byktira. e jony 
kichuTa somoyer proyOjon royeche bole ovimot ta^der. ar tai biniyOgokarIder dhOIrry dharoN koraroO poramorrS diyechen ta^ra. proNOdonay byangkogulOke zesob subidha deOya hoyeche, segulOr bastobayone bangladeS byangk got brrihospotibaroi projNGapon jari kore. esob subidhar fole Seyarobajare byangkogulOr biniyOg sokShomota onekoTai baRobe bole mone kore oyasOsiyeSon ob byangkarrs bangladeS (oebibi). bangladeS byangk janiyeche, Seyar bybosay niyOjit byangkogulO tader sohozOgI protiShThane ze mUlodhon jOgan diyeche, ekhon theke ta ar Oi byangker aini biniyOg sImar hisabe dhora hobe na. emonoki kOnO kOmpanir Seyare byangker dIrrghomeyadi biniyOgokeO aini sImar baire rakha hobe. zOgazOg kora hole ebibir sovapoti O siTi byangker bybosthapona poricalok ke mahomud sattar

Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sovapoti Sakil rijovI boleno, proNOdonar sufol

ekhon ucit grahoker prantik rriNer (omarrjin lOno) nirrvorota komiye dIrrghomeyadi mUlodhoni biniyOg baRanO. e jony biniyOgokarI O rriNodata protiShThaner modhye zOUth biniyOg skim calu kora zete pare. somoporimaN mUlodhon biniyOg O munafa vagavagir madhyme ei skim calu korole biniyOgokarIder jhu^ki onekangSe komobe. paSapaSi marrcenT byangkogulOr jony ovinn suder har nirrdharoN O ta zOUktik porryaye namiye anar supariS koren tini. tini janano, ekodike esob protiShThan seba maSulosoh nana name ucc hare sud nicche, paSapaSi lenodener komiSon thekeO munafa koroche. bangladeS marrcenT byangkarrs oyasOsiyeSoner (obiemobie) sovapoti mOhammod e hafij boleno, âoSeyarobajare byangkogulOr biniyOger kShetre zesob suzOg deOya hoyeche, ta niye vulo-obOjhabujhir ar

cay. esob kShetrer bidyman somosya Sigogir somadhan hobe bole montrI protinidhidoloke aSwst koren. protinidhidoler prodhan karrl arrnesT brOnar baNijymontrIr kache pakistanoke jiesopi subidha deOyar biShoye bangladeSer obosthan janote can. montrI jobabe boleno, âobonyadurrgot hoOyay pakistaner proti amader sohanuvUti ache. tobe manobik sohayota O baNijy miliye fela Thik hobe na.â protinidhidole fraNgkofurrT komarrs byangker poricalona porrShoder sodosy marrkas barrnaro, amman gruper ceyaromyan buDO bajolo, Oyelohem ji klasen kOmpanir swtwadhikarI piTori klasenosoh 14 jon bybosayI uposthit chilen. e somoy baNijysocib mO. gOlam hOsenoO uposthit chilen. boR protiShThane swyongkriyovabe mUsoker hisab rakhote hobe mUly songzOjon kor (omUsoko) prodano-oprokriya sohoj korote hisab songrokShoNer jony 
boR boR protiShThanoke jatIy rajosw bOrrD (oenobiaro) onumOdit sofoToOyyar bybohar korote hobe. agamI januyari mas theke e niyom calu hobe. mUsok fa^ki rOdhe e podokShep neOya hoyeche. tobe protiShThan O sofoToOyyar nirrwaconosoh onyany anuShoNggik karrykrom poricalonar jony enobiarer ekhonO zotheShT prostuti nei. enobiar oboSy unnot maner sofoToOyyar nirrwaconer kaj Suru koreche. enobiarer korrmokorrtader soNgge alap kore jana geche, boR boR protiShThaner hisab songrokShoNojonit truTir jony bipul porimaN mUsok theke boNGcit hocche enobiar. procolit orrthe khata-okolome mUsoko-osongkrant hisab rakha hoy. fole mUsok fa^kir proboNota beRe geche. e rokom prekShapoTe coloti bochorer 29 jun ek adeSe ek bochore 50 lakh Taka ba 
tar odhik orrth mUsok diyeche emon protiShThanoke enobiaro-onirrdharit sofoToOyyare mUsoko-osongkrant doliladi O hisabopotr rokShoNabekShoNer badhybadhokota arOp kora hoyeche. tobe boR protiShThanogulO nirrwacon korobe songSliShT komiSonareT karryaloy. enobiar sUtrogulO boloche, coloti orrthobochorer prothom pa^c mase kOn kOn sofoToOyyar protiShThanogulO bybohar korote hobe, ta nirrdharoN korote pareni enobiar. fole onek udyOkta ta^der bybosaprotiShThane sofoToOyyar sonnibeSon korote parochen na. abar alOcy somoye enobiar kOn kOn protiShThanoke sofoToOyyar bybohar korote hobe, ta-oO nirrwacon kore deyoni. edike, sofoToOyyar nirrwaconer jony vyaT O eksaij (oDhaka dokShiNo) komiSonareTer komiSonar abodul kafIke ahwayok kore ekoTi komiTi goThon kora hoyeche. e komiTi sofoToOyyar nirrmaN O soroborahokarI nirrwacon korobe. e 
jony Sigogir doropotr ahwan kora hobe bole jana geche. enobiarer sodosy (omUsoko) foridouddin prothom alOke janano, swyongkriyo-obybosthay hisab songrokShoN hole mUsok fa^kir proboNota kome zabe. abar protiShThanogulOr hisab rakhoteO subidha hobe. borrtomane sara deSe 60 hajar protiShThan mUsok diye thake. er modhye koyek hajar protiShThan 50 lakh Takar beSi mUsok dey bole jana geche. sabomerin kebol kOmpani asobe Seyarobajare agamI bochorer Surutei bangladeS sabomerin kebol kOmpani limiTeDoke (obiesosisielo) Seyarobajare niye asa hobe bole janalen TelizOgazOgosocib O biesosisieler ceyaromyan sunIl kanti bOs. sunIl kanti bOs boleno, TelizOgazOgo-osongSliShT pa^c kOmpanir modhye protiShThar por thekei biesosisiel zotheShT lavojonok obosthay royeche ebong sorokaroke soboceye

pore ta UrrdhwmukhI hoy. din SeShe Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok 113 poyenT beRe pa^c hajar 268 poyenTe giye da^Riyeche. kom. efobisisiaiyer sova: Seyarobajare sthitiSIlota anote sorokar ghOShit proNOdona gucch bastobayoner lokShye kaj kora hobe bole janiyechen Seyarobajar niye goThit efobisisiaiyer sTyanDing komiTir ceyaromyan mO. rokibur rohoman. gotokal bikele motijhiler feDareSon voboner sommelonokokShe komiTir ek bOIThok SeShe tini esob kotha bolen. rokibur rohoman boleno, âoghOShit proNOdona gucch bastobayoner kichu supariS tOIri korechi. O ceyaromyano: prostabit modhumoti byangker ceyaromyan hisebe nam royeche humayun kobIrer. kintu sUtrogulO boloche, er onytom udyOkta poricalok hisebe royechen aOyamI lIgodolIy sangsod fojole nUr tapos. prostabit meghona byangker ceyaromyan hisebe royechen aOyamI lIgodolIy kOShadhykSh eic en aSikur rohoman. sorokari protiShThanosongkrant songsodIy sthayI komiTir ceyaromyan mohIuddIn khan alomogIrer prostabit byangker nam farrmaros byangk. prostabit pipolos byangker ceyaromyan hocchen sangsod khondokar asadujjaman. dy pipolos byangker prostabit ceyaromyan hocchen mirrja ajom. prostabit miDolyanD byangker ceyaromyan hocchen monirujjaman khan khondokar. prostabit selof emoployomenT byangker ceyaromyan hisebe nam ache mahobuba kobIrer. sUtrogulO boloche, ei byangker mUl udyOkta holen jatIy odhyapok kobIr cOUdhurI. biSiShT bybosayI 
neta O enovoy gruper ceyaromyan kutubouddin ahomeder prostabit byangker nam hocche glObal byangk. enojiO byktitw odhyapika hOsone ara begomer prostabit byangker nam Tiemoesoes kShudr pu^ji byangk. biarobi kebloser mojibur rohomaner prostabit byangker nam rural inovesTomenT byangk. em e haSemer prostabit byangker nam feDarel byangk. niTol gruper ceyaromyan abodul matolub ahomader prostabit byangker nam hocche koTok bangla byangk. sabek orrthosocib motiul isolam ceyaromyan hisebe inofrasTrakocaral DevelopomenT byangker jony abedon korechen. byangk ba arrthik protiShThan theke rriN niye khelapi hoye thakole tini byangker udyOkta hisebe abedon korote paroben na. kOnO adalot ba Traibyunale khelapisongkrant kOnO byktir mamola bicaradhIn thakole tiniO udyOkta hote paroben na. Seyarobajare poramorrS diye karagare kOTipoti hote ta^ke ghorer baire zete hoyoni, korote hoyoni koThOr kOnO poriSrom. nijer beDorume bose OyebosaiTe Seyar kenabecar poramorrS diye matr 21 bochore boyosei 15 lakh paunD uparrjon korechen zuktorajyer norrth TenisaiDer huiToli be Sohorer toruN alekojanDar hanTar. tobe SeSh rokSha hoyoni. obOIdhovabe poramorrS deOyar ovizOge ta^ke aTok koreche puliS. matr 16 bochor boyose zuktoraShTrer Seyarobajar theke kIvabe dwiguN lav kora zay biniyOgokarIderoke 
sei poramorrS deOyar jony 20o0o7 sale ekoTi OyebosaiT khOlen hanTar. hajar hajar biniyOgokarIO sei poramorrS neOyar jony humoRi kheye poRe ta^r OyebosaiTe. e jony nirrdiShT ekoTi orrth niten hanTar. eropor ar pechon fire takate hoyoni hanTaroke. tin bochore sei ayer porimaN 15 lakh paunDeroO beSi. tobe biniyOgokarIder kach theke protaroNa kore e orrth neOyar ovizOge ta^ke aTok koreche puliS. zuktorajyer fainyansiyal sarrvises oyanD marrkeTing oyakTo-o20o0o0 onuzayI obOIdh bybosa O protaroNa korar ovizOge hanTar ekhon ovizukt. e mamolar Sunani SeShe adalot ta^ke ek bochorer karadoND O protaroNa kore hatiye neOya orrth ferot deOyar adeS diyechen. hanTar Sudhu ze biniyOgokarIder orrth dwiguN 
korar poramorrS diteno, ta kintu noy. nijeO Seyar bybosar soNgge joRit chilen. buddhi khaTiye Seyar kenar poramorrS diten biniyOgokarIder. ar zokhonoi odhik laver aSay Seyar kenar jony biniyOgokarIra chuToteno, omoni nijer kine rakha SeyarogulO toRighoRi kore bece diten hanTar. fole biniyOgokarIder bodole dwiguN lav hotO hanTareroi. eroporoi naTokIyovabei kome zet nirrdiShT Seyarer dam. ekoporryaye biniyOgokarIra biShoyoTi zuktoraShTrer sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSoner nojore ane. eropor poroi ta^ke aTok kore adalote paThay puliS. e prosoNgge puliS korrmokorrta jim myakol bolecheno, âoonolainer madhyme e dhoroner ghoTona ghoTanOr karoNe, ta todont koraTa khuboi koThin hoye da^Ray. zuktoraShTrer korrtrripokSher soNgge biShoyoTi niye kaj koray amora 
hanTarer basa khu^je pai ebong ta^ke aTok kori. ekhon tini ta^r krritokorrmer folafol vOg korochen.â âohanTar skuler ony chatroder ceye onek cotur chilen. tini ta^r OyebosaiTer madhymei e orrth uparrjon kore khub gorrw onuvob koroten. kintu hanTarer e biShoyoTike sobai moja hisebe dhore niyechil. tai keui hanTarer kotha biSwas koreni, pattaO deyoni.â gotokal rate emonoTai bolochilen hanTarer ek protibeSI. tobe soboceye obak hoOyar biShoy poribarer sobar soNgge bosobas koroleO keu hanTarer protaroNar biShoyoTi ghuNakShoreO Ter payoni.âoDeili meil onolain obolomwne. bajar baRanOr dike jhu^keche Teri TaOyel choy bochor age roptani baNijye 10 kOTi Dolarer mailofolok otikrom korar por valOvabei ogrosor hocchil 
khatoTi. bideSe roptanir probrriddhiO chil sontOShojonok. kintu got 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore ese boR dhoroner dhakka khay ogrozatra. 20o0o9-o10 orrthobochorer tulonay roptani kome zay saRe 23 SotangS. mUlot got bochorer majhamajhite antorrjatik bajare sutar dam oswavabik beRe zaOyar netibacok provabe emonoTi ghoTeche bole janan u t''padok O roptanikarokera. ta^der ovizOgo, onek spining miler malik tokhon suta varote pacar kore den. ete cahidamotO suta na paOyay TaOyel bybosayIder lOkosan gunote hoy. e somoy pray deSer 50 SotangS protiShThan u t''padon bondh kore dite badhy hoy. fole swavabikovabei got orrthobochore khatoTi roptani ayer lokShymatra orrjone byrrth hoy. tobe ei dhara theke beriye asar ceShTa 
korochen TeriTaOyel prostutokarok O roptanikarokera. e jony ta^ra sutar niyomit jOgan niScit korar Opor jOr dicchen. ar Sudhu bideSer bajar noyo, deSIy bajareO u t''padokoder monOzOg baRoche. karryt deSer TaOyeler cahidar odhikangSoi sthanIy u t''padokera meTan. sompUrrN deSIy ka^camal nirrvor hoOyay er sthanIy mUly songzOjoner haroO onek beSi. bangladeS roptani unnoyon byurOr (oipibi) tothyanuzayI, 20o0o3-o0o4 orrthobochor theke 20o0o9-o10 orrthobochor porrynt ei khater roptani aye sorrwnimn choy theke sorrwOcc 88 SotangS probrriddhi hoyeche. got noyoTi orrthobochorer modhye 20o0o9-o10 orrthobochorei Teri TaOyel roptani kore sorrwOcc 15 kOTi 70 lakh Dolar ay hoyeche. za ager bochorer 13 kOTi 25 lakh Dolarer ceye 18 
doSomik 48 SotangS beSi. ipibir tothymote, 20o0o7-o0o8 orrthobochorer ei khater roptani ay chil 11 kOTi 28 lakh Dolar. za ager orrthobochorer 10 kOTi 95 lakh Dolarer ceye 32 doSomik 23 SotangS beSi. tobe roptani aye soboceye beSi 88 doSomik 30 SotangS probrriddhi hoy 20o0o3-o0o4 orrthobochore. Oi orrthobochorer pa^c kOTi 75 lakh Dolar roptani ay hoy. 20o0o2-o0o3 orrthobochore zekhane ei ay chil matr dui kOTi 96 lakh Dolar. bybosayIra janano, deSe borrtomane Sopo, batho, golofo, bico, glaso, Ti TaOyelo, flOr myaTo, hoj ehoramo, nyapokinosoh 30 theke 35 dhoroner Teri TaOyel poNy tOIri hocche. esob poNyer boR bajar amerika. e chaRa iurOpiyan 
iuniyonovukt sob deSo, kanaDa, osTreliya O japane roptani hocche. deSer senabahinI, nOUbahinI O bimanobahinI nijeder byboharer jony bipul porimaN Teri TaOyel deSIy u t''padokoder kach theke karryadeS diye kroy kore thake. khO^j niye jana zayo, 1988 sale coTTogramer ipijeDe sorrwprothom glObal febrikos praiveT limiTeD namer ekoTi protiShThan Teri TaOyel tOIri Suru kore. pore 1990 sal theke roptanite zay protiShThanoTi. biSw bajare byapok cahida thakay O sompUrrN deSIy ka^camaler karoNe kaler biborrtone khatoTite biniyOg koren onek udyOkta. borrtomane coTTogram chaRaO Dhaka, narayoNogoNGjo, rUpogoNGjo, ToNggI, gajIpuro, savaro, kaliyakOIro, SrIpurosoh bivinn elakay Teri TaOyel tOIrir karokhana goRe uTheche. egulOr odhikangS purOpuri roptanimukhI holeO 
deSIy bajare soroborah korochen keu keu. bangladeS Teri TaOyel oyanD linen myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSoner (obiTiTieloemoie) tothy onuzayI, sara deSe Sotadhik protiShThan Teri TaOyel u t''padon koroche. er modhye oyasOsiyeSoner nibondhit protiShThaner songkhya 76. biTiTieloemoie er socib mO. mujibur rohoman prothom alOke boleno, sara deSe protidin sommilitovabe pray aRai S Ton Teri TaOyel u t''padon hocche. khatoTir soNgge bivinn porryaye pray orrdh lakh manuSh joRit achen. mujibur rohoman aroO janano, deSei Teri TaOyel tOIri hoOyay bideS theke amodani bondh hoyeche. karoN Teri TaOyel amodani korole 35 SotangS vyaT dite hoy. oboSy guTikoyek osadhu bybosayI deSe tOIri TaOyele bivinn deSer silo-ochappor 
mere bikri kore. biSwer soboceye boR TaOyel amodanikarok amerikar cahidar pray 65 SotangS jOgan dey varoto, cIn O pakistan. tobe bangladeSoO bajar pacche. poNyer man valO hoOyay somproti maloyeSiya theke bipul porimaN karryadeS paOya zacche. japan thekeO onek kreta deSe ese khO^jokhobor nicchen bole janan bybosayIra. tobe ekadhik u t''padok boleno, Teri TaOyeler prodhan ka^camal OyesT koTon (ojhuT suta) cahida onuzayI soroborah paOyai khatoTir boR somosya. borrtomane deSer spining milogulOi ei sutar jOgan dey. tobe onek somoy cahida onuzayI suta soroborah koren na sthanIy bybosayIra. abar antorrjatik bajare dam baRar soNgge soNgge deSer bybosayIra sutar dam baRiye den. ipibir tothyanuzayI, 
20o10o-o11 orrthobochore Teri TaOyel roptani ay hoy 12 kOTi Dolaro, za ager orrthobochorer 15 kOTi 70 lakh Dolarer ceye 23 doSomik 52 SotangS kom. coloti orrthobochorer prothom car mase (ojulai-ookTOboro) ei khater roptani ayer lokShymatra chil tin kOTi 88 lakh Dolar. tobe ay hoyeche tin kOTi 29 lakh marrkin Dolar. za got orrthobochorer ekoi somoyer car kOTi 75 lakh Dolarer ceye ta pray 30 doSomik 80 SotangS kom. khO^j niye jana zayo, songkoTokalIn somoye bybosayIder denodorobare SeSh porrynt sorokar proti paunD OyesT koTon car Dolar 60 senT mUly nirrdharoN kore dey. age ei dam chil dui Dolar 20 senT. ekoi 
soNgge sorokar suta roptanite 25 SotangS Sulk arOp kore. abar got sepTemwr theke antorrjatik bajareO sutar dam komote Suru kore. biTiTieloemoier ceyaromyan mOhammod anisujjaman prothom alOke boleno, sorokari siddhanter karoNe suta pacar bondh hoyeche. fole bajare ekhon mOTamuTi sthitiSIlota eseche. sutar dam ekhonokar motO sthitiSIl thakole bochor SeShe roptani ayer lokShymatra ebar ar byrrth hobe na. mOhammod anisujjaman aroO boleno, sutar dam baRoleO bybosayIra sei onupate TaOyeler dam baRate paren na. amerikar kretara nijerai hisab koShe ekoTa u t''padon khoroc be^dhe den. e chaRa antorrjatik bajare parrSwborrtI deSogulOr soNgge protizOgita tO achei. sutar soroborah swavabik rakhar jony sat theke 20 
kaunTer suta Teri TaOyel bybosayIder sorasori amodanir suzOg deOya proyOjon bole mone koren tini. oyasOsiyeSoner siniyor vais ceyaromyan je e anosarI prothom alOke boleno, sorokar tOIri pOSak khater motO Teri TaOyeleO pa^c SotangS nogod sohayota dey. kintu sompUrrN deSIy ka^camalonirrvor SilpoTite zodi 10 theke 15 SotangS hare nogod sohayota deOya proyOjon. ekoi soNgge Teri TaOyaloke alada khat hisebe bibecona korar dabi janan tini. je e anosari aroO boleno, bigot koyek bochore boR boR udyOkta khatoTite biniyOg korechen. ekhon cahidamotO bidyu t'', gyas O sutar soroborah niScit kora gele protiShThanogulO koyek guN u t''padon baRate parobe. ete Teri TaOyal khate Sotovag 
probrriddhi somvob. santahare adhunik prozuktir calokol udwOdhon boguRar adomodIghi upojelar santaharer bagobaRIte mOU oyagrO oyarOmeTik oTOmeTik rais milos namer adhunik prozuktir ekoTi calokol udwOdhon kora hoyeche. poribeS O bon montroNaloyosongkrant songsodIy sthayI komiTir sovapoti abodul mOmin talukodar somproti calokoloTir udwOdhon koren. udwOdhonI onuShThane boktoby den marrkenTail byangker bybosthapona poricalok (oemoDi) e ke em Sohidul hok O DiemoDi abodul jolilo, aisibir mohabybosthapok ifotekhar uj jaman O upomohabybosthapok nasorin sulotana, bangladeS byangker mohabybosthapok sirajul isolamo, adomodIghi upojelar nirrwahI korrmokorrta mijanur rohoman mOlla, mOU oyagrO oyarOmeTik oTOmeTik rais miloser emoDi nurul isolamo, noOga^ jela dhano-ocal aRotodar O bybosayI somitir sovapoti nIrod boroN saha, 
sadharoN sompadok mO. akobor alI mOlla, Thakuroga^O cemwarer sovapoti mahomud hasan ebong noOga^ cemwarer sabek jyeShTh sohosovapoti noOSer alI promukh. Thakuroga^Oye marrkenTail byangker Sakha udwOdhon marrkenTail byangker ceyaromyan sangsod mO. abdul jolil somproti Thakuroga^Oye byangker 67tom Sakha udwOdhon koren Thakuroga^Oyer aSromopaRay kolej rODer afosar uddin cOUdhurI plajay marrkenTail byangk limiTeDer 67tom Sakha khOla hoyeche. byangker ceyaromyan sangsod mO. abdul jolil prodhan otithi hisebe somproti SakhaTir udwOdhon koren. udwOdhonI onuShThane byangker poricalok e ke em sahid reja, bybosthapona poricalok O prodhan nirrwahI e ke em SohIdul hoko, upobybosthapona poricalok cOUdhurI mOstak ahomed ebong notun SakhaTir prodhan mO. hojorot alIsoh Urrdhwton korrmokorrtara 
uposthit chilen. onuShThane aroO boktoby den Thakuroga^O upojela ceyaromyan sulotanul ferodOUs cOUdhurI, vais ceyaromyan aSoraful hok cOUdhurI ebong Thakuroga^O cemwar ob komarrser sovapoti mO. mahomud hasan raju. itibacok dharay pu^jibajar aj budhobar lenodener Surute sUcok osthir thakoleO SeSh porrynt itibacok dhara fire ase deSer pu^jibajare. din SeShe Dhaka sTok eksoceNGje (oDiesoi) sUcok 113 poyenT baRe. soNgge beReche lenoden hoOya dui Sotadhik protiShThaner Seyarer dam. edike doropoton Thekate ajoO Diesoir todaroki dol bajare sokriy chil bole Diesoi sUtre jana geche. doloTi bivinn brOkarej hause giye doropoton Thekate sokriy thake. fole Surute sUcok nimnomukhI thakoleO pore UrrdhwmukhI hoy bole mone korochen bajaro-osongSliShT 
byktira. Diesoir OyebosaiT sUtre jana zayo, din SeShe Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok 113 poyenT beRe 5268 poyenTe da^Riyeche. sUcoker nimnomukhI proboNotar modhy diye aj Diesoite lenoden Suru hoy. pa^c miniTer mathay sUcok gotokaler ceye 25 poyenT kome zay. tobe 15 miniTer mathay sUcok baRe 17 poyenT. eropor abaroO nimnomukhI hoy sUcok. bela saRe 11Tar dike sUcok kome zay 16 poyenT. er por theke sUcok baRote Suru kore, za sara dinoi obyahot thake. aj Diesoite mOT 260oTi protiShThaner Seyar O miucuyal fanDer lenoden hoyeche. er modhye 240oTiroi dam beReche. komeche 16Tir ar oporiborrtit royeche caroTi protiShThaner Seyarer dam. sTok eksoceNGjoTite aj 319

bangladeS byangke pa^c bochor meyadi sorokari Trejari bonDer 50o0 kOTi Takar nilam hoy. e kShetre ontorrnihit suder har 8 doSomik 50 SotangSe oporiborrtit thake. sUtro: siTibyangk enoe, bangladeS. baTeksopOr udwOdhonI onuShThane prodhanomontrI sorokar daridrryer har 21 SotangSe namiye anote kaj koroche rajodhanIr boNggobondhu antorrjatik sommelon kendre baTeksopO-o20o11 anuShThanikovabe udwOdhoner por pOSakopoNy dekhochen prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina bolecheno, krriShi O Silp khater unnoyoner madhyme ta^r sorokar car bochorer modhye daridrryer har 31 doSomik 5 SotangS theke 21 doSomik 5 SotangSe namiye anote nirolosovabe kaj kore zacche. gotokal Sonibar tin dinobyapI 22tom bangladeS oyaparel oyanD TeksoTail eksopOjiSoner (obaTeksopO-o20o11) udwOdhonI onuShThane 
prodhanomontrI esob kotha bolen. tini boleno, âodaridrry hraser lokShy orrjone sorokar pOSakoSilper bikaSe sob dhoroner sohozOgita dite prostut.â khobor basos O iuenobir. prodhanomontrI Sromikoder kolyaNe aroO podokShep neOyar jony tOIri pOSak O bostr khater udyOktader proti ahwan janiye boleno, Sromiko-omalik susomporrk bojay thakole sorrwOcc ut''padon orrjon somvob. ete maliko-oSromik uvoyei lavoban hoben. boNggobondhu antorrjatik sommelon kendre ayOjit udwOdhonI onuShThane onyanyer modhye paT O bostromontrI abodul lotif siddikI, sthanIy sorokaro, pollI unnoyon O somobayomontrI sOIyod aSoraful isolamo, SilpomontrI dilIp boRuya, baNijymontrI ji em kadero, besamorik biman O porryTonomontrI faruk khano, nOUporibohonomontrI Sajahan khan promukh boktrrita koren. bijiemoier sovapoti saiful isolam mohiuddiner 
sovapotitwe onuShThane prothom sohosovapoti nasir uddin cOUdhurI O dwitIy sohosovapoti em siddikur rohomanoO boktrrita koren. besorokari khater somprosaroNe notun SilponIti proNoyoner kotha ullekh kore prodhanomontrI boleno, ekhane 21Ti khatoke thrasT sekTor hisebe cihnit kora hoyeche. Silpoke ut''sahit korote orrthonOItik oNGcol sthaponer udyOg neOya hoyeche. bangladeS itimodhyei varoto, cIno, maloyeSiya, japan O dokShiN kOriyay Sulkomukt roptani-osubidha pacche. pOSak roptanikarokoder somoy O orrther saSroyer jony bijiemoieke ut''ser deS theke sonod isyu korar kShomota deOya hoyeche ullekh kore Sekh hasina boleno, ei prothom deSer 270oTi rugN O bondh tOIri pOSak karokhanar rriN hisebe tarolyer bybostha neOya hoyeche. bonD laisens nobayoner somoyosIma baRanO hoyeche. 
prodhanomontrI boleno, âoTeksoTail O tOIri pOSak khater unnoyonoke amora boraboroi ogradhikar diye asochi.â roptanimukhI poNyer drut zatayat niScit korote deSer zOgazOgobybostha O bondorer unnoyone ta^r sorokarer grrihIt bivinn podokSheper ullekh kore prodhanomontrI boleno, soRoko, nOU O rel zOgazOgobybosthar drut unnoti hocche. coTTogram O mongla bondorer dokShota baRanO hoyeche. konoTeinar O karrgO hyanDoling karrykromoke oTOmeSon kora hoyeche. Dhaka-ocoTTogram mohasoRok car lene unnIt kora hocche. Dhakay eliveTeD eksopresoOye O uRalosoRok nirrmit hocche. Sekh hasina boleno, Dhaka O coTTogram ipijeDoke somprosaroN ebong aroO choyoTi ipijeD sthaponer paSapaSi besorokari khate ipijeD protiShThar jony ain kore coTTograme ekoTi besorokari ipijeD protiShTha kora hoyeche, za theke 
borrtomane poNy roptani hocche. deSer 36 lakh pOSakoSromiker kolyaNe grrihIt bivinn podokShep grohoNer ullekh kore prodhanomontrI boleno, ta^der swasthy-osocetonota brriddhi O sontanoder lekhapoRar suzOg srriShTi, aSuliyay Sromikoder abasoner udyOg ebong reSoning-obybostha calu kora hoyeche. ta^r sorokar Sromikoder nyUnotom mojuri ek hajar 662 Taka theke baRiye tin hajar Takay unnIt koreche. prodhanomontrI 20o21 saler modhye bangladeSoke ekoTi modhym ayer deSe poriNot korote ekozOge kaj korar ahwan janan. bybosayIder motoke gurutw diye mUsok ain cURant hobe hoyoranisoh sob dhoroner somosya somadhane bybosayIder motamotoke gurutw diyei prostabit mUly songzOjon kor (omUsoko) ainoTi cURant kora hobe. e chaRa bikolp birOdh niShpottite zOUth pyanele bybosayI 
protinidhiO ontorrvukt kora hobe. ete korodatara nyayobicar paben. gotokal Sonibar prostabit mUsok ain niye onuShThit ek korrmoSalay jatIy rajosw bOrrDer (oenobiaro) ceyaromyan nasirouddin ahomed esob kotha bolen. Dhaka cemwar ob komarrs oyanD inDasTri (oDisisiai)o, inTaronyaSonal finyans koropOreSon (oaiefosi) ebong polisi risarrc inosTiTiuT (opiaroai) zOUthovabe e korrmoSalar ayOjon kore. Dhaka cemwar milonayotone e korrmoSala onuShThit hoy. ullekhy, agamI januyari mas theke bikolp birOdh niShpottibybostha calu korote zacche enobiar. ete korodatara mamola-omOkoddomay na giye bikolp birOdh niShpottir madhyme aposorofa korote paroben. tobe enobiarer ceyaromyan janano, bikolp birOdh niShpotti korote sob pokSher protinidhi chaRaO prothom tin maser jony aiefosi theke ekojon sohayotakarI niyOg 
korote pare enobiar. tini aroO boleno, enobiar boR dhoroner swyongkriy ba oTOmeSon bybosthay zacche. amodanikarokoder subidharrthe agamI januyari theke coTTogram kasTomos hause (oamodani) rat 10oTa porrynt byangking seba calu rakha hobe. enobiarer ceyaromyan janano, bybosayI somprodayer motamoter vittitei mUsok ain proNoyon kora hobe. tini boleno, deSe ekoTi bybosabandhob poribeS srriShTi korar lokShye enobiar kaj kore zacche. tini kor nItimalar soNgge samoNGjosy-opUrrNovabe proSasonik obokaThamO punorrgoThoner Opor jOr den. korrmoSalay Disisiaiyer sovapoti asif ibrahIm boleno, mUsok ainer mUl lokShy holOâokor prodano-oprokriya sohojIkoroNo, tothy O prozuktinirrvor kor prodano-obybostha calukoroN ebong âokyasokeDing ifekToâ eRanO. tini rajoswbandhob ebong bybosay vyaTobandhob bybostha calu korar Opor gurutwarOp
