somvob. gotokal rObobar hOTel sOnaroga^Oye poribeSobandhob saSroyI mUlyer iT tOIrir prozukti SIrrShok korrmoSalay jwalani biSeShojNGora esob kotha bolen. bangladeSe obosthit brajil dUtabaso, jarrmanovittik unnoyon songstha jiaijeD ebong besorokari songstha onweSha grup ei korrmoSalar ayOjon kore. ï»¿ kreDiT karrD curir ghoTonay greptar carojon rimanDe DakozOge asa kreDiT karrD curir soNgge joRit sondehe greptar hoOya carojonoke dui diner rimanDe niyeche Dhaka mohanogor gOyenda puliS (oDibi). gotokal Sonibar eder adalote hajir kore 10 diner rimanDer abedon janale adalot protyeker dui diner rimanD moNGjur koren. gOyenda puliSer korrmokorrtara janano, prathomik jijNGasabade carojonoi swIkar korecheno, guloSan Dakoghorer piyon abodur robo, roSId O jalal DakozOge asa 
kreDiT karrD bitoroN na kore bikri kore diten. sUtr janayo, kreDiT karrD curir ghoTonay puliS guloSan Dakoghorer piyon abodur robo, kamal ahomed Orofe nUrul amino, ta^r sohozOgI rasel ahomed ebong anOyar hOsenoke greptar kore. greptarer por jijNGasabade Dakopiyon abodur rob Dibir jijNGasabade janano, DakozOge asa parrsel theke kreDiT karrD pelei segulO nibondhon khatay na likhe nijer kache rekhe diten tini. pore esob karrD nurul aminer kache 10 hajar Taka kore bikri koroten. Dibir jyeShTh sohokarI komiSonar moSiur rohoman janano, e cokrer neta nurul amin Dak bivager korrmocarIder kach theke kreDiT karrD kine arek sodosy raseloke diten. rasel esob karrD karrDer 
malik seje Dhaka O coTTogramer bivinn bipoNibitan theke ilekoTronikoso-osamogrI O asobabopotr kinoten. pore esob jinisopotr 10 theke 15 SotangS komiSone bikri koren. greptar hoOya nurul amin janano, kreDiT karrD diye ta^ra deSe O deSer baire theke tOIri pOSak O prosadhonI kine Dhakar namokora dOkane bikri koroten. ï»¿ bOIdeSik ay diye byy miToche na samal deOya zacche na bOIdeSik khat. ay diye byy miToche na. tai hisab melate himoSim khete hocche sorokaroke. protidinoi komoche bideSi mudrar mojud (orijarrvo). baRoche Dolarer dam. ar er provabe mUlysfItir Opor cap baRoche. got choy bochorer beSi somoy dhore coloti khater ayo-obyye chil udwrritt. kintu gel 
okTObor maser hisabe dekha zacche, sekhaneO ekhon ghaToti. ete oswstite poRechen nItinirrdharokera. besamorik biman colacol O porryTonomontrI faruk khaner (osody sabek baNijymontrI) netrritwe ekodol bybosayI got june afrikay krriShijomi kinote mUlodhon akare deS theke bideSi mudra niye zete byapok tot''porota caliyechilen. tokhon bola hocchilo, bangladeS byangk netibacok drriShTivoNggi niye bipul porimaN bOIdeSik mudrar rijarrv dhore bose ache. kintu koyek masei poristhiti ulTe geche. rijarrv neme eseche 925 kOTi (o5 Disemwrer din SeSher hisabe) Dolare. e diye matr 70o-o72 diner amodani byy meTanO somvob. sadharoNovabe bola hoyo, ontot tin maser amodani byyer porimaN rijarrv thaka proyOjon. bOIdeSik khater ei varosamyhInotay samoShTik 
orrthonItite songkoT dekha diyeche. roptani-oaye probrriddhi holeO tar ceye beSi hare beReche amodani. et din ei baNijy ghaToti meTanO hotO probasIder paThanO ay (oremiTyanso) diye. kintu biSw-oorrthonItite mondar paSapaSi modhypracyjuRe rajonOItik osthirotay e khate probrriddhi ar ager motO nei. abar aSanurUp bOIdeSik sahazyO miloche na, kintu byy porikolpona ager motOi. eroi modhye purO bochorer byy meTanOr orrth itimodhyei sorokar byangk khat theke dhar kore niyeche. prokolp sahazyer bOIdeSik mudra na eleO sthanIy mudrar binimoye ta amodani kora hoyeche. ete samprotik somoye bOIdeSik lenodener varosamye boR dhoroner cap tOIri hoyeche. antorrjatik mudra tohobiler (oaiemoefo) ekoTi miSon deSe obosthan koroche. bangladeSoke 10o0 
kOTi Dolarer rriNosohayota deOya zay ki na, tar bicaro-obiSleShoN koroche doloTi. sorokari sUtrogulO janacche, aiemoefer drriShTivoNggi holO, saSroyI mUlye rriN pete hole orrthonItir nana kShetre SrriNgkhola thakote hobe. samogrik biShoy niye bangladeS byangker sabek govorrnor salehouddin ahomed prothom alOke boleno, bohumatrik cyaleNGjer modhye poReche deSer orrthonIti. et din ovyntorIN kShetre kichu cyaleNGj chilo, kintu ekhon antorrjatik poristhiti tar soNgge zukt hoyeche. tini poramorrS deno, ekhonoi sorokaroke esob swIkar kore proyOjonIy bybostha nite hobe. byy songkOconer paSapaSi ovyntorIN cyaleNGjogulO valO bybosthaponay anote ebong bideS theke orrth anote soThik podokShep nite hobe. lenodeno-oporisthiti: got okTObor mase coloti hisabe ghaToti hoyeche 37 kOTi

e somoye neT bOIdeSik ay hoyeche matr 88 lakh Dolar. amodanite nojorodari: poristhiti samolate bangladeS byangk amodani byyer bivinn kShetre nojorodari baRanOr podokShep nicche. biSleShoN kora hocche tothy-oupatt. koyekoTi kShetre hoThat'' otirikt amodaniO nojore eseche. somproti baNijy montroNaloy kendrIy byangker kache oproyOjonIy amodani poNyer talika ceyechil. kintu bangladeS byangk boloche, tader kache oproyOjonIy poNy bole kOnO talika nei. mudranItir podokShepo: sUtr boloche, gel soptahe byangk khate kichuTa otirikt taroly srriShTi hoyechil. antobyangk mudra bajare kolomanir suder haroO chil beS nimnomukhI, 6-o7 SotangS. ei tarolyer karoNe amodani baRar proboNota ebong arek dofa mUlysfItir aSoNgka theke zay. e bibeconay Disemwrer Surute bangladeS

jOgan proyOjon. esob karoNe sarrwvOUm rriN neOyar porikolpona coloche. zodiO itali somproti bonD cheRe ze rriN niyeche, tar sudohar chil saRe 7 SotangS. e poristhitite bangladeSer motO chOT O durrwl orrthonItir deS bonD chaRole bideSider kache ta akorrShoNIy hobe ki na, se proSnoO royeche. abar bangladeSe bideSi mudrar rijarrvoO kom. ei obosthay bonDer sudoO beSi hobe. maloyeSiya theke bonD cheRe sostay orrth songgroh kora hobe bole sorokarer bivinn pokSh theke bola hocche. e niye somalOconaO royeche. kenona, maloyeSiyay sara biSwer onek kalOTaka (oobOIdh ayo) joma ache, zar modhye bangladeSideroO orrth royeche. obOIdhovabe maloyeSiyay paThanO orrth deSe DhOkatei ejatIy rriN nite 
keu keu ut''sah dicche ki na, se proSnoO uTheche. ï»¿ Tana choy diner doropotone sUcok komol 422 poyenT Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer samone biniyOgokarIder bikShOv deSer Seyarobajare Tana choy din dhore doropoton ghoTeche. coloti maser prothom karrydibos theke Suru hoOya ei doropoton gotokal rObobaroO obyahot chil. choy diner Tana doropotone prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok komeche pray 422 poyenT. er modhye gotokal ek dinei Diesoir sadharoN sUcok pray 85 poyenT kome neme eseche car hajar 847 poyenTe. got 15 novemwrer por eTii Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcoker sorrwnimn obosthan. gotokal rObobar sokale esoisir SIrrShosthanIy korrmokorrtader soNgge ek bOIThoke soforokarI aiemoefer protinidhidoler sodosyra esob tagid den. esoisi punorrgoThoner por aiemoef protinidhidoler soNgge eTii chil prothom anuShThanik bOIThok. saloman ef rohomaner Seyar kenar ghOShoNa: Seyarobajare talikavukt beksimokO limiTeD O beksimokO farrmar pa^c lakh kore mOT 10 lakh Seyar kenar ghOShoNa diyechen kOmpani duTir onytom udyOkta poricalok saloman ef rohoman. 30 karrydiboser modhye bajaromUlye tini e Seyar kinoben. gotokal e khobor Diesoir OyebosaiTe prokaS kora hoy. talikavukt kOmpanir udyOkta poricalokoder nyUnotom Seyar dharoNer badhybadhokota arOper por e ghOShoNa deOya holO. edike kOmpanir kaje gotokal esoisir ceyaromyaner soNgge sakShat'' koren saloman ef rohoman. 
sakShat'' SeShe sangbadikoder tini boleno, coloti maser SeShe othoba januyarir prothom soptahe bajar sthitiSIlokoroN tohobiler karrykrom Suru hobe. bajar poristhiti somporrke tini boleno, âoesoisi zesob podokShep niyeche segulO bastobayit hole bajar swavabik hoye asobe. tobe e kShetre somoyer proyOjon royeche.â ï»¿ 84 keji alur dam 50 Taka! niScit lOkosaner kotha vebe joyopurohaTer akkelopure ekoTi himagare rakha 15 hajar bosta alu keu tulote asoche na. himagar korrtrripokSh khoroca OThate proti bosta alu (o84 keji) 50 Takay bikri koroche. gOpInathopur himagar sUtre jana geche, coloti bochor ei himagare 90 hajar bosta alu songrokShoN kora hoy. esob alu tulote got 15 novemwr porrynt

poNy khalasokarI sioyanDoef protiShThaner korrmocarIra probeS korote paroten. kintu ete biSrriNgkhola srriShTi hoOyay gotokal theke korrmocarIder esob kokShe Dhukote deOya hoyoni, borong kokSher baire kaunTar diye dolilopotr joma neOyar notun bidhan calu hoy. ete Sulkayone beSi somoy lagar ovizOge korrmocarIra baire ese bikShOv michil koren. bela 11Ta theke pray car ghoNTa ta^ra bikShOv koren. ei poristhitite dupure sioyanDoef ejenTos asOsiyeSon O korrmocarI iuniyoner netader soNgge bOIThoke bosen kasTom hauser Urrdhwton korrmokorrtara. bOIThoke siddhant neOya hoyo, sioyanDoef protiShThaner poricoyopotr chaRa Sulkayon kokShe keu Dhukote paroben na. e chaRa proti soptahe ekobar sioyanDoef ejenTos O korrmocarI iuniyoner netader soNgge bose udvUt somosyar 
somadhan kora hobe boleO siddhant neOya hoy. pore bela tinoTa theke poristhiti swavabik hoy. coTTogram kliyaring oyanD foroOyarrDing ejenTos korrmocarI iuniyoner sovapoti abul kaSem prothom alOke boleno, dIrrghodiner hoyoranir karoNe mUlot ei bikShOv hoyeche. amodani poNyer sorrwOcc mUlyer Opor Sulko-okor nirrdharoNo, kasTom hauser nicer store fail onumOdone somoyokShepoNoâoesob karoNe korrmocarIra kShubdh hoye OThen. kasTom hauser otirikt komiSonar motiur rohoman boleno, Sulkayono-osongkrant biShoye keu hoyoranir Sikar hole Urrdhwton korrmokorrtader kache ovizOg janate paren. kintu somosyar kotha na janiye evabe bikShOv kora ucit hoyoni. Sulkayon prokriyay bilomwer ovizOg prosoNgge motiur rohoman boleno, Sulko-okor nirrdharoN hoOyar poroO onek amodani calaner biporIte Sulko-okor joma

Diesoite syamoson cOUdhurIr smoroNosova onuShThit deSer prokhyat bybosayI O SilpOdyOkta proyat syamoson eic cOUdhurI smoroNe ek sovar ayOjon kore Dhaka sTok eksoceNGj (oDiesoi). aj brrihospotibar bikel caroTay Diesoir mUl vobone ei smoroNosovar ayOjon kora hoy. smoroNosovay swagot boktobye Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI boleno, ekojon valO SilpOdyOkta hote hole zesob guN

kOmpani pu^jibajare talikavukt hoteO agrohI. UrrdhwmukhI holO Seyarobajar Tana car din potoner por gotokal budhobar deSer Seyarobajare mUlysUcok beReche. tobe bajare lenoden ager diner ceye samany kome geche. prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGje (oDiesoi) gotokal dinoSeShe sadharoN mUlysUcok beReche pray 66 poyenT. opor Seyarobajar coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok edin pray 163 poyenT beReche. got dui diner boR doropotoner dharabahikotay gotokaloO Dhakar bajare lenodener prothom ghoNTay mUlysUcoker beS OThanama chil. kintu dupurer por mUlysUcoker ei osthirota komote thake ebong ta UrrdhwmukhI hoy. bajarosongSliShT byktira bolocheno, got dui diner doropoton chil oprotyaSit. deSer samogrik orrthonIti niye nana moholer boktoby O

bochore amar ek hajar 70o0 Taka beSi khoroc hobe. e chaRa ekhon dhaner za dam hoyoche, tate ek moNe dujon kiShener dam hoy na. tai dhan lagaye bipode poRoti caine.â koyorar krriShok abodul khalek boleno, âogot bochor TrakTor diye 30o0 Taka ekore jomi coSha zatO. e bochor hoThat'' teler dam baRay ta 40o0 Taka necche.â jwalani teler khucora bikreta abodul mojid mOlla boleno, âoekodiki dhaner dam komo, onydiki teler dam beSi. por por tinobar teler dam baRay krriShok khub bipode poRiche. ekhon dhan rOyar somoy. ekodiki teler damo, taropor khaOya diye kiShener mojuri 350 theke 40o0 Taka poRotiche. badhy hoye

kintu malikera Sromikoder beton baRacche na. montrI vaRa baRiye malikoder swarrth dekholeO amader swarrth dekhol na.â khulona oNGcole ka^ca toritorokarir boR mOkam cukonogor. cukonogorer soboji bybosayI minarul isolam boleno, cukonogor theke khulona porrynt chOT Traker vaRa age chil 90o0 Taka. ekhon ta beRe ek hajar 20o0 theke ek hajar 30o0 Taka hoyeche. age boR Traker vaRa ek hajar 60o0 Taka chil. ekhon ta beRe dui hajar theke dui hajar 10o0 Taka hoyeche. khulona Sohorer jORageT elakar soboji bikreta anOyar alI boleno, âoekhon SIt mOUsume sobojir dam kom thakar kotha. kintu haTette kine Trake ba nochimone anoti vaRa beSi diti hocche 
bole dam beSi poRe zacche. age Sim proti keji 16 Takay becoti paroleO ekhon 20 Takay becoti hocche.â khulona boR bajar bybosayI somitir sadharoN sompadok Syamol halodar boleno, jwalani tele damer soNgge sobokichur damoi beReche. kintu manuSher tO ay baReni. tai manuSher koShToO beReche. bima khater jony pa^c nirrdeSona jari bima khate swcchota O jobabodihi firiye anar udyOg niyeche bima unnoyon O niyontroN korrtrripokSh (oaiDiaroe). ekoi soNgge songsthaTi e khate dokSh O medhabI manobosompod tOIrir protiO tagid diyeche. eroi ongS hisebe somoy be^dhe diye aiDiaroe jIbon bIma koropOreSono, sadharoN bIma koropOreSono, 43Ti sadharoN bima O 18Ti jIbon bima kOmpanir jony 
badhytamUlok pa^coTi biShoy poripalon korote bola hoyeche. egulO hocche: manobosompod nItimala proNoyono, protinidhi stor sImit rakha, jIbon bimay oyakocuyariyal bivag thaka, primiyamer soNgge ony khoroc somonwy na kora ebong betono, komiSon ityadi byangk hisabe dey ceker madhyme prodan kora. er modhye caroTi biShoy oboSy jIbon bima khater soNgge somporrkit. aiDiaroe got budhobar ek projNGapon jari kore âobima khater zothazoth unnoyon niScit korar swarrtheâ esob nirrdeSona dey. ete koropOreSon O kOmpaniâouvoyer jonyi cakori bidhimala-osomporrkit manobosompod nItimala thaka badhytamUlok kora hoyeche. e jony somoy deOya hoyeche agamI 29 februyari porrynt. e somoyer modhye tader manobosompod nItimala aiDiaroer kache dakhil korote hobe. besorokari 
jIbon bima kOmpanigulOke purO iuniTer protinidhir stor duiyer beSi na rakhar kotha bola hoyeche. eTi karrykor hobe agamI 1 februyari theke. jana geche, bima kOmpanigulOte borrtomane protinidhider pa^c theke 10oTi kore stor royeche. nirrdeSona onuzayI, jIbon bima kOmpanigulOte ekhon theke oyakocuyariyal bivag thakote hobe. e bivager dayitw dite hobe oyakocuyariyal kaje dharoNasomponn chatrochatrIder. ta^der ontot oyakocuyariyal bijNGaner ekoTi ongS (oparrTo) somponn kora thakote hobe. tobe chatrochatrIder odhyyoner sotyta zacaiyer jony ta^der porIkSha paser ogrogotir protibedon choy mas ontor aiDiaroer kache paThate hobe. e biShoyoTi karrykor korote hobe agamI 30 marrcer modhye. bima primiyamer soNgge kOnO dhoroner khoroco, prapy, dabi, komiSon 
ityadi somonwy kora zabe na. eTi karrykor korote hobe agamI 1 epril theke. beton O vata, komiSono, rilij O onyany proNOdona kebol byangker hisabe dey (ooyakaunT peyi) ceker madhyme songSliShT protinidhi ba protinidhir niyOg kora byktike deOya zabe. borrtomane nogod Takay deOya hoy bole ek dhoroner biSrriNgkhola coloche bole jana geche. eTi karrykor korote hobe agamI 1 jun theke. got 22 Disemwr bima kOmpanir mukhy korrmokorrtader soNgge aiDiaroe onuShThit ek bOIThoker siddhanter poriprekShitei emon nirrdeSona deOya hoyeche bole jana geche. zOgazOg korole aiDiaroer ceyaromyan em Sefak ahomed prothom alOke boleno, bima otynt somvabonamoy khat. deSer orrthonOItik unnoyone e khater gurutwpUrrN 
obodan rakhar suzOg royeche. tobe khatoTi ekhonO totoTa suSrriNgkhol noy. gOTa bima khate swcchota anar swarrthei projNGaponoTi jari kora hoyeche. ekoTi besorokari jIbon bima kOmpanir bybosthapona poricalok prothom alOke boleno, oyakocuyariyal bivag badhytamUlok korar biShoye aroO somoy deOyar dorokar chil. jonmogot be^Teke Tene lomwa kora zay na montoby kore tini proSn rakheno, âoSuru thekei zekhane biSrriNgkhola coloche, olp dine kIvabe er somadhan somvobo?oâ edike aiDiaroer nirrdeSonake swagot janiyeO kichu biShoye dwimot pOShoN korechen bangladeS inosyurens oyasOsiyeSoner (obiaie) sovapoti Sekh kobir hOsen. prothom alOke biaier sovapoti boleno, âooyakaunT peyi ceker madhyme bima protinidhider prapy poriSOdher biShoyoTi Thikoi ache. aro, kOmpanite protinidhider 
storoO borrtomane onek beSi. tobe hoThat'' kore duiye namiye anar kotha bolaTaO khub songgot noy. e jony tader zotheShT somoy deOya dorokar.â primiyamer soNgge khoroc ba komiSon somonwyer biShoyoTiO ta^r kache bOdhogomy noy bole janan Sekh kobir hOsen. gaRi amodani komeche coTTogram kasTom hause rajosw adayer ekok boR khat hisebe got dui orrthobochore SIrrShosthane chil mOTor gaRi khat. kintu coloti orrthobochorer prothomarrdhe coTTogram bondor diye gaRi amodani byapok hare hras paOyay e khate rajosw adayoO kome geche. got choy maser (ojulai-oDisemwr 20o11) hisabe, ei khate lokShymatrar ceye 823 kOTi Taka rajosw aday kom hoyeche. bondor O kasTom hauser nothipotr theke 
esob tothy jana geche. coTTogram bondor sUtre jana geche, coloti orrthobochorer prothom choy mase ager orrthobochorer ekoi somoyer tulonay gaRi amodani orrdheke nemeche. ei somoyokale, orrthat'' julai theke Disemwr porrynt choy mase coTTogram bondor diye tin hajar 318Ti gaRi amodani hoyeche. er modhye dui hajar 333Ti ekobar bybohUt (orikonDiSonDo) O 985Ti notun gaRi. 20o10o-o11 orrthobochorer ekoi somoye amodani hoyechil choy hajar 993Ti gaRi. er modhye pa^c hajar 279Ti bybohUt O ek hajar 714Ti notun. onydike coTTogram kasTom hauser nothite dekha zayo, coloti orrthobochorer prothom choy mase e khate rajosw adayer lokShymatra chil ek hajar 932 kOTi Taka. ekoi somoye aday 
hoyeche ek hajar 10o4 kOTi Taka. janote caile kasTom hauser otirikt komiSonar motiur rohoman prothom alOke boleno, gaRi amodani ager ceye onek komeche. e karoNe lokShymatra onuzayI rajosw aday hocche na. tobe onyany khat theke aday beReche. kasTom hauser tothye dekha zayo, 20o0o9-o10 orrthobochore e khat theke aday hoy tin hajar 124 kOTi 80 lakh Taka. 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore aday hoy tin hajar 258 kOTi Taka. ei dui orrthobochore rajosw adayer dwitIy khate thaka jwalani tel ekhon SIrrShosthane uThe eseche. 20o0o9-o10 O 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore jwalani khat theke rajosw ase zothakrome dui hajar 24 kOTi ebong dui hajar 586 kOTi Taka. ar 
coloti orrthobochorer prothom choy mase rajosw aday hoyeche dui hajar 332 kOTi Taka. purOnO gaRi amodanikarokoder songgoThon bangladeS rikonDiSonD vehikyalos impOrrTarrs oyanD Dilarrs oyasOsiyeSoner (obaroviDa) sohosovapoti habibur rohoman prothom alOke boleno, âosorokaroke amora soboceye beSi rajosw dii. kintu ekhon e khate durobostha coloche. byangkogulOO orrthayon korote paroche na.â abaroO doropoton komeche lenoden deSer Seyarobajare gotokal brrihospotibar abaroO boR dhoroner doropoton ghoTeche. prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok ei din pray 10o8 poyenT komeche. opor Seyarobajar coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok komeche pray 236 poyenT. paSapaSi soptaher SeSh karrydibose gotokal Diesoir lenoden neme eseche saRe 30o0 kOTi TakaroO 
nice. notun bochore ekhon porrynt eTii Diesoite sorrwnimn lenoden. dui bajare lenoden hoOya kOmpanigulOr modhye Diesoite pray 92 SotangS ebong siesoite 88 SotangSeroi dam komeche. bajaro-osongSliShTora bolocheno, biniyOgokarIder atmobiSwase abaroO kichuTa ciR dhoreche. ar sei suzOge nana mohol nana gujob choRiye eTike aroO noRoboRe kore dicche. zOgazOg kora hole pu^jibajar biSleShok O besorokari iunaiTeD inTaronyaSonal biSwbidyaloyer bijones skuler odhyapok mOhammod mUsa prothom alOke boleno, âokichu kichu Seyare mUly songSOdhoner proyOjon chil. bajarer niyome seTii hocchil. kintu hoThat'' kore seTi boR doropotone rUp nil. borrtomane biniyOgokarIder modhye ek dhoroner vIti kaj koroche. e karoNe valO-omond nirrwiSeShe sob Seyarer dam komoche. zodiO 
eTi kaNgkShit noy.â mUsa aroO boleno, âodam zokhon komote thake tokhon ekodol biniyOgokarI kom lOkosane holeO drut Seyar bikri korote Suru koren. ta^der dharoNa, dam hoyotO aroO kome zabe. amader motO bajare tai zOUktik karoNer ceye monostattwik karoNoi beSi kaj kore.â gotokal din SeShe Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok neme eseche pray pa^c hajar 114 poyenTe. got 16 diner bybodhane eTii Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcoker sorrwnimn obosthan. er age got 20 Disemwr sorrwSeSh Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok pa^c hajar 89 poyenTe chil. paSapaSi gotokal Diesoir sUcokoTi notun bochorer sorrwnimn obosthane neme ase. songSliShT sUtrer tothy onuzayI, bajare pratiShThanik biniyOgokarIder ongSogrohoN beS kome geche. e 
karoNe gotokal doropotoner ekoporryaye beS kichu Seyar kretaSUny hoye poRe. doropoton Suru hole byktiSreNIr biniyOgokarIder Seyar bikrir cap beRe zay. kintu se tulonay pratiShThanik biniyOgokarIr ongSogrohoN chil na. edike soptaher SeSh karrydibose gotokal Diesoite pray 328 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye 78 kOTi Taka kom. er age sorrwSeSh got 18 Disemwr Diesoite sorrwnimn 210 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyechil. din SeShe gotokal Dhakar bajare 261 kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye 241Ti Seyarer dam komeche, beReche matr 15Tir ar oporiborrtit chil pa^coTi Seyarer dam. onydike, siesoir sarrwik mUlysUcok soptah SeShe neme eseche 14 hajar 613 poyenTe. 
coTTogramer bajare ei din 189Ti kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye 167Ti Seyarer dam komeche, beReche matr 20oTir ar oporiborrtit chil duTi Seyarer dam. din SeShe siesoite 34 kOTi Takar Seyar lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye noy kOTi Taka kom. pyaksepOr udwOdhon onuShThane bybosayIder ahwan byangkorriNer sud komate hobe boNggobondhu antorrjatik sommelon kendre pOSak khater soroNGjamosoh ekozOge tinoTi prodorrSonI gotokal Suru hoyeche. udwOdhonI dine ekoTi sTole zontropati dekhanO hocche byangkorriNer suder har komate sorokarer proti ahwan janiyechen pOSak khater songSliShT bybosayI netara. ekoi soNgge ta^ra e biShoye sorokarer boktoby spoShT korar dabi janan. boNggobondhu antorrjatik sommelon kendre 
gotokal brrihospotibar sokale tin dinobyapI âopyaksepOâ melar udwOdhonI onuShThane bybosayIra esob kotha bolen. onuShThane prodhan otithi chilen orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit. tOIri pOSak khater soroNGjamo, prozukti O mORokojat poNysamogrI niye ei âopyaksepO-o20o12â antorrjatik mela boseche. bangladeS garrmenTos eksesorij oyanD pyakejing myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSon (obijiepiemoie) melaTir ayOjon koreche. pyaksepOr paSapaSi aroO duTi mela Suru hoyeche. 11tom âogarrmenTekoâ ebong trritIy âoiyarrn oyanD febrikos sOrrsing feyar SOâ mela duTir zOUth ayOjok jakariya TreD oyanD feyar inTaronyaSonal ebong eesoke TreD oyanD eksibiSon. udwOdhonI onuShThane bybosayIra boleno, deSer Silpayon thomoke ache. 18 theke 20 SotangS sude byangkorriN niye bybosayIra biniyOg korote can na. 
onydike gyaser songkoT tIbr. songzOg thakar poroO cahidar eko-otrritIyangS gyas paOya zay na. bybosayIra aroO boleno, got bochor pOSak roptani kore ek hajar 80o0 kOTi Dolar ay hoyeche. er modhye âopoScat''mukhI songzOgoâ hisebe soroNGjam O mORok poNyer obodan onek. age soroNGjamer jony car mas age karryadeS dite hotO. ar ekhon sokale karryadeS dile bikelei paOya zay. ete pOSak khater liD Taim kome geche. onuShThane sarrk cemwarer sovapoti anisul hok boleno, pOSak khate songkoT ele sorokar deuliya hoye zabe. samoyikovabe seTa samal deOya zabe na. e khater soNgge 40 lakh Sromiker vagyO joRit. tai sorokaroke pOSak khatoke sorrwOcc ogradhikar dite hobe. 
anisul hok aroO boleno, pOSak khat zodi âooyaTom bOmaâ hoyo, tobe âosoroNGjamoâ khatoTi hocche tar gurutwpUrrN cipos. cipos na hole bOma faTobe na. tini soroNGjam khater bikaSe proyOjonIy sob korote orrthomontrIr drriShTi akorrShoN koren. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit boleno, udyOkta O Sromikoder kolyaNei pOSakoSilper ajoker ei obosthan. ei SilpoTike ghire aroO onek kShudr O majhari SilpoprotiShThan goRe uThoche. borrtoman sorokar kShomotay asar por Sromikoder beton deR guN kora hoyeche bole janan orrthomontrI. tobe byangkorriNer suder har komanOr biShoye kOnO montoby korenoni tini. onuShThane aroO boktoby den eSiyan pyakejing feDareSoner sovapoti sofiullah cOUdhurI, bijiemoier sovapoti sofiul isolamo, bikeemoier sohosovapoti mOhammod 
hatemo, eesoke TreDer poricalok nondogOpalo, jakariya TreD oyanD feyarer prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta iliyas jakariya promukh. onuShThane sovapotitw koren bijiepiemoier sovapoti rafej alom cOUdhurI. soboSeShe orrthomontrI melar udwOdhon koren. ony otithider soNgge tini melar bivinn sTol poridorrSon koren. prodorrSonI: mela udwOdhoner por thekei dorrSonarrthIra melay viR korote thaken. onekei sTologulO ghure bivinn poNyer khO^jokhobor nen. oneke abar poNyer bistarit biboroN songbolit kyaTalog niye gechen. pOSak khater soroNGjamo, zontrangSo, prozukti O mORokojatokoroNer poNy niye tin melay bangladeSo, varoto, cIno, pakistano, taiOyano, jarrmanisoh bivinn deSer car Sotadhik protiShThan ongS niyeche. pyaksepOte polibyago, byakobOrrDo, ilasTiko, kolar inosarrTo, baTaroflai, kolar bOno, Tyapo, jiparo, sTikaro, baTono, 
hyaNggaro, sTOparo, nek bOrrDo, suing threDo, prais Tyago, foTObOrrDo, gamoTep ityadi poNy prodorrSon koroche deSi O bideSi protiShThan. garrmenTek melay zontrer madhyme suta O kapoR tOIri, tOIri pOSak khater soroNGjamo, mORokojatokoroN O prozuktir prodorrSon koroche ongSogrohoNokarI protiShThanogulO. e chaRa âoiyarrn O febrikosoâ melay suta, tOIri bostro, finiSo, Denimo, niTing ityadi samogrI prodorrSit hocche. melay asa pOSak khater ek bybosayI boleno, âomelagulO amader cOkh khule diyeche. prrithibIte kI ghoToche, ta ek chader nice paOyaTa onek gurutwpUrrN. zacai-obachai kore ekadhik protiShThane karryadeS deben boleO janan tini. ayOjokera janano, aj O kal tOIri pOSak khater soroNGjam O mORokojatokoroNer Opor duTi antorrjatik seminar hobe 
mela praNggoNe. syamoson cOUdhurIke smoroN korol Diesoi deSer biSiShT Silpopoti O udyOkta syamoson eic cOUdhurIr smoroNe gotokal ek smrriticaroNa sovar ayOjon kore Dhaka sTok eksoceNGj (oDiesoi). DhakayoDiesoi vobone ayOjit ei sovay boktara proyat syamoson cOUdhurIr jIboner bivinn korrmokaND O otIt itihas tule dhoren. Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI, poricalok rokibur rohoman O ahomed roSId lalI, sodosy abodur rohoman chaRaO syamoson cOUdhurIr chele topon cOUdhurI ete boktoby den. boktara boleno, ekojon sofol O valO SilpOdyOkta hote zesob guN lage, tar soboi chil syamoson eic cOUdhurIr modhye. deSer pu^jibajarer unnoyone ta^r obodan osamany. pu^jibajarer madhyme Silp unnoyon ze somvobo, seTa tini mone-opraNe biSwas 
koroten. topon cOUdhurI boleno, âoamar baba sob somoy boloten nijer modhye poriborrton anole deSer poriborrton asobe. kokhonO tini Taka-opoyosar biShoyoTike boR kore dekhoten na.â lalomonirohaTe ipibir bipoNonobiShoyok seminar trriNomUl porryay theke roptani brriddhite bybosayIder udwuddh korote roptani unnoyon byurOr (oipibi) rajoSahI karryaloy ebong lalomonirohaT Silp O boNik somitir zOUth udyOge bipoNonobiShoyok ek seminar onuShThit hoyeche. lalomonirohaT boNik somitir karryaloye got budhobar onuShThit Oi seminare lalomonirohaTer jela proSasok mOkholechar rohoman sorokaro, boNik somitir sovapoti Sekh abodul hamido, ipibir poricalok iuchuf alI, ipibir rajoSahI karryaloyer upoporicalok mOyajjem hOsen promukh boktoby den. seminare boktara boleno, lalomonirohaT jelar buRimarI stholobondor diye jelay ut''padit krriShi 
O hostojatosoh onyany poNy roptani somvob. e kShetre sthanIy proSason O bybosayIder sorrwatmok udyOg nite hobe. ta chaRa byangk O arrthik protiShThanogulOke proyOjonIy rriNosohayotaO dite hobe. varote amer Sa^se prosadhonIr tel tOIri varote ebar amer Sa^s diye tOIri hoyeche ek dhoroner telo, za prosadhonI tOIrite bybohar kora hocche. gujoraT rajyer nobosari krriShi biSwbidyaloy biSeSh dhoroner ei tel tOIrir notun poddhoti abiShkar koreche. ei tel bivinn prosadhonI tOIrite bybohar kora zabe. biSeSh kore lOSono, krimo, sabano, konDiSonar ityadi tOIrite. dhano-opaTer por alu-ope^yajo-osobojiroO dam pacchen na caShi, ut''padon beSi holeO khoroc uThoche na krriShoker mathay hat munsigoNGjer gojariya elakar ekoTi himagare poce 
zaOya alu baire fele rakha hoyeche dhano, paTo, alur por ebar soboji niye bipake poRechen krriShok. ut''padon baRoleO dam pacchen na krriShok. abar krriShoker kache kom dame poNy kine bajare coRa dame bikri korochen bybosayIra. calo, alu theke Suru kore sob dhoroner krriShipoNyer dam got ek mase 20 theke 35 SotangS beReche. alu O soboji krriShok porryayer tulonay tin guN beSi dame vOktader kache bikri hocche. maThoporryaye dhaner dam niyomitovabe komoleO caler damer Urrdhwgoti theme nei. sorokari songstha TreDing koropOreSon ob bangladeSer (oTisibi) hisabe got ek mase cikon O mOTa caler dor 3 theke 8 SotangS beReche. onukUl abohaOya ar 
got bochor valO dam paOyay aroO ut''sah niye maThe nemechilen krriShok. folonoO ager zekOnO bochorer tulonay valO. krriShi montroNaloyer hisabe, ebar got bochorer tulonay sat lakh 27 hajar meTrik Ton beSi soboji ut''padit hoyeche. alur folonoO got bochorer tulonay pray 15 lakh Ton beSi. kintu dam poRotir dike. biSeSh kore, alu O SItokalIn soboji maThoporryaye panir dore bikri hocche. alu bece himagare rakhar khoroc O coTer damoO uThoche na krriShoker. oneke himagarer paSe alu ebong haTe soboji fele cole zacchen. krriShokera bolocheno, got pa^c bochorer modhye alu O sobojir emon durrdin ar aseni. paTer bajaroO monda. sorokari paTokologulOte pray ek 
hajar 70o0 kOTi Takar paT obikrIt obosthay poRe ache. tai notun paT kenaO bondh. paTer ut''padon khoroc O dam pray soman hoye geche. proti moN nimnomaner paT got bochorer tulonay pray orrdhek orrthat'' ek hajar Takar nice neme eseche. ikOnomik risarrc gruper gobeShoNa poricalok O orrthonItibid sajjad johIr e byapare prothom alOke boleno, rajonItibidera beSir vag kShetre Sohure vOktader kotha mathay rekhe khadypoNyer dam komanOr ceShTa koren. koyek bochor dhore beSir vag krriShipoNyer dam baRay krriShimojur O Sohure dinomojurer pariSromik beRechil. kintu ekhon krriShipoNyer dam komay krriShoker swarrthokeO bibeconay anote hobe. noile krriShok ut''padon komiye deben. alu niye bipodo: sadharoNot 
Disemwrer SeSher dike bajare notun alu OTha Suru kore. tar age purOnO alu SeSh hoye zay. got bochorer tulonay ebar alur folon valO hoyeche. sorokari hisabe ebar 83 lakh 26 hajar meTrik Ton alu hobe. tobe besorokari hisabe alu ut''padoner porimaN ek kOTi Toner kachakachi pOU^chabe. bangladeS himagar oyasOsiyeSon sUtre jana geche, e bochor ekhonO himagarogulOte dui lakh bosta alu roye geche. dam kom hoOyay krriShok Oi alu ar ferot nicchen na. onydike februyari theke himagare notun alu asa Suru korobe. tai himagarer malikera purOnO alu himagarer baire fele dicchen. himagarer geTe 80 keji Ojoner ek bosta alu 80 theke 
120 Takay bikri hocche. ekoTi notun coT O poribohon khoroc zOg korole proti keji alur dam da^Ray ek TakaroO kom. notun OTha alur dam got koyek bochore 15 Takar nice nameni. ebar pa^c Takar Opore uThoche na. tobe Tisibir hisabe got mase proti keji alur dam 8 theke 12 Takay bikri hoyeche. coloti mase ta 12 theke 15 Taka. bangladeS kondal (oalujatIyo) gobeShoNakendrer hisabe proti keji alur ebar ut''padon khoroc poReche pa^c theke choy Taka. du-otin hat ghure himagarer khoroc jugiye bosta O poribohon khoroc zOg kore proti keji alu 10 Takay bikri korote na parole krriShoker lOkosan hobe bole 
songsthaTir ek hisabe dekha geche. bangladeS himagar oyasOsiyeSoner sovapoti josim uddin prothom alOke boleno, alucaShi O himagarer malik got koyek bochorer modhye etoTa bipode kokhonO poRenoni. besorokari udyOge e bochor pray dui lakh Ton alu roptani hoyeche. sorokar udyOg niye alu roptanir porimaN baRate parole krriShok O bybosayIra etoTa somosyay poRoten na. pe^yajer jha^j komo: pray protibochoroi pe^yaj niye bajare songkoT dekha dey. got bochor pe^yajer dor proti keji 45 Taka porrynt uThechil. valO dam paOyay e bochor krriShok otirikt sat hajar hekTor jomite pe^yajer caSh korechen. kintu mOUsumer Surute pe^yajer dam komote komote coloti soptahe 15 Takay giye Thekeche. 
Tisibir hisabe proti keji pe^yaj 15 theke 22 Takay bikri hocche. ek soptaher bybodhane pe^yajer dor 35 SotangS komeche. ar ek bochore komeche 55 SotangS. deSer cahidar 20 theke 30 SotangS pe^yaj amodani hoye thake. bangladeS krriShi gobeShoNa inosTiTiuTer (obari) krriShi orrthonIti bivager hisab onuzayI, proti keji pe^yajer maThoporryaye ut''padon khoroc poReche 11 Taka. poribohon O songrokShoN khoroc zOg korole proti keji pe^yajer pechone krriShoker khoroc hocche 15 TakaroO beSi. dam kom pele poroborrtI bochor krriShok amodaninirrvor ei krriShipoNyer ut''padon komiye dite paren. SIter sobojir bajar ThanDa: SItokalIn sobojir obostha aroO kharap. got pa^co-osat bochorer modhye et kom dame soboji 
bikri hoyoni. biSeSh kore, TomeTO O fulokopir dam ebar soboceye kom. krriShok porryaye proti keji TomeTO dui theke tin Takayo, ekekoTi fulokopi ek theke tin Taka dore bikri hocche. ekekoTi lau bikri hocche tin theke pa^c Taka kore. othoc bajare dam tin theke car guN beSi. barir hisabe ek keji TomeTOr ut''padon khoroc dui Taka 59 poyosa. tobe poribohon O songrokShoN khoroc zOg korole ek keji TomeTOte krriShoker khoroc poRe aT Taka, ar krriShok bikri korochen tino-ocar Takay. dhaner bajar theme ache: dui mas dhore dhaner dam poRotir dike, tobe ek soptah dhore dam kichuTa sthir. amon dhane krriShoker nyazymUly 
niScit korote sorokar dui lakh Ton cal kineche. kintu ete krriShoker lav hoyoni, munafa geche calokol malikoder pokeTe. karoNo, sorokarivabe calokol malikoder kach theke sorasori cal kena hoyeche. biSeShojNGora krriShoker kach theke sorasori dhan kenar poramorrS dileO khady bivag ta amole neyoni. fole dhaner dam ekhonO krriShoker protyaSa onuzayI baReni. abar dhaner dam kom holeO caler dam kintu beRei coleche. krriShi montroNaloyer hisabe proti moN dhaner ut''padon khoroc 550 Taka. ar ta bikri hocche 50o0 theke 60o0 Takay. Tisibir hisabe bajare proti keji mOTa cal got maser tulonay 3 SotangS beRe 32 theke 35 Takay bikri hocche. majhari maner caler 
dor pray 9 SotangS beRe 36 theke 38 Taka keji dore bikri hocche. bangladeS unnoyon gobeShoNa protiShThaner (obiaiDieso) gobeShoNa poricalok em asadujjaman prothom alOke boleno, Dijeler mUly koyek dofa brriddhi ebong deSer zOgazOgobybostha veNge poRay krriShipoNyer poribohon khorocoO beReche. onek kShudr O majhari udyOkta jela porryaye ba boR haTe poNy na ene sthanIy porryaye bikri kore dicchen. evabe colote thakole et din krriShipoNyer ut''padon ze hare baRochilo, samoner dinogulOte sei hare komote thakobe. ete vobiShyte khadynirapotta bighnit hobe. sUcok goNonay fri floTer songjNGa nirrdharoNI bOIThok aj deSer sTok eksoceNGje sUcok goNonar kShetre fri floTer songjNGa nirrdharoNe kal rObobar bOIThok korobe 
sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSoner (oesoisi) goThon kora komiTi. got 11 januyari ei komiTir bOIThok onuShThit hoOyar kotha thakoleO 10 Disemwr esoisir upoporicalok abu rayohan mOhammod mutasim billah swakShorit ek ciThite kal e bOIThoker siddhant neOya hoy bole jana geche. esoisi sUtre jana zayo, got 26 Disemwr fri floTer (olenodenozOgy Seyaro) vittite sTok eksoceNGjer mUlysUcok goNonar siddhant ney esoisi. ekoi soNgge fri floTer songjNGa nirrdharoNer jony ekoTi komiTi goThon kora hoy. komiTir ahwayok holeno, esoisir sodosy arif khan. e chaRa komiTite Dhaka sTok eksoceNGj (oDiesoi)o, coTTogram sTok eksoceNGj (osiesoi) O senTral DipOjiTori bangladeS limiTeDer (osiDibielo) protinidhi royeche. komiTike 15 diner modhye 
e biShoye komiSoner kache protibedon joma dite bola hoy. prosoNggoto, got 20 Disemwr esoisite Diesoir mUlysUcok punorrwinyas niye goThit komiTir sodosyder bOIThok onuShThit hoy. Oi bOIThoke komiTir sodosyra vul sUcoker poriborrte notunovabe mUlysUcok calur pokShe nijeder motamot tule dhoren. er age 12 okTObor esoisi ei komiTi goThon kore. pOSak khater soroNGjam O mORok ekhon deSoj poNy pOSak khater bivinn dhoroner soroNGjam ebong pOSakosoh ony khater mORok poNy ut''padone got dui doSoke boR safoly eseche bangladeSe. bOtamo, hyaNggar theke Suru kore pOSak khater anuShoNggik sob soroNGjam zemon ekhon deSe ut''padit hocche, temoni onyany khater mORok poNyer cahidar pray soboTukui ekhon jOgan 
dite sokShom deSoj ut''padon. Sudhu ovyntorIN cahida meTanOi noyo, deSer baireO ei khatoTir bivinn poNy roptani kora hocche. protibochoroi baRoche roptani. 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore khatoTi pray 275 kOTi 11 lakh marrkin Dolarer poNy roptani koreche. sorokarer sohozOgita pele 20o18 saler modhye e khater roptani ay ek hajar 20o0 kOTi Dolare da^Rabe bole janan songSliShT bybosayIra. antorrjatik poramorrSok protiShThan myakokinose ek gobeShoNay boleche, bangladeSer tOIri pOSak khater roptani 20o15 sale borrtoman somoyer ceye dwiguN ebong 20o20 sale tin guN hobe. biShoyoTi ullekh kore songSliShT bybosayIra boleno, pOSak roptani baRole soroNGjamer cahidaO baRobe. tokhon cahidamotO soroNGjamer jOgan dite na parole uvoy khatoi kShotigrost 
hobe. soroNGjam O mORok poNy tOIrir esob protiShThaner baNijyik swarrthosongSliShT biShoy niye kaj korote 1991 sale bangladeS garrmenTos oyaksesorij oyanD pyakejing myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSon (obijiepiemoie) protiShThit hoy. oboSy somitiTir pUrrwer nam chil bangladeS korOgeTeD karrTon oyanD oyaksesorij myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSon (obisisieemoie). got bochorer novemwre proyOjonIy onumOdon niye nam poriborrton kore bijiepiemoie kora hoy. sara deSe somitir sodosysongkhya ek hajar 50. e chaRa ache aroO kichu protiShThan. protykSho-oporOkShovabe khatoTir soNgge joRit achen pray dui lakh manuSh. borrtomane e khate mOT biniyOger porimaN pray pa^c hajar kOTi Taka. songSliShT bybosayIra janano, pOSak khater 30 theke 35 dhoroner soroNGjam O onyany 
khater mORok tOIri kore e khater protiShThanogulO. er modhye ache: karrTono, polibyago, hyaNggaro, bOtamo, bOtamer Tyago, mUly Tyago, lebelo, jiparo, hyangTyago, gamoTep ityadi. esob poNyi pOSako, camoRa, khady, OShudh ityadi roptanipoNyer âopoScat''mukhI songzOgoâ hisebe bideSe zay. ekoi soNgge ut''padit poNyer 15 theke 20 SotangS pUrrw iurOpo, modhypracy, dokShiN afrika, hongkong, dUropracysoh beS koyekoTi deSe sorasori roptani koren ut''padokera. esob soroNGjam diyei pOSak khater pray 40 SotangS mUly songzOjon kora hoy bole ta^ra janan. khO^j niye jana zayo, aSir doSoker Surute pOSak khater utthaner somoyoi kagojer karrTon prothom ut''padon Suru kore koyekoTi protiShThan. er tino-ocar bochor por theke polibyago, byakobOrrDo, hyanD 
Tyago, prais Tyag ut''padon hote thake. pore ei dharabahikotay zukt hoy aroO onek protiShThan. 1995 sal theke pOSak khater pray sob dhoroner soroNGjam O mORok poNy ut''padon Suru kore deSIy protiShThanogulO. tobe esob poNyer ka^camal jarrmani, cIno, thailyanDo, maloyeSiyasoh bivinn deS theke amodani korote hoy. ek dhoroner karrTon tOIrite Sudhu deSIy kagoj bybohar kora hoy. oyasOsiyeSoner ek bybosayI neta boleno, e khate deS ekhon swabolomwI. pOSakoSilper cahidar somoporimaN soroNGjam O mORok ut''padone sokShom deSIy protiShThanogulO. kintu onek somoy bideSi kretader Sorrt manote olpobistor amodani koren pOSakoSilper bybosayIra. ekadhik bybosayI boleno, deSIy cahida meTanOr poroO khatoTir byapok somvabona ache. karoNo, sara 
biSwe khatoTir ontot car hajar kOTi Dolarer bajar ache. poNyer man aroO unnot ebong sorokari sohozOgita pele sorasori roptani kore antorrjatik bajar baRanO somvob. roptani unnoyon byurOr tothyanusare, 1983-o84 saler 47 lakh Dolarer roptani ay theke beRe sorrwSeSh 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore 275 kOTi Dolare da^Riyeche. 20o0o4-o0o5 orrthobochor porrynt khatoTir roptani ay chil 10o0 kOTi Dolarer nice. tobe 20o0o5-o0o6 orrthobochore da^Ray 118 kOTi Dolar. 20o0o9-o10 orrthobochore ei ay chil 191 kOTi 95 lakh Dolar. porer orrthobochorei khatoTir 43 doSomik 97 SotangS roptani probrriddhi hoy. sUtr janayo, poNyer man niyontroNe oyasOsiyeSon nij udyOge ekoTi porIkShagar sthapon koreche. ekhane karrToner man porIkSha kora hoy. 
tobe onyany poNyer man niyontroN O unnotomaner poNy ut''padone ekoTi inosTiTiuT goRote sorokarer soNgge bohu denodorobar koreO ekhon porrynt sofol hononi e khater bybosayIra. bijiepiemoier sovapoti rafej alom cOUdhurI boleno, pOSakoSilper jony khatoTi khuboi gurutwpUrrN. karoNo, deSe esob soroNGjam ut''padon kora na holeO swavabikovabei bideS theke amodani korote hotO. tokhon Sudhu soroNGjam amodanitei dui theke tin mas somoy lege zet. tate liDo-oTaim (opoNy ut''padon theke Suru kore jahajIkoroN porrynt somoyo) beSi lagot. protizOgitamUlok antorrjatik bajare tokhon Tike thakai muSokil hotO. rafej alom cOUdhurI aroO boleno, gurutwpUrrN holeO ei khatoTike sevabe âogurutwâ deyoni sorokar. aj porrynt ek DolaroO nogod sohayota panoni 
bybosayIra. emonoki kShudr O majhari Silp hisebeO temon kOnO suzOgo-osubidha payoni e khater protiShThanogulO. sovapoti aroO boleno, vobiShyter kotha cinta kore ekhonoi e khater somprosaroN proyOjon. kintu sei poribeS nei. 18 theke 20 SotangS byangk sude bybosayIra biniyOg korote sahos pacchen na. e soptaher sakShat''kar songkoTer mUle royeche uccavilaShI bajeT Taka chapiye kendrIy byangk theke ar rriN na nite sorokaroke poramorrS deOya hoyeche. ei poriprekShite orrthonItir obostha niye prothom alOr soNgge kotha bolechen bangladeS orrthonIti somitir sadharoN sompadok tOUfik ahomod cOUdhUrI prothom alO: bangladeSer orrthonItite ekhon ze ekoTa songkoT dekha diyeche, tar karoNoTa kI? tOUfik ahomod cOUdhUrI: sorokar coloti orrthobochorer 
jony ze bajeT koreche, seTai ei songkoTer mUl. got jun mase bajeT deOyar poroi amora eTake uccavilaShI bole akhyayit korechilam. kenona, ei bajeTe boR boR byy nirrwaher porikolpona kora hoyeche. se onuzayI sorokar byy Suru koroleO ze ayer proyOjono, ta ThikomotO hoyoni. biSeSh kore boR prokolpogulOr jony. ar boR bajeT byyer kShetre ayer ut''sogulOr ekoTate ghaToti dekha dilei TanapORen Suru hoy. sorokar ekhane bideSi ut''s theke rriNo-oonudanogulO protyaSa onuzayI payoni. fole, beSi kore rriN nite hocche, zar boR ongSoi asoche sorasori kendrIy byangk theke Taka chapiye. orrthobochorer prothom car masei tO sorokarer byangkorriN lokShymatra chaRiye geche. prothom alO: songsodIy komiTir 
bOIThoke sorokaroke ar Taka chapiye byy na meTanOr poramorrS deOya hoyeche. eTa ki sorokar korote parobe? tOUfik ahomod cOUdhUrI: Taka na chapanOr mane holO, bangladeS byangk theke sorasori rriN grohoN na kora. eTa na korole byangkobybostha theke rriN baRate hobe. se kShetre abar besorokari khater rriN paOyar suzOg kome zabe. ekhane ekoTa somosya holO, sorokar Trejari bonD diye 11Ti praimari Dilar byangker kach theke procur orrth rriN niyeche. ekhon ei byangkogulO nijeder proyOjone ei bonD bikri korote paroche na. kenona, amader ekhane bonD bajaroTi goRe OTheni. bonDer sekenDari maarrkeT ba niyomit becakenar bajar thakole praimari Dilarora ei bajare lenoden korote 
parot. tate ekodike zemon tader tarolyer songkoT kome asoto, onydike suder haroO bajarovittik hotO. prothom alO: tahole bonD bajar goThoner kOnO ceShTa kora hocche na keno? tOUfik ahomod cOUdhUrI: sorokarer edike temon agroh nei bolei hoyotO sevabe ceShTaTa hocche na. abar sorokarer agroh na thakaroO karoN ache. bonD bajar thakole tO sorokarokeO sekhane ongS nite hobe, bajarovittite rriN nite hobe. ekhonokar motO kendrIy byangk niyomitovabe sorokarer ghaToti miTiye debe na. asole eTa ekhon gurutwer soNgge cinta kora ucit. orrthoboh ekoTi bonD ba rriNobajar goRe tulote hobe. varot O pakistane za ache. sekhanokar motO ekhaneO kendrIy byangk theke sorokarer rriN grohoNer 
aini sIma arOp kora ucit. prothom alO: rajosw aday poristhiti tO valO. ekhane ki sorokarer ay baRanOr suzOg ache? tOUfik ahomod cOUdhUrI: hya^, jatIy rajosw bOrrD rajosw adaye valO safoly dekhacche. tobe rajosw ay baRanOTa ekoTa nirontor prokriya. tat''kShoNikovabe ei ay baRobe na. tobe ekhane sorokarer ay baRanOr aroO onek suzOg ache. e kShetre ayokorer dike monOzOg deOya ucit. bochore ek kOTi Taka ba er beSi ayokor den matr 46 jon. othoc e rokom ayokorodatar songkhya tO koyek hajar hoOya ucit. ekhane biraT ekoTa fa^ki ache. Dhaka Sohore Dojon khanek flyaTer malik hoyeO matr koyek lakh Taka ayokor den keu 
keu. ayokor aday baRate hole sorokarer SoktiSalI rajonOItik sodiccha proyOjon. prothom alO: bideSi sohayotar kShetre ekhon antorrjatik mudra tohobiler (oaiemoefo) rriN ebong sarrwvOUm bonD cheRe rriN neOyar kotha bola hocche. egulO kotokhani Thik hobe? tOUfik ahomod cOUdhUrI: aiemoefer kach theke rriN grohoNer biShoyoTi onek din dhore alOcit hocche. eTa paOya gele ekhon khanikoTa capomukt hoOya zabe. ar sarrwvOUm bonD cheRe antorrjatik arrthik bajar theke rriN grohoNer kothaTi eseche bOIdeSik mudrar rijarrve zen hat dite na hoyo, se jony. bangladeSer ekhon ze rriNoman (okreDiT reTing)o, ta ei rriN pete khub beSi sud gunote hoyotO hobe na. tobe ekoTu sotorrkota proyOjon. [osakShat''kar 
niyechen asojadul kiboriya] esoisir nirrdeSona manote kOTa pUroNe byst poricalokera pu^jibajare talikavukt sob kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokoder sommilitovabe nij kOmpanir komopokShe 30 SotangS ebong byktigotovabe komopokShe 2 SotangS Seyarer malik hote hobe. got bochorer 22 novemwr sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi) e-osongkrant nirrdeSona jari kore. esoisir nirrdeSonar por 30 SotangSer kom SeyarodharI udyOkta-oporicalokera notun kore Seyar kena Suru korechen. tobe oneke niyom onuzayI nijer poribarer sodosyder modhyeO Seyar hostantor O grohoN korochen. esoisir nirrdeSonar por e porrynt tinojon poricalok pa^c kOTi 58 lakh pa^c hajar 326Ti Seyar hostantor korechen. e chaRa aroO carojon udyOkta-oporicalok ek kOTi 91 lakh 83 hajar 816Ti Seyar 
poribarer sodosyder kach theke grohoN korechen. Dhaka sTok eksoceNGj (oDiesoi) sUtr jana zayo, esoisir nirrdeSona jarir por mOT satojon udyOkta-oporicalok Seyar hostantor ba grohoN somponn korechen. e chaRa dujon poricalok nij kOmpanir Seyar grohoNer ghOShoNa diyechen. pu^jibajare talikavukt navana sienoji limiTeDer onytom udyOkta-oporicalok Sofiul isolam ta^r meye farohana isolamoke got 9 januyari 10 lakh Seyar hostantor koren. tini 5 januyari ei Seyar hostantorer ghOShoNa den. khulona paOyar kOmpani limiTeDer (okepisielo) udyOkta samiT inDasTriyal marrkenTail koropOreSon limiTeD kepisieler pa^c kOTi 39 lakh 55 hajar 326Ti Seyar samiT paOyar limiTeDoke hostantor somponn koreche. 4 januyari kepisieler pokSh theke Diesoir OyebosaiTe ei ghOShoNa 
deOya hoy. afotab oTOmObailoser onytom udyOkta-oporicalok Sofiul isolam ta^r strI khaleda isolamo, chele saiful isolam O sajedul isolamo, meye farohana isolamoke ta^r kache thaka aT lakh 50 hajar Seyar hostantor somponn korechen. edike pUbalI byangk limiTeDer udyOkta-oporicalok mOstofa Sahoriyar ahomed ta^r baba monir ahomeder kach theke ek kOTi 44 lakh 24 hajar 0o66Ti Seyar grohoN korechen. enosisi byangker udyOkta-oporicalok nurul neOyaj ta^r strI Saheda akotaro, meye Samima neOyaj O Sakila neOyajer kach theke 26 lakh Seyar grohoNer ghOShoNa diyechen 11 januyari. ekoi byangker arek poricalok abul baSar ta^r ma fatema khatuno, bOn sajiya aOyal O vai asif mahomuder kach theke 
19 lakh 26 hajar 50o0oTi Seyar grohoN korechen. oyapeks Tyanarir poricalok moNGjur elahi ta^r strI nilufar moNGjur O meye munij moNGjur khosorur kach theke dui lakh 33 hajar 250oTi Seyar kroy korechen. onydike, isTarrn byangk limiTeDer poricalok SoOkot alI 69 lakh ebong pUbalI byangker habibur rohoman ek kOTi 27 lakh 96 hajar 431Ti Seyar grohoNer ghOShoNa diyechen Diesoir OyebosaiTe. e byapare Diesoir poricalok ahomed roSid lalI prothom alO onolainoke boleno, poribarer sodosyder modhye Seyar hostantor ba grohoN ainosiddh. ete kOnO somosya nei. tobe ain onuzayI poribarer bairer kOnO lOker kache Seyar hostantor ba karoO kach theke Seyar grohoN kora zabe 
na. deSe garrmenTos polli goRe tOla hobe: baNijymontrI baNijymontrI ji em kader bolecheno, pOSakoSilper prosarer jony sorokar deSe âogarrmenTos polliâ goRe tOlar udyOg niyeche. aj Sonibar rajodhanIte boNggobondhu antorrjatik sommelon kendre bangladeS garrmenTos eksesorij ebong pyakejing myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSon ayOjit ek seminare tini esob kotha bolen. baNijymontrI boleno, garrmenTos eksesorij ebong pyakejing poNy bideS theke amodani na kore deSe utpadon koray bOIdeSik mudra saSroy ebong deSe korrmosongsthaner suzOg hocche. deSer cahida pUroN kore esob poNy bideSe roptani korote hobe. tini aroO boleno, garrmenTos eksesorij ebong pyakejing poNy khat theke bochore pray 30o0 kOTi marrkin Dolar bOIdeSik mudra orrjit hoy. 
e porimaN aroO baRate hobe. bangladeS garrmenTos eksesorij ebong pyakejing myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSoner sovapoti refaj alom cOUdhurIr sovapotitwe seminare biSeSh otithi hisebe boktoby den orrthonItibid debopriy voTTacarry. seminare mUl probondh uposthapon koren mokobul ahomed khan. khobor tothybiboroNI. hoThat'' TrolarovaRa baRay rUposapare kShOv teler dam baRar ojuhate got budhobar theke khulonar rUposa kheyaghaTe hoThat'' Trolar (oSyalO iNGjinocalit nOUka) vaRa baRanO hoyeche. ete zatrIder modhye tIbr kShOver srriShTi hoyeche. rUposaparer manuSher soNgge kotha bole jana geche, vOIrob noder poScim pare khulona nogore asa-ozaOyar jony bohu bochor dhore pUrrw parer rUposa-oterokhadar manuSh nOUkay kore parapar hoye asoche. Sudhu rUposa kheyaghaT diye khulona 
nogore protidin pray 50 hajar manuSh iNGjinocalit nOUkay kore asa-ozaOya kore. sompUrrN bykti-oudyOge Trolaromajhira beS koyek bochor dhore zatrIproti dui Taka, mOTorosaikeloproti 10 Taka kore niye protiTi nOUkay 25 theke 30 jon zatrI parapar koroten. kintu budhobar theke hoThat'' majhira zatrIproti tin Taka, mOTorosaikeloproti 15 theke 20 Taka kore aday korochen. got brrihospotibar bela 11Ta theke dupur saRe 12Ta porrynt zatrI O majhider soNgge ei protibedoker kotha hoy. majhi abodul gofur 48 jon zatrIsoh ta^r TrolaroTi rUposapare ene veRan. krriShoko, sorokari O besorokari karryaloyer korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIsoh nana SreNI-opeSar manuSh bipake poReche. got sOm O moNggolobar boriSal nogorer bivinn bajaro, basosTyanD O bipoNibitaN ghure teler mUlybrriddhir provab somporrke manuSher soNgge kotha hoyeche. ta^der soNgge alapocaritay nana somosyar kotha prokaS peyeche. macher bajare jha^jo: moNggolobar nogorer notun bajare macher dam odhik ha^kay kShubdh hon vaTikhana elakar mO. jamal hOsen. tini bagibotoNDa Suru kore den mach bybosayIr soNgge. karoNo, ek soptah age ze macher dam 50o0 Taka chilo, sei macher dam 80o0 Taka caOya hoyeche. dam beSi caichen keno, janote caile mach bybosayI boleno, âotyaler dam komano, poribohon khoroc komano, amoraO kom dame 
becomu.â mach bybosayI sayed Sikodar boleno, teler dam baRay sob jiniser dam baRoche. er provab macher bajareO poReche. ka^cabajaroO coRa: nogorer bivinn ka^cabajare giye dekha geche, sob dhoroner sobojir dam kejiproti tin theke pa^c Taka baRanO hoyeche. notun bajarer bybosayI mO. alomas khan boleno, âoamora zoSOr theke Trake ka^camal ani. 15 din age Trak vaRa diyechi 15 hajar Taka. jwalani teler dam baRay ei soptahe sei vaRa 24 hajar Taka hoyeche. otirikt Taka kOtha theke asobe. tai badhy hoye sobojir dam baRiye sadharoN kretader kach theke sei Taka OThanO hocche.â poribohon khateO biSrriNgkhola: got 29 Disemwr theke dUropallar basozatrIder vaRa

âopu^jibajare marrcenT byangker vUmikaâ SIrrShok ek seminare prodhan otithir boktobye tini e kotha bolen. esoisir ceyaromyan marrcenT byangker karrykromer somalOcona kore boleno, marrcenT byangkogulO tader mUl karrykrom theke sore eseche. tara karrykrom poricalonay nijera lavoban hote pareni, biniyOgokarIderoO lavoban korote pareni. borong uvoye kShotigrost hoyeche. sutorang poramorrSoseba O gobeShoNaseba prodaner madhyme tader pu^jibajarer unnoyone kaj caliye zete hobe. biemobier sovapoti e hafijer sovapotitwe seminare onyanyer modhye esoisir sodosy amojad hOseno, arif khano, abodus salam sikodaro, inosyurens oyasOsiyeSon bangladeSer (oaiebi) sovapoti Sekh kobir hOseno, Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sovapoti Sakil rijovI, coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sovapoti al maruf khano, senTral DipOjiTori 
bangladeSer (osiDibielo) siiO em eic samad promukh boktoby den. onuShThan soNGcalona koren biemobier sohosovapoti tanojil ahomed. pyaksepO SeSh hocche aj soroNGjam O mORok khate sohayota deOyar aSwas pyaksepOte e rokom bivinn poNy prodorrSon kora hoy tOIri pOSak khater soroNGjamo, prozukti O mORokojat poNysamogrI niye car dinobyapI âopyaksepO-o20o12â antorrjatik mela aj rObobar SeSh hocche. edike got dui dine mela praNggoNe e khater Opor duTi seminar onuShThit hoy. ete sorokarer dujon montrI tOIri pOSaker soroNGjam O mORok khater bikaSe sohayota deOyar aSwas den. bangladeS garrmenTos eksesorij oyanD pyakejing myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSon (obijiepiemoie) melaTir ayOjon koreche. pyaksepOr paSapaSi aroO duTi mela Suru 
coloche. 11tom âogarrmenTekoâ ebong trritIy âoiyarrn oyanD febrikos sOrrsing feyar SOâ mela duTir zOUth ayOjok jakariya TreD oyanD feyar inTaronyaSonal ebong eesoke TreD oyanD eksibiSon. boNggobondhu antorrjatik sommelon kendre mela tinoTi got brrihospotibar Suru hoy. melar trritIy din gotokal Sonibar sokale âomORok poNyâ niye seminar onuShThit hoy. ete prodhan otithi chilen SilpomontrI dilIp boRuya. biSeSh otithi chilen senTar for polisi Dayaloger (osipiDi) nirrwahI poricalok mOstafijur rohoman. seminare mUl probondh uposthapon koren inDiyan inosTiTiuT ob pyakejing poricalok en si saha. sovapotitw koren bijiepiemoier sovapoti rafej alom cOUdhurI. seminare mOstafijur rohoman boleno, âotOIri pOSak roptanite biSeSh obodan rakhoche pyakejing Silp. age pyakejing 
poNy amodani korote hotO. borrtomane deSei ut''padit hocche. er fole liD Taim kome geche ebong bOIdeSik mudrar saSroy hocche.â tini SilpoTir bikaSe sohayota dite sorokarer proti ahwan janan. SilpomontrI dilIp boRuya boleno, âosorokarer bighOShit nIti hocche deSoke Silpayon kora. roptanimukhI onyany SilpoprotiShThaner motO soroNGjam O mORokopoNy ut''padonokarI protiShThan nogod sohayota paOyar zOgyta rakhe. karoN SilponItite bOIShomy rakha hoyoni.â montrI deSe ekoTi pyakejing inosTiTiuT korar biShoye sohozOgitar aSwas den. edike got Sukrobar pOSak khater soroNGjam niye arekoTi seminar onuShThit hoy. ete prodhan otithi chilen baNijymontrI gOlam mOhammod kader. bijiepiemoie sovapoti rafej alom cOUdhurIr sovapotitwe seminare biSeSh otithi hisebe boktoby den biSiShT 
orrthonItibid debopriy voTTacarry. seminare mUl probondh uposthapon koren mokobul ahomed khan. seminare baNijymontrI gOlam mOhammod kader boleno, pOSakoSilper prosarer jony sorokar deSe âogarrmenTos polliâ goRe tOlar udyOg niyeche. baNijymontrI aroO boleno, garrmenTos eksesorij ebong pyakejing poNy bideS theke amodani na kore deSe ut''padon koray bOIdeSik mudra saSroy ebong deSe korrmosongsthaner suzOg hocche. deSer cahida pUroN kore esob poNy bideSe roptani korote hobe. montrI aroO boleno, garrmenTos eksesorij O pyakejing poNy khat theke bochore pray 30o0 kOTi marrkin Dolar bOIdeSik mudra orrjit hoy. e porimaN aroO baRate hobe. lOkosaner mukhe kuShTiya cinikol cuktiboddh caShira akh dicchen na cuktiboddh caShira akh na 
deOyay kuShTiya sugar milos ebar byapok lOkosaner mukhe poRoche. jana geche, caShira akh niye milomukhI hocchen na. ta^ra akh ut''padoner por ta gOpone baire beSi dame bikri kore dicchen kingba nijerai guR tOIri korochen. korrmokorrtader sUtre jana zayo, ek lakh 80 hajar Ton cini ut''padonokShomotasomponn sorokari ei karokhanaTite ebar cini ut''padoner lokShymatra dhora hoy matr 25 hajar Ton. othoc caShider kach theke ekhon porrynt ze porimaN akh paOya geche, ta diye matr saRe tin hajar Toner motO cini ut''padit hote pare. cinikoloTir bybosthapona poricalok ajijur rohoman janano, rriNo, bIjo, sar O kITonaSok diye cuktiboddh caShider akh caShe sohozOgita kora hoy. 
othoc caShira akh ut''padoner por ta sorokari kroyokendrer madhyme karokhanay na ene onytr bikri kore dicchen. kingba ta^ra odhik munafar lOve nijerai guR tOIri korochen. e karoNe cinikoler cahida onuzayI maTh theke akh paOya zacche na. songSliShT byktira janano, meheropurer gangnI; kuShTiyar veRamara, dOUlotopuro, miropuro, kumarokhalI ebong jhinaidoher SOIlokupa upojelar ekangSer caShider soNgge kuShTiya sugar miloser cukti royeche. ebar pa^c hajar 60o0 ekor jomite koyek jater akher caSh hoyeche. kintu mil peyeche matr tin hajar 30o0 ekor jomir akh. karokhanaTir akh songgroher lokShymatra 70 hajar Ton holeO peyeche matr 38 hajar Ton akh. caShira janano, proti moN akher sorokari mUly 
10o0 Taka, za baire 120 Taka dore bikri kora zay. ta chaRa akh diye guR banaleO valO lav hoy. se jony ta^ra cinikole akh dite agroh hariyechen. Seyarobajaro: saptahik porryalOcona doropotoner ekoTi soptah got Sukrobar soptaher SeSh karrydibose eSiyar Seyarobajare chil miSr proboNota deSer Seyarobajar doropotoner arekoTi soptah par korol. notun bochorer dwitIy soptahe ei doropotoner ghoTona ghoTol. bajaro-osongSliShTora bolocheno, deSer samogrik orrthonIti niye bivinn moholer SoNgka, asonn mudranIti O nanamukhI gujobe bajare oswavabik doropoton ghoTeche. zodiO esob biShoye biniyOgokarIder vIt hoOyar motO zOUktik kOnO karoN chil na. prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGje (oDiesoi) ek soptaher bybodhane sadharoN mUlysUcok pray 
saRe choy SotangS ba 352 poyenT kome geche. paSapaSi ekoi somoyer dOInik goR lenodener porimaN neme eseche pray saRe 40o0 kOTi Takay. soptahojuRe Dhakar bajare lenoden hoOya kOmpanigulOr modhye pray 91 SotangS Seyarer dam komeche. soptaher pa^c karrydiboser modhye car dinoi Diesoite doropoton hoyeche. zOgazOg kora hole Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI prothom alOke boleno, got soptaher doropoton chil oprotyaSit. zodiO ei doropotoner pechone beS koyekoTi biShoy kaj koreche. deSer orrthonIti niye bivinn mohol theke zesob boktoby tule dhora hocche, tate biniyOgokarIder modhye vIti tOIri hoyeche. paSapaSi mudranIti O onyany kichu biShoy niye bajare gujob choRanO hocche. Sakil rijovIr mote, deSer 
orrthonIti kichuTa caper modhye royeche, seTa Thik. kintu e niye ze dhoroner boktoby tule dhora hocche, orrthonItir obostha totoTa kharap ekhonO hoyoni. Diesoi sovapoti aroO boleno, âoza^ra eroi modhye Seyar bikri kore diyecheno, ta^der ekoTi ongS bajare aroO doropoton ghoTanOr ceShTa korochen. e jony nana gujob choRanO hocche. zate kore ta^ra aroO kom dame Seyar kinote paren. ar sadharoN biniyOgokarIra esob gujob amole niye Seyar bikri kore lOkosaner mukhe poRochen. biniyOgokarIder ucito, gujobe kan na diye valO mOUlovittir Seyare biniyOg kore kichuTa dhOIrry dharoN kora.â bajaro-osongSliShTora janano, sadharoN biniyOgokarIder atoNgkit hoye Seyar bikrir caper karoNe bajare oswavabik doropoton ghoToche. kintu 
sei tulonay doropoton rOdhe pratiShThanik biniyOgokarIder ongSogrohoN nei. pratiShThanik biniyOgokarIra zothazothovabe biniyOge egiye ele ei dhoroner bikrir cap samal deOya somvob hotO. edike, got soptah SeShe Diesoite mOT lenodener porimaN kome da^Riyeche dui hajar 295 kOTi Takayo, ager soptahe zar porimaN chil pray tin hajar 460 kOTi Taka. sei hisabe ek soptaher bybodhane Dhakar bajare lenoden komeche 33 doSomik 67 SotangS ba ek hajar 165 kOTi Taka. paSapaSi dOInik goR lenodener porimaN neme eseche 459 kOTi Takayo, ager soptahe zar porimaN chil pray 692 kOTi Taka. sei hisabe dOInik goR lenoden komeche pray 233 kOTi Taka. soptahojuRe Dhakar bajare 272Ti 
kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye 247Ti Seyarer dam komeche, beReche matr 19Tir ar oporiborrtit chil caroTi Seyarer dam. soptah SeShe Diesoir sadharoN sUcok neme eseche pray pa^c hajar 114 poyenTe. zodiO bochorer prothom soptahe Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok pray car SotangS ba 20o9 poyenT beRechil. got soptah SeShe Diesoite Seyarer mUly ay onupater (opii reSiO) goR varitw kome da^Riyeche 13 doSomik 43-oe. lenodenozOgy Seyarer songjNGa nirrdharoNe bOIThoko: Seyarobajare notun sUcok calur age lenodenozOgy Seyarer (ofri-oflOTo) songjNGa nirrdharoNe aj rObobar bOIThoke bosoche niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi) komiTi. got 26 Disemwr esoisir sodosy arif khaner netrritwe ei 
komiTi goThon kora hoy. komiTite Dhaka sTok eksoceNGj (oDiesoi)o, coTTogram sTok eksoceNGj (osiesoi) O senTral DipOjiTori bangladeS limiTeDer (osiDibielo) protinidhiO royechen. jana zayo, eroi modhye komiTi lenodenozOgy Seyar biShoye bivinn pokSher motamot songgroh koreche. sesob motamoter vittite fri-oflOT Seyarer songjNGa nirrdharoN kora hobe. edike, Sudhu fri-oflOT Seyarer vittite bajare notun mUlysUcok nirrdharoNer siddhant niyeche esoisi. khulona SipoiyarrDe ekotre 14Ti jahajer nirrmaNokaj coloche sorokari jahaj nirrmaNokarI protiShThan khulona SipoiyarrD limiTeDer 54 bochorer itihase ei prothom ekosoNgge sorrwOccosongkhyk jahajer nirrmaNokaj coloche. er modhye deSe prothom zuddhojahajoO royeche. khulona SipoiyarrDe borrtomane 14Ti jahaj ekosoNgge nirrmit hocche. er modhye royeche nOUbahinIr pa^coTi zuddhojahajo, zar 
nirrmaNokaj prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina got bochor 6 marrc udwOdhon koren. aroO royeche tinoTi boR dhorone oyel Tyangkar (otelobahI jahajo)o, ekoTi mot''sy gobeShoNa jahajo, ekoTi ogninirrwapok jahajo, ekoTi senabahinIr Tyangk bohonokarI jahaj O duTi poNybahI jahaj. paSapaSi coloche bivinn barrj O ponTun meramoter kaj. edike got orrthobochore protiShThanoTi pray 25 kOTi Taka munafa koreche. eTiO ezabot''kaler modhye sorrwOcc munafa. jana geche, khulona SipoiyarrD protiShThar por theke odhikangS somoyoi lOkosaner modhy diye geche. tobe 1999 saler 3 okTObor bangladeS ispat O prokOUSol songstha (obiesoisi) theke nOUbahinIr kache hostantorer por thekei protiShThanoTi ghure da^Rate Suru kore ebong 12 bochor dhore deSer munafar mukh 
dekhe. othoc lagatar lOkosaner karoNe 1990 sale tot''kalIn sorokar eTike rugN Silp hisebe ghOShoNa korechil. 1999 theke 20o11 sal porrynt ei protiShThanoTi 113 kOTi 32 lakh Taka munafa koreche. goRe proti bochor munafa hoyeche noy kOTi 44 lakh Taka. protiShThaner upomohabybosthapok komanDar motiur rohoman prothom alOke janano, 72 kOTi Taka dayodena niye âo99 saler 3 okTObor nOUbahinI khulona SipoiyarrDer dayitw grohoN kore. eropor theke khulona SipoiyarrDoke ar pechone takate hoyoni. nOUbahinI dayitw neOyar por theke e porrynt SipoiyarrD 45Ti notun jahaj nirrmaN ebong 366Ti jahaj meramot koreche. e protiShThane sthayI Sromiko-okorrmocarI achen 214 jon. korrmokorrta achen 71 jon. er modhye 
12 jon nOUbahinIr. osthayI Sromiko-okorrmocarI 472 jon ebong korrmokorrta achen 24 jon. protiShThaner mohabybosthapok kyapTen munirul isolam janano, kOnO dhoroner sorokari arrthik sahazy chaRai sompUrrN swnirrvorovabe protiShThanoTi dIrrgh 12 bochor dhore tar sob byyovar bohon kore zacche. sorokarer sob dhoroner paOna poriSOdher por bigot pa^c bochore ayokor O vyaT babod joma diyeche pray saRe 32 kOTi Taka. e prosoNgge khulona SipoiyarrDer bybosthapona poricalok komODor riyajouddin ahomed prothom alOke boleno, bivinn besamorik jahaj nirrmaNer por somproti bangladeS nOUbahinI O senabahinIr jony zuddhojahaj nirrmaN Suru koreche khulona SipoiyarrD. aroO boR jahaj nirrmaNer uddeSye mongla theke 12 kilOmiTar dUre sundoroboner joyomonigOl elakay 43 
ekor jomi odhigrohoN kora hoyeche. prosoNggoto, mohanogor khulonar rUposa nodIr tIr ghe^She pray 69 ekor jomir Opor 1954 sale protiShTha kora hoy deSer onytom brrihot'' jahaj nirrmaN protiShThan khulona SipoiyarrD limeTeD. 1957 saler 23 novemwr protiShThanoTi anuShThanikovabe zatra Suru kore. swadhInota-oporoborrtI ei protiShThanoTi dayitw ney bangladeS ispat O prokOUSol songstha (obiesoisi). khOla poNy khalase biSeShayit Tarrminal nirrmaNer udyOg jahajer khOle kore ana khOla poNy khalaser jony biSeShayit Tarrminal nirrmaNer udyOg niyeche coTTogram bondor korrtrripokSh. bondorer lalodiyar cor elakay ei Tarrminal nirrmaN kora hote pare. bondor sUtr janayo, got 10 Disemwr biSeShayit Tarrminaler ek hajar miTar jeTi nirrmaNer somvabyta somIkSha protibedon 
joma diyeche buyeTer byurO ob risarrc TesTing oyanD konosaloTeSon (obiaroTisi) bivag. protibedone Tarrminal nirrmaNer pokShe mot deOya hoy. bondor korrtrripokSher prathomik hisab onuzayI, bondorer 14 theke 15 nomwr khaler majhamajhi elakay ei Tarrminal nirrmaNe anumanik 80o0 kOTi Taka khoroc hote pare. bondorer bohirrnONgor theke kOnO ba^k otikrom na kore ei Tarrminale jahaj veRanOr suzOg thakobe. borrtomane bondor cyaneler duTi jhu^kipUrrN ba^k otikrom kore mUl jeTite jahaj veRanO hocche. bondorer ceyaromyan komODor em anoOyarul isolam prothom alOke boleno, ei Tarrminale khadySosy, simenT klingkarosoh khOla poNy khalaser jony biSeShayit jeTi nirrmaNer porikolpona royeche. esob jeTite swyongkriy poddhotite poNy khalaser bybostha rakha hobe. 
tini boleno, somvabyta somIkSha protibedon zacai kore montroNaloye prostab paThanO hobe. bondorer korrmokorrtara janano, 20 bochor age theke bondore konoTeinare poNy poribohon jonopriyota pay. eropor sob unnoyon korrmokaND hoyeche konoTeinar poribohonokendrik. konoTeinar OThanamay gyanTri kren chaRaO konoTeinar bybosthaponay calu hoyeche otyadhunik swyongkriy poddhoti. esob udyOger karoNe konoTeinar jahajer poNy OThanamar dokShotar sUcoke ogrogoti hoyeche. kintu sadharoN poNy OThanamay kOnO adhunik bybostha na thakay esob poNy khalaser dokShotar sUcoker kOnO ogrogoti nei. borong poNy amodani baRar soNgge sUcokoO nimnogamI hoyeche. janote caile nOUporibohon montroNaloyo-osongkrant songsodIy komiTir sovapoti nUre alom cOUdhurI liTon muThOfOne prothom alOke boleno, âonirrmaNo, poricalona O hostantor (obiOTi)oâ vittite 
ei Tarrminale besorokari opareTor niyOg deOya hobe. swyongkriy poddhotite poNy khalaser zontropati songzOjoner Sorrt deOya hobe niyOg paOya opareToroke. bondor sUtr janayo, bondore porIkShamUlokovabe calu thaka enosiTisoh bidyman tinoTi Tarrminaler mOT 19Ti jeTi royeche. er modhye khOla O bostabondI poNy khalas hoy choyoTi jeTite. esob jeTite khOla poNy khalase adhunik zontropati nei. sonaton poddhotite jahajer khOle thaka khOla gom prothome Tiner baks diye bostay voren Sromikera. ony Sromikera sesob bosta selai kore jahaj ba bondorer SOr krene diye Trake bOjhai koren. ei prokriyay somoy O orrth beSi khoroc hoy. bondorer bivinn tothy-oupatt theke dekha zayo, bondore zot poNy OThanama hoy 
tar pray tin vager dui vagoi hocche konoTeinarobihIn sadharoN poNy. 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore coTTogram bondore zot poNy amodani-oroptani hoyeche, tar modhye saRe 65 SotangS poNyi konoTeinar chaRa khOla O bostabondI akare poribohon kora hoy. beReche viRo, miloche nana chaR baNijy mela jomojomaT Dhaka antorrjatik baNijy melar ekoTi sTole poNy dekhay byst kretara masobyapI Dhaka antorrjatik baNijy mela ekhon purOpuri jomojomaT. protidin hajar hajar manuSh melay asoche. porryayokrome becabikri baRoche. biSeSh kore chuTir dine upoce poRa viR hocche. ete melay ongS neOya odhikangS bybosayI sontOSh prokaS korechen. melar coturrdoS din gotokal Sonibar dupure giye dekha zayo, mela praNggoNe dolobe^dhe asoche manuSh. dupur 
par hoye bikel goRaitei viR beRe zay koyek guN. tobe probeS TikiT kroyer porryapt buth thakay melay Dhukote khub ekoTa beg pete hoyoni dorrSonarrthIder. melay grrihosthali O ilekoTronik poNysamogrIr sTologulOte tulonamUlok beSisongkhyk kreta viR korote dekha zay. deSi-obideSi esob sTole ha^Ri-opatil theke Suru kore Oveno, Tivi, frijosoh nityproyOjonIy onek jinisopotr zacai-obachai kore kinechen onekei. deSIy ilekoTronik poNyer brryanD OyaloToner pyaviliyone viR chil cOkhe poRar motO. saSroyI mUlye manosommot deSIy poNy hoOyay edike beSi agroh bole janalen koyekojon kreta. onydike kretasadharoNoke akrriShT korote notun onekogulO poNy eneche protiShThanoTi. mela upolokShe sat SotangS mUlochaRosoh skrryac karrDer madhyme akorrShoNIy upoharoO dicche tara. OyaloToner 
bybosthapok (okoropOreT selos oyanD marrkenTing) asadujjaman boleno, âokretader kach theke ebarer melay ovabonIy saRa peyechi. soboceye beSi bikri hocche frij. protidin pray 35 theke 40oTi.â asadujjaman aroO janano, OyaloToner frij 21 theke 39 hajaro, roNgin Tivi 11 hajar 80o0 theke 13 hajar 50o0o, elosiDi Tivi 23 theke 70 hajar 90o0 Takay bikri hocche. e chaRa ache eloiDi Tivi, mOTorosaikelo, Oveno, jenareToro, mObail fOnoseTo, OyaSing meSino, SItatoponiyontrit zontro, ayoron ityadi. brryak enTaropraijeser mini pyaviliyone brryaker 18Tir modhye pa^coTi enTaropraij ongS niyeche. egulO hocche: brryak silko, brryak risaikeloD hyanDomeiD peparo, brryak narrsari, brryak cikon O brryak sOlar. silk SaRi, hostojat poNy, sOUroSoktir 
poNy, bivinn dhoroner orrkiD theke Suru kore narrsari poNy O murogir mangs paOya zacche ekhane. mela upolokShe silk SaRite pa^c SotangS mUlychaR O sOlar pyanele bivinn upohar dicche protiShThanoTi. brryak enTaropraijeser bybosthapok SiSir kumar nath boleno, nirrdharit kretarai beSi asoche. tobe poNyer man valO hoOyay notun kretaraO asoche. jatIy mohila songsthar mini pyaviliyone ekosoNgge aToTi sTol ache. hostoSilpo, SaRi, byago, SOpis theke khabarer dOkan porrynt ache ei pyaviliyone. fole ekobar holeO Dhu^ maroche onekei. melay asa dorrSonarrthI O bybosayIder byangking subidha dite ache sOnalI, jonota O Dac-obangla byangker mini pyaviliyon. Taka tOlar subidha dite melar dui paSe marrkenTail O isolamI 
byangker prrithok duTi osthayI eTiem buthoO sthapon kora hoyeche. pa^coTi eTiem O duTi âoDipOjiToâ meSin ache Dac-obangla byangker mini pyaviliyone. fole melatei ekhon Taka joma deOya O tOlar subidha pacchen kreta O bybosayIra. e chaRa mObail byangking, bivinn seba O tothy diye sohayota korochen byangker korrmokorrtara. byangkoTir korrmokorrta Sahanur isolam boleno, protidin pray ek hajarer beSi manuSh eTiem bybohar korochen. e chaRa bybosayIra kOnO dhoroner jhokkijhamela chaRai Taka joma dicchen. Sahanur aroO boleno, deSer zekOnO byangk kingba deSer bairer byangker karrD bybohar kore Dac-obanglar eTiem theke Taka tulote paroben ze keu. melay bivinn dhoroner soroNGjamo, pOSako, karrpeTo, prosadhono, sOUndorryborrdhok samogrI,

Diesoir barrShik sadharoN sova 15 marrc deSer prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) car poricalok pode nirrwaconer tarikh ghOShoNa kora hoyeche. agamI 11 marrc ei nirrwacon onuShThit hobe. nirrwacon somponn hoOyar por 15 marrc protiShThanoTir barrShik sadharoN sova SeShe (oejiemo) nirrwacit poricalokoder vOTe notun poricalona porrShod goThit hobe. got soptahe Diesoir borrtoman poricalona porrShoder sovay agamI 15 marrc sadharoN sovar tarikh nirrdharoN kora hoy. ekoi sovay car poricalok pode nirrwacon poricalonar jony Dhaka biSwbidyaloyer SikShok O Diesoir poricalok abul hasemoke prodhan kore tin sodosyer nirrwacon komiSon goThon 
kora hoyeche. komiSoner opor dui sodosy holen songsthaTir poricalok Oyakarujjaman O sodosy em kamalouddin. paSapaSi nirrwaconI birOdh niShpottir jony tin sodosyer ekoTi apil bOrrDoO goThon kora hoyeche. em akoborI alIke prodhan kore goThit apil bOrrDer ony dui sodosy holen Diesoir poricalok e ke em rokiful isolam O bangladeS byangker nirrwahI poricalok sudhIr condr das.
