Diesoite siiO-osiefoOr zOgodan Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta (osiiO) hisebe mOhammod mOSarorof hOsen ebong prodhan orrth korrmokorrta (osiefoO) hisebe Suvr kanti cOUdhurI zOgodan korechen. aj 
rObobar ta^ra uvoye zOgodan koren bole Diesoir prokaSona O jonosongzOg bivager upomohabybosthapok Sofikur rohoman swakShorit ek songbad bijNGoptite jananO hoy. bijNGoptite bola hoyo, got 13 Disemwr Diesoir poricalona porrShod mOhammod mOSarorof hOsenoke siiO hisebe niyOger siddhant ney. pore 27 Disemwr pu^jibajar niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi) onumOdon dey. e chaRa somproti Diesoir porrShod sovay Suvr kantike siefoO hisebe niyOger biShoyoTi onumOdon deOya hoy. korrmoSalay ovimot paTer ovyntorIN O antorrjatik bajare nojor deOyar tagid paTopoNy bybohare bangladeSoke ovyntorIN bajare nojor deOyar paSapaSi biSwbajare byapok cahida thakar suzOg ba roptanir somvabona kaje lagate hobe. rajodhanIr brryak senTare gotokal Sonibar kyaTalisT 
ayOjit paT O bangladeSer orrthonItibiShoyok ek korrmoSalay boktara e tagid den. korrmoSalay boktara boleno, biSwbyapI din din paTopoNyer proti agroh baRoche. fole paT khate roptani ay baRar bipul somvabona royeche. kintu suzOgoTi kaje lagate paroche na bangladeS. e chaRa paTer ovyntorIN bajaroTiO beS boRo, kintu obohelit. ovyntorIN bajar soboceye valOvabe kaje lagiyeche varot. se onuzayI paTopoNy bybohare bangladeSokeO varoter motO ovyntorIN bajarer dike nojor dite hobe. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit e korrmoSalay prodhan otithi chilen. ete biSeSh otithi chilen bostr O paTomontrI abodul lotif siddikI. korrmoSalay boktoby den bangladeS paTokol songsthar (obijeemosi) ceyaromyan Ti Di mitro, bangladeS juT spinarrs 
oyasOsiyeSoner (obijeesoe) sovapoti mOhammod Samos uj jOha ebong bangladeS paTokol somitir (obijeemoe) sovapoti nojorul hok. kyaTalisTer SahorOj jolil korrmoSalay swagot boktoby den. korrmoSalay senTar for polisi Dayalog (osipiDi) O bangladeS prokOUSol biSwbidyaloy (obuyeTo) duTi alada somIkSha protibedon uposthapon kore. protibedonogulO uposthapon koren zothakrome sipiDir jyeShTh gobeShoNa felO khondokar gOlam mOyajjem O buyeTer SikShok nUr al kuddus. korrmoSalay soNGcalok chilen sangbadik jahidujjaman faruk. somIkSha protibedone bola hoyeche, polipropailiner (opipi) soNgge protizOgita kore paToke Tike thakote hocche. tobe aSar kotha ze biSwbyapI pipir bybohar komoche. ar e suzOgoTi kaje lagiyeche varoto, cIn O pakistan. nijeder protizOgitaSIl kore tuleche tara. kintu bytikrom bangladeS. 
roptani onek baRanO dUre thako, ovyntorIN bajaroTiroi zothazoth bybohar korote paroche na ei deS. somIkShay bola hoyeche, 20o10 sale pas hoOya badhytamUlok paTer byag bybohar ainoTi bastobayon kora geleO bochore deSe 84 kOTi pis paTer byager dorokar hobe. ar ekekoTi byag tinobar bybohar koroleO cahida da^Ray 28 kOTi pis. othoc borrtomane bybohar hocche matr 90 hajar pis. orrthat'' purO somvabonai poRe royeche, kintu kaje laganO hocche na. paTonIti proNoyon O paT khater jony gotiSIl netrritw tOIri kora ebong chOTokhaTO poriborrton ene ut''padonoSIlota baRanO, varoter samprotik Sulkomukt roptani ghOShoNar suzOg grohoNo, mojuri baRiye holeO karokhanay dokSh Sromikoder dhore rakha, narIder jony 
kaj korar suzOg tOIri kora, paT khater proti byangkogulOr netibacok drriShTivoNggir poriborrton ebong paT khate notun projonmer udyOkta SreNI goRe OThar proti gurutwarOp kora hoy protibedon duTite. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit boleno, âoamader jomi komo, kintu ut''padon baRate hobe.â protibedone paTer krriShi ongSoTi bad poReche bole somalOcona koren tini. orrthomontrI boleno, âo140 bochor age theke paToSilpe biSwnetrritwer vUmikay thekeO aj amora pichiye. somoyer soNgge tal miliye poNyer bohumukhinota O prozuktigot unnoyon korote na paray emonoTi hoyeche.â biSwbajare paTopoNyer Seyar totoTa na baRar kotha ullekh kore orrthomontrI ontot borrtoman obosthan dhore rakhar biShoye tagid den. ekoi soNgge krriShi O Silper 
soNgge joRit bole orrthonItite paT boR obodan rakhote pare bole tini biSwas koren. bostr O paTomontrI abodul lotif siddikI janano, badhytamUlok paTer byag bybohar ainoTi pas kora holeO ta proyOg korote parochen na tini. montrI boleno, âoain proyOg korote giye dekhi ami ni:soNggo, keu sohozOgita koroche na.â tobe khady O krriShi montroNaloy sohozOgita koreche bole swIkar koren tini. Silp montroNaloyer vUmikar byapare bolote giyeO theme zan tini. bijeemosir ceyaromyan Ti Di mitr boleno, bangladeS rosayon Silp songstharoi (obisiaisi) bochore choy kOTi byag dorokar. kintu ta bybohar koroche na tara. badhytamUlok paTer byag byboharer ain karrykorer biShoye gurutwarOp koren tini. bijeesoer 
sovapoti Samos uj jOha boleno, paToke krriShivittik Silp ghOShoNa kora holeO bastobe krriShivittik hisebe morryada deOya hoy na. fire dekha 20o11 nitypoNyer bajare najehal manuSh nitypoNyer uccomUly bochorojuRei sadharoN manuSher vOgantir karoN chil. cini, vOjytelo, chOla, Dalo, gu^Ra dudho, sobojisoh beS kichu poNy kinote rItimotO najehal hoyeche kretara. oboSy SIter sobojir agomone bochorer SeSh somoyoTay ka^cabajarer uttap onekoTai keTe geche. nirrwaconI iSotehare aOyamI lIg drobomUly sohonIy rakhar biShoyoTike ogradhikar talikay rekhechil. kintu drobymUlyi SeSh porrynt sorokaroke soboceye beSi somalOconar mukhe feleche. faruk khaner montroNaloy bodoloO e karoNe hoyeche bole rajonOItik somalOcokera mone koren. kemon chil bajaro: 20o10 saler 31 Disemwr 
liTaroproti soyabin teler dam chil 94 theke 96 Taka. Thik ek bochor por gotokal Sonibar soyabin tel kinote kretake gunote hocche 124 theke 128 Taka. ek bochore soyabin teler dam beReche 32 doSomik 63 SotangS. ei tothy sorokareroi protiShThan TreDing koropOreSon ob bangladeSer (oTisibi). borrtomane proti keji cini bikri hocche 56 theke 58 Takay. ek bochor age bikri hotO 55 Takay. apatodrriShTite cinir bajar sthir bolei mone hote pare. tobe got bochor ze poNyTi vOktader beSi vugiyeche, seTi hocche cini. romojaner ek mas ageO 58 theke 60 Takay bikri hoOya cini hoThat'' kore hoye zay 65 theke 70 Taka. sorokar 
65 Taka dor be^dhe dile bajar thekei udhaO hoye zay cini. pore cinir mukh dekha geleO dam hoye zay 75 theke 80 Taka. romojan mase chOla niyeO naToker komoti chil na. ek bochorer bybodhane chOlar dam beReche 36 SotangS. 46 Takar chOla bochor SeShe 60 theke 70 Takay bikri hocche. ar romojane uThechil 90 Taka porrynt. ek bochore moyodar damoO beReche 16 SotangS. kejiproti moyoda bikri hocche 42 theke 45 Takay. tobe got bochor cal niye temon durrvOg hoyoni. mOTa caler dam 33 theke 36 Takar modhye sthir chil. dam ekhonO ta-oi. oboSy soru calo, biSeSh kore najiroSail O minikeTer 
dam chil OTha-onamar modhye. bajare ekhon dam kom holeO bochorojuRe pe^yajer jha^je vugeche manuSh. bochorer majhamajhi somoye hoThat'' varot pe^yaj roptanir Opor niShedhajNGa arOp korole ratarati deSer bajare dam 35 theke beRe 45 Taka hoy. tobe ek bochore ovabonIyovabe dam komeche rosuner. 73 SotangS kome ekhon proti keji rosun (odeSi O amodani kora) bikri hocche 35 theke 50 Takay. adar damoO komeche 42 SotangS. bochorojuRei ka^cabajare lege chil agun. sobojir dam chil coRa. begun kinote hoyeche 60 theke 70 Takay. kalO beguner dam tO 80 Taka porrynt uThechil. romojan mase 10o0 gram ka^camoric kinote hoy 30 theke 35 Takay. tobe 
sobojir dam ekhon kom. ekoi obostha macher bajareO. iliSer dam ek bochore beReche 60 SotangSeroO beSi. 350 theke 40o0 Takar iliS kinote hoy ekhon 70o0 theke 750 Takay. orrthonItibidoder mote, 5 theke 6 SotangS porrynt mUlysfIti sohonIy. seTa 10 SotangS chaRiye gele orrthonItir songkoT beRe zay. deSe ekhon sei obosthai coloche. mUlysfItir har 11 doSomik 58 SotangS. got januyarite mUlysfItir har chil 9 doSomik 0o4 SotangS. Sudhu ze khadymUlyer sUcokoi beReche ta noyo, khadybohirrvUt poNyeO mUly beReche bochorer SeSh koyek mase. ucc mUlysfItir ei agune sImit O swlp ayer manuSher jIbonozatray boR dhoroner provab feleche. koShTe ache sadharoN manuSh. Seyarobajare 
bochorojuRe doropoton ar biniyOgokarIr arrtonad Diesoir samone emon bikShOv barobar dekha geche osthitiSIl O doropotoner ekoTi bochor par korol deSer Seyarobajar. 20o11 saler purOTa somoyoi bajarer sob koTi sUcoker byapok poton ghoTeche. er modhy diye Seyarobajar keleNgkari abaroO aOyamI lIg sorokarer Sasonamoler soNgge zukt hoyeche. ebar bajarer utthanoporrwe biniyOgokarIsoh oneke abaroO 1996 saler keleNgkarir ghoTonar aSoNgka korechilen. kintu sorokarer SIrrSh moholosoh songSliShT byktider oneke barobar sei aSoNgkake uRiye diye biniyOgokarIder ovoy diyechilen. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhitosoh bajarosongSliShT byktira bolechileno, âo33 lakh biniyOgokarIr bajare ar kOnO âo96 saler punorabrritti ghoTobe na. karoNo, ei 33 lakh biniyOgokarIi bajarer boR Sokti.â SeSh 
porrynt sei 33 lakh biniyOgokarIr bajarei keleNgkari ghoTe geche. 1996 saler bajarer soNgge 20o11 saler bajarer kaThamOgot poriborrtoner karoNei hoyotO keleNgkarir dhoronoTa palTeche. kintu âo96 sale zemon onek biniyOgokarI pu^ji hariye ni:sw hoyecheno, 20o11 saleO ekoi ghoTona ghoTeche. borong bajarer byapti baRar karoNe ebar ni:sw biniyOgokarIr songkhya bohuguNe beReche. 20o11 saler odhikangS somoyei Dhakay Diesoi voboner samoner soRok bikShubdh biniyOgokarIder dokhole chil. doropotoner protibade deSojuRe bikShOv hoyeche. sara jIboner soNGcoy hariye biniyOgokarIder modhye atmohotyar ghoTonaO ghoTeche. pu^jibajar todont komiTir protibedoner vittite bajar niyontroNe byrrthotar daye sorokar got eprile niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi) veNge diye seTi punorrgoThon kore. 
punorrgoThit komiSonoO bajare doropoton thamate pareni. dharabahik doropoton colote thake. e obosthay poton Thekate O mrrit bajare praN ferate songSliShT byktider abedone bajeTe oprodorrSit orrth ba kalOTaka biniyOger suzOg deOya hoy. kalOTaka biniyOger suzOge bajeTo-oporoborrtI pray ek mas doropotoner brritt theke beriye esechil bajar. kintu seTa dIrrghosthayI hoyoni. julaiyer SeSh dike bajare abaroO doropoton Suru hoy. ei doropoton thamate SeSh porrynt prodhanomontrI Sekh hasinake hostokShep korote hoy. esoisi, bangladeS byangkosoh bajarosongSliShT byktider niye 16 novemwr prodhanomontrI dIrrgh bOIThok koren. Oi bOIThoker por esoisi bajare sthitiSIlota firiye anote swlpo, modhy O dIrrghomeyadi 22 dofa proNOdona ghOShoNa kore; zar pUrrN bastobayoner kaj 
ekhonO coloche. 20o10 sale cahida O jOganer modhye corom varosamyhInota tOIri hoOyay bajarer dhos onibarry hoye OThe. 20o11 saler prothom prantiker prothom dofa dhosoke bajarosongSliShT byktira onibarry hisebe meneO niyechilen. kintu julai mas theke Suru hoOya dwitIy dofa dhos chil sobar kachei oprotyaSit. tai prothom dofa dhoseO za^der pu^jite a^coR lageni, ta^ra dwitIy dofa dhose denar jale aToke poRen. bajar porryalOconay dekha zayo, 20o10 saler 5 Disemwr prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN sUcok chil aT hajar 919 poyenTo, 20o11 sal SeShe ta neme eseche pa^c hajar 258 poyenTe. sei hisabe Diesoi sadharoN mUlysUcok komeche pray tin hajar 661 
poyenT. 30 Disemwr 20o10 saler sUcoker hisab dhorole ek bochorer bybodhane seTi komeche pray tin hajar 32 poyenT. 20o10 saler SeSh karrydibose Diesoite lenodener porimaN chil ek hajar 783 kOTi Taka. 20o11 saler SeSh karrydibose seTi kome da^Riyeche pray 560 kOTi Takay. ei ek bochorer bybodhane dOInik lenoden komeche ek hajar 223 kOTi Taka. ekoi somoyer bybodhane Diesoir bajar mUlodhon 89 hajar kOTi Taka kome da^Riyeche dui lakh 61 hajar kOTi Takay. Seyar keleNgkari khotiye dekhote krriShi byangker ceyaromyan khOndokar ibrahim khaledoke prodhan kore sorokar goThit car sodosyer komiTi 30 dofa supariSosoh 320 prriShThar todont protibedon orrthomontrI abul mal abodul 
muhiter kache joma dey. tate Seyarobajar dhoser jony niyontrok songsthar kShomotar opobyboharo, aini durrwlota, plesomenT bybosar name durrnIti, ekodol songghoboddh biniyOgokarIr karosaji, ainer modhye theke kichusongkhyk udyOkta O kOmpani maliker onOItik korrmokaND O rajonOItik hostokShepoke dayI kora hoy. sei onuzayI esoisir SIrrSh porryayer korrmokorrta theke Suru kore ekodol biniyOgokarIr biruddhe sunirrdiShT tothypromaNosoh aini bybostha grohoNer supariS kore komiTi. Oi supariSer boR ongSoi ekhonO bastobayon kora hoyoni bole komiTir prodhan somproti ek seminare janiyechen. e karoNe bajare corom asthar songkoT tOIri hoyeche boleO tini janan. opor dike prodhanomontrIr hostokSheper por bajar kichuTa swavabik goti fire pete Suru koreche. bochorer SeSh soptaher 
lenoden porryalOcona kore bajarosongSliShT byktira bolocheno, ei goti bojay thakole notun bochore bajar sthitiSIl O swavabik dharay colobe. notun bochore sobar protyaSa sthitiSIl pu^jibajar osthirota noyo, notun bochore ekoTi sthitiSIl pu^jibajarer protyaSa koren biniyOgokarIra. biniyOgokarIder paSapaSi songSliShT bivinn pokShoO ekoi protyaSar kotha bykt koreche. pu^jibajarer soNgge songSliShT byktira bolocheno, got bochor pu^jibajare osthirota biraj koroleO sorokarer pokSh theke beS kichu songskarer kaj hate neOya hoyeche. kichu itibacok udyOgoO neOya hoyeche. egulO bastobayit hole oboSyi pu^jibajare er valO provab poRobe. e biShoye bangladeS pu^jibajar biniyOgokarI OIky poriShoder sanggoThonik sompadok Sahadat ullah firOj prothom alO onolainoke boleno, otIter sob koShTo, bedona vule 
notun bochore notun kichui korochi. amader protyaSa ekoTi sthitiSIl bajar. tini boleno, âoamora got bochorer motO du:swpner modhy diye bybosa korote cai na. amader swpn ekoTi sthitiSIl O SoktiSalI bajar. amar biSwaso, notun bochore amader ei protyaSa pUroN O swpn bastobayit hobe.â OIky poriShoder sovapoti mijan ur roSid cOUdhurI boleno, âogel bochor pu^jibajare corom osthirota biraj koreche. amora Suru thekei ei osthirotar biruddhe andOlon kore asochi. oboSeShe novemwre prodhanomontrIr hostokSheper por beS kichu udyOg neOya hoy. er fole kichuTa holeO bajare sthitiSIlota firote Suru koreche.â ar Oi sob udyOg bastobayoner madhyme ekoTi dIrrghomeyadi sthitiSIl pu^jibajarer protyaSa koren tini. coTTogram sTok 
eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sabek sovapoti fokhor uddin alI ahomed prothom alO onolainoke boleno, âonotun bochore ekoTi sthitiSIl pu^jibajar protyaSa kori.â e kShetre biniyOgokarI, udyOkta O sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSonoke (oesoisi) zothazoth vUmika rakhote hobe. sobai mile ekosoNgge kaj korole bajare sthitiSIlota dhore rakha somvob bole mone koren tini. Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI boleno, otIt theke SikSha niye samoner dike egOle vobiShyt valO zabe bola zay. tini boleno, samoner dine notun notun volO protiShThan bajare asobe. ete biniyOgokarIra aSanwit hoben. sutorang hotaS hoOyar kichu nei, coRai-outoraiyer por oboSyi somvabona asobe. Seyarobajar biSeShojNG O besorokari biSwbidyaloy iunaiTeD inTaronyaSonal iunivarrsiTir odhyapok mO. musa boleno, 
âoajoker bajarer ze iNggito, ta dekhe mone hoyo, pratiShThanik biniyOgokarIra sokriy royechen. eTi ekoTi valO lokShoN.â e obostha biraj korole bajare valO provab poRobe bole tini aSabad bykt koren. nyazymUlyer dabite bikShOv korechen poScimoboNgger krriShok krriShipoNyer nyazymUly prodaner dabite Sukrobar rajyer bivinn elakay dhano, paTo, Sakosoboji puRiye bikShOv prodorrSon korechen poScimoboNgger krriShokera. ete rajyer bivinn jelar jatIy soRok oboruddh hoye poRe O zan colacol byahot hoy. e korrmosUcir Dak dey sara varot krriShokosova. ta^ra rajy sorokaroke nyazymUlye dhano, calo, paTo, alu kroy kore krriShokoder ba^canOr dabi janiyechen. tara rajyer murrSidabado, nodIya, pUrrw O poScim medinIpuro, dokShiN dinajopurosoh onyany jelay bajar 
ebong soRok oborOdh kore. ei oborOdher fole murrSidabado, pUrrw O poScim medinIpuro, nodIya O dokShiN dinajopur jelar jatIy soRoker bohu sthan oboruddh hoye poRe. ei protibad andOloner netrritw den poScimoboNgger sabek montrI cokrodhor maikapo, sipiemer bidhayok roNojit'' kumar moNDolosoh krriShokosovar netara. bangladeS byangker dikonirrdeSona arrthik protiShThaneO 10o% hare mUlodhon songrokShoN badhytamUlok notun e bochor theke obyangking arrthik protiShThanogulOke 10 SotangS hare mUlodhon songrokShoN korote hobe. bangladeS byangk got brrihospotibar e biShoye proyOjonIy dikonirrdeSona jari koreche. kendrIy byangk baNijyik byangkogulOr por deSer arrthik protiShThanogulOr sokShomota brriddhiteO nana proceShTa niye coleche. er age bangladeS byangk byangkingye antorrjatik manosongkrant byasel komiTir supariS onusare 
arrthik khate jhu^kinirrvor sompoder vittite 10 SotangS hare mUlodhon songrokShoNer badhybadhokotar pothonokoSa dey. ar brrihospotibar bangladeS byangker arrthik protiShThan O bajar bivag theke cURant dikonirrdeSona jari kora hoy. bangladeS byangk sUtr janacche, arrthik protiShThanogulOte byasel nItimala bastobayoner kaj 20o10 sal theke ekoTi rODomyaper madhyme jari kora hoy. se alOke protiShThanogulO porIkShamUlokovabe trOImasik vittite protibedon joma dey. tobe januyari theke cURantovabe protibedon dite hobe. kendrIy byangker sepTemwrovittik tothy onuzayI, arrthik protiShThanogulOte borrtomane mUlodhon songrokShoNer goR har da^Riyeche 17 doSomik 0o8 SotangS. er modhye 24Ti protiShThane royeche 10 SotangSer beSi, 19Tite 12 SotangSer beSi ebong 15 SotangSer beSi royeche 17Ti arrthik protiShThane. 
e chaRa borrtomane zesob protiShThaner nyUnotom poriSOdhit mUlodhon royeche 50 kOTi Taka, agamI jun theke ta 10o0 kOTi Takay unnIt korote hobe. aj Suru hocche masobyapI antorrjatik baNijy mela baNijy melay ongSogrohoNokarI protiShThanogulOr sTolo-opyaviliyon nirrmaNer kaj pray SeSh deSer bybosayI O Silp udyOktader poNy prodorrSonIr soboceye boR asor Dhaka antorrjatik baNijy mela-o20o12 (oDiaiTiefo) aj rObobar Suru hocche. rajodhanIr Serebangla nogore masobyapI ei melar udwOdhon koroben prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina. melar ayOjon koreche roptani unnoyon byurO (oipibi) O baNijy montroNaloy. eTi hocche DiaiTiefer 17tom asor. 12Ti deSer 47Ti protiShThan ebarer melay ongS nicche. ongSogrohoNokarI deSogulO holO: cIno, varoto, irano, dokShiN kOriya, pakistano, 
thailyanDo, zuktoraShTro, turosko, siNggapuro, maloyeSiya, songzukt arob amirat O morokkO. ebarer melay pyaviliyono, primiyar pyaviliyono, mini pyaviliyono, sadharoN sTolo, resTurenTo, ekoTi binOdon parrkosoh 50o6Ti sTol thakobe. esob sTole bivinn dhoroner soroNGjamo, karrpeTo, kosomeTikoso, sOUndorryborrdhok samogrI, ilekoTronik poNy, paTojat poNy, camoRajat poNy O paduka, khelar samogrI, khelona, sTeSonari, juyelari, siramikos poNy, asobabopotro, hostojatosoh nana dhoroner poNy prodorrSit hobe. bangladeSer itihas O boNggobondhu somporrke janate melay âoboNggobondhu ebong bangladeSoâ SIrrShok ekoTi biSeSh pyaviliyon rakha hoyeche. ebarer melay boyoskoder jony 20 Taka ebong SiSuder jony 10 Taka probeSomUly dhora hoyeche. ayOjokera aSa korocheno, ei mela poNyer prostutokarok O kretader modhye somporrker unnoyon ghoTabe. 
er fole notun notun poNy tOIrite udyOktara agrohI hoben. ta chaRa melay ongS neOya bideSi protiShThanogulOO bangladeSer bajar somporrke dharoNa nite parobe. mela praNggoNe gotokal Sonibar ek songbad sommelone baNijymontrI ji em kader boleno, âoamora aSa korochi, ebarer melay protidin ek lakher beSi dorrSonarrthI hobe ebong tat''kShoNik karryadeSer porimaNoO beSi hobe.â 20o11 sale onuShThit baNijymelay 25 kOTi Takar tat''kShoNik karryadeS paOya giyechil. 20o10 sale er porimaN chil 22 kOTi 86 lakh Taka. baNijymontrI janano, melay nicchidr nirapotta niScit korote mela praNggoNer bivinn sthane 80oTi klOj sarrkiT kyamera (osisiTivi) bosanO hoyeche. ek proSner jobabe baNijymontrI janano, baNijy mela ayOjoner jony Dhakar 
pUrrwacole ekoTi sthayI venyu ba jayoga tOIrir kaj coloche. rajouker soNgge alOcona kore pUrrwacole 20 ekor jayoga cihnit kora hobe. songbad sommelone boktoby den baNijysocib gOlam hOsen. Diemopir bijNGopti: gotokal ek bijNGoptite Dhaka meTrOpoliTon puliS (oDiemopi) janayo, mela colakale sorokari chuTir dine khamarobaRi theke agaroga^O porrynt rikoSa, vyano, ThelagaRisoh ozantrik zan colacol bondh thakobe. bijNGoptite bola hoyo, Sukro-oSonibarosoh chuTir dine agaroga^O lingk rOD (onotun soRoko) bybohar kore boNggobondhu antorrjatik sommelon kendr krosing hoye melay DhOka zabe na. tader agaroga^O laiT krosing hoye melay probeS korote hobe. Diemopi janayo, melay nirrdiShT fi diye gaRi parrking kora zabe. nijosw gaRi niye asa 
byktider nirrdiShT sthane parrking korote hobe. ar Trafik niyontroN kokSher samone nirrdharit sthane mOTorosaikel rakhote hobe. melay asa-ozaOyar kShetre Trafiko-obybostha somporrke zekOnO biShoye janote mela praNggoNe obosthit Trafik niyontroN kokSher soNgge 0o1745292392 nomwre zOgazOg korar onurOdh janiyeche Diemopi. koThin ek bochor par korol antorrjatik Seyarobajar zuktoraShTroke bad dile biSwjuRe boR boR Seyarobajar koThin ek bochor par korol. antorrjatik orrthonItite songkoTer karoNe bidayI 20o11 sale odhikangS Seyarobajare mUlysUcok beS poRe zay. tobe zuktoraShTrer Seyarobajarer mUlysUcok UrrdhwmukhI proboNotar modhy diye alOcy bochor SeSh kore. biSleShokera bolechen ze iurOper bivinn deSer orrthonOItik songkoTer karoNei mUlot 20o11 sale bOISwik Seyarobajare byapok hare netibacok provab 
poRe. bidayI bochore franser siesi 40 sUcok 17 doSomik 5 SotangSo, jarrmanir Dyaks sUcok 14 doSomik 7 SotangSo, zuktorajyer efoTiesoi 10o0 sUcok 5 doSomik 6 SotangS kome. jOnathon sudariya namer brOkarej kyapiTal spreDoser ekojon Dilar boleno, iurOp O eSiyar odhikangS Seyarobajarer mUlysUcoke dui oNgker poton dekhei biniyOgokarIra 20o11 saloke biday dilen. eSiyar brrihottom orrthonIti japaner Seyarobajare bidayI bochore 17 SotangS poton ghoTe. got Sukrobar japaner nikki sUcok kome aT hajar 425 poyenTe neme ase. 1982 saler por ar kokhonOi japaner Seyarobajare mUlysUcok etoTa nice neme bochor SeSh koreni. biSeSh kore bochorer prothom dike marrce deSoTite voyabohotom sunamir karoNe orrthonItir onyany 
khater motO Seyarobajare netibacok provab poRe. Oi sunamite japane pray 20 hajar manuSh mara zay. bidayI bochore cIner sanghai somonwit sUcok 22 SotangS komeche. varoter Seyarobajare alOcy bochore got ek doSoker modhye soboceye boR poton lokSh kora geche. bOmwe sTok eksoceNGjer senoseks mUlysUcok 24 SotangS kome pray 15 hajar 544 poyenTe neme ase. e bochore varoter mudra rupir binimoy har marrkin Dolarer biporIte 16 SotangS kome. saipraser Seyarobajare voyaboh poton ghoTe 20o11 sale. e bochore deSoTir Seyarobajare potoner har da^Ray 72 SotangS. eTai holO biSw-oSeyarobajare alOcy bochorer sorrwOcc poton. Seyarobajarer dwitIy sorrwOcc 52 SotangS poton dekha zay iurOper mondakobolit deS 
grise. bidayI 20o11 sale biSwer olp koyekoTi deSer Seyarobajare utthanoO oboSy lokSh kora zay. er modhye sorrwOcc 79 SotangS dam baRe venejuyelar Seyarobajare. utthaner din theke er poroi royeche moNggOliya O jamwiya. edike libiyasoh modhypracyer koyekoTi deSe ovyutthano-obiplob O rajonOItik palabodoler karoNe bochorer prothom dike antorrjatik bajare oporiSOdhit jwalani teler dam baRote Suru kore. alOcy bochore biSwbajare swrrNer dam beRe sorrwkaler sorrwOcc porryaye OThe. antorrjatik mudrabajare iurOper ekok mudra iurOO zen binimoy harer morryada O Tike thakar loRaiye bochorojuRe himoSim khay. iurOr binimoy har 15 maser sorrwnimn porryaye neme zaOyar modhy diye bochor SeSh kore. korrmoSalay ovimot paTer ovyntorIN O 
antorrjatik bajare nojor deOyar tagid paTopoNy bybohare bangladeSoke ovyntorIN bajare nojor deOyar paSapaSi biSwbajare byapok cahida thakar suzOg ba roptanir somvabona kaje lagate hobe. rajodhanIr brryak senTare gotokal Sonibar kyaTalisT ayOjit paT O bangladeSer orrthonItibiShoyok ek korrmoSalay boktara e tagid den. korrmoSalay boktara boleno, biSwbyapI din din paTopoNyer proti agroh baRoche. fole paT khate roptani ay baRar bipul somvabona royeche. kintu suzOgoTi kaje lagate paroche na bangladeS. e chaRa paTer ovyntorIN bajaroTiO beS boRo, kintu obohelit. ovyntorIN bajar soboceye valOvabe kaje lagiyeche varot. se onuzayI paTopoNy bybohare bangladeSokeO varoter motO ovyntorIN bajarer dike nojor dite hobe. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul 
muhit e korrmoSalay prodhan otithi chilen. ete biSeSh otithi chilen bostr O paTomontrI abodul lotif siddikI. korrmoSalay boktoby den bangladeS paTokol songsthar (obijeemosi) ceyaromyan Ti Di mitro, bangladeS juT spinarrs oyasOsiyeSoner (obijeesoe) sovapoti mOhammod Samos uj jOha ebong bangladeS paTokol somitir (obijeemoe) sovapoti nojorul hok. kyaTalisTer SahorOj jolil korrmoSalay swagot boktoby den. korrmoSalay senTar for polisi Dayalog (osipiDi) O bangladeS prokOUSol biSwbidyaloy (obuyeTo) duTi alada somIkSha protibedon uposthapon kore. protibedonogulO uposthapon koren zothakrome sipiDir jyeShTh gobeShoNa felO khondokar gOlam mOyajjem O buyeTer SikShok nUr al kuddus. korrmoSalay soNGcalok chilen sangbadik jahidujjaman faruk. somIkSha protibedone bola hoyeche, polipropailiner (opipi) soNgge protizOgita 
kore paToke Tike thakote hocche. tobe aSar kotha ze biSwbyapI pipir bybohar komoche. ar e suzOgoTi kaje lagiyeche varoto, cIn O pakistan. nijeder protizOgitaSIl kore tuleche tara. kintu bytikrom bangladeS. roptani onek baRanO dUre thako, ovyntorIN bajaroTiroi zothazoth bybohar korote paroche na ei deS. somIkShay bola hoyeche, 20o10 sale pas hoOya badhytamUlok paTer byag bybohar ainoTi bastobayon kora geleO bochore deSe 84 kOTi pis paTer byager dorokar hobe. ar ekekoTi byag tinobar bybohar koroleO cahida da^Ray 28 kOTi pis. othoc borrtomane bybohar hocche matr 90 hajar pis. orrthat'' purO somvabonai poRe royeche, kintu kaje laganO hocche na. paTonIti proNoyon O 
paT khater jony gotiSIl netrritw tOIri kora ebong chOTokhaTO poriborrton ene ut''padonoSIlota baRanO, varoter samprotik Sulkomukt roptani ghOShoNar suzOg grohoNo, mojuri baRiye holeO karokhanay dokSh Sromikoder dhore rakha, narIder jony kaj korar suzOg tOIri kora, paT khater proti byangkogulOr netibacok drriShTivoNggir poriborrton ebong paT khate notun projonmer udyOkta SreNI goRe OThar proti gurutwarOp kora hoy protibedon duTite. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit boleno, âoamader jomi komo, kintu ut''padon baRate hobe.â protibedone paTer krriShi ongSoTi bad poReche bole somalOcona koren tini. orrthomontrI boleno, âo140 bochor age theke paToSilpe biSwnetrritwer vUmikay thekeO aj amora pichiye. somoyer soNgge tal miliye poNyer bohumukhinota O 
prozuktigot unnoyon korote na paray emonoTi hoyeche.â biSwbajare paTopoNyer Seyar totoTa na baRar kotha ullekh kore orrthomontrI ontot borrtoman obosthan dhore rakhar biShoye tagid den. ekoi soNgge krriShi O Silper soNgge joRit bole orrthonItite paT boR obodan rakhote pare bole tini biSwas koren. bostr O paTomontrI abodul lotif siddikI janano, badhytamUlok paTer byag bybohar ainoTi pas kora holeO ta proyOg korote parochen na tini. montrI boleno, âoain proyOg korote giye dekhi ami ni:soNggo, keu sohozOgita koroche na.â tobe khady O krriShi montroNaloy sohozOgita koreche bole swIkar koren tini. Silp montroNaloyer vUmikar byapare bolote giyeO theme zan tini. bijeemosir ceyaromyan Ti 
Di mitr boleno, bangladeS rosayon Silp songstharoi (obisiaisi) bochore choy kOTi byag dorokar. kintu ta bybohar koroche na tara. badhytamUlok paTer byag byboharer ain karrykorer biShoye gurutwarOp koren tini. bijeesoer sovapoti Samos uj jOha boleno, paToke krriShivittik Silp ghOShoNa kora holeO bastobe krriShivittik hisebe morryada deOya hoy na. Seyar kinoben tin poricalok pu^jibajare talikavukt tinoTi kOmpanir tinojon udyOkta-oporicalok Seyar kenar ghOShoNa diyechen. aj sOmobar Diesoir OyebosaiTe e khobor prokaS kora hoyeche. kOmpani tinoTi holOâosauthoisT byangko, finiks inosyurens O sTanDarrD byangk limiTeD. sauthoisT byangker udyOkta-oporicalok jOsona ara kaSem tin lakh 33 hajar Seyar kenar ghOShoNa diyechen. finiks inosyurenser udyOkta-oporicalok ivana fahomida 
mOhammad ek lakh Seyar kinoben. borrtomane ta^r kache pa^c lakh 56 hajar 61Ti Seyar royeche. sTyanDarrD byangker udyOkta-oporicalok mOhammad iusuf cOUdhurI choy lakh 50 hajar 50o0oTi Seyar kenar ghOShoNa diyechen. borrtomane ta^r kache 66 lakh 28 hajar 30o0oTi Seyar royeche. bidyman bajaromUlye agamI 30 korrmodiboser modhye sTok eksoceNGjer madhyme e Seyar kinoben. prosoNggoto, got 22 novemwr esoisir pokSh theke kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokoder sommilitovabe komopokShe nij kOmpanir 30 SotangS ebong byktigotovabe dui SotangS Seyar kenar byapare badhybadhokota arOp kora hoy. jhuT kapoR roptani obyahot rakhar dabi bybosayIder pOSakoSilper poritykt jhuT kapoR roptani bondher podokSheper protibad koreche bangladeS garrmenTos oyanD TeksoTailos OyesTej eksopOrrTarrs 
oyasOsiyeSon (obijiTiDobliuie). oyasOsiyeSoner netara jhuT kapoR roptani obyahot rakhar dabi janiyechen. e dabite bijiTiDobliuie Dhakar jatIy presoklaber samone got Sonibar manobobondhon kore. ete oyasOsiyeSoner sovapoti es em samosuuddino, jyeShTh sodosy subrot ghOSho, sodosy motiur rohomano, faruk hOsenosoh onyra uposthit chilen. manobobondhone likhit boktoby paTh koren oyasOsiyeSoner sodosysocib aminul isolam. ete bola hoyo, deSer pOSak karokhana theke protidin ze porimaN jhuT kapoR ber hoyo, tar matr 10 SotangS sthanIyovabe bybohar kora hoy. obybohUt baki 90 SotangS e oyasOsiyeSoner sodosyra varoto, cIn O amerikasoh iurOper bivinn deSe roptani korochen. somitir netara janano, bochore ek hajar theke ek hajar 20o0 meTrik Ton jhuT 
kapoR roptani kore 10 kOTi marrkin Dolar ay hoy. khatoTir soNgge beS koyek lakh lOker korrmosongsthan joRit. boktobye ovizOg kora hoyo, somproti bangladeS Tyarif komiSon muShTimey du-oekoTi gOShThIr dwara provabit hoye jhuT kapoR roptani bondher supariS koreche. eTi sorokarer roptani somprosaroN nItir poriponthI ullekh kore bola hoyo, ete deSer orrthonItite netibacok provab poRobe. byangkogulOr ucc poricalon munafa bidayI 20o11 sale deSer besorokari O raShTrIy malikanadhIn baNijyik byangkogulO valO poricalon munafa koreche. tobe 30oTi besorokari byangker modhye 10oTi byangker poricalon munafa ager bochorer tulonay komeche, beReche 20oTir. raShTrIy khater caroTi baNijyik byangkeroO ucc poricalon munafar hisab mileche. bochorojuRe byangkogulOte taroly-osongkoTer kotha 
bola hocchil. pu^jibajareO chil monda. kendrIy byangk nanavabe mudra soroboraher raS Tanote ceyeche. tobe Dolarer mUlybrriddhi, antorrjatik bajare poNymUly brriddhi ebong deSe amodani-oroptani brriddhir karoNe byangkogulOr mUl byangking valO hoyeche bole mone kora hocche. odhikangS byangker pu^jibajarovittik brOkarej bybosa O marrcenT byangk ache. paSapaSi byangkogulO nijosw tohobil Seyarobajare khaTiyeche. er ageO tader tohobil khaTanO chil. tobe e khat theke ebar valO ay aseni. biSwmonda poristhitike bibeconay niye koyek bochor dhore deSer byangkogulOke krriShirriN bitoroNe byapokovabe provabit kora hoyeche. krriShi ebong kShudr O majhari Silp khate rriN bitoroNe suder haroO nirrdharoN kora royeche. abar roptani khateO suder har nirrdharit ache. egulO 
ucc munafar kShetre ontoray. probasI-oay (oremiTyanso) deSe asar gotite kichuTa vaTa chil. fole e khate ayoO komeche byangkogulOr. byangkarora oboSy bolocheno, nana khate bybosa baRate tot''porotay chilen ta^ra. tobe bochorer trritIy prantike ese onek byangker ze hisab paOya giyechilo, bochor SeSher ogrogoti zen tar soNgge mele na. songSliShT karoO karoO mote, ei ze boR oNgker poricalon munafa, tar modhyeO boR dhoroner hisaber fa^k ba âouinDO Dresingâ thakote pare. tobe, ei poricalonogot munafa byangker prokrrit munafa noy. niT munafai byangker prokrrit ay. poricalonogot munafa theke rriNer biporIte soNGciti (oproviSono) ebong kor (o42 doSomik 5 SotangSo) bad diye niT munafa nirrdharit hoy. 
fole niT munafa onekoTa kome asobe. er Opor byangk biSeShe sadharoN rijarrv khate orrth boradd rakha hoy. fole Seyarobajare biniyOgokarIke opekSha korote hobe niT ba prokrrit munafar hisab paOya porrynt. abar onek kShetrei niT munafa holeO tar sompUrrN orrth lovyangS akare bitoroN kora hobe na. tai Seyare biniyOgokarIder lovyangS paOyar hisab koShote opekSha korote hobe byangker ejiemer ager poricalona porrShoder sovar siddhant porrynt. onydike byaselo-o2 bastobayoner jony 20o11 saler modhye byangkogulOke mUlodhon 40o0 kOTi Taka ba jhu^kinirrvor sompoder 10 SotangSoâoei duiyer modhye za beSi sei porimaN orrth songrokShoN korar kotha. zar modhye poriSOdhit mUlodhon hocche 20o0 kOTi Taka. abar byaselo-o3-oe 
zete bangladeS byangk byangker mUlodhon baRate nirrdeSona debe bole jana zacche. fole onek byangker munafa bitoroN kome asote pare. chOT poriSOdhit mUlodhoner byangkogulO hoyotO lovyangS bitoroN na kore bOnas Seyar dite pare. songbadopotrer tothy praptite nana badha royeche. fole emonoO hote pare, kOnO byangk sUtr ekoTi kachakachi oNgker munafar tothy diyeche. 10o0 vag soThik tothy na-oO hote pare. ta sottweO biSwbyapI poricalon munafa prokaS ekoTi swIkrrit biShoy. zodiO bangladeSe byangking khate ei poricalon munafa prokaSe nana bidhiniShedh royeche. ei bidhiniShedh eseche esoisir onurOdhe bangladeS byangk theke. tobe Seyarobajare za^ra protiniyot kenabeca koren ebong za^der kOnO byangker Seyare biniyOg royeche, ta^ra 
bykti zOgazOger madhymei e tothy pan. sUtre paOya tothye dekha zayo, boraborer motO besorokari khate 20o11 saleO poricalon munafar porimaNer dik theke sorrwadhik ay koreche isolamI byangk. isolamI byangker poricalon munafa hoyeche ek hajar 470 kOTi Taka. ager bochor chil ek hajar 143 kOTi Taka. tobe deSer byangk khat bibecona korole gotobarer motO raShTrIy khater jonota byangk sorrwadhik poricalon munafa koreche. ei byangkoTir poricalon munafa hoyeche ek hajar 50o0 kOTi Taka. ager bochor chil ek hajar 152 kOTi Taka. isolamI byangker amanot O biniyOg (orriNo) poddhoti vinn. fole tader hisaboO vinn. uporontu byangkoTir amanoter porimaN besorokari ony ekok kOnO byangker

Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) lenoden chaRiyeche 60o0 kOTi Taka. opor Seyarobajar coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) lenodenoO edin 50 kOTi Taka chaRiye geche. Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok gotokal dinoSeShe 94 poyenT beRe hoyeche pa^c hajar 352 poyenT. siesoir sarrwik mUlysUcok ager diner ceye pray 215 poyenT beRe da^Riyeche 14 hajar 42 poyenTe. janote caile Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI prothom alOke boleno, âobochorer sUconaTi beS aSabyNGjok hoyeche. aSa korochi, bochorojuRei amora bajarer swavabik acoroN dekhote pab. got bochor pray purOTa somoyoi biniyOgokarIder modhye corom osthirota dekha geche. e karoNe bajarer swavabik gotiTi amora dekhote paini.â rijovI aroO boleno, âogot Disemwrer majhamajhi somoy 
theke amora dekhochi, bajare osthirota onekoTa kome geche. aSa korochi, notun bochore ei osthirota ekebarei dUr hoye zabe.â mUlysUcoker Urrdhwgoti diyei gotokal Diesoite lenoden Suru hoy. prothom deR ghoNTar modhye sadharoN sUcok ager diner ceye 10o0 poyenT beRe zay. lenodener ekoporryaye ta ager diner ceye 128 poyenT pa^c hajar 386 poyenTe OThe. zodiO dinoSeShe sUcoker sei obosthan theke kichuTa nice neme ase. Suru thekei lenodener goti beS valO chil. dinoSeShe Diesoite 670 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye 110 kOTi Taka beSi. er age sorrwSeSh 20o10 saler 23 novemwr Dhakar bajare ek hajar 51 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyechil. 
bajarosongSliShT byktira bolocheno, byangk O arrthik protiShThaner hisab bochor SeSh hoyeche. ekhon tara notun bochorer hisabo-onikaS Suru koreche. e obosthay notun kore byangk O arrthik protiShThanogulOr biniyOgo-osokShomotaO tOIri hoyeche. paSapaSi beSir vag byangker poricalon munafa ager bochorer ceye beReche bole bivinn songbadopotre khobor prokaSit hoyeche. eTiO gotokaler bajarer Urrdhwgotir pechone boR vUmika rekheche. edike Dhakar bajare gotokal mOT 261Ti kOmpani O miucyuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye 196Tir dam beReche, komeche 60oTir ar oporiborrtit chil pa^coTir dam. coTTogramer bajare dinoSeShe 191Ti kOmpani O miucyuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye 153Tiroi dam beReche, komeche 31Tir ar oporiborrtit chil satoTir dam. rObobar 
siesoite pray 57 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye 13 kOTi Taka beSi. songkucit hocche khulonar biesosi karryaloy bangladeS Siping koropOreSoner (obiesosi) mongla bondorokendrik khulona karryaloyer karrykrom songkucit korar siddhant neOya hoyeche. tobe koropOreSoner korrmokorrtara ovizOg korecheno, karryaloyoTi bondh korotei korrtrripokSh nanamukhI tot''porota Suru koreche. itimodhye khulona karryaloye du-oekojon korrmocarI rekhe bakider coTTogram karryaloye bodolir siddhantoO niyeche. er ongS hisebe somproti choyojonoke coTTogram karryaloye bodoli kora hoyeche. ta^der 3 januyarir modhye sekhane zOg deOyar nirrdeSoO diyeche korrtrripokSh. esob udyOgoke biesosir khulona karryaloy bondh korar alamot bole mone korochen sekhanokar korrmokorrtara. tobe biesosir bybosthapona poricalok komODor mOkosumul kader prothom 
alOke boleno, âokhulona karryaloyoke ekebare guTiye fela hocche na. lOkosan komate kichuTa songkucit kora hocche.â tini aroO boleno, mongla bondore ze kaj tate et korrmIr proyOjon nei. tai kIvabe lOkosan komiye lav hobe se udyOg neOya hocche. 1963 sale tot''kalIn nyaSonal Siping koropOreSoner odhIne mongla bondorokendrik ei karryaloy khOla hoy. 1972 sal theke ta bangladeS Siping koropOreSoner odhIne poricalit hoye asoche. tokhon e karryaloye 80 jon korrmokorrta-okorrmocarI thakoleO ekhon korrmIr songkhya matr 13. khulona karryaloyer ekadhik sUtr janayo, khulona O mongla bondore besorokari jahaj kOmpanigulOr karryaloy royeche. sorokaroO biesosir jahaj bohor baRanOr siddhant niyeche. somproti Seyarobajare 350 kOTi Takar SeyaroO 
bikri koreche biesosi. othoc biesosi korrtrripokSh nijeder bybosa somprosarit na kore mongla bondorer karrykrom guTiye neOyar siddhant niyeche. khulona karryaloyer korrmokorrtader ovizOgo, biesosir car sodosyer poricalona porrShoder tinojonoi coTTogramer basinda. ta^ra mongla bondorer karrykrom bondh kore biesosike Sudhu coTTogram bondorer Opor nirrvoroSIl kore rakhote agrohI. somproti mongla bondor theke roptani poNy jahajIkoroN korote jahaj caile biesosi korrtrripokSh janayo, 10 diner modhye 10 hajar Ton poNy jahaje bOjhai kore bondor chaRanOr niScoyota dilei jahaj deOya hobe. korrmokorrtara janano, age koyekobar biesosir jahaj mongla bondore asar somoy rokSha korote na paray roptanikarokera astha hariye felechen. tai mongla bondore jahaj na asa porrynt 
roptanikarokera barrjo-okorrgOte poNy bOjhai koren na. abar khulona O monglay barrjer songkhya kom thakay prayoi korrgO bOjhai hote deri hoy. e chaRa durryOgopUrrN abohaOyar karoNeO onek somoy poNy bOjhaiye deri hoy. kintu e biShoyogulO amole na niye khulona karryaloyer Opor Sorrt arOp kore mongla bondore jahaj deyoni korrtrripokSh. janote caile khulona karryaloyer varoprapt mohabybosthapok sirajul isolam prothom alOke boleno, sorokar zokhon mongla bondoroke gotiSIl O adhunik bondor hisebe goRe tulote kaj koroche, tokhonoi biesosi mongla bondorer bybosa bondh korar udyOg niyeche. tini ovizOg koreno, coTTogram bondore maser por mas jahaj bose thakole kShoti hoy na. othoc mongla bondore somoyomotO jahaj 
na diyei ozOUktik Sorrt arOp kora hocche. tobe mOkosudul kader boleno, sUci onuzayI mongla bondore jahaj deOya holeO diner por din segulO bosiye rakhay biesosike lOkosan gunote hoyeche. evabe lOkosan deOya somvob noy. biesosir khulona karryaloy niye kOnO aNGcolikota hocche na boleO montoby koren tini. freS milker tin masobyapI bikroy karrykrom coloche meghona grup ob inDasTrijer gu^RO dudh brryanD freS ful krim milk pauDarer tin masobyapI bikroy karrykrom ekhon coloche. rajodhanIr ekoTi restOra^y somproti ek songbad sommelone âofreS milk khele vagy zabe khuleâ SIrrShok e bikroy karrykrom ghOShoNa kora hoy. ete meghona grup ob inDasTrijer poricalok tahomina binote mOstofa O 
tanojima mOstofa, nirrwahI poricalok (obipoNono) asif ikobalosoh Urrdhwton korrmokorrtara uposthit chilen. e karrykromer aOtay vOktader jony freS milk kenar biporIte bivinn puroskar jetar suzOg royeche. er modhye prothom puroskar hisebe royecheâoduTi ToyOTa gaRi. dwitIy puroskare choyoTi DayomonD haro, trritIy puroskare 18Ti elosiDi Tivi, coturrth puroskare 45Ti lyapoTopo, poNGcom puroskare 60oTi aipieso, ShoShTh puroskare 75Ti 21 iNGci roNgin Tivi ebong soptom puroskare bina mUlye 20o0oTi freS poNy royeche. 8 januzo09BCari jiesopi fainyanser saboskripoSon Suru pu^jibajare talikavukt hote zacche jiesopi fainyans kOmpani (obangladeSo) limiTeD. e lokShye 8 januzo09BCari protiShThanoTir prathomik goNoprostaber (oaipiO) saboskripoSon Suru hobe. colobe 12 januzo09BCari porrynt. ar onabasI bangladeSider 
jony saboskripoSon colobe 8 theke 21 januzo09BCari porrynt. protiShThanoTir prosopekTas onuzazo09BCI jiesopi fainyans bajare dui kOTi Sezo09BCar cheDo09BCe 50 kOTi Taka songgroh korobe. e kShetre 10 Taka ovihit mUlyer protiTi Sezo09BCarer dam 25 Taka nirrdharoN kora hozo09BCeche. 15 Taka primizo09BCam neOzo09BCa hobe. protiShThanoTir isyu bybosthapoker dazo09BCitwe rozo09BCeche aisibi kyapiTal myanejomenT limiTeD. sorrwSeSh hisab onuzazo09BCI protiShThanoTir Sezo09BCaroproti azo09BC (oipieso) 3.o51 Taka. onolaine inosyurens primiyam deOyar subidha bangladeSer onytom i-okomarrs sebaprodanokarI protiShThan esoesoel komarrs bima protiShThan finiks inosyurens kOmpanir soNgge tader polisi grohItader onolain primiyam prodaner cukti swakShor koreche. got 26 Disemwr 20o11 finiks inosyurenser dilokuSa karryaloye ek onuShThane ei cukti swakShorit 
hoy. ei cuktir fole Sigogiroi finiks inosyurenser polisi grohItara sthanIy O antorrjatik kreDiT O DebiT karrDer madhyme tader primiyamer orrth finikser OyebosaiT (owowowo.opohoooeonoioxoionosouoroaonocoeo.ocooomo.obodo) theke prodan korote parobe. cuktite finiks inosyurens kOmpanir mohaporicalok jomirul isolam O esoesoel komarrser mohabybosthapok anisul isolam nij nij protiShThaner pokShe swakShor koren. onuShThane onyanyer modhye uposthit chilen esoesoel komarrser bybosa unnoyon bybosthapok jubayer hOsen siniyor marrkeTing oyasOsiyeT mamunur roSId khan ebong finiks inosyurenser ceyaromyan mOhammod SOyeb O otirikt mohaporicalok imam SahIn. mUly songSOdhone dui bajare komeche lenoden deSer Seyarobajare gotokal sOmobar kichuTa mUly songSOdhon hoyeche. ete bochorer dwitIy karrydibose dui bajarei mUlysUcok O lenodener porimaN komeche. 
prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok ager diner ceye pray 18 poyenT kome da^Riyeche pa^c hajar 333 poyenTe. coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok 87 poyenT kome hoyeche pray 13 hajar 955 poyenT. rObobar bochorer prothom karrydibose dui bajare mUlysUcok O lenoden beRechil. zOgazOg kora hole bangladeS marrcenT byangkarrs oyasOsiyeSoner (obiemobie) sovapoti mOhammod e hafij prothom alOke boleno, gotokaler bajare kichuTa mUly songSOdhon hoyeche. munafa tule neOyar proboNota beSi thakay emonoTi ghoTeche. eTi bajarer swavabik acoroN. hafij aroO boleno, biniyOgokarIder atmobiSwase ekhonO kichuTa ghaToti royeche. e karoNe bajare kichuTa mUly songSOdhon holei bikrir capoTa beRe zacche. tobe koyek 
din dhore lenodene beS goti eseche. eTi bajarer jony itibacok. edike, poricalon munafar bibeconay Seyarobajare talikavukt byangkogulOr beSir vagoi ucc munafa koreche. tar poroO bajare byangk khater Seyarer mUly songSOdhon hoyeche. ucc poricalon munafar poroO Seyarer dorobrriddhite byangk khat pichiye thakoleO swlp ba chOT mUlodhoner talikavukt kOmpanigulO mUlybrriddhite egiye chil. Dhakar bajare gotokal sOmobar mUlybrriddhir SIrrSh 10oTi kOmpanir talikay chil zothakrome ke oyanD kiu, sinObangla, kOhinUr kemikyaloso, nyaSonal haujing, Dhaka insyurenso, rongpur Deiri, farrsT biesoaroeso, oyapeks Tyanari, aisibi O iunaiTeD insyurens. er modhye aisibi O nyaSonal haujing chaRa baki aToTi kOmpaniroi poriSOdhit mUlodhon 50 kOTi Takar nice. Dhakar bajare gotokal 
pray 594 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye pray 76 kOTi Taka kom. edin Diesoite 264Ti kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye dam beReche 144Tiro, komeche 110oTir ar oporiborrtit chil 10oTir dam. siesoite gotokal diner SeShe pray 50 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye pray sat kOTi Taka kom. coTTogramer bajare edin 197Ti kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye dam beReche 86Tiro, komeche 97Tir ar oporiborrtit chil 14Tir dam. 45 hajar Ton soyabin tel eseche bondore 45 hajar meTrik Ton oporiSOdhit soyabin tel niye got rObobar coTTogram bondore ekoTi Tyangkar viReche. brajil 
O arrjenTina theke ei tel amodani koreche coTTogramer es alom grup. jana geche, âoemoTi velebiToâ namer Tyangkare amodani kora soyabin teler dam saRe 40o0 kOTi Taka. rObobarer bajarodor onuzayI, poriSOdhon korar por ei teler bajarodor hobe pray 60o0 kOTi Taka. amodanir hisab onuzayI, ek Tyangkar soyabin tel diye sara deSe pray ek maser cahida pUroN kora somvob. es alom gruper vais ceyaromyan abodus samad prothom alOke janano, agamI 10o-o15 diner modhye ei tel poriSOdhon kore bajarojat kora Suru hobe. fole deSe teler songkoT ar thakobe na. bivinn jahaj kOmpanir korrmokorrtara janano, bondore socoracor ekoTi jahaje ekosoNgge et tel amodani kora 
hoy na. sadharoNot aT theke 20 hajar TonobahI vOjyteler jahaj bondore beSi ase. tobe got julaiye âoemoTi Torrm jaroTarrDoâ namer ekoTi jahaje kore 43 hajar 340 Ton oporiSOdhit soyabin tel esechil. vOjytel bybosayIra janano, novemwr theke februyari porrynt car mase SIter karoNe soyabin teler cahida beSi thake. baRoti cahida thakar karoNe protibochor e mOUsume er amodani baRiye den ta^ra. kasTom hauser hisab onuzayI, got bochorer okTObore soyabin tel amodani hoy saRe 33 hajar Tono, novemwre pray 70 hajar Tono, Disemwre er porimaN chil 51 hajar Ton. coloti maser Surutei 45 hajar Toner TyangkaroTi chaRaO aT hajar 70o0 Ton tel niye 
arekoTi Tyangkar du-otin diner modhye asar kotha royeche. 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore mOT 13 lakh 31 hajar Ton vOjytel amodani kora hoy. er modhye soyabin teler porimaN 30 SotangS kingba car lakh Tono, bakiTa pamotel. Disemwre probasI-oaye 18% probrriddhi bidayI bochorer Disemwr mase rekorrD porimaN probasI-oay (oremiTyanso) deSe eseche. got koyek mase probasI-oaye ze nimnogoti tOIri hoyechilo, Disemwr mase ta ucc ay hoye notun kore ut''saher jayoga tOIri koreche. e niye coloti orrthobochorer prothomarrdhe (ojulai-oDisemwro) mOT probasI-oay da^Riyeche 60o6 kOTi Dolarer beSi. orrthobochorer poNGcom maso, orrthat'' novemwr mase probasI-oay beS khanikoTa kome zayo; ta zemon chil ager maser tulonayo, temoni got bochorer 
ekoi maser ceye kom. kintu Disemwr mase sob rekorrD veNge probasI bangladeSira deSe paThiyechen 114 kOTi 43 lakh 80 hajar Dolarer somoporimaN bOIdeSik mudra. er age ek mase et beSi probasI-oay deSe aseni. ager bochore, orrthat'' 20o10 saler Disemwr mase probasIra deSe paThiyechilen 96 kOTi 90 lakh 90 hajar Dolarer somoporimaN bOIdeSik mudra. se hisabe coloti Disemwre probasI-oayer probrriddhi hoyeche 18 SotangS. deSe Dolarer biporIte ager zekOnO somoyer ceye ekhon beSi Taka paOya zacche. ekhon probasI-oayer proti Dolarer biporIte 81 doSomik 90 theke 82 doSomik 40 Taka porrynt paOya zay. mUlot e karoNei probasIra ager zekOnO somoyer ceye beSi orrth 
byangking cyanele deSe orrth paThate ut''sahit hocchen bole byangkogulOr sUtr janiyeche. paSapaSi bOIdeSik lenodene varosamy rokSha korote ebong bideSi mudrar rijarrv dhore rakhote bangladeS byangk nana tot''porota calacche. bideSi mudra ber hoye zaOyar protiTi kShetre kendrIy byangk nojorodari koroche. ekoi soNgge probasI-oay kIvabe baRanO zayo, tar jony byangkogulOr soNggeO kendrIy byangk alOcona kore coleche. er age novemwr mase probasIra deSe paThiyechen 90 kOTi 87 lakh 90 hajar marrkin Dolarer somoporimaN bOIdeSik mudra. ager bochorer novemwr mase probasIra paThiyechilen 99 kOTi 86 lakh 40 hajar Dolar. orrthobochorer prothom car mase, orrthat'' julai theke okTObor mase, ager bochorer tulonay probasI-oaye probrriddhi hoyo; 
kintu novemwr mase ar probrriddhi dhore rakha zayoni, zodiO samogrikovabe pa^c mase probrriddhi chilo, tobe ta matr 7 SotangS. okTObor mase probasIra deSe paThiyechilen 10o3 kOTi 94 lakh 80 hajar marrkin Dolarer somoporimaN bOIdeSik mudra, sepTemwr mase 85 kOTi 54 lakh 40 hajar Dolaro, agosT mase 110 kOTi 17 lakh 90 hajar Dolar ebong julai mase paThiyechilen 10o1 kOTi 55 lakh 80 hajar Dolar. ager bochorer okTObor mase probasIra deSe paThiyechilen 92 kOTi 38 lakh 50 hajar marrkin Dolarer somoporimaN bOIdeSik mudra, sepTemwr mase 83 kOTi 77 lakh 10 hajar Dolaro, agosT mase 96 kOTi 39 lakh 20 hajar Dolar 
ebong julai mase paThiyechilen 85 kOTi 73 lakh 10 hajar Dolar. er age 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore probasI bangladeSira deSe paThan pray ek hajar 165 kOTi Dolarer somoporimaN bOIdeSik mudra. e bochor probasI aye probrriddhi hoy matr 6 doSomik 0o3 SotangS. taroO age, orrthat'' 20o0o9-o10 orrthobochore probasIra deSe paThiyechilen pray ek hajar 99 kOTi Dolarer somoporimaN bOIdeSik mudra. se bochor probasI aye ager bochorer ceye probrriddhi hoyechil 13 doSomik 25 SotangS. Diesoite lenoden 70o0 kOTi Taka chaRiyeche deSer pu^jibajare aj moNggolobar UrrdhwmukhI proboNotar modhy diye lenoden SeSh hoyeche. din SeShe dui bajarei sUcok O lenoden beReche. ar prodhan bajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGje 
(oDiesoi) aj lenoden 70o0 kOTi Taka chaRiyeche, za pray deR maser modhye sorrwOcc. er age got 23 novemwr Diesoite ek hajar 51 kOTi Takar lenoden hoy. bajaro-osongSliShT byktira bolocheno, sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSoner (oesoisi) somproti grohoN kora beS kichu siddhant eroi modhye bastobayon hote Suru hoyeche. er modhye kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokoder Seyar songrokShoNo-osongkrant nirrdeSona onuzayI oneke Seyar kena Suru korechen. er provab bajare poRote Suru koreche bole mone korochen ta^ra. tobe biniyOgokarIder dhOIrry O sotorrkotar soNgge biniyOg koraroO poramorrS diyechen songSliShT byktira. Diesoite aj 261Ti protiShThaner Seyar O miucuyal fanD lenoden hoyeche. er modhye 20o0oTiroi dam beReche. komeche 44Tir ar oporiborrtit royeche 17Ti protiShThaner Seyarer dam. sTok eksoceNGjoTite aj 710 kOTi Taka lenoden hoyeche, za gotokaler ceye 116 kOTi Taka beSi. din SeShe Diesoite lenodene SIrrShe thaka 10oTi protiShThan holO fu-oOyang siramikoso, iunaiTeD eyaro, gramINofOno, aroen spining, beksimokO, keya kosomeTikoso, afotab oTO, pipolos lijing oyanD finyansiyal sarrviseso, marrkenTail byangk O fu Oyang fuD. onydike coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok 174.o54 poyenT beRe 15249.o80 poyenTe da^Riyeche. siesoite lenoden 
hoOya 195Ti protiShThaner modhye 150oTiroi dam beReche. komeche 33Tir ar oporiborrtit royeche 12Ti protiShThaner Seyarer dam. siesoite aj 62 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyeche, za gotokaler ceye 12 kOTi Taka beSi. elojir laki kupon Dr elojir âoId Dabol anond ofaroâ SIrrShok bikroy karrykromer laki kupon Dr hoyeche. ete khulonar dOUlotopurer begom munnujan Dhaka-okuyalalamopuro-oDhaka, pabonar gOpalopurer abu sayId Dhaka-okolomwO-oDhaka ebong kiSOrogoNGjer motolobopurer nojorul isolam Dhaka-okaThomanDu-oDhaka pother duTi kore biman TikiT lav koren. baTaroflai marrkeTing limiTeDer Dhakar motijhiler prodhan karryaloye gotokal sOmobar ayOjit ek onuShThane prothom alOr sompadok motiur rohoman bijoyI kUponogulO uttOlon koren. onuShThane baTaroflai marrkeTingyer ceyaromyan O bybosthapona poricalok em e 
mannano, bikroy O bipoNon poricalok mustafijur rohoman sajido, poricalok mahobubur rohoman sojIbosoh onyany korrmokorrta, bijNGaponI songstha fronTolain komiunikeSonser bybosthapona poricalok ferodOUs alom mojumodaro, prothom alOr bipoNon mohabybosthapok roSidur rohoman sobur O goNymany byktira uposthit chilen. ei bikroy karrykromer aOtay tinoTi ruT ba pothe choyoTi biman TikiT chaRaO kretader jony Sotovag bina mUlye eloji poNy O nogod mUlychaRer subidha laver suzOg chil. biSwmondar modhyeO orrthonIti valO royeche: atiur farrsT sikiuriTi byangker onuShThane oyamwulenser cabi tule den kendrIy byangker govorrnor atiur rohoman biSwmondar modhyeO deSer orrthonIti valO obosthay royeche bole mone koren bangladeS byangker govorrnor atiur rohoman. tini bolecheno, âocIno, varotosoh biSwer 
unnot deSogulOr orrthonItite monda zacche. sei tulonay bangladeSer orrthonIti onek valO obosthay royeche.â govorrnor farrsT sikiuriTi isolamI byangker samajik dayoboddhota (osiesoaro) karrykromer ek onuShThane gotokal esob kotha bolen. tini byangker pokSh theke poNGcogoR O dinajopurer fulobaRI upojelar SItarrtoder modhye tin hajar pis komwl bitoroN O zoSOrer rOTari helth senTaroke ekoTi oyamwulenser cabi hostantor koren. onuShThane byangker emoDi e e em jakariya, bangladeS byangker nirrwahI poricalok es ke sUr cOUdhurI, byangker DiemoDi abodul kuddus O sOIyod Oyasek mO. alI boktoby den. govorrnor boleno, bidayI bochore byangk khat siesoar karrykrome 355 kOTi Taka byy koreche. ar ei 20o12 sale e khate byy

Seyarobajare lenoden niShpottir somoy komoche deSer Seyarobajare lenoden niShpottir somoy ek din komote zacche. eroi modhye bajar niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi) dui sTok eksoceNGjer e-osongkrant bidhaner songSOdhonI onumOdon koreche. er fole lenoden niShpottir somoy komiye anar esoisir siddhant karrykorer kShetre ar kOnO joTilota roil na. eTi karrykor hole car karrydiboser poriborrte Seyarobajare sorrwnimn tin karrydibose lenoden niShponn hobe. esoisi sUtre jana zayo, somproti esoisir niyomit sovay lenoden niShpotti-osongkrant bidhaner songSOdhonI onumOdon kora hoy. zodiO gotokal porrynt e-osongkrant ciThi sTok eksoceNGjer songSliShT byktider hate pOU^chayoni. niyom onuzayI, songSOdhonI bidhan 
onumOdoner ciThi hate paOyar por dui sTok eksoceNGj lenoden komiye anar siddhant karrykore proyOjonIy bybostha grohoN korobe. er age got 18 okTObor dui sTok eksoceNGjer supariSer poriprekShite esoisi Seyarobajarer lenoden niShpottir somoy ek din komiye anar siddhant ney. tobe jeD kyaTagorivukt durrwl mOUlovittir Seyarer belay ei siddhant karrykor hobe na boleO songsthaTi janay. kintu sei siddhant karrykorer age dui sTok eksoceNGjer e-osongkrant aini bidhan (oseTelomenT reguleSono) songSOdhoner proyOjon dekha dey. aine car karrydibose lenoden niShpottir biShoyoTi ullekh royeche. tai sTok eksoceNGjer pokSh theke Oi bidhan songSOdhon kore ta onumOdoner jony esoisite paThanO hoy. kintu bajarer sarrwik poristhiti bibeconay esoisi songSOdhonITi 
onumOdone kichuTa kOUSolI obosthan ney. dui sTok eksoceNGjer netara mone koreno, lenoden niShpottir somoy komole ta bajare itibacok provab felobe. ager ceye kom somoye biniyOgokarIra Seyarer malikana O orrth bujhe paben. lenodener sokShomotaO baRobe. borrtomane pu^jibajare âoeâo, âobiâo, âojiâo, âoenoâ ebong âojeDoâ miliye mOT pa^c kyaTagorir kOmpani royeche. eder modhye Sudhu jeD kyaTagorir Seyarer lenoden niShpotti hote sorrwnimn 10 karrydibos (oTi+o9) lage. onygulOr Seyarer lenoden sorrwnimn car karrydibose (oTi+o3) niShponn hoy. erisTOfarrmar barrShik bikroy sommelon rajodhanIte somproti erisTOfarrmar barrShik bikroy sommelon onuShThit hoy rajodhanIr ekoTi konovenoSon senTare somproti erisTOfarrma limiTeDer barrShik bikroy sommelono-o20o11 onuShThit hoyeche. sommelone jananO hoyo, 1986 sale

theke esob poNyer Sulk har nirrdharoN orrthat'' SulkayonoO kora hoy. Sulk har nirrdharoN kora hoy 67 lakh 86 hajar 897 Taka. niyomanuzayI, ei Taka kasTom hause obosthit sOnalI byangker kasTomoser hisabe joma diye byangk theke ekoTi nomwr neOya hoy. sei nomwr dekhiye kasTom hauser âoTrejari spiDoâ Sakha theke poNy khalaser onumoti ba chaRopotr deOya hoy. kasTom hauser sUtr janayo, amodanikaroker protinidhi e oyanD es ejensi Sulk kor joma deOyar jal chaRopotr tOIri kore. got brrihospotibar ei chaRopotr neOya hoyeche bole jal kagoje dekhanO hoy. ei jal chaRopotr dekhiye Siping ejenT O bondor theke proyOjonIy kagojopotr songgroh kore protiShThanoTi. ekoi din 
oti drutotay sob anuShThanikota SeSh kore sondhyar somoy bondorer sisiTi-o1 geT diye konoTeinar ber kore neOya hoy. kasTom haus sUtr janayo, gotokal sokale ei jaliyatir ghoTonar khobor pan otirikt komiSonar mO. motiur rohoman. khobor peye tini zugm komiSonar sOIyod muSofikur rohomanoke dayitw den. er poroi asol ghoTona beriye ase. e prosoNgge kasTom hauser otirikt komiSonar mO. motiur rohoman prothom alOke boleno, âokasTom hause zate kOnO oniyom hote na pare se jony purOpuri swyongkriy poddhoti calu korar podokShep neOya hocche. karoN swyongkriy poddhoti purOpuri calu kora gele e dhoroner jaliyatir ghoTona ghoTot na.â kasTom haus sUtr janayo, niyomanuzayI geT diye malamal 
neOyar somoy onolaine chaRopotr nomwr diye Sulk kor poriSOdh kora hoyeche ki naâota zacai kora hoy. kintu sisiTi-o1 geTe onolain poddhoti ocol thakay biShoyoTi Sonakt korote parenoni kasTom hauser songSliShT dayitwSIl korrmokorrta. jal kagojopotre dekha zayo, chaRopotrer nomwr deOya hoyeche 9178. byangke Taka poriSOdher nomwr deOya hoyeche 150o3. ei duTi nomwroi vuya bole kasTomos korrmokorrtara Sonakt koren. ei nomwre kOnO Taka joma hoyoni. e biShoye janote sioyanDoef ejenT mesarrs e oyanD es ejensijer karryaloye fOn kora hole mO. ripon namer ek bykti prothom alOke boleno, âoprotiShThaner malik amake bosiye rekhe baire cole gechen.â biShoyoTi niye tini kotha bolote raji hononi. 
eropor dofay dofay zOgazOg kora holeO kauke paOya zayoni. kasTom hauser nothite dekha zayo, mesarrs e oyanD ejensi kasTom haus theke 1996 sale poNy khalaser laisens pay. kasTom hauser ekojon korrmokorrta janano, ei protiShThaner got choy maser poNy khalaser tothy songgroh kora hocche. e chaRa ei protiShThan khalas korobe emon kOnO poNy bondore ache ki na, taO zacai kora hocche. enobiarer projNGapon Seyare obOIdh orrth biniyOg kora zabe na bOIdh upaye oprodorrSit ay Seyaro-obajare biniyOg korole kOnO proSn korobe na jatIy rajosw bOrrD (oenobiaro). gotokal rObobar e-osongkrant ekoTi projNGapon jari kore songsthaTi boleche, enobiar ainer baire ony kOnO aine borrNit 
oporadh songghoToner madhyme orrjit ayer kShetre projNGaponer e subidha prozOjy hobe na. enobiar kalOTaka ullekh na kore boleche, bOIdh upaye orrjit kor onarOpit ay. projNGapon onuzayI, coloti orrthobochor 10 SotangS hare kor diye Seyarobajare kalOTaka biniyOg kora zabe. e jony coloti bochorer 15 julaiyer modhye songSliShT upokor komiSonarer kache nirrdharit choke biniyOgosongkrant ghOShoNa dite hobe. ghOShoNapotrer soNgge kor poriSOdhosongkrant pe-oorrDaro, biniyOg kOSh ba pOrrTofOliO biboroNI ebong biO (obenifiSiyari Onarrso) hisaber lejar kopiO joma dite hobe. ei ghOShoNar madhyme biniyOg kora Taka 20o13 saler 30 juner modhye uttOlon ba sthanantor kora zabe na. e chaRa 20o11 saler 30 juner modhye karoO 
kor fa^ki udghaTit hoOyar por ayokor odhyadeS onuzayI karrykrom poricalit hole tini ei subidha paben na. enobiar sUtre jana geche, coloti orrthobochorer bajeT ghOShoNar somoy bina proSne 10 SotangS hare kor diye oprodorrSit ay Seyarobajare biniyOger suzOg dey enobiar. kintu ei suzOg niye za^ra Seyarobajare biniyOg korobeno, ta^der ayer ut''s somporrke sorokarer ony songsthagulO biSeSh kore durrnIti domon komiSon (odudoko) proSn korobe ki na, ta niye bivranti tOIri hoy. bivranti dUr korotei e projNGapon jari korol enobiar. edike, got novemwr mase mudra pacarobirOdhI antorrjatik songstha eSiya pyasifik grup on mani lonDaringyer ek protinidhidol bangladeS sofor kore. soforokale protinidhidol sorokarer kache 
proSn tOle, pacar kora orrth kingba sontrasI karrykrome bybohUt orrth Seyarobajare biniyOg hole ta kIvabe cihnit kora hobe. ei soforer poroi enobiar nijer obosthan byakhya kore. doropotone binizo09BCOgokarIder bikShOv deSer pu^jibajare aj sOmobar doropotoner modhy dizo09BCe lenoden coloche. ete pu^ji harizo09BCe bikShubdh binizo09BCOgokarIra rajodhanIr motijhile Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) samone bikShOv Suru korechen. ekoporryazo09BCe Diesoir samoner soDo09BCoker ekopaSe zan colacol bondh hozo09BCe zazo09BC. eTi notun bochore binizo09BCOgokarIder prothom bikShOv. protykShodorrSIra janazo09BCo, aj bela sOzo09BCa 12Tar dike Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok 10o0 pozo09BCenT beSi poDo09BCe gele binizo09BCOgokarIra rastazo09BC neme asen. ta^ra Diesoir samone obosthan nizo09BCe bikShOv Suru koren. bela pOUne ekoTar dike 
ta^ra Diesoir samoner soDo09BCoke oborOdh kore bikShOv korote thaken. ete Oi soDo09BCoker ek paSe zan colacol bondh hozo09BCe zazo09BC. pore bela pOUne caroTar dike soDo09BCoke zan colacol swavabik hozo09BC. e somozo09BC binizo09BCOgokarIra orrthomontrI, bangladeS byangker govorrnoro, esoisir cezo09BCaromyan O Diesoir sovapotir biruddhe bivinn slOgan den. e chaDo09BCa doropotoner karoN hisebe ta^ra enobiarer ekoTi projNGaponoke dazo09BCI koreO boktoby den. oprodorrSit orrth pu^jibajare binizo09BCOger byapare gotokal rObobar enobiar Oi projNGapon jari kore. projNGapone bola hozo09BCo, âobOIdh upazo09BCe oprodorrSit azo09BC Sezo09BCarobajare binizo09BCOg korole kOnO proSn korobe na jatIzo09BC rajosw bOrrD (oenobiaro)oâ. projNGapone songsthaTi aroO janazo09BCo, enobiar ainer baire ony kOnO aine borrNit oporadh 
songghoToner madhyme orrjit azo09BCer kShetre projNGaponer e subidha prozOjy hobe na. marrcenT byangkoke mUl kaje thakar ahwan marrcenT byangkogulOr karrykrome ain voNgg kora O omonibas hisaber madhyme karosaji hoOyar ovizOg koreche pu^jibajar niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi). esoisir korrmokorrtara notun notun kOmpanike bajare ana, potrokOSh (opOrrTofOliO) bybosthapona O anDaro-oraiTingyer kaje jOr deOyar jony marrcenT byangkarogulOke tagid den. oboSy er jobabe marrcenT byangker omonibas hisab karosajir hatiyar noy bole dabi korechen marrcenT byangkarora. ta^ra bolecheno, Seyarobajare lenodener kShetre omonibas hisab biSwbyapI swIkrrit ekoTi pontha. eTi kOnO vuture hisab noy. swcchotar soNggei omonibas hisab poricalit hoy. ta^ra oboSy eO boleno, 
bicchinnovabe omonibas hisabe kichu oniyom ghoTe thakote pare. tobe seTi biO (obenifiSiyari Onarrso) hisaber belayoO ghoTote pare. gotokal Dhakar ekoTi hOTele bangladeS marrcenT byangkarrs oyasOsiyeSon (obiemobie) ayOjit âopuu^jibajare marrcenT byangkaroder vUmikaâ SIrrShok ek seminare proSnOttor porrwe marrcenT byangkarora e boktoby den. er age sokale ei onuShThane esoisir sodosy e salam sikodar ovizOg koreno, âomarrcenT byangker omonibas hisaber odhIne onek niyomobohirrvUt korrmokaND calanO hocche, za bajarer jony khuboi kShotikor.â salam sikodar aroO boleno, prantik rriN (omarrjin lOno) bitoroNer kShetre odhikangS marrcenT byangk ain voNgg koreche. rriNo-oozOgy SeyareO tara rriN diyeche. marrcenT byangkogulOr e dhoroner acoroN karoO kamy noy. onuShThane esoisir opor 
sodosy arif khan boleno, âomarrcenT byangkogulO tader mUl dayitw ba kaj theke sore eseche. byangkogulO ekhon Sudhu prantik rriN bybosthaponar kaj koroche.â arif khan janano, pu^jibajaroke hujug O gujob theke ber kore anote agamI tin maser modhye peSagot gobeShoNa O poramorrSoseba calu kora hobe. e jony bidhimala O gaiDolain proNoyoner kaj coloche. eTi cURant holei poramorrSosebar jony songSliShT byktider laisens deOya hobe. seminare prodhan otithir boktobye esoisir ceyaromyan em khayorul hOsen rriNonirrvor karrykromer baire poramorrSosebasoh nana dhoroner seba calur jony marrcenT byangkogulOr proti ahwan janiyechen. biemobier sovapoti mOhammod e hafijer sovapotitwe seminare aroO uposthit chilen esoisir sodosy amojad hOseno, senTral 
DipOjiTori bangladeS limiTeDer bybosthapona poricalok em e samado, Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer sovapoti Sakil rijovI, coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer sovapoti al maruf khan ebong bangladeS inosyurens oyasOsiyeSoner sovapoti Sekh kobir hOsen. seminare brryak ipiel inovesTomenT limiTeDer bybosthapona poricalok O prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta (osiiO) khaled farajI ebong aiDielosi inovesTomenTer prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta monirujjaman duTi probondh uposthapon koren. jwalani drut pOU^chate telobahI relogaRir adhunikayon hocche sOIyodopur reloOye karokhanay telobahI relogaRir goti baRate songzOjon kora hocche vyakuyam brek sOIyodopure obosthit deSer brrihottom reloOye karokhanay ekhon Tyangk Oyagon ba telobahI gaRir goti baRanOr karrykrom jOreSOre coloche. sOIyodopur reloOye karokhana sUtre jana zayo, ekhanokar Oyagon Sope eroi 
modhye 30oTi puraton Tyangk Oyagone (obiTiO) vyakuyam brek songzOjon kora hoyeche. e chaRa e Tyangk theke drut tel khalaser jony boTom Delivari sisTem calu korechen karokhanar karigorera. er fole ekhon theke ar mandhata amoler joTil upaye tel khalas korote hobe na. esob Tyangk Oyagoner sob koTii broDogej (oboRo) lainer. esob Oyagon khulonar fuyel DipO theke tel songgroh kore ta deSer bivinn tel DipOr uddeSye niye zabe. songSliShT reloOye prokOUSolIra janano, dIrrghodiner puraton esob Tyangk Oyagone adhunik breko-obybostha chil na. vyakuyam brek bybostha na thakay egulOr gotiO chil monthor. matr 40 kilOmiTar gotite colot esob Oyagon. ze karoNe gontobye jwalani pOU^che 
dite onek somoy lagot. e obosthay sec mOUsume drut krriShoker kache jwalani pOU^che dite reloOye korrtrripokSh Tyangk OyagonogulOte vyakuyam brek songzOjoner udyOg ney. ete kore Tyangk OyagonogulO ekhon dwiguN gotite orrthat'' 80 kilOmiTar gotite colacol korote parobe. karokhanar korrmokorrtara janano, protiTi Oyagon meramote matr pa^c lakh Taka byy hoyeche. sOIyodopur reloOye karokhanar bivagIy tottwabodhayok (oDieso) moNGjuro-oulo-oalom cOUdhurI prothom alOke janano, âoDijel O farrnes Oyel poribohone Tyangk Oyagon biSeSh vUmika rakhoche. amora er goti baRate Urrdhwton korrtrripokSher nirrdeSe OyagonogulO apogreD korar udyOg niyechi.â dui maser modhyei dOUlotogoNGj stholobondor abar calu hobe dui maser modhye cuyaDaNggar dOUlotogoNGj stholobondor notunovabe calu kora hobe. 
eTi hole poScimoboNgger nodIyar majhodiya hoye soRokopothe dui deSer modhye baNijyik zOgazOg baRobe. dOUlotogoNGjo-omajhodiya stholobondor punoray calur somvabyta zacai SeShe got Sonibar bangladeS stholobondor korrtrripokSher ceyaromyan e ke em iyahiya cOUdhurI sangbadikoder esob tothy janan. stholobondoroTir obokaThamO porrybekShoN O somvabyta zacaiyer jony stholobondor korrtrripokSher ceyaromyan Sonibar Oi elaka poridorrSon koren. ta^r soNgge chilen cuyaDaNggar jela proSasok vOla nath de, 35 borrDar garrD byaTaliyoner odhinayok le. korrnel sulotan ahomedo, stholobondor korrtrripokSher tottwabodhayok prokOUSolI khondokar abu monosur ahomedo, upojela nirrwahI korrmokorrta sajedur rohomano, cuyaDaNgga cemwarer sovapoti habibur rohomano, kuShTiyar kasTom korrmokorrta es em Samosujjamano, rajosw korrmokorrta provaSh kumar biSwas promukh. korrtrripokSher ceyaromyan 
pore jIbononogor sioyanDoef bybosayI ebong sthanIy protinidhider soNgge motobinimoy koren. sthanIy sioyanDoef bybosayI somitir sadharoN sompadok abodul hok boleno, ei stholobondor calu hole Dhaka theke kolokatar dUrotw 10o0 kilOmiTar kome zabe. bybosayIraO arrthikovabe lavoban hoben. ta chaRa benapOl stholobondorer OporoO cap komobe. tin din dhore zomuna sar karokhanay ut''padon bondh jamalopurer soriShabaRIte obosthit zomuna sar karokhana kOmpani limiTeDer (ojeefosielo) oyamOniya plyanTe konTrOl balw khule zaOyay tin din dhore sar ut''padon bondh royeche. jana geche, got Sukrobar vOrer dike jeefosieler oyamOniya plyanTe konTrOl balw khule zay. e somoy bikoT Sobd hoOyay karokhanar aSopaSer elakay atoNgk choRiye poRe. konTrOl balw khule zaOyar 
karoNe jeefosiele oyamOniya O iuriya uvoy plyanTe sar ut''padon bondh hoye zay. zomuna sar karokhana kOmpani limiTeDer (ojeefosielo) bybosthapona poricalok ocinty kumar deb e prosoNgge prothom alOke janano, oyamOniya plyanTe zantrik truTi dekha deOyay sar ut''padon bondh royeche. Sigogiroi e truTi sariye karokhanay abar sar ut''padone zaOya somvob hobe bole tini ullekh koren pu^jibajare byapok doropoton deSer pu^jibajare aj sOmobar byapok doropoton hoyeche. diner lenoden SeShe dui sTok eksoceNGje lenoden hoOya pray sob kOmpanir doropoton hoyeche. er fole sUcoker byapok poton hoyeche. ar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok aj 50o0o0 poyenTer nice neme eseche. bajaro-osongSliShT byktira bolocheno, mudrabajare suder 
harer ze sIma chilo, bangladeS byangker pokSh theke ta tule deOya ebong oprodorrSit orrth pu^jibajare biniyOger byapare jatIy rajosw bOrrDer (oenobiaro) gotokal jari kora projNGapon biniyOgokarIder modhye birUp provab feloche, za doropotoner onytom karoN. e byapare Diesoir poricalok ahomed roSid lalI boleno, emonitei pu^jibajare tarolysongkoT biraj koroche. e obosthay mudrabajare suder har beRe zaOyay pu^jibajar theke mudrabajare orrth cole zacche. er fole oneke mudrabajare biniyOge agrohI hoccheno, za pu^jibajare doropotoner onytom karoN. e chaRa enobiarer gotokal jari kora projNGaponoO biniyOgokarIder modhye birUp provab feleche. ei duTi biShoy mUlot doropoton twranwit koreche boleO mone koren tini. e obosthay enobiarer pokSh theke 
biShoyoTi byakhya deOya ucit bole montoby koren tini. Diesoir OyebosaiT sUtre jana zayo, aj Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok 3.o33 SotangS ba 167.o69 poyenT kome 50o0o0 poyenTer nice neme 4864.o30 poyenTe da^Riyeche. er age got 18 Disemwr sorrwSeSh sUcok 4996 poyenTe name. sUcoker nimnomukhI proboNotar modhy diye aj Diesoite lenoden Suru hoy. pa^c miniTer mathay sUcok 125 poyenT kome zay. sUcoker nimnomukhI ei proboNota sara din obyahot thake. aj Diesoite mOT 256Ti protiShThaner Seyar O miucuyal fanD lenoden hoyeche. er modhye 242Tiroi dam komeche. beReche matr 10oTir ar oporiborrtit royeche caroTi protiShThaner dam. aj sTok eksoceNGjoTite 318 kOTi Takar Seyarer lenoden hoyeche, 
za gotokaler ceye 71 kOTi Taka beSi. din SeShe Diesoite lenodene SIrrShe thaka 10oTi protiShThan holO gramINofOno, enobielo, iunaiTeD eyaro, aroen spining, beksimokO, sayoham TeksoTailo, sOsyal isolamI byangko, afotab oTO, keya kosomeTikos O fu-oOyang siramikos. onydike coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok 334.o60 poyenT kome 140o29.o18 poyenTe da^Riyeche. siesoite lenoden hoOya 184Ti protiShThaner modhye 167Tiroi dam komeche. beReche matr choyoTir ar oporiborrtit royeche duTi protiShThaner Seyarer dam. siesoite aj 42 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyeche, za gotokaler ceye 11 kOTi Taka beSi. lenodenozOgy Seyarer songjNGa nirrdharoN bad poRobe pa^c dhoroner Seyar Seyarobajare talikavukt kOmpanir lenodenozOgy Seyarer (ofri-oflOTo) songjNGa nirrdharoN koreche niyontrok 
songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi) goThit komiTi. gotokal rObobar komiTir ek bOIThoke e songjNGa nirrdharoN kora hoy. tobe ekhonO ta komiSoner kache joma deOya hoyoni. komiSon sUtr janiyeche, komiTir protibedon hate paOyar por porryalOcona kore esoisi fri-oflOTer songjNGa cURant korobe. er age esoisi janiyeche, Sudhu lenodenozOgy Seyarer vittite Seyarobajare notun sUcok calu kora hobe. kintu et din lenodenozOgy Seyarer sunirrdiShT kOnO songjNGa chil na. tai komiSon lenodenozOgy Seyarer songjNGa Thik korote esoisir sodosy arif khaner netrritwe ekoTi komiTi goThon kore. komiTike 15 diner modhye tader protibedon joma dite bola hoy. se nirrdeSona onuzayI, gotokal rObobar arif khaner netrritwe goThit 
komiTi fri-oflOT Seyarer songjNGa nirrdharoN kore. ajokaler modhye ta anuShThanikovabe komiSone joma deOya hobe. komiSonoi e byapare cURant siddhant grohoN korobe. songSliShT sUtr janayo, komiTi fri-oflOTer ze songjNGa nirrdharoN koreche, tate bola hoyeche, talikavukt kOmpanir udyOkta, plesomenTo, lokoin (obikri niShiddho) O sorokarer hate thaka Seyar Oi kOmpanir lenodenozOgy Seyar hisebe goNy hobe na. paSapaSi kOnO protiShThan ba byktir hate zodi kOnO kOmpanir 5 SotangSer beSi Seyar thake, tahole Oi ongSoTukuO fri-oflOT Seyar hisebe goNy hobe na. 5 SotangSer beSi SeyarodharoNoke komiTi kOUSologot dharoN hisebe bibeconay niyeche. sob miliye pa^c dhoroner (okyaTagori) Seyaroke lenodenozOgy hisebe dhora hoyoni. tobe zokhon esob Seyar 
sorasori bajare lenodene cole asobe (ozemono: lokoin sIma SeSh hole)o, tokhon abar ta lenodenozOgy bibecit hobe. ullikhit pa^c dhoroner Seyarer baire kOmpanir zesob Seyar thakobe, segulOi kebol lenodenozOgy Seyar hisebe bibecona kora hobe. dhora zako, talikavukt kOnO ekoTi kOmpanir mOT Seyarer porimaN dui lakh. er modhye udyOktader hate royeche 25 hajaro, plesomenTe boradd royeche 25 hajaro, sorokarer hate ache 25 hajar O lokoine royeche aroO 25 hajar Seyar. sob miliye e car dhoroner kOmpaniTir ek lakh Seyar boradd royeche. ar pratiShThanik O byktiSreNIr biniyOgokarIr hate kOUSologot karoNe kOmpaniTir 5 SotangS ba 10 hajar Seyar royeche. fri-oflOTer notun songjNGa onuzayI, talikavukt 
Oi kOmpanir 90 hajar Seyaroi kebol lenodenozOgy Seyar hisebe bibecit hobe. bima protinidhider biShoye aiDiaroer projNGapon age primiyamer orrth joma pore ceke komiSoner Taka deSer sadharoN bima kOmpanigulOte vuya protinidhider (oejenTo) name byapokovabe aino-okanuner loNgghon coloche. byangk bybosthapok O kOmpani korrtrripokSh zOUthovabei emon ghoTonar soNgge joRit. biShoyoTi nojore asay ta dUr korar udyOg niyeche bima unnoyon O niyontroN korrtrripokSh (oaiDiaroe). aiDiaroe gotokal rObobar deSer 43Ti sadharoN bima kOmpanir uddeSe ek projNGapon jari kore boleche, dIrrghodin thekei protinidhider name bima kOmpanigulOte osadhu corrca coloche. bimaSilper swarrthe ekhon theke ar bima protinidhider komiSoner Taka primiyamer soNgge somonwy kora zabe na. age primiyamer 
oNgk joma dite hobe, taropor protinidhider komiSoner Taka poriSOdh kora hobe. Sudhu tai noyo, komiSoner Taka ekhon theke byangk hisabe dey (ooyakaunTopeyi) ceker madhyme poriSOdh korote hobe. biShoyoTi karrykor hobe agamI 1 marrc theke. projNGapone bola hoyeche, kOnO obosthatei bima kOmpanir polisi othoba kovaronOTer Taka primiyamer soNgge somonwy kora zabe na. aro, ekoTi polisi khOla hole protinidhider ze komiSon deOya hoyo, ta ta^der dite hobe ceker madhyme. abaro, aiDiaroe theke nibondhon neOya protinidhi ba brOkar chaRa keu ei komiSon paben na. ete bola hoyo, ekhon theke bima kOmpanir prodhan karryaloyo, mukhy karryaloy O Sakha karryaloyoke tader sob byangk hisaber tothy

hisebe kaj korar jony laisens dey aiDiaroe. kintu kagoje-okolome nam thakoleO protinidhi hisebe bastobe eder beSir vageroi kOnO ostitw nei. tai protinidhider komiSon babod purO Takai hoy vagavagi hocche, noy primiyamer soNgge somonwy kora hocche. bima aino, 20o10 onumOdit holeO bidhimala tOIri na hoOyay ekhonO deSer bima khat poricalit hocche 1938 saler bima ain onuzayI. ei ainer 40o(o1) dhara onuzayI bima bybosar komiSon paOyar kotha bima protinidhider. zOgazOg korole aiDiaroer ceyaromyan em Sefak ahomed vU^iya bima protinidhir ostitwer kotha swIkar koren. prothom alOke tini boleno, dIrrghodin dhore obohelit thakar karoNe et din bima khate onek bidhibohirrvUt kajoi hoyeche. aiDiaroer pokSh

Diesoir ek songbad bijNGoptite ei tothy jananO hoyeche. sovay Seyarobajarer samprotik doropotono, sorokarer bivinn siddhanter biShoye alOcona hobe bole songSliShT sUtr janiyeche. aj DobliuaipiOr protinidhidol asoche swyongkriy hocche pyaTenT nibondhoner kaj biSwer bivinn deSe zokhon pyaTenT nibondhoner kajoTi hoy kompiuTaro-ovittik swyongkriy poddhotite, tokhon bangladeSe e kajoTi hocche sonatonI (omyanuyalo) poddhotite. ete pyaTenT nibondhoner kaje zemon bilomwit hocche, temoni udvabonI poNy ba dharoNa zacai-obachaiyer kShetre jhamelay poRote hocche pyaTenT nirIkShokoder. ta chaRa pyaTenT Dijain O TreDomarrk (onokoSa O marrka) odhidoptore royeche nirIkShoko-osongkoT. jonoboler ovabeO somoyomotO nibondhoner kaj kora zacche na. e obosthay pyaTenT nibondhoner kajoke
