Oi protibedon niye odhidoptorer biSeShojNG O DobliuaipiOr protinidhidol alOcona kore zOUth siddhante pOU^chaben. se alOkei odhidoptorer karrykrom swyongkriy korar kaj Suru hobe. odhidoptorer karrykrom swyongkriyokoroNer cuktir ongS hisebe aj moNggolobar DobliuaipiOr ekoTi protinidhidol odhidoptor poridorrSone asoche bole jana geche. odhidoptorer ekojon korrmokorrta janano, pyaTenT nibondhoner jony purOpuri swyongkriyokoroN proyOjon. karoN keu zokhon tar udvabit poNyer swtw nibondhon korote cano, tokhon nirIkShokoke biSwer bivinn deSe khO^jo-okhobor niye dekhote hoy ze, 
emon poNy ar keu tOIri koreche ki na. eTa khuboi koThin O somoyosapekSh kaj. sorokarer pyaTenT ain onuzayI, abedoner 18 maser modhye kOnO poNy ba udvaboner nibondhon grohoN kingba protyakhyan korote hoy. tobe ei somoyer modhye nibondhon SeSh na hole uvoy pokSher modhye alOcona sapekShe somoy aroO tin mas baRanO zay. odhidoptorer Oi korrmokorrta mone koreno, swyongkriyokoroN hoye gele pyaTenT nibondhon drut O ager ceye onek sohoj hobe. odhidoptorer nibondhok bi em kamal e prosoNgge boleno, âopyaTenT nibondhoner kaj swyongkriy korote na paray amora ekhonO pisiTi-ovukt (opyaTenT kO-oopareSon TriTi) hote parini. amora zodi swyongkriy hote pari, tahole biSwer zekOnO deSer 
udvabokerai amader ekhan theke tader poNy ba udvaboner pyaTenT korate paroben ebong ta antorrjatikovabe swIkrrit hobe.â ullekhy, pyaTenT holO notun udvabit kOnO poNy ba dharoNar swtwadhikarer ainogot swIkrriti. eke bola hoy somajer soNgge udvaboker cukti. nirIkShoko-osongkoTo: odhidoptor sUtr janayo, pyaTenT nibondhoner kaj suShThuvabe korar jony odhidoptorer ogranOgrame pyaTenT nirIkShoker 10oTi pod royeche. got bochor sorokari korrmokomiSoner (opiesosi) madhyme pa^cojonoke nirIkShok hisebe niyOg deOya hoyechil. ta^der modhye dujon cakori cheRe diyechen. arekojon bisies porIkSha diye eesopi nirrwacit hoyechen. tiniO Sigogiroi cakori cheRe deben. tahole nirIkShok thaken matr dujon. odhidoptorer sohokarI nibondhok em forohad hOsen khan prothom alOke boleno, pyaTenT holO khub 
ucc karigori biShoy. ar beSir vag abedonokarIi bideSi. tai odhidoptore biShoyovittik nirIkShoker proyOjon. afrikay biSwbyangker ceye boR rriNodata cIn cIner mudra iuyan rakha hocche byangke antorrjatik kShetre biSwbyangker ceye boR rriNodata hoye uTheche cIn. ar cIner esob rriNer beSir vagoi zacche afrikar unnoyonoSIl O gorib deSogulOy. 20o10 sale afrikar 36Ti deSe biSwbyangk ek hajar 140 kOTi Dolarer somoporimaN rriN deOyar biShoyoTi cURant kore. ekoi somoy ghanake ek hajar 30o0 kOTi Dolarer rriN dite raji hoy cIn. cIner byangkogulO esob rriN dicche. er modhye onytom holO eksopOrrTo-oimopOrrT (oeksimo) byangk. 20o10 sale biSwbyangk zekhane kyamerunoke rriN diyeche tin kOTi Dolaro, sekhane cIner 
eksim byangk diyeche 74 kOTi 30 lakh Dolar. ekoivabe biSwbyangk naijeriyake diyeche 89 kOTi Dolaro, sekhane cIn diyeche 90 kOTi Dolar. abar biSwbyangk jamwiyake diyeche saRe noy kOTi Dolar. cIn diyeche saRe 31 kOTi Dolar. e chaRa ripabolik ob koNggO biSwbyangk theke dui kOTi 55 lakh Dolar rriN peleO cIn theke peyeche 74 kOTi 30 lakh Dolar. afrikasoh bivinn deSe notun rasta, bidyut''kendro, hasopatal ebong onyany obokaThamO binirrmaN O unnoyone cIn esob rriN dicche. biSwbyangker ceye cIner kach theke rriN paOyar Sorrt onek sohoj hoOya biSwbyapI cIna rriN beRe zaOyar onytom karoN. zemono, got bochor komwODiya 60 kOTi Dolar rriN 
pete biSwbyangker soNgge denodorobar Suru korole biSwbyangk durrnItibirOdhI podokSheposoh bivinn dhoroner Sorrt arOp kore. ei porryaye cIn bina Sorrte 60 kOTi 10 lakh Dolar rriN dite egiye ele komwODiya biSwbyangkoke ekorokom taRiye dey. cIn eroi modhye biSwbyapI tin lakh kOTi Dolar biniyOger porikolpona koreche, zar boR ongS rriN akare orrthayoner madhyme. e kShetre deSoTi ekhon latin amerikar bivinn deSer dike drriShTi dite Suru koreche. rriNoman hraser provabe biSw Seyarobajar eSiyay potono, iurOpe miSr fraNgkofurrT sTok eksoceNGjer ekangSe lenodenorot karobarira fransosoh iurO oNGcole noyoTi deSer antorrjatik rriNoman kome zaOyar netibacok provab poReche eSiyar Seyarobajare. got Sukrobar rriNoman nirrNoyokarI onytom antorrjatik songstha 
sTyanDarrD oyanD puOros (oesooyanDopi) ei rriNoman komiye dey. tobe gotokal arekoTi rriNoman nirrNoyokarI songstha muDis franser rriNoman âoeeeâ oporiborrtit rakhar kotha janiyeche. gotokal sOmobar soptaher prothom karrydibose eSiyar Seyarobajare doropoton ghoTeche. tobe iurOper bajare chil miSr proboNota. gotokal din SeShe japaner TOkiO sTok eksoceNGjer nikki sUcok pray deR SotangS kome giyeche. ony prodhan SeyarobajarogulOr modhye dokShiN kOriyar siul pray pOUne 1 SotangSo, taiOyan 1 SotangSo, siNggapur sOya SotangSo, hongkong 1 SotangS O cIner sanghai pOUne 2 SotangS hare kome giyeche. biSleShokera bolocheno, koyek mas age marrkin zuktoraShTrer rriNoman obonomoner por got Sukrobar franser rriNoman ek dhap kome zaOyaTa khub bismoyokor 
kOnO byapar noy. kenona, gOTa iurO oNGcolojuRei arrthik songkoT coloche. ar rriNoman poRe zaOya kichuTa netibacok provab bOISwik Seyarobajare poRote badhy. tobe gotokal diner prothom vage iurOper beSir vag Seyarobajare chil UrrdhwmukhI proboNota. ullekhy, rriNoman kOnO deSer antorrjatik arrthik bajar theke rriN grohoNer O ta poriSOdher sokShomota nirrdeS kore. rriNoman kome gele esob deSer bonDer suder har beRe zete pare. orrthat'' antorrjatik bajar theke rriN grohoN kora esob deSer jony byyobohul hoye poRobe. âopyaksepOâ mela SeShe bybosayIra soroNGjam O mORok ut''padon Silpe notun matra zOg hobe âopyaksepOâ antorrjatik melay deSIy poNyer soNgge bideSi onek protiShThaner unnot prozukti prodorrSit hoyeche. deSi-obideSi 
kretara itibacok saRaO diyecheno, za deSer pOSak khater soroNGjam O mORok ut''padon Silpe notun matra zOg korobe. got rObobar car dinobyapI pyaksepO mela SeShe songSliShT khater bybosayI netara evabe nijeder ovimot bykt koren. ekoi soNgge deSer nItinirrdharokera melay uposthit hoye proyOjonIy sohayotar aSwas deOyay ta^ra sontOSh prokaS korechen. tOIri pOSak khater soroNGjamo, prozukti O mORokojatokoroNer poNysamogrI niye ei âopyaksepO-o20o12â 12 januyari Suru hoy. bangladeS garrmenTos eksesorij oyanD pyakejing myanufyakocararrs oyanD eksopOrrTarrs oyasOsiyeSon (obijiepiemoie) melaTir ayOjon kore. pyaksepOr paSapaSi aroO duTi mela hoy. 11tom âogarrmenTekoâ O trritIy âoiyarrn oyanD febrikos sOrrsing feyar SOâ mela duTir zOUth ayOjok chil jakariya TreD oyanD

jony proyOjonIy aSwas diyechen.â bijiepiemoie dwitIy sohosovapoti mIr mahomud alI boleno, gotobarer ceye ebarer melay valO saRa paOya geche. evabe protibochor melar ayOjon kora gele Silpayone byapok vUmika rakhobe bole mone koren tini. ayOjokera janano, ebarer melay epief pyakejing khate car kyaTagorite âoeSiya sTar oyaOyarrDoâ prodan koreche. ete 128 jon deSi-obideSi protizOgI ongS nen. puroskar paOya byktider modhye car bangladeSiO achen. tin melay bangladeSo, varoto, cIno, pakistano, taiOyano, jarrmanisoh bivinn deSer car Sotadhik protiShThan ongS ney. pyaksepOte polibyago, byakobOrrDo, ilasTiko, kolar inosarrTo, baTaroflai, kolar bOno, Tyapo, jiparo, sTikaro, baTono, hyaNggaro, ityadi poNy prodorrSon koroche deSi O bideSi protiShThan. garrmenTek melay 
zontrer madhyme suta O kapoR tOIri, tOIri pOSak khater soroNGjamo, mORokojatokoroN O prozuktir prodorrSon kore ongSogrohoNokarI protiShThanogulO. e chaRa iyarrn O febrikos melay suta, tOIri bostro, finiSo, Denimo, niTing ityadi samogrI prodorrSit hoy. biSeSh orrthonOItik oNGcol goRa hocche sileTe: baNijymontrI baNijymontrI ji em kader bolecheno, âosileTe speSal ikOnomik jOn (obiSeSh orrthonOItik oNGcol ba esoijeDo) protiShThar biShoyoTi ta^r montroNaloy soboceye beSi gurutw dicche. probasIder deSe biniyOger kShetr prosarit korotei ei oNGcol goRa hocche.â got rObobar rate sileT cemwar milonayotone bivager car jelar cemwar netader somonwye onuShThit bybosa-obaNijy unnoyono-osongkrant seminare prodhan otithir boktrritay ji em kader esob kotha bolen. sileT cemwarer sovapoti 
faruk ahomod michobaher sovapotitwe seminare sileT inTaronyaSonal iunivarrsiTir upacarry akomol mahomudo, jela ainojIbI somitir sovapoti emad ullah Sohidul isolamo, efobisisiaiyer poricalok hasin ahomod amontrit alOcok hisebe boktoby den. biSeSh otithi hisebe sileT mohanogor puliS komiSonar omuly vUShoN boRuya, aOyamI lIger kendrIy sanggoThonik sompadok misobahouddin siraj ebong otirikt jela proSasok (osarrwiko) mijanur rohoman boktoby den. baNijymontrI boleno, âoporryTon khateO sileTer byapok somvabona royeche. probasIder nirrmit SOIlpik baRigulO porryTokoder jony akorrShoNIy kore tOla zete pare.â seminare sileT chaRaO sunamogoNGjo, mOUlovIbajaro, hobigoNGjer cemwar netara uposthit chilen. baNijymontrI oboSy boleno, âoesoijeD sthaponer biShoyoTi baNijy montroNaloyer ekok siddhanter modhye nei bole bilomwit hocche. tobe ta 
oboSyi hobe.â joyopurohaT cinikole akh nei, maRai bondh akh caShira cahidamotO akh soroborah na koray nirrdiShT somoyer agei joyopurohaT cinikoler akh maRai bondh hoye geche. 12 januyari rat theke cinikoloTi bondh ache. ebaroO cinikoloTi lOkosaner mukhe poRoche bole aSoNgka kora hocche. got mOUsume cinikoloTite 12 kOTi Takar lOkosan hoyeche. caShider ovizOgo, coloti mOUsume cinikoloTir kache caShider paOna chil pa^c kOTi Taka. ar cinikol korrtrripokSh janayo, ut''padit cini bikri na hoOyar akh caShider paOna poriSOdh korote paroche na. joyopurohaT cinikoler bybosthapona poricalok SohId ullah prothom alOke janano, akher ovabe miloTir akh maRai bondh hoye geche. karoNo, caShira beSi dame guR bybosayIder 
kache akh bikri kore diyechen. guR bybosayIder kache nogod mUly paOyay cinikole akh soroborah korote ut''sahI non caShira. cinikol sUtr janayo, coloti mOUsume (o20o11-o12 orrthobochore) 80 hajar meTrik Ton akh maRaiyer lokShymatra niye joyopurohaT cinikol 25 novemwr ut''padone zay. kintu akher ovabe 63 hajar 91 Ton akh maRai kora hoy. ta theke cini ut''padit hoy matr car hajar 294 Ton. othoc ebarer lokShymatra chil choy hajar Ton. orrthat'' ek hajar 70o6 Ton cini kom ut''padit hoyeche. jana zayo, bajare guRer dam beSi hoOyay cinikol elakar onek caShi guR bybosayIder kache beSi dame akh bikri korechen. cinikole akher mUly zekhane 10o0 
Taka moNo, sekhane guR bybosayIra dicchen 120 Taka. ebar cinikol elakay 10 hajar 34 ekor jomite akher caSh hoyechil. baNijy melay oniyom ipibir upoporicalokoke protyaharer supariS roptani unnoyon byurOte (oipibi) preShoNe korrmorot upoporicalok sOIyod belal hOsenoke joruri vittite protyaharer supariS koreche baNijy montroNaloy. baNijy montroNaloy theke jonoproSason montroNaloyer sociber kache gotokal sOmobar paThanO ek ciThite e supariS kora hoy. ciThite bola hoyo, âosOIyod belal hOsener biruddhe ipibir 168 jon korrmokorrta-okorrmocarI ghuSho-odurrnItir ovizOg dakhil kore. tini zehetu dIrrghodin ipibite korrmorot achen ebong ta^r biruddhe sobaroi ovizOg royeche, tai Oi protiShThan theke ta^ke protyahar kora joruri.â protyahar kore joruri vittite uposocib podomorryadar 
ekojonoke preShoNe podayoner supariSoO kora hoy ciThite. ovizOgokarIder modhye upoporicaloko, sohokarI poricaloko, gobeShoNa korrmokorrta, tothy korrmokorrta, todontokarI, hisaborokShoN korrmokorrtasoh prodorrSonI korrmokorrta, proSasonik korrmokorrta, enalisTo, jonosongzOg korrmokorrta, kompiuTar opareToro, hisab sohokarI, ovyrrthonakarI, gaRicaloko, mudrakShorik O emoeloesoesora royechen. ovizOge bola hoyo, sOIyod belal hOsen coloman Dhaka antorrjatik baNijy mela, 20o12 (oDiaiTiefo) socibaloyer sodosysocib. kintu pyaviliyon O sTol boradde tini bivinn oniyom korechen. zOgazOg kora hole ipibir vais ceyaromyan SuvaSis bosu prothom alOke boleno, sOIyod belal hOsener biruddhe kOnO todont kora hoyoni bole kichu bola zacche na. ar jonoproSason montroNaloy theke kOnO ciThiO ipibite aseni. er baire tini kichu bolote raji non. sOIyod 
belal hOsen prothom alOke boleno, âosob ovizOg mithya. ovizOgokarIra soThik dayitw palon koreni bole ami tader onuposthit dekhiyechi. e karoNe tara khepeche.â sorokari korrmocarIra biniyOg korote parobe na pu^jibajarer jony ayokor ain songSOdhon koroche sorokar. songSOdhit aine miucuyal fanD theke orrjit ay koromukt korar kotha bola hoyeche. e chaRa lenodener Opor ut''se kor doSomik 10 SotangS theke komiye doSomik 0o5 SotangS kora hoyeche. gotokal sOmobar socibaloye montrisovar bOIThoke pu^jibajar gotiSIl korar lokShye ayokor ainer esob songSOdhonI prostab onumOdit hoy. e chaRa montrisova pu^jibajare orrth biniyOg korar biShoye sob porryayer sorokari korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIder kShetre bidhiniShedh arOp korote songSliShT korrtrripokSher proti nirrdeS diyeche 
bole sorokari songbad songstha basos janay. e chaRa bOIThoke pu^jibajare sorokari korrmokorrtader biniyOg niye alOcona hoyeche boleO jana geche. e biShoye sorokari korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIder pu^jibajare biniyOg na kora niScit korar kotha bola hoyeche. cakoribidhi soThikovabe karrykor korotei e niye alOcona hoy bole jana geche. ekadhik montrIr soNgge kotha bole jana zayo, bOIThoke prodhanomontrI boleno, zehetu Seyarobajare biniyOg jhu^kipUrrNo, tai er dayodayitw biniyOgokarIkei nite hobe. nij dayitwe biniyOg korote hobe. lav zemon nijero, temoni lOkosanoO nijer. tini Seyarobajarer jhu^ki somporrke manuShoke sotorrk kore dite bolen. sUtr janayo, bOIThoke prodhanomontrI sorokari cakorir bidhimala somporrke janote can. e somoy songSliShT byktira prodhanomontrIke janano, 1979 
sale jiyaur rohomaner Sasonokale ze bidhimala kora hoyo, tate sorokari samoriko-obesamorik korrmokorrtader cakorirot obosthay bybosa-obaNijye ba lavojonok khate biniyOg na korar byapare niShedhajNGa ache. e somoy prodhanomontrI 1979 saler ei ainoTi notun kore procar korar nirrdeS den. sorrwOcc mojuri 560o0 Taka: jatIy mojuri O ut''padonoSIlota komiSon 20o10o-oer supariS gotokal montrisovar bOIThoke onumOdon deOya hoyeche. supariS onuzayI, sorrwOcc mojuri pa^c hajar 60o0 Taka kora hoyeche. ete sorrwnimn mojuri nirrdharit hoyeche car hajar 175 Taka. prodhanomontrIr pres socib janano, komiSoner e supariS 20o10 saler julai mas theke karrykor hobe. ete baRivaRa dharry kora hoyeche Sotokora 50 vag. cikit''sa vata dhora hoy 70o0 
Taka. e chaRa ut''sob bOnas dui masero, zatayat 150 ebong Tifin babod 150 Taka nirrdharoN kora hoyeche. pres socib janano, montrisovar bOIThoke ainoSrriNgkhola bighnokarI oporadh (odrut bicaro) (osongSOdhono) aino, 20o12-oer khosoRa nItigot O cURant onumOdon deOya hoyeche. ei ainoTi prothome 20o0o2 saler 10 epril proNoyon kora hoy. prothome ainoTi dui bochor porrynt karrykor chil. eropor protibaroi ainoTi dui bochor kore baRanO hoy. gotokaler bOIThoke ainoTi 20o14 saler 10 epril porrynt baRanOr siddhant hoy. bOIThoke manob pacar protirOdh O domon aino, 20o12-oer khosoRar nItigot O cURant onumOdon deOya hoy. prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina bOIThoke sovapotitw koren. amolatantrik joTilotay bideSi biniyOg asoche na: 
baNijymontrI baNijymontrI ji em kader bolecheno, bideSi biniyOg na asar karoN hisebe onekei bole thaken obokaThamO na thakar kotha. kintu er mUl karoN holO amolatantrik joTilota O durrnIti. biSeSh kore uttoradhikar sUtre paOya durrnIti. antorrjatik bajarer karoNe deSe kichu poNyer bajar osthir hocche. e chaRa kichu poNy niye karosajiO hocche. esob byapare sorokar sojag ache. aj moNggolobar dupure rajodhanIr ekoTi hOTele âobangladeSe bybosa korar cyaleNGj O subidhaâ SIrrShok sovay prodhan otithir boktobye somoy baNijymontrI esob kotha bolen. amerikan cemwar ob komarrs Oi vOjosovar ayOjon kore. ji em kader boleno, bideSi biniyOgokarIder jony bangladeSer bajar unmukt. protykSh bideSi biniyOg asar jony

Sulk korrtrripokSh. vuya chaRopotrer biShoyoTi fa^s hoOyar por gotokal sOmobar 68 lakh Taka Sulkokor poriSOdh koreche ovizukt amodanikaroker protinidhi. got brrihospotibar 68 lakh Takar Sulkokor joma deOyar nokol chaRopotr baniye 11 konoTeinar rasayonik droby khalas kore ney sioyanDoef ejenT eoyanDoes ejensi. pray ek kOTi 11 lakh Taka mUlyer esob rasayonik amodani kore Dhakar niu seven sTar kemikyal. ei amodanikaroker pokShe poNy khalaser dayitw pay eoyanDoes ejensi. biShoyoTi niye prothom alOte gotokal ekoTi protibedon prokaSit hoy. e ghoTonar por gotokal ekoi eoyanDoes ejensir esiD O rasayonikovorrti aroO pa^coTi konoTeinarer khalas sthogit ebong ilekoTronikos poNyvorrti duTi konoTeinar silogala kora hoyeche. ei satoTi 
konoTeinar zacai-obachai kore khalas deOya hobe bole Sulk korrmokorrtara janan. gotokal sangbadikoder soNgge alaper somoy Sulk bivager otirikt komiSonar mO. motiur rohoman boleno, e ghoTonar soNgge joRit byktider khu^je ber korote todont hocche. todonte dOShIder Sonakt kore ta^der biruddhe mamola kora hobe. got brrihospotibar 11 konoTeinar poNy khalaser somoy sisiTi-o1 geTer kompiuTar ken noShT chil ebong noShT thakar poroO Urrdhwton korrmokorrtader ken jananO hoyoniâobiShoyoTi niyeO todont hocche bole tini janan. edike, 11 konoTeinarer ghoTonar por bondorer aToTi geT diye poNy khalaser somoy nojorodari baRate koRakoRi podokShep neOyar siddhant niyeche coTTogram kasTom haus korrtrripokSh. eoyanDoes ejensi poricalonakarI mO. poriSOdh korar por gotokal prothom alOr kache dabi koreno, ta^r protiShThaner korrmocarI (oje Ti sorokaro) joyonal abedIn ei oniyom korechen. soyabin teler mUlybrriddhi modhyswtwvOgIder dayI korol songsodIy komiTi khucora bajare soyabin teler dam baRar jony modhyswtwvOgIder dayI koreche baNijy montroNaloyo-osomporrkit songsodIy komiTi. gotokal sOmobar songsod vobone onuShThit baNijy montroNaloyo-osomporrkit komiTir bOIThoke e mot deOya hoy. bOIThok SeShe komiTir sovapoti e bi em abul kasem sangbadikoder janano, antorrjatik bajare oporiSOdhit vOjyteler dam komoleO deSer bajare er kOnO provab nei. e jony modhyswtwvOgIra dayI. tara otirikt munafar jony beSi dame tel bikri koroche. tini boleno, komiTi e biShoye zothazoth bybostha neOyar jony

baNijymontrI) faruk khan. komologoNGje ba^So-obet SilpIder michil O smarokolipi peS âoba^So-obetoSilpI ba^caO, pu^ji daOâoâoei dabite komologoNGj upojela sodore michil O upojela nirrwahI korrmokorrtar kache smarokolipi peS korechen ba^S O betoSilpIra. komologoNGjer adomopur O isolamopur iuniyoner ei Silper soNgge joRit lOkojon gotokal sOmobar sokale e korrmosUci palon koren. bela 11Tay bet karigor somobay somitir sovapoti rOkeya begom O sadharoN sompadok richan ahomeder netrritwe SilpIra upojela nirrwahI korrmokorrta (oiuenoO) prokaSokanti cOUdhurIr kache smarokolipi den. smarokolipi grohoN kore nirrwahI korrmokorrta ba^S O betoSilpIder uddeSe boktobye boleno, itimodhye biShoyoTi gurutwsohokare jela komiTir sovay uposthapon kora hoyeche. ei Silper soNgge joRit lOkojonoke rriN deOyar jony

meramot kore sar ut''padone zete bilomw hocche. zomuna sar karokhana kOmpani limiTeDer bybosthapona poricalok ocinty kumar deb janano, Sromiko-okorrmocarI iuniyon karokhanay korrmobiroti palon koreche. drut dhonI hoOyar lOv dekhiye emoeloem bybosa kora zabe na drut dhonI hoOyar lOv dekhiye ar malTi level marrkeTing (oemoeloemo) bybosa kora zabe na. mithya bijNGapon diye protaroNa kora zabe na kauke. emoeloemer nam vaNgiye bikri kora zabe na kOnO obostugot ba olIk poNy. somoyer dharabahikota ba porryayokromik prokriyakoroNer madhyme vobiShyte bipoNonozOgy hobeâoemon poNy ba sebaO niShiddh kora hobe. emoeloeme Sudhu bostugot poNy bikri kora zabe ebong esob poNye mORok bybohar badhytamUlok. e mORoke abar poNyer 
ut''padoko, porimapo, Ojono, sorrwOcc khucora mUly, meyadOttIrrNer tarikh ityadi ullekh thakote hobe. esob bOISiShTy niye agamIkal sOmobar onuShThey montrisovar bOIThoke onumOdoner jony uposthapon kora hocche DairekT sel aino, 20o12-oer khosoRar ekoTi songkShipto-osar. baNijy montroNaloyer tOIri kora ainer e khosoRay 13Ti odhyayo, 50oTi dhara O duiTi tofosil royeche. ei ain karrykor hoOyar por piramiDosodrriS bikroy karrykrom niShiddh bole goNy hobeâoe kotha ullekh kore montrisovay uposthaponer jony khosoRay emoeloemo-oke poNy ba seba bipoNoner âoovinob kOUSoloâ hisebe ovihit kora hoyeche. khosoRay aroO bola hoyeche, varoto, cIno, kanaDa, maloyeSiyasoh biSwer onek deSei emoeloem bybosa poricalonar sunirrdiShT ain ba nItimala royeche. bangladeSe ta nei. othoc 
e dhoroner bybosa bangladeSeO din din baRoche. ete bola hoyeche, zOUth mUlodhoni kOmpani O farrmogulOr poridoptor (orejosokO) theke nibondhon niye ebong emonoki nibondhon chaRaO oneke emoeloem bybosa koroche. egulOy kOnO swcchota O jobabodihi nei. ucc munafar lOv dekhiye tara hoyorani O protaroNa koroche jonogoNer soNgge. onek kOmpani gocchit orrth atmosat'' koreO manuShoke sorrwswant koroche. e obosthay emoeloem bybosake aini kaThamOr modhye ana joruri. emoeloemer paSapaSi e dhoroner poddhoti neToOyarrk marrkeTing, piramiDosodrriS bikri karrykromo, dware dware bikri, Teli marrkeTing, i-omarrkeTing, DairekT marrkeTing sisTemo, TimoOyarrk marrkeTing sisTemo, friDom enTaropraijo, hOm beijoD marrkeTing, holiDe bijones ityadi name poricit bole songkShipto-osare ullekh kora hoyeche. 
bola hoyeche, amader deSe egulO kOmpani ainer aOtay nibondhit. onek kShetre Sudhu TreD laisenser madhymeO bybosa poricalit hocche. khosoRay bola hoyeche, 10 bochor age 16Ti thakoleO 20o10 sal nagad 70oTi kOmpani emoeloem rejosokOte nibondhit. tobe baNijy montroNaloyer nirrdeSe rejosokO borrtomane nibondhon bondh rekheche. ete aroO bola hoyeche, deSe borrtomane emoeloemer name Seyarobajare biniyOgo, somobay somiti, porryTon O holiDe pyakejo, abason O bonayoner paSapaSi veShoj O harobalo, krriShipoNy ut''padon O bajarojatokoroN ebong grrihosthali O nity byboharry poNy kenabeca hocche. e poddhotir itibacok dik hoccheâobipul porimaN manuSher komiSon hisabe ayer suzOg. ar netibacok dik hoccheâootirikt mUlye poNy bikri, orrth atmosat'', protaroNa ityadi. 
Sudhu ain proNoyon noyo, e ainer uddeSy bastobayone ekoTi poridoptor kora hobe, za âoDairekT sel niyontroN poridoptoroâ name ovihit hobe. poridoptorer ekojon niyontrok thakobeno, zini hoben er prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta. niyontroker dayitw O kShomotar modhye acheâoDairekT sel ba sorasori bikroy karrykromer laisens deOya, laisenser karrykarita sthogito, batil O punorrwhal kora; kreta, kreta poribeSok O vOkta odhikarobirOdhI karry protirOdh ebong ta loNgghoner ovizOg niShpotti; oporadh somporrke todont poricalona ityadi. ain pas hoOyar ag porrynt orrthat'' borrtomane zesob kOmpani DairekT sel bybosay joRito, tader ain jarir 90 diner modhye nibondhoker kach theke laisens nite hobe. ainer kOnO dhara loNgghoner oporadhe kOnO bykti 
ba protiShThanoke tin theke pa^c bochorer karadoND ebong onodhik 50 lakh Taka jorimana korar bidhan rakha hoyeche. zOgazOg korole baNijysocib mO. gOlam hOsen prothom alOke boleno, orrth montroNaloyo, swraShTr montroNaloyo, bijNGan ebong tothy O zOgazOgoprozukti montroNaloyo, bangladeS byangko, inosTiTiuT ob carrTarrD oyakaunoTenToso, bangladeSer (oaisiebi) motamot niye ainer khosoRaTi tOIri kora hoyeche. montrisovay eTi pas hole ebong ainoTi karrykor hole deSer emoeloem bybosa SrriNgkholar modhye asobe bole tini aSabadI. nOU-oproTOkole TranojiT maSul neOyar pokShe enobiar bangladeS O varoter modhykar nOU-oproTOkoler aOtay TranojiTo-osubidha byboharer kShetre maSuler arOper pokShe mot diyeche jatIy rajosw bOrrD (oenobiaro). paSapaSi obokaThamO na thakay aSugoNGj nOUbondor bybohar kore 
TranojiT deOya apatot bondh rakhar poramorrS deOya hoyeche. somproti nOU-oproTOkoloTi porrybekShoN kore sorokarer kache esob motamot diyeche enobiar. itimodhye ei porrybekShoN protibedon nOU montroNaloye paThiye deOya hoyeche. prosoNggot agamI 31 marrc dui deSer modhykar .nOU-oproTOkoler meyad SeSh hocche. proTOkoloTir meyad baRanOr udyOg niyeche nOU montroNaloy. ar emon prekShapoTe enobiar nOU-oproTOkoloTir Opor motamot diyeche. nOU-oproTOkoler kOn kOn ongSe songSOdhon kora hote pare sei biShoye coloti soptahei songSliShT montroNaloyogulOr soNgge bOIThoke bosobe nOU montroNaloy. coloti maser dwitIy soptahe nOU-oproTOkoler Opor tader porrybekShoN O motamot nOU montroNaloye paThay enobiar. ete mUlot pa^coTi biShoyer Opor motamot deOya hoyeche. nOU-oproTOkoler aOtay et din bina maSule 
TranojiT neOyar suzOg chil. kintu enobiar notun kore maSul arOper pokShe mot diyeche. proti Tone 580 Taka hisabe kasTomoso-osongkrant maSul neOyar prostab kora hoyeche. TranojiTer aOtay poribahit poNyer jony TranojiT prodanokarI deS poNyer Opor kOnO SulkarOp korote pare na. tobe poNybahI zanobahon deSe O deS theke ber hoOyar kShetre bivinn porIkSha-onirIkShasoh proSasonik O prokriyakoroNer seba prodaner biporIte maSul nite pare. taroi alOke kasTomoso-osongkrant maSuler supariS kora hoyeche. kasTomoso-osongkrant maSul nirrdharoNer kShetre kagojopotr prokriyakoroNo, TranoSipomenTo, skyaning, marrcenT OvaroTaimo, nirapotta, prohora O aisiTi maSul bibeconay ana hoyeche. onydike TranojiT poNyer somoporimaN Sulk byangk gyaranTi hisabe rakhar pokSheO mot diyeche enobiar. songsthaTi boloche, 
antorrjatik prekShapoTeO ei dhoroner corrca hoy. aSugoNGj nOUbondor bybohar kore stholopothe akhauRa stholobondor hoye varoter uttoro-opUrrwaNGcolIy rajy tripurar rajodhanI agorotolay varotIy poNy neOyar suzOgoTiO apatot karrykor na korar poramorrS deOya hoyeche. ei pothoTite ekhonO TranojiT upozOgI obokaThamO goRe na OThai er karoN hisebe bola hoyeche. e chaRa nOU-oproTOkoler 23(o2) onucchedoTi apatot bilOp korar supariS koreche enobiar. ei onucchede TranoSipomenTer suzOg deOya hoyeche. beSi DrafoTosomponn (opoNybahI jahajer ze ongS panir nice thake) jahaj theke poNy DrafoTosomponn jahaje poNy sthanantor kingba kom DrafoTosomponn jahaj theke beSi DrafoTosomponn jahaje poNy sthanantor kore ei subidhaTi bybohUt hote pare. enobiar ta apatot bondh rakhar pokShe. 
ullekhy, nabyta songkoTer karoNe ei onuccheder suzOg niye prothomobarer motO varotIy jahaj lal bahadur SastrIr poNygulO aSugoNGj nOUbondor theke chOT chOT jahaje kore somproti korimogoNGj diye varote neOya hoyeche. onydike nOU-oproTOkole jokigoNGjer Seropur porrynt nOUpothe niye tino-ocar kilOmiTar soRokopothe sImant porrynt poNy neOyar suzOg royeche. kintu ei pothoTi kokhonO bybohar koreni varotIy bybosayIra. tai ei suzOgoTi batil korar supariS koreche enobiar. enobiar korrmokorrtara bolecheno, sorokar zehetu varotoke TranojiT deOyar biShoyoTi sokriyovabe bibecona koroche, ar tate maSul neOyar kothaO bola hocche tai nOU-oproTOkoler aOtay maSul neOya ucit. ta^ra aroO boleno, biSw prekShapoTe ekhon zekOnO dhoroner TranojiT bybosthay prodanokarI deS maSul niye 
thake. ar porryapt obokaThamO ache emon pothei TranojiT deOya hoy. 1972 sale bangladeS O varoter modhye bidyman ovyntorIN nOUpoth otikrom O baNijy proTOkol swakShorit hoy. er aOtay bangladeSer ovyntore nOUpothe varot poNy ana-oneOya kore thake. e jony nodI khononosoh bochore saRe pa^c kOTi Taka dey varot. proti dui bochor por por ei cuktiTi nobayon kora hoy. tobe gotobochor cuktiTi ek bochorer jony nobayon kora hoy. dui bochorer poriborrte ek bochor nobayoner pechone karoN chilo, borrtoman sorokar brrihottor aNggike varotoke TranojiT deOyar biShoyoTi sokriyovabe bibecona koroche. abar 1980 sale swakShorit dui deSer modhykar baNijy cuktir aOtay nOU-oproTOkoloTi poricalit hoy. ar baNijy 
cuktir meyad SeSh hocche agamI 1 epril. baNijy cuktiTi nobayon na korole nOU-oproTOkol karrykor kora somvob hobe na. itimodhye baNijy montroNaloy dui deSer modhykar baNijy cukti nobayon korar udyOg niyeche. prosoNggot proti tin bochor ontor ei cuktiTi nobayon kora hoy. sorrwSeSh 20o0o9 sale borrtoman sorokar kShomotay ese cuktiTi nobayon koreche. nOU-oproTOkol somporrke nOU montroNaloyer zugm socib mOhammod alauddin gotokal TelifOne prothom alOke janano, dui deSer baNijy cuktir nobayon kora hobe ki na, tar Opor nirrvor koroche nOU-oproTOkoler vobiShyt''. cuktiTi nobayon somporrke baNijy montroNaloyer siddhanter opekShay royeche nOU montroNaloy. enobiarer porrybekShoN somporrke mOhammod alauddin boleno, porrybekShoN motamotoTi ekhonO ta^r hate ese

kora zabe. etOdin grrihayon rriNer kShetre ei onupat chil 80o:o20. orrthat'' ekhon theke jomi ba baRir jony rriN dite hole grahoker ongS beSi hote hobe. sud harer bybodhan deSer baNijyik byangkogulOke rriN O amanoter suder harer modhykar bybodhan nimnotor porryaye ek oNgke bojay rakhar nirrdeS diyeche bangladeS byangk. gotokal rObobar kendrIy byangk theke jari kora ek sarrkulare e nirrdeS deOya hoy. ete bola hoyeche, âouccotor jhu^kibahI vOktarriN (okreDiT karrD rriNosoho) O esoemoi rriN chaRa ony khate rriNer suder har ebong amanot songgroher goRovarit suder harer bybodhan ba nimnotor ek oNgker porryaye sImit rakhar jony nirrdeSona deOya zacche.â zOgazOg kora hole

bostut rriNer UrrdhwsIma tule neOyar por bivinn byangk amanot songgroher jony suder har baRate Suru koreche. amanote borrdhit suder harer provabe rriNer suder haroO baRote Suru koreche. rriNer suder har beRe zaOyay bybosayI mohol theke itimodhyei apotti uTheche. ta^ra bolocheno, coRasude rriN niye bybosa-obaNijye orrthayon byyobohul hoye poRobe. e obosthay bangladeS byangk gotokal e nirrdeSona jari korol. er age biSwmondar somoy bangladeS byangk 20o0o8 saler epril mase ek projNGaponer madhyme krriShi khato, brrihot'' O majhariSilpegu meyadi rriNo, coloti mUlodhon rriNo, grrihayoN O baNijy orrthayon rriNer kShetre sorrwOcc suder har 13 SotangS nirrdharoN kore dey. ekoi bochorer jun mase ony ek 
projNGapone o-obyangk arrthik protiShThanogulOke deOya byangkorriNer suder haroO sorrwOcc 13 SotangSe be^dhe deOya hoy. bangladeSe pUrrN karryaloy khulote agrohI aiDibi jedday aiDibir prodhan karryaloy bangladeSe pUrrNaNgg nijosw karryaloy poricalona korote cay isolami unnoyon byangk (oaiDibi). itimodhye e-osomporrkit ekoTi prostab orrthonOItik somporrk bivagoke (oiaroDi) diyeche protiShThanoTi. e jony aiDibir choy sodosyer ekoTi protinidhidol bangladeS sofor koroche. gotokal rObobar aiDibir protinidhidol iaroDir socib ikobal mahomuder soNgge bOIThok kore. protinidhidoler netrritw den aiDibir poricalok (okanTri DiparrTomenTo) mOhammod jamal al sati. iaroDi karryaloye ei bOIThok onuShThit hoy. iaroDir korrmokorrtara janano, bangladeSe aiDibir rriN O onudaner porimaN din din baRoche. tai aiDibi bangladeSe ekoTi pUrrNaNgg 
karryaloy sthapon kore karrykrom poricalona korote agrohI. mUlot sei karryaloyer sthaponosongkrant prostab O er ogrogoti niyei bOIThoke alOcona hoyeche. jana geche, borrtomane ekoTi maTh porryayer karryaloyer madhyme bangladeSe aiDibir karrykrom poricalit hoye asoche. kintu zekOnO biShoye jedday obosthit prodhan karryaloyer onumOdon neOyar proyOjon hoy. er fole onek somoy siddhant grohoN prolomwit hoy. tai bangladeSe karryrot onyany data songsthar (ozemono: biSwbyangk O eSIy unnoyon byangko) motO ekoTi swyongsomponn karryaloy sthapon korote cay aiDibi. iaroDi sUtre jana geche, aiDibir prostabe bangladeSer pokSh theke itibacok monOvab dekhanO hoyeche. tai Sigogiroi pororaShTr montroNaloyer soNgge aiDibir karryaloy sthaponosongkrant cukti swakShorit hobe. aiDibi protinidhidoler sodosyder pororaShTromontrI 
dIpu moni, swraShTromontrI sahara khatuno, ainomontrI Sofik ahomedo, montriporiShoder socib mOSaroraf hOsain vu^iya, jatIy rajosw bOrrDer (oenobiaro) ceyaromyan nasirouddin ahomeder soNgge sakShat'' korar kotha royeche. aiDibir kach theke e porrynt 70o0 kOTi Dolar paOya geche. er modhye 640 kOTi Dolar eseche baNijy orrthayon hisebe biSeSh kore jwalani tel amodanir jony. baki 60 kOTi Dolar paOya geche prokolp sohayota hisebe. borrtomane 10oTi prokolpe aiDibi orrthayon koroche. 7% hare probrriddhi na-oO orrjit hote pare bangladeSer orrthonItir samprotik sUcokogulO theke ze pUrrwavas miloche, tate coloti 20o11-o12 orrthobochore deSer mOT deSoj ut''padoner probrriddhir harer lokShymatra sat SotangS orrjit na-oO hote pare. inTaronyaSonal cemwar ob 
komarrs bangladeS (oaisisibi) ei ovimot prokaS koreche. baNijy songgoThonoTir trOImasik halonagad prokaSonar sompadokIyote eTi prokaS peyeche. aisisibir prokaSonay bola hoyeche, samprotik masogulOy lenodener varosamy poristhitir ullekhozOgy obonoti hoyeche. bigot koyek mase jwalanisoh bivinn poNy O sebar amodani byy beRe zaOya ebong probasI-oay probah kome zaOyay roptani probrriddhir orrjon mlan hoye geche. aisisibi aroO boleche, mudrabajare caper fole Dolarer biporIte Takar boR dhoroner obomUlyayon ghoTeche. got koyek mase marrkin Dolarer dam beReche pray 16 SotangS. abar coloti orrthobochorer prothom pa^c masei sorokarer byangkorriN grohoNer porimaN 21 hajar 321 Takay pOU^cheche, za ki na purO orrthobochorer nirrdharit lokShymatra 18 hajar 957 kOTi 
Takar ceye beSi. ei tothy ullekh kore aisisibir porisongkhyane aroO bola hoyeche, besorokari khate biniyOger orrthayone ghaToti dekha diyeche. kenona, byangke tarolysongkoT dekha diyeche. tobe esob mondavab sottweO bangladeSer orrthonItir somvabona zotheShT valO bole mone koroche aisisibi. e prosoNgge aisisibir prokaSonay jarrmano-obangladeS cemwar ob komarrser pokShe antorrjatik poramorrSok protiShThan myakenojir samprotik ek gobeShoNar ullekh kora hoyeche. bola hoyeche, myakenojir pUrrwavas onusare 20o15 saler modhye bangladeSer tOIri pOSakoSilp theke roptani ay dwiguN hobe ebong poroborrtI 10 bochorer modhye pray tin guN hobe. ar 20o20 saler modhye Sudhu tOIri pOSakoSilp khatei saRe 35 lakh lOker korrmosongsthaner suzOg srriShTi hobe. aisisibir mote, e 
lokShymatra orrjon kora zabe zodi eSiya, latin amerika O afrikar bivinn deSe notun bajar srriShTi kora zay. aisisibi aroO mone kore, OShudho, jahaj nirrmaNo, camoRajat poNy, paT O manobosompod roptanir madhymeO bangladeSer roptani ay onek baRote pare. tobe aisisibir aSoNgka holO, biSwer coloman orrthonOItik songkoTer provabe antorrjatik arrthik protiShThanogulO (ozemono: biSwbyangko, antorrjatik mudra tohobil O eSIy unnoyon byangko) rriN ebong onudan dite sokShom na-oO hote pare. eTa bangladeSer orrthonItir jony ekoTa cap tOIri korobe. doropotoner suzOg nicchen poricalokera! Seyarobajare doropotoner protibade gotokal rajodhanIr motijhile Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer samone ayOjit somabeSe hotaS ek biniyOgokarI Seyarobajarer Tana doropotoner suzOg kaje lagacchen talikavukt 
kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokera. zokhonoi bajare boR dhoroner doropoton ghoToche, tokhonoi udyOkta-oporicalokoder Seyar kenar ghOShoNa baRoche. niyontrok songstha sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSoner (oesoisi) bidhan onuzayI, talikavukt kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokoder sommilitovabe sob somoy nij kOmpanir 30 SotangS ebong ekokovabe 2 SotangS Seyar dharoN korote hobe. Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) samprotik ek hisab onuzayI, borrtomane Seyarobajare talikavukt kOmpani-ogulOr pray deR hajar poricaloker hate 2 SotangSer kom Seyar royeche. esob poricalokoke nij pode thakote hole bajar theke bipul porimaN Seyar kinote hobe. samprotik bajar porryalOconay dekha zayo, nyUnotom Seyar dharoNer Sorrt poripalone zokhonoi swavabik bajare kOnO kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalok Seyar kenar ghOShoNa deno, tokhonoi Oi kOmpanir Seyarer 
dam baRoche. e obosthay onek poricalok ghOShoNa diye Seyar kenar poriborrte nikoTojonoder kach theke Seyar upohar ba grohoN korochen. abar zokhonoi bajare doropoton ghoToche, tokhonoi poricalokoder ghOShoNa diye Seyar kenar proboNota baRoche. Diesoir OyebosaiTer tothy onuzayI, got tin karrydibose (o18, 19 O 22 januyari) talikavukt 12 kOmpanir 13 udyOkta-oporicalok pray 37 lakh 34 hajarer beSi Seyar kenar ghOShoNa diyechen. er modhye 19 januyari iunaiTeD eyar O ripabolik inosyurenser dui poricalok mile nij nij kOmpanir mOT ek lakh 48 hajar Seyar kenar ghOShoNa den. 19 januyari Diesoite mUlysUcok beRechil. sedin Oi dui poricaloker Seyar kenar ghOShoNa bajare ase. ar 18 O 
22 januyari bajare boR dhoroner doropoton ghoTole ei dui dine 10 kOmpanir 11 poricaloker kach theke pray 35 lakh 86 hajarer beSi Seyar kenar ghOShoNa ase. kOmpanigulO holO: zomuna byangko, biesoaroemo, nyaSonal laif inosyurenso, takaful inosyurenso, isolamik finyanso, provatI inosyurenso, siTi byangko, inTaronyaSonal lijing, praim byangk O grinoDelTa inosyurens. e karoNe bajarer bidyman osthirotar soNgge talikavukt kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokoder badhytamUlok Seyar kenar biShoyoTir zOgosUtr thakote pare bole keu keu dharoNa korochen. zOgazOg kora hole pu^jibajar biSleShok O besorokari iunaiTeD inTaronyaSonal iunivarrsiTir SikShok mOhammod mUsa prothom alOke boleno, âozot din porrynt udyOkta-oporicalokoder Seyar kenar badhybadhokotar meyad SeSh hocche na, tot din porrynt 
bajar purOpuri sthitiSIl hobe bole ami mone kori na. kOnO na kOnOvabe bajare osthirota thakobe.â er karoN hisebe tini boleno, âoza^der Seyar kinote hobe, ta^ra sob somoyoi caiben Seyarer dam zen khub beSi beRe na zay. e jony proyOjon hole ta^ra ta^der hate kOmpanir zesob mUly songbedonoSIl tothy royeche, segulOke nijeder swarrthe bybohar koroben. kharap ghOShoNa diye kOmpanir Seyarer damoke ekoTi porryaye dhore rakhar ceShTa korobeno, eTai swavabik. poricalokoder belayoO er bytyy ghoTobe bole ami mone kori na. tai e kShetre niyontrok songsthasoh songSliShT sobaike khuboi sojag thakote hobe, zate sadharoN biniyOgokarIra kShotigrost na hon.â sob SeShe mOhammod mUsa boleno, 
talikavukt kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokoder nyUnotom Seyar dharoNer biShoye esoisi ze bidhan koreche, tar sufol swlp meyade paOya na geleO dIrrgh meyade bajarer jony eTi valO fol boye anobe. prothom narI DepuTi govorrnor najonIn sulotana bangladeS byangker prothom narI DepuTi govorrnor holen najonIn sulotana. aj sOmobar aroO dujon DepuTi govorrnorosoh ta^r nizo09BCOgo-osongkrant ciThi bangladeS byangke ese pOU^cheche. ei pode nizo09BCOg paOzo09BCa opor dujon holenoâoabu hena mOhammod rajI hasan O sitangSu kumar sur cOUdhurI. ta^ra tin bochorer jony ei pode nizo09BCOg pelen. nizo09BCOgopraptoder modhye abu hena mOhammod rajI hasan O sitangSu kumar sur cOUdhurI kendrIzo09BC byangke nirrwahI poricalok hisebe korrmorot rozo09BCechen. ar najonIn

Sromik kolyaNe munafar 5 SotangS dite hobe, noile Sasti Sromik kolyaN faunDeSon (osongSOdhono) aino-o20o12-oer nItigot onumOdon diyeche montrisova. fole ekhon protiTi kOmpanir munafa theke Sromikoder kolyaNe goThit tohobile 5 SotangS joma deOya badhytamUlok kora hoyeche. ar ei niyom loNgghon korole Sastir bidhanoO rakha hoyeche. aj sOmobar socibaloye montriporiShod bivager sovakokShe prodhanomontrI Sekh hasinar sovapotitwe e bOIThok onuShThit hoy. bOIThok SeShe montriporiShod bivager zugm socib iSoteyak hOsen pres brifing kore sangbadikoder e tothy janan. e somoy montriporiShod bivager socib mOSarorof hOsen vU^iya uposthit chilen. bOIThoke bangladeS sorokari korrmocarI obosor aino-o20o12-oer khosoRaO 
onumOdon deOya hoy. ekoi soNgge sorokari korrmokaNDer Opor trOImasik protibedonoO uposthapon kora hoy. sOnar dam baRoche kalo, proti vori 58 hajar Taka deSe sOnar dam kal moNggolobar theke abaroO baRoche. dam beRe valO maner 22 kyareT voriproti sOnar dam hocche 57 hajar 736 Taka. e chaRa 21 O 18 kyareT ebong sonatonI hisebe poricit deSi sOnar damoO voriproti ek hajar 50 theke ek hajar 30o0 Taka porrynt baRoche. bangladeS juyelarrs somitir (obajuso) karrynirrwahI sovay aj sOmobar swrrNer dam baRanO biShoye alOcona hoy. sovar siddhant onuzayI kal theke swrrNer dam baRanOr ghOShoNa dey bajus. eropor aj rate e-osongkrant songbadobijNGopti paThiye biShoyoTi 
niScit kore juyelarrs somiti. sorrwSeSh 14 januyari bajus sob dhoroner swrrNer dam baRay. kal theke karrykor hoOya notun dam onuzayI, 22 kyareT voriproti (o11 doSomik 664 gramo) swrrNer dam 57 hajar 736 Taka; 21 kyareT proti vori 55 hajar 170 Taka O 18 kyareT 47 hajar 297 Taka. ar sonatonI hisebe poricit deSi swrrNer vori 36 hajar 158 Taka. tobe swrrN bybosayIra bolocheno, proti vori swrrNalongkar kinote kretake ekhon goRe mojuri hisabe car hajar Taka ebong mUly songzOjon kor hisebe 2 SotangS hare orrth dite hoy. sei hisabe 22 kyareT swrrNer goyonar dor poRobe proti vori pray 62 hajar 890 
Taka. aj porrynt 22 kyareT vori proti swrrNer dam 56 hajar 453 Taka; 21 kyareT proti vori 53 hajar 887 Taka O 18 kyareT 46 hajar 189 Taka ebong deSi swrrNer vori 35 hajar 10o8 Takay becakena hoyeche. sei hisabe voriproti 22 kyareTe dam beReche ek hajar 283 Taka, 21 kyareTe ek hajar 293 Taka, 18 kyareTe ek hajar 10o8 Taka O deSi swrrNe ek hajar 50 Taka. bajuser sadharoN sompadok deOyan aminul isolam prothom alOke boleno, Dolarer dam baRay badhy hoyei swrrNer dam baRanOr siddhant niyeche somiti. tini aroO boleno, âoamora koyek din opekSha korochi. kintu antorrjatik bajare swrrNer 
dam obyahotovabe baRoche. dam na baRale protibeSI deSogulOte obOIdh pothe pacar hoOyar aSoNgka thake.â khO^j niye jana zayo, got bochorer januyari theke Disemwr mas porrynt 16 dofay swrrNer dor beReche pray 30 SotangS. got bochorer januyarir prothom dike 22 kyareT swrrNer dam chil proti vori 42 hajar 165 Taka. sei hisabe got ek bochore vori proti swrrNer dam beReche 15 hajar 571 Taka. orrthat dam beReche pray 36 SotangS. doropoton coloche Diesoir mUlysUcok dui bochorer modhye sorrwnimn Seyarobajare doropoton colochei. gotokal sOmobaroO dui sTok eksoceNGjer sob koTi sUcokoi komeche. bajarosongSliShT byktira bolocheno, sorokari korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIder Seyare biniyOgoke ghire tOIri hoOya osthirotar 
jer dhore bajare ei doropoton ghoToche. prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok gotokal din SeShe pray deR SotangS ba 71 poyenT kome geche. opor Seyarobajar coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok pray 1 doSomik 84 SotangS ba 252 poyenT komeche. doropotoner protibade gotokaloO rajodhanIr motijhile Diesoir samoner soRoke biniyOgokarIra byapok bikShOv korechen. e karoNe Oi elakay beS koyek ghoNTa zan colacol bondh chil. diner lenodener Suru thekei dui bajare mUlysUcoker byapok utthano-opoton ghoTeche. din SeShe Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcok neme eseche pray car hajar 639 poyenTe. got pray dui bochorer modhye eTii Diesoir sadharoN mUlysUcoker sorrwnimn obosthan. er age 
20o10 saler 3 januyari sorrwSeSh Diesoir sadharoN sUcok car hajar 568 poyenTer sorrwnimn obosthane chil. tobe 20o11 saler 15 novemwr eTi car hajar 649 poyenTe nemechil. coTTogramer sarrwik mUlysUcok gotokal din SeShe neme eseche pray 13 hajar 428 poyenTe. dui bajare sOmobar lenoden hoOya kOmpanigulOr modhye Diesoite 69 SotangS ebong siesoite pray 80 SotangSeroi dam komeche. Dhakar bajare sOmobar mUlysUcoker poton diyei lenoden Suru hoy. zodiO prothom pa^c miniT por ta UrrdhwmukhI hoy. 15 miniTer mathay sadharoN mUlysUcok ager diner ceye pray 31 poyenT beRe car hajar 741 poyenTe OThe. eropor abar sUcoker poton ghoTote thake, za diner SeSh porrynt

Diesoite e din 257Ti kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer Seyar lenoden hoy. er modhye 178Tiroi dam komeche, beReche 63Tir ar oporiborrtit chil 16Ti kOmpanir Seyarer dam. Diesoite lenodener SIrrSh 10 kOmpanir talikay chil zothakrome grrramINofOno, beksimokO, aroen spining, iunaiTeD eyaro, nyaSonal byangko, sOsyal isolamI byangko, fu Oyang siramikoso, bikon farrma O biesoaroem sTil. coTTogramer bajare e din pray 36 kOTi Takar lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye car kOTi Taka kom. siesoite 
gotokal 179Ti kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer Seyarer lenoden hoy. er modhye 144Tiroi dam komeche, beReche 26Tir ar oporiborrtit chil noyoTi kOmpanir Seyarer dam. pujibajare doropoton obyahot Diesoite 25 maser modhye sorrwnimn sUcok deSer pu^jibajare aj moNggolobaroO doropoton obyahot rozo09BCeche. obyahot ei doropotone prodhan bajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok dui bochorer modhye sorrwnimn obosthane neme eseche. aj Diesoir sadharoN sUcok 2 doSomik 85 SotangS komeche. ar coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok komeche 2 doSomik 17 SotangS. ar dui bajarei aj lenoden komeche. edike pu^jibajarer borrtoman poristhitite sobaike dhOIrry dhorar ahwan janizo09BCechen Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI. dupure sangbadikoder soNgge 
alapokale tini e kotha bolen. tini boleno, pu^jibajare utthano-opoton thakobe. ekosomozo09BC Diesoite dOInik matr ek kOTi Taka lenoden hotO. sei lenoden ekoporryazo09BCe tin hajar kOTi Takazo09BC pOU^chechil. tobe ekhon lenoden onek kom hocche. ete cintit hoOzo09BCar kichu nei. bajar tar nijer gotite abaroO ghure da^Do09BCabe bole aSabad bykt koren tini. pollI korrmo-osohayok faunDeSoner (opikeesoefo) ceyaromyan kajI kholIkujjoman ahomod. mUl probondh uposthapon koren aisiebir kaunsil sodosy mosih malik cOUdhurI. boktoby den paNGjab biSwbidyaloyer imeriTas odhyapok khaja amojad sayIdo, Dhaka sTok eksoceNGj (oDiesoi) sovapoti Sakil rijovI, coTTogram sTok eksoceNGj (osiesoi) sovapoti al maruf khano, aisiebi sovapoti saiful isolam. seminare sovapotitw koren aisiebir kaunsil sodosy abwas uddin khan. kajI kholIkujjoman boleno, borrtomane bangladeSer Seyarobajar zothazothovabe coloche na. ei Seyarobajarer bybosthaponar dayitwpraptoder karrykrome hostokShep na kore bajaroTike swadhInovabe colote deOya ucit. borrtoman Seyarobajar poristhiti somporrke kholIkujjoman aroO boleno, âoei deSe zekOnO ekoTa biShoye agroh dekha dile ta otimatray beRe zay. zemono, zokhon kShudrorriN karrykrom 
elo, tokhon Sot Sot besorokari songstha (oenojiO) ei kShudrorriNe joRiye poRol. abar besorokari biSwbidyaloy onumOdon deOya Suru hole ta maSorumer motO gojiye uTheche.â samprotik somoye Seyarobajarer kShetreO ta hoyeche ullekh kore kholIkujjoman boleno, âoekhane laver aSay lakh lakh manuSh SeyarobajaromukhI hoyechen. oneke kShudr soNGcoy veNge, goyona bikri kore Seyarobajare gechen. bajar poRe zaOyay ta^rai beSi kShotigrost hoyechen.â kholIkujjomaner mote, orrthonOItik probrriddhir jony biniyOg dorokar. ar korrmosongsthan O poNy ut''padone besorokari khater vUmika soboceye beSi. ei besorokari protiShThanogulO pu^jir jony Seyarobajare zete pare. khaja amojad sayId boleno, Seyarobajar holO orrthonItir ekoTi sUcok. ar daridrry bimOconer jony dorokar orrthonOItik probrriddhi. orrthonItir mUl

Sakil rijovI boleno, 20o10 sale sorokar zodi aroO beS kichu kOmpani niye asoto, tobe bajarer ei obostha hotO na. niyontrokoder aroO karrykor hoOya ucit. al maruf khan boleno, ainogot subidhar ovabe e deSer Seyarobajare bideSi pOrrTofOliO totha biniyOg nei bololei cole. ar sthanIy biniyOgokarIra biSw arrthik poristhitir soNgge somprrikt non. maruf khan janano, Seyarobajar theke kom khoroce tohobil songgroh kora zay. ar ei subidha jati nite pare. mosih malik cOUdhurI ta^r mUl probondhe Seyarobajarer

soNgge kanaDar baNijyik lenoden O zOgazOg beSi.â mahobubul alom boleno, 20o10 orrthobochore bangladeS kanaDay 83 kOTi 60 lakh Dolar mUlyer poNy roptani O er biporIte 59 kOTi 50 lakh Dolarer poNy amodani koreche. mOhammod emodadul hok cOUdhurI coTTogram cemwar O bangladeSe kanaDar haikomiSoner zOUth udyOge vobiShyte âoTreD SOâ ba baNijy prodorrSonI ayOjoner onurOdh janan. bOIThok SeShe kanaDar haikomiSonar coTTogramer bivinn bybosa O SilpoprotiShThan poridorrSon koren. ghaT Sromikoder korrmobirotite poNy khalas bondh coTTogram bondore ghaT Sromikoder korrmobirotir karoNe aj moNggolobar sokal aToTa theke korrNofulI nodIr 15Ti besorokari ghaTe poNy khalas bondh royeche. mojuri brriddhisoh noy dofa dabite Sromikera e korrmobiroti palon 
korochen. coTTogram ghaT O gudam Sromik songgram poriShoder byanare e korrmobiroti coloche. songgoThoner sovapoti alomogIr SorIf dabi aday na hoOya porrynt korrmobiroti caliye zaOyar ghOShoNa diyechen. bondorer bohirrnONgore obostharorot boR jahaj theke chOT jahaje poNy bOjhai kore ene esob ghaTe khalas kora hoy. e elakay mOT 16Ti ghaT ebong poNy khalaser jony 15Ti chOT jahaj ache. esob ghaTe sadharoNot dine sat hajar theke aT hajar Ton poNy khalas hoy. zOgazOg kora hole poNy khalaser Thikadar abul haSem boleno, amodanikarokera Taka beSi na dile Sromikoder beSi Taka deOya somvob na. bondorer pailoT bOTer dhakka Tyangkar fuTO hoye nodIte vOjytel coTTogram bondorer 
pailoT bOTer dhakkay gotokal telobahI ekoTi Tyangkar fuTO hoye gele er vOjytel korrNofulI nodIte choRiye poRe. kichu SiSu sei tel songgroher ceShTa koroche coTTogram bondorer pailoT bOTer dhakkay ekoTi Tyangkar fuTO hoye korrNofulI nodIte vOjytel choRiye poReche. gotokal sOmobar bela sOya 11Tar dike e ghoTona ghoTe. bondor O songSliShT sUtr janayo, gotokal bondorer 8 nomwr rivar muringye emoTi jaka namer ekoTi chOT akarer Tyangkar theke oporiSOdhit soyabin tel khalas kore mesarrs be-ofiSing koropOreSoner Tarrminale rakha hocchil. bela sOya 11Tar dike hoThat'' kore bondorer pailoT bOT telobahI TyangkaroTike dhakka dey. e somoy Tyangkarer paSe fuTO hoye oporiSOdhit soyabin nodIte choRiye poRe. 
durrghoTonar por sthanIy lOkojon panir Opor theke vOjytel songgroh kore ney. er poroO jOyaro-ovaTar Tane ei tel korrNofulI nodIte choRiye poRe. bondorer uposongrokShok kyapTen najomul alom prothom alOke boleno, durrghoTonar por choRiye poRa vOjyteler beSir vagoi nodI theke tule neOya hoyeche. tini janano, durrghoTonar karoN khotiye dekhote ek sodosyer todont komiTi goThon kora hoyeche. ghoTonar por poribeS odhidoptorer poricalok jafor alom O poridorrSok saiful aSrab ghoTonasthol poridorrSon koren. e somoy vOjytelomiSrit panir nomuna songgroh kora hoy. e biShoye poridorrSok saiful aSrab boleno, anumanik 40 theke 50 Ton vOjytel panite miSrit hoyeche. panir nomuna porIkShar por dUShoNer matra nirrdharoN kore e 
biShoye podokShep neOya hobe. vOjytel amodanikarok Ti ke gruper bybosthapona poricalok em e kalam boleno, Tyangkar theke vOjytel khalas SeSh hoOyar por jana zabe, kI porimaN vOjytel nodIte poReche. montrisovay ainer khosoRa onumOdon Sromik kolyaNe munafar 5 SotangS deOya badhytamUlok hocche Silpokarokhanay barrShik orrjit munafar 5 SotangS orrth Sromik kolyaN tohobile joma deOya badhytamUlok kora hocche. ei niyom loNgghone Sastir bidhanoO rakha hoyeche. e-osongkrant bangladeS Sromik kolyaN faunDeSon (osongSOdhono) aino, 20o12-oer khosoRa gotokal sOmobar montrisovar bOIThoke nItigot onumOdon deOya hoyeche. e chaRa montrisova sorokari korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIder cakorir boyososIma dui bochor baRanO-osongkrant ain onumOdon diyeche. bOIThok SeShe montriporiShod socib mOSarorof hOsain vU^iya 
songbad brifingye esob tothy janan. socibaloye ei bOIThoke sovapotitw koren prodhanomontrI Sekh hasina. montriporiShod socib boleno, orrjit munafar ekoTi ongS Sromikoder jony rakhote âobangladeS Sromik kolyaN faunDeSon ainoâ royeche. kintu tohobile orrth joma na dile Sastir bidhan na thakay malikera ta bastobayon korochilen na. tai ainoTi songSOdhon kore Sastir bidhan zukt kora hoyeche. tini boleno, kI Sasti hobe, ta montrisovar bOIThoke nirrdharoN kora hoyoni. eTi nirrdharoN kore motamotosoh khosoRa montrisovay uposthapon korote ain montroNaloyoke dayitw deOya hoyeche. tader motamotosoh prostab pelei ainoTi paser jony jatIy songsode paThate montrisova cURant onumOdon debe. gotokaler bOIThoke âobangladeS sorokari korrmocarI (oobosoro) (osongSOdhono) aino, 20o12âo-oer 
khosoRaO onumOdon deOya hoy. e songSOdhonI karrykor hole sorokari korrmocarIder obosorer boyososIma dui bochor baRiye 59 bochor kora-osongkrant raShTropotir odhyadeSoTi aine poriNot hobe. montriporiShod socib boleno, bOIThoke e porrynt jari hoOya sob odhyadeS drutotar soNgge aine poriNot korar udyOg nite prodhanomontrI songSliShToder nirrdeS diyechen. muktizOddha kOTay dui bochorer borrdhit meyade korrmorot sorokari korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIder obosorer boyososIma onyder motO aroO dui bochor baRanO hobe ki na, janote caile tini boleno, montrisovay e biShoye kOnO alOcona hoyoni. bOIThoke turosker dUtabaser jony rajodhanIr baridharay car hajar 741 borrgomiTar jomi 99 bochorer jony lij onumOdon deOya hoy. ekoi porimaN jomi turosker rajodhanI aNgkaray bangladeS dUtabasoke 
99 bochorer jony lij deOya hoyeche. e jony turosker soNgge dUtabaser jomi binimoyo-osongkrant proTOkol onusomorrthoner biShoyeO onumOdon deOya hoy. montriporiShod socib janano, montrisovay got tin bochore neOya bivinn siddhant O tar bastobayon ebong pUrrwborrtI sorokarer prothom tin bochorer siddhant O bastobayoner tulonamUlok citr tule dhora hoy. ete dekha zayo, borrtoman sorokarer siddhant grohoN O bastobayoner har onek egiye. Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sovapoti Sakil rijovI boleno, ajoker bOIThoke byangkogulOr Seyarobajare biniyOgo, goNomadhym nItimala, aipiO, plesomenT O bajarer gujob niye alOcona hoyeche. tini aroO boleno, kOnO dhoroner gujober madhyme keu zate bajare provabit korote na pare, se byapare esoisike nojor rakhote bola hoyeche. e chaRa kOnO kOmpani tader ipieser kShetre sotyikarer ghOShoNa dicche ki na, se byapare dui sTok eksoceNGj O esoisi kheyal rakhobe. coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sovapoti alo-omaruf khan boleno, bOIThoke bideSi biniyOg bangladeSer Seyarobajare asar byapare alOcona hoyeche. e chaRa inosaiDar TreDing, poramorrS seba, dui sTok eksoceNGjer sUcok O gujober biShoy niyeO alOcona hoyeche. tini aroO

vobon podmay bajarosongSliShT sobaike niye uccoporryayer bOIThok koren. hobe bole amora mone kori.â er age baNijyik byangkogulOr jony ekoi dhoroner suzOg deya hoy. dabi adaye sera krriShoko-ogobeShokoder niye komiTi goThit krriShokoder dabi adayer jony rajoSahIte jatIy swrrNopodokoprapt SreShTh krriShoko, songgoThok O krriShi gobeShokoder niye 10o1 sodosyer ekoTi komiTi goThon kora hoyeche. nogorer Syamopur elakar ekoTi proSikShoN kendre got sOmobar bangladeS farrmaros oyasOsiyeSon ayOjit ek sommelone e komiTi ghOShoNa kora hoy. ete Sahojahan alI badoSake sovapoti, abodul bachit selimoke sadharoN sompadok O siddikur rohoman moyejoke sanggoThonik sompadok kora hoyeche. sommelone deSer 20oTi jelar 72 jon SreShTh krriShoko, 10 jon krriShi gobeShoko, pa^cojon krriShibid O 15 jon krriShok songgoThok uposthit 
chilen. sommelone sovapotitw koren bangladeS farrmaros oyasOsiyeSoner ahwayok Sahojahan alI badoSa Orofe pe^pe badoSa. ete onyanyer modhye boktoby den siddikur rohoman moyejo, abodul bachit selimo, odhyapok em monojur hOseno, abodul kadero, abodul jolil kitabo, jahidul isolamo, abodul barI, alI ajogor morrtuja, biai siddikI, odhyapok abodur rohimo, krriShok songgoThok aiyub hOsen O belI begom. sommelon theke sorokarer kache krriShokoder ut''padit poNyer nyazymUly niScitokoroNer dabi jananO hoy. zomuna sar karokhanay korrmobiroti, dui ghoNTa sar poribohon bondh jamalopurer soriShabaRIr zomuna sar karokhana kOmpani limiTeDer (ojeefosielo) Sromiko-okorrmocarI iuniyon mojuri komiSon bastobayoner dabite gotokal moNggolobar sokal noyoTa theke 11Ta porrynt korrmobiroti palon koreche. ete karokhanaTi 
theke dui ghoNTa sar poribohon bondh chil. Sromiko-okorrmocarI iuniyon jeefosieler proSasonik voboner samone korrmobiroti palon SeShe sekhane sova kore. ete boktoby den iuniyoner sohosovapoti raSedul hoko, krIRa sompadok kholilur rohomano, muktizOddha Sohidur rohoman promukh. sovay bola hoyo, 20o0o9 saler 1 julai theke mojuri komiSon bastobayon kore protyek Sromiker mUl mojurir soNgge 20o% moharrgh vata dite hobe. Sromiko-okorrmocarI iuniyoner sadharoN sompadok motiyar rohoman janano, jatIy mojuri komiSoner supariSokrrit mojuri bastobayon kora na hole koThOr andOloner madhyme karokhanar ut''padon bondh kore deOya hobe. e byapare jeefosieler bybosthapona poricalok ocinty kumar deb prothom alOke janano, Sromiko-okorrmocarIra dui ghoNTa korrmobiroti palon koray Oi somoye 
sar poribohon bondh chil. bangladeSoke niye jolobidyut'' kendr sthapone agrohI nepal bangladeSer soNgge zOUthovabe tin hajar megaOyaT kShomotasomponn jolobidyut''kendr sthapone agrohI nepal. TranojiTer aOtay deSoTi mongla bondoroO bybohar korote cay. socibaloye gotokal moNggolobar orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhiter soNgge sakShat'' kore nepali orrthomontrI borrSha man pun e duTi prostab den. bOIThoker por muhit sangbadikoder esob kotha janan. tini boleno, jolobidyut'' ut''padoner jony himaloyokonya nepal biSal somvabonamoy ek deS. kintu biniyOger ovabe deSoTi e byapare temon kichui korote paroche na. nepal cayo, mUlodhoni ongSIdarer (oikyuiTi parrTonaro) vittite dui deS mile ekoTi jolobidyut''kendr sthapit hOk. ut''padit bidyut'' vagavagi hobe uvoy deSer modhye. 
Sudhu nepal noyo, vuTaner soNggeO ekoi poddhotite bidyut''kendr sthaponer kotha cinta kora hocche boleO janan muhit. orrthomontrI boleno, nepalo, varot O vuTaner soNgge TranojiT prosoNggo; bonyaniyontroN ba^dh nirrmaN ebong panisompod unnoyoner byapare nepali orrthomontrIr soNgge alOcona hoyeche. orrthomontrI aroO boleno, âonepal amader mongla bondor bybohar korote cay. bondor porrynt tader Trak asobe. amoraO cai asuk. kintu majhokhane varoter 17 kilOmiTar rastar obokaThamO tot valO noy.â nepaler soNgge dwipokShIy baNijy baRanOr lokShye Sigogir zOUth orrthonOItik komiSoner (ojeisi) ekoTi bOIThok Daka hobe bole janan orrthomontrI. tini boleno, âodeSoTir soNgge baNijy brriddhir somvabona ebong er pechoner ontorayogulO khotiye dekhote baNijysocib Sigogiroi nepal zaben.â 
TranojiT calur kotha royecheâoemon sob deSei kOr komiTir protibedonoTi paThanO hobe. aro, sobokichu ThikoThak kora hobe deSogulOr soNgge alOconar madhyme. orrthomontrI boleno, âoagamI marrce varoter soNgge TranojiTo-osongkrant nOU-oproTOkoler meyad SeSh hocche. tar agei TranojiT maSul cURant korote cai. er modhye zodi cURant siddhante na asa zayo, tahole nOU-oproTOkol borrtomane za ache, ta-oi thakobe. ek proSner jobabe TranojiT biShoye goThit kOr komiTir supariSer vittite maSul (ofi) nirrdharoN kora hobe bole ullekh koren orrthomontrI. tini boleno, ei maSul emonovabe nirrdharit hoOya ucito, zate sob deSoi lavoban hoy. orrthomontrI boleno, apelosoh kichu fol ebong krriShijat poNye Sulk chaR pete cay nepal. nepaler orrthomontrI 
mOUkhikovabe ta^ke bolechen. bangladeSer pokSh theke vuTaner jony itimodhyei kichu Sulk chaR deOya hoyeche. nepaler kShetreO ta-oi hote pare. anuShThanikovabe varotIy sonod pel biesoTiai bangladeS sTyanDarrDos oyanD TesTing inosTiTiuToke (obiesoTiai) anuShThanikovabe oyakriDiTeSon sonod diyeche varoter nyaSonal oyakriDiTeSon bOrrD for sarrTifikeSon boDis (oenoebisibi). sarrkovukt deSogulOr modhye bangladeSoi prothom ei sonod pel. biesoTiai mone koroche, ei sonod paOyar modhy diye bangladeSi poNyer antorrjatik grohoNozOgytar suzOg somprosarit hobe. rajodhanIr tejoga^Oye biesoTiaiyer karryaloye gotokal moNggolobar biesoTiaiyer mohaporicalok e ke fojolul ahader hate oyakriDiTeSon sonod tule den enoebisibir prodhan nirrwahI bi veNgkaTaraman. e somoy uposthit chilen bangladeS oyakriDiTeSon bOrrDer mohaporicalok mO. abu abodullah. biesoTiai theke 
paThanO ek bijNGoptite e tothy jananO hoy. mohaporicalok aroO janano, biesoTiaiyer rosayono, khady, maikrObayOloji, simenT ebong TeksoTail TesTing porIkShagulO got bochorer 18 marrc varoter nyaSonal oyakriDiTeSon bOrrD for TesTing lyaboreTorijer (oenoebielo) oyakriDiTeSon orrjon kore. ta chaRa biesoTiaiyer bybosthapona poddhoti noroOyer noroOyejiyan oyakriDiTeSon boDir oyakriDiTeSon sonodoO lav koreche. biesoTiai korrtrripokSh janayo, porIkSha-onirIkShar nana dhap periye prathomikovabe biesoTiaike pa^coTi khadypoNyer kShetre tin bochorer jony orrthat'' e bochorer 9 januyari theke 20o15 saler 8 januyari porrynt somoyer jony ei sonod deOya hoy. porryayokrome biesoTiai sotyayit sob poNyi enoebisibir swIkrriti pabe. 8 mase 266 kOTi Taka ay theke boNGcit inokaming koler dam baRanOr sufol 
pacche na biTiarosi bideS theke asa koler dam (oinokaming koler TarrmineSon reTo) baRanOr sufol pacche na sorokari protiShThan bangladeS TelizOgazOg niyontroN komiSon (obiTiarosi). er karoN damer borrdhit ongS vagavagir bybostha na rakha. ete protiShThanoTi got aT mase 265 kOTi 73 lakh 24 hajar 60o2 Taka ay theke boNGcit hoyeche. biTiarosi sUtr janayo, protiShThanoTi got bochorer 23 me ek adeSe inokaming koler dam proti miniT tin senT theke baRiye tin doSomik 45 senT kore. tobe adeSe bola hoyo, rajosw vagavagi miniToproti tin senTer Opor hobe. othoc inTaronyaSonal long DisoTyans TelikomiunikeSon sarrviser (oaieloDiTieso) nItimala onuzayI, inTaronyaSonal geToOye (oaijiDobliu) protiShThanogulO tader rajosw ay 
theke sorokaroke 51 doSomik 75 SotangSo, ekses neToOyarrk sarrvisoke (oeenoeso) 20 SotangS ebong inTarokanekoSon eksoceNGjoke (oaisiekso) 15 SotangS debe. bakiTa aijiDobliur. kintu 23 mer adeSer fole miniToproti baRoti SUny doSomik SUny 45 senTer purOTai pacche caroTi aijiDobliu protiShThan. egulO holO: novOTelo, mIr Telikomo, bangla Trryak komiunikeSons ebong sorokari protiShThan bangladeS TelikomiunikeSons kOmpani limiTeD (obiTisielo). ony geToOye opareTor orrthat'' eenoes O aisieksoO tader ayer ekoTi ongS biTiarosike dey. dam brriddhir fole baRoti ay vagavagir bybostha na rakhay biTiarosir motO eenoes O aisieksoO er vag pacche na. biTiarosir hisabe, bideS theke dOInik goRe pa^c kOTi miniT inokaming kol ase. ager dam onuzayI 
proti miniTer jony aijiDobliu protiShThanogulOr ay dui Taka 89 poyosa (otin senTo). er modhye aijiDobliu protiShThan 38 poyosa rekhe baki dui Taka 51 poyosa har onuzayI sorokaro, eenoes O aisieksoke dit. koler dam baRanOy aijiDobliu protiShThanogulOr dine baRoti ek kOTi 88 lakh 32 hajar 50o0 Taka ay holeO ta vag hocche na. e biShoye mIr Telikomer bybosthapona poricalok O efobisisiair sabek sovapoti mIr nasir hOsen prothom alOke boleno, âoet din kol miniToproti tin senT thakay amora aijiDobliu protiShThanogulO onek lOkosane chilam. ekhon za^ra baRoti SUny doSomik 45 senT niye ovizOg korochen ta Thik noy ba ta^ra e kShetre karigori biShoye 
kichui bOjhen na.â biTiarosi sUtr janayo, baRoti ei ayoO vagavagi hole aijiDobliu theke protidin biTiarosi aroO 97 lakh 45 hajar 819 Taka, eenoes opareTor 37 lakh 66 hajar 50o0 Taka ebong aisieks opareTor 28 lakh 24 hajar 875 Taka baRoti pet. eenoes Oi ay theke biTiarosike dine dui lakh sat hajar 158 Taka ebong aisieks opareTor 18 lakh 57 hajar 355 Taka dit. sob miliye dine biTiarosir baRoti ay hotO ek kOTi 18 lakh 10 hajar 332 Taka. ei hisabe 23 me theke coloti bochorer 9 januyari porrynt biTiarosi 265 kOTi 73 lakh 24 hajar 60o2 Taka baRoti ay theke 
boNGcit hoyeche. 23 mer adeSer biShoye biTiarosir ceyaromyan jiya ahomed boleno, âoeTi biTiarosi noyo, Dak O TelizOgazOg montroNaloyer supariSe kora hoyeche. biTiarosir pokSh theke Sudhu aijiDobliur Tyarifer sIma baRanOr prostab kora hoy. kintu rajosw vagavagir biShoyoTi Thik kore ciThi diyeche montroNaloy.â Dak O TelizOgazOg montroNaloyo-osomporrkit songsodIy komiTir sovapoti hasanul hok inu boleno, âohoThat'' kore inokaming koler Tyarif baRanO ebong baRoti Tyarif theke rajosw vagavagi na hoOya niye biTiarosi O songSliShT montroNaloyer kache jobab caOya hoyeche. tader protibedon na paOya porrynt e biShoye kichu bola zabe na.â orrthonItir kalO chaya orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit jatIy songsode gotokal moNggolobar bolecheno, âoamora 
protiniyot orrthonItir ekoTi kalO chayar modhye royechi.â orrthonItir ei kalO chayar biboroN diyechen bybosayIder SIrrSh songgoThon efobisisiaiyer sovapoti e ke ajad. gotokaloi arekoTi onuShThane tini bolecheno, cahidanuzayI gyas O bidyut'' na paOyay ebong byangker ucc suder karoNe bybosayIra niShpeShit hocchen. er soNgge notun matra zOg hoyecheâorajonOItik osthitiSIlota. sthitiSIlota na anote parole biniyOg bighnit hobe, orrthonIti songkoTe poRobe. tobe er palTa boktoby diye baNijymontrI gOlam mOhammod kader boleno, rajonOItik osthirotar jony orrthonIti songkoTe poRobe na. borong orrthonItite osthirota dekha dile rajonItite songkoT baRobe. tini oboSy rajonOItik kShetre kichuTa osthirota ache swIkar kore niye bolecheno, prrithibIr kOnO deSei rajonOItik osthirotar karoNe orrthonIti 
songkoTe poRar nojir nei. gotokal moNggolobar bikele masobyapI Dhaka antorrjatik baNijy melar somaponI onuShThane baNijymontrI O efobisisiaiyer sovapoti esob kotha bolen. ar songsode proSnOttor porrwe orrthomontrI boleno, deSer orrthonItite mUl somosya bOIdeSik biniyOger ovabo, mUlysfIti ebong odhik hare vorrtuki deOya. tini e somoy bOISwik orrthonItir monda theke rehai paOyar kotha bololeO borrtomaner kichu somosyar kotha janan. deSer orrthonItir ei caper kotha sorokar et din swIkar na koroleO ekhon bivinn onuShThane montrIra songkoTer kotha bolochen. paSapaSi hoThat'' kore rajonOItik osthirota Suru hole notun kore udwign hoye poRechen bybosayIra. ei udweger kotha janiye mela praNggoNe onuShThit sovay efobisisiaiyer sovapoti boleno, protidin potrikar 
patay laSer chobi chapa hole bideSer goNomadhymeO ta folaO kore chapa hoy. ete bideSer biniyOgokarIra nirut''sahit hon. emonoki bideSi kretara somoyomotO poNy paben ki na, sei biShoye duScintay thaken. e ke ajad aroO boleno, iurOp O amerikay monda coloche. tar poroO got bochor dui hajar tin kOTi Dolar roptani ay hoyeche. aSa korochi, e bochor dui hajar choy kOTi Dolar roptani ayer lokShymatra orrjit hobe. bideSe bangladeSer poNy somadrrit hocche. emonoTi colole pa^co-ochoy bochore amader roptani ay pa^c hajar theke choy hajar kOTi Dolare da^Rabe. edike gotokal songsode ekoTi sompUrok proSner jobabe orrthomontrI boleno, bOIdeSik mudrar mojud cheRe diye bajaroke 
provabit kora Thik noy. karoNo, mojud beSi kome gele orrthonOItik sthitiSIlota niye proSn dekha dey. mojud ba rijarrv dhore rakhole ocirei mudrabajare sthitiSIlota asobe. bajare bOIdeSik mudrar rijarrv theke Dolar cheRe deOyar proSn kora hole orrthomontrI e kotha janan. arekoTi sompUrok proSner jobabe orrthomontrI boleno, sorokarer lokShy chil amodani komiye ana. kintu amodani beRe geche. za mudrabajarer Opor provab feleche. arek sompUrok proSner jobabe orrthomontrI boleno, ekhon somosya hocche vorrtuki dite hocche ebong sorokar cahidamafik bOIdeSik biniyOg pacche na. orrthomontrI soboSeShe aSar baNI Suniye nObel bijoyI OyalTar luiser ekoTi boktoby uddhrrit kore boleno, ze deS Tana 10 bochor krriShi kShetre 
4 SotangS probrriddhi dhore rakhote pare, se deSer cintar kichu nei. amader krriShite probrriddhi 4 SotangS. bidyuter somosya thakoleO Silp khate 10 SotangS probrriddhi hoyeche. cintar biShoy hocche kebol bOIdeSik biniyOg O vorrtuki. ekhonO uttoroNer poth khu^joche esoisi Seyarobajarer coloman songkoT O ta theke uttoroNer upay khu^jote abaroO songSliShT sob pokShoke niye pray aRai ghoNTa bOIThok korol sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSon (oesoisi). bOIThok SeShe bajare sthitiSIlota firiye anar motO sunirrdiShT podokSheper kotha janate pareni esoisi. bOIThok SeShe esoisir nirrwahI poricalok O mukhopatr saifur rohoman janiyecheno, alOconar madhyme songkoT ba somosya somadhaner upay khO^ja hocche. bajarer coloman songkoTer jony kI kI 
somosya cihnit kora hoyeche ar ta somadhaner podokShep niye sangbadikera janote caile tini boleno, ajoker (ogotokalo) alOconar madhyme tinoTi prodhan somosya cihnit kora hoyeche. segulO holOâogujobo, astha O tarolysongkoT. tini boleno, âobajarer borrtoman obostha zemon ekodine tOIri hoyoni, temoni ekodinei e obosthar uttoroN somvob noy.â edike esoisir ei bOIThokoke ghire got dui dine deSer dui sTok eksoceNGje mUlysUcoker boR dhoroner utthano-opoton ghoTeche. sOmobar bOIThoker khobore Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) mUlysUcok 10o3 poyenT beRechil. ar gotokal bOIThok SeSher ek ghoNTar doropotone Diesoir sadharoN sUcok komeche 132 poyenTeroO beSi. orrthat'' bOIThoker khobore sUcoker zotoTa utthan ghoTechilo, bOIThok SeShe tar ceye beSi poton 
ghoTeche. er age gotokal bela saRe 11Ta theke bela duiTa porrynt songSliShT bivinn pokSher soNgge bajarer poristhiti niye alOcona kore esoisi. tate uposthit sobai nij nij obosthane theke ta^der boktoby tule dhoren. jana zayo, bOIThoke talikavukt kOmpanir udyOkta-oporicalokoder nyUnotom Seyar dharoNer biShoye alOcona hoy. e biShoye esoisi tader nijosw obosthan uposthit sobar samone tule dhore bole, kOnO obosthatei ei nirrdeSona poriborrton kora hobe na. emonoki nyUnotom Seyar dharoNer jony ze somoyosIma be^dhe deOya hoyeche, taroO kOnO poriborrton ghoTobe na. paSapaSi agamI 1 marrc theke dui sTok eksoceNGje Sudhu lenodenozOgy Seyarer vittite notun mUlysUcok calur biShoye alOcona hoy. e kShetre dui 
sTok eksoceNGjoke prostuti neOyar jonyO esoisir pokSh theke bola hoy. bOIThok SeShe songbad sommelone inovesTomenT koropOreSon ob bangladeSer (oaisibi) bybosthapona poricalok mOhammod fayekujjaman boleno, 1996 sale Diesoir sUcok 360o0 poyenT theke kome 40o0 poyenTe nemechil. ebar ontot se dhoroner poristhiti ThekanO geche. borrtomane Seyarer dor onek nice neme eseche. Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI boleno, gujob choRiye keu zate bajaroke provabit korote na pare ebong kOmpanigulOr somproti prokaSit arrthik biboroNIr proti esoisike biSeShovabe nojor rakhar poramorrS deOya hoyeche. coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sovapoti al maruf khan boleno, tarolysongkoT Seyarobajare somosya tOIri koroche. bangladeS marrcenT byangkarrs oyasOsiyeSoner (obiemobie) sovapoti muhammod e hafij 
boleno, âoamora bolechi bajar niye sorokari bykti O protiShThan kOnO montoby korote caile ta zen esoisir soNgge alOcona kore kora hoy.â oyasOsiyeSon ob byangkarrso, bangladeSer (oebibi) sovapoti mO. nurul amin boleno, sob byangkoi Seyar kena obyahot rekheche. prodhanomontrIr kache podma setu tOIrir prostab maloyeSiyar maloyeSiya sorokar podma setu prokolpe pUrrN orrthayonosoh setu nirrmaNer prostab diyeche. maloyeSiyar prodhanomontrIr obokaThamObiShoyok biSeSh dUt (ovarot O dokShiN eSiya) datO seri es sami vellu gotokal moNggolobar sokale prodhanomontrI Sekh hasinar soNgge ta^r karryaloye sakShat''kale e prostab den. bOIThoke dwipokShIy swarrthosongSliShT bivinn biShoy sthan pay. khobor basoser. bOIThoke onyanyer modhye prodhanomontrIr biSeSh dUt em jiyauddino, mukhy 
socib mO. Oyahedujjamano, Dhakay maloyeSiyar haikomiSonar jamal uddin bin sahebo, setu bivager socib anoOyarul isolam O prodhanomontrIr pres socib abul kalam ajad uposthit chilen. er age got sOmobar maloyeSiyar biSeSh dUt zOgazOgomontrI Obayodul kaderer soNgge ta^r karryaloye sakShat'' kore anuShThanikovabe podma setu nirrmaNe orrthayoner prostab den. tini prostabosongbolit ekoTi ciThi montrIr hate tule den. e chaRa dokShiN kOriya, indOneSiya, cInosoh bivinn deSer kOmpani 297 kOTi marrkin Dolarer ei biSal prokolpe orrthayone agroh dekhiyeche. biSwbyangker kothit durrnItir ovizOge pa^c mas age prokolper kaj sthogit hoye zay. eropor setuTi nirrmaNe maloyeSiyai prothom anuShThanik prostab dil. biSwbyangk got agosTe durrnItir ovizOg ene podma 
setu prokolper sohayota sthogit kore. tobe sorokar ei ovizOg nakoc kore dey. somproti biSwbyangker rriNer somoyosIma choy mas baRanO hoyeche. lOna pani tule cingRir caSh obOIdh deSer upokUlIy jelagulOte krriShi O bonovUmite jOropUrrwk lOna pani tule cingRir caSh obOIdh ghOShoNa kore ray diyechen haikOrrT. aj budhobar bicaropoti e eic em Samosuddin cOUdhurI O bicaropoti jahaNggIr hOsener somonwye goThit haikOrrT beNGc e ray den. adalot ekoi soNgge krriShi O bonovUmite jOropUrrwk lOna pani uttOlon bondhe karrykor podokShep nite nirrdeS diyechen. deSer upokUlIy jelagulOte jOropUrrwk lOna pani tule baNijyikovabe cingRir caSh rOdhe 20o10 saler 10 januyari riT abedon kore bangladeS poribeS ainobid 
somiti O besorokari unnoyon songstha âonijera koriâ . prathomik Sunani niye adalot rul jari koren. ekoi bochorer 15 februyari adalot ek adeSe krriShi O bonovUmite jOropUrrwk lOna pani tule cingRir caSh kora theke birot thakar nirrdeS den. ruler Opor cURant Sunani SeShe aj adalot ray den. adalote riT abedoner pokShe sOIyoda rijoOyana hasan O ikobal kobir Sunani koren. vUmi montroNaloyer pokShe monojil mOrosedo, pani unnoyon bOrrDer pokShe delOyar hOsen O motsy montroNaloyer pokShe DepuTi oyaTorrni jenarel e bi em alotaf hOsen chilen. pore ikobal kobir prothom alO onolainoke boleno, adalot vUmi montroNaloyo, upokUlIy jelagulOr jela proSasokosoh songSliShT korrtrripokShoke krriShi O 
bonovUmite jOropUrrwk lOna pani tule cingRir caSh bondhe bybostha nite boleche. bajar poristhiti nizo09BCe Diesoi-osiesoi bOIThok borrtoman pu^jibajar poristhiti nizo09BCe bOIThok koreche Dhaka sTok eksoceNGj (oDiesoi) O coTTogram sTok eksoceNGje (osiesoi) korrtrripokSh. aj sOmobar bikele Diesoir sovakokShe ei bOIThok onuShThit hozo09BC. bOIThoke bidyman suder haro, marrkeT mekarer prozo09BCOjonIzo09BCota, miucuzo09BCal fanDer karrykorI vUmika, rriN somonwzo09BCo, arrthik biboroNIr swcchotar biShozo09BC nizo09BCe alOcona hozo09BC. e somozo09BC DrafoT fainyansizo09BCal ripOrrTing oyakT drut aine karrykor korar byapareO ekomot hozo09BC sTok eksoceNGj duTi. e sob prostab bastobazo09BConer lokShe bOrrDer somonwzo09BCe ekoTi komiTi O myanejomenTer somonwzo09BCe arekoTi komiTi goThoner biShozo09BCe dui sTok eksoceNGj sommot hozo09BC.
