Sakil rijovI O siesoir sovapoti alo-omaruf khanosoh dui sTok eksoceNGjer poricalona porrShoder sodosyra bOIThoke uposthit chilen. Diesoir ek pres bijNGoptite e tothy jananO hozo09BC. boR doropotone nana proSn deSer Seyarobajarer biniyOgokarIra gotokal rObobar arekoTi boR dhoroner doropoton dekholen. zodiO beS kichudin dhore bajare Tana doropoton cole asoche. tobe gotokaler doropotonoTi chil samprotik somoyer modhye soboceye boR. tobe byapok doropoton holeO rajodhanIr motijhile Diesoi voboner samone kOnO dhoroner bikShOver ghoTona ghoTeni. sokal thekei Oi elakay otirikt puliSi nirapotta chil. keu joRO hoOyar ceShTa korolei puliS tader soriye dey. bajarosongSliShT byktira bolocheno, gotokaler ei doropoton chil onekangSe oprotyaSit O onakaNgkShit. er sunirrdiShT 
karoNoO keu janate parenoni. tobe keu keu gotokaler ei potoner jony rajonOItik osthirotake dayI korechen. palTapalTi rajonOItik korrmosUcir karoNe gotokal rajodhanIsoh bivagIy SohorogulOte sova-osomabeSer Opor niShedhajNGa arOp kora hoy. zOgazOg kora hole sabek tottwabodhayok sorokarer upodeShTa O sikiuriTij oyanD eksoceNGj komiSoner (oesoisi) sabek ceyaromyan mirrjja ajijul isolam prothom alOke boleno, âodoropotoner pechone zOUktik kOnO karoN nei. biniyOgokarIder modhye vIti ba atoNgk tOIri hoOyar motO kOnO poristhiti tOIri hoyoni. tai amar kache doropotonoTike ozOUktikoi mone hocche.â rajonOItik osthirotaO bajarer Opor netibacok provab feleche bole mone koren na mirrjja ajij. tini boleno, âoami mone kori na, rajonOItik osthirota e dhoroner doropotoner kOnO 
karoN. er age 20o0o6 saler SeShodike deSe zokhon rajonOItik sohingsota colochilo, tokhonO e dhoroner doropoton ghoTeni.â Diesoir bajar tothy porryalOconay dekha zayo, gotokal talikavukt boR mUlodhon O valO mOUlovittir kOmpanigulOr Seyareroi beSi doropoton ghoTeche. sei tulonay kom mOUlovitti ba durrwl mOUlovittisomponn kOmpanigulOr doropotoner har ba matra kom chil. Diesoir hisab onuzayI, bajarer protidiner sUcoker utthano-opotone boR vUmika rakhe boR mUlodhoner kOmpanigulO. esob kOmpanir Seyarer dam baRa-okoma sUcokoke provabit kore. esob Seyarer beSir vagoi gotokal dam komar sorrwnimn store (osarrkiT brekaro) lenoden hoy. songSliShT byktira janano, diner Surute esob Seyarer dam ullekhozOgy hare kome gele tate sUcok potonomukhI hoy. tai keu 
keu mone korocheno, biniyOgokarIder modhye atoNgk srriShTi korote lenodener Surute boR mUlodhoner kOmpanigulOr Seyarer damoke sorrwnimn store namiye deOyar kShetre porikolpit kOnO karosajir ghoTonaO ghoTe thakote pare. biShoyoTi todonter jony songSliShT byktira esoisir proti ahwan janiyechen. e biShoye mirrjja ajij boleno, âoboR mUlodhon O mOUlovittir kOmpanigulOr modhye beS koyekoTir mUly-oayer onupat (opii reSiO) akorrShoNIy porryaye neme eseche. e obosthay esob kOmpanir Seyarer byapok doropotoner zOUktik kOnO karoN thakote pare na.â mirrjja ajij aroO boleno, boR bajar mUlodhoner kOmpanigulOr Seyarer ken byapok doropoton ghoTol ebong er soNgge kOmpanir poricalokoder Seyar kena ba ony kOnO karosajir ghoTona royeche ki na, seTi valOvabe 
khotiye dekha dorokar. japaner niT pOSaker bajare probeSe bangladeSer aSabad baNijymontrI ji em kader bolecheno, japaner biSal bajare probeSer sob rokom pUrrwSorrt ekhon bangladeS pUroN korote sokShom. se jony tini japani amodanikarokoder bangladeSe giye niT pOSakoSilper borrtoman poristhiti porrybekShoNer onurOdh janiyechen. japaner rajodhanI TOkiOr prodorrSonIkendr bigosaiTe onuShThit antorrjatik fyaSon SOr dwitIy dine got brrihospotibar bangladeS dUtabas ayOjit ek songbad sommelone tini ei onurOdh janan. songbad sommelone aroO boktoby den roptani unnoyon byurOr (oipibi) vaiso-oceyaromyan SuvaSISh bosu O bangladeSer niT pOSakomalikoder songgoThon bikeemoier sohosovapoti (oorrtho) asolam sani. ta^ra bangladeSer niToOyyaroSilper borrtoman obostha O roptanicitr tule dhoren ebong japane bajar somprosaroNe sohayota 
korar jony japani songbadomadhymer proti ahwan janan. ji em kader aSa prokaS kore boleno, japan protibochor ze deR hajar kOTi marrkin Dolar mUlyer niT pOSak ba boyonobostr amodani koroche, tate bangladeS vobiShyte ongSIdari baRate sokShom hobe. ullekhy, japaner niT pOSak amodani khate ekhon porrynt bangladeSer ongSIdari ek SotangSeroO kom. TOkiO antorrjatik fyaSon SO got Sukrobar SeSh hoy. ebarer prodorrSonIte bangladeSer 38Ti buth chil. ete zOg dite deS theke mOT 140 jon protinidhi japane asen. sorokari protinidhidoler netrritw den baNijymontrI ji em kader. ar bikeemoier protinidhidoler netrritw den songgoThoner sohosovapoti mO. monosur ahomed. coTTogram bondorer Sulkayon kajer somoyosIma baRoche 1 marrc 
theke agamI 1 marrc kingba tar agei coTTogram bondorer kasTomos hauser korrmodibos O korrmoghoNTa baRanO hocche. ekhon theke Sulkayon karrykrom sokal noyoTa theke rat 10oTa porrynt colobe. ar saptahik chuTir din ek din komiye SonibaroO sokal noyoTa theke bikel pa^coTa porrynt Sulkayoner kaj kora zabe. e somoy bivinn byangker songSliShT SakhagulOO khOla thakobe. jatIy rajosw bOrrDer (oenobiaro) ceyaromyan nasir uddin ahomed esob kotha janiyechen. borrtomane coTTogram bondorer kasTom haus Sukr O Sonibar chaRa soptaher baki pa^c din khOla thake sokal noyoTa theke bikel pa^coTa porrynt. rajodhanIr motijhile bangladeS Silp O boNik somiti feDareSoner (oefobisisiai) karryaloye ek alOconay gotokal rObobar tini 
e kotha bolen. sovar ayOjon kore efobisisiai. tobe sovay bybosayIra coTTogram bondorer Sulkayon karrykrom soptaher sat dinoi 24 ghoNTa khOla rakhar ahwan janan. oboSy bybosayIder keu keu mone koreno, ekhonoi 24 ghoNTa e karrykrom khOla rakhar dabiTa uccakaNgkShI. porryayokrome eTi bastobayon kora zete pare. sovar biSeSh otithi enobiarer ceyaromyan nasir uddin ahomed boleno, âobenapOlo-opeTrapOl stholobondore 24 ghoNTa Sulkayon karrykrom calu rakhar udyOg ekhonoi neOya somvob hobe na. eTi karrykor korar motO proyOjonIy subidha hoyotO amader ekhane ache, kintu peTrapOle ekhonO onek durrwlota ache.â sovar prodhan otithi prodhanomontrIr antorrjatikobiShoyok upodeShTa goOhor rijovI e karrykrom somporrke boleno, âozodiO amora coTTogram bondor diye 
e karrykrom Suru korochi, aste aste sob bondore eTi somprosaroN kora hobe. amader lokShy hocche, bochorer 365 dinoi 24 ghoNTa kore bondorer Sulkayon karrykrom poricalona kora. e kShetre dekhote hobe, baNijyik cahida ache ki na. byangkogulO zodi grahok na payo, tahole tara beSi somoy byangk khOla rakhobe na.â prodhanomontrIr karryaloyer ogradhikarer karoNe kasTom hauser korrmodibos baRanOr siddhantoTi drut bastobayit hocche boleO ullekh koren prodhanomontrIr ei upodeShTa. goOhor rijovI boleno, e sorokar otirikt bybosabandhob. sorokar onek kichu korote pare, abar onek kichu korote pare na. se karoNei prodhanomontrI sorokari-obesorokari ongSIdarike (opipipi) gurutw dicchen. sovay efobisisiair sovapoti e ke ajad boleno, âoamora 
sorokarer kach theke nIti-osohayota pacchi na. byangkorriNer sudoharer sIma tule neOya hoyeche. ete orrthonItite ocolabosthar srriShTi hoyeche. eTa bybosabandhob noy.â tini boleno, sorokarer ghaToti puShiye nite bideSi byangk theke rriN neOyar prostab koren. e ke ajad boleno, tin bochor age Dhaka-ocoTTogram mohasoRok car lene unnIt korar kaj Suru hoyeche. eTa ekhonO SeSh hoyoni. kobe ta SeSh hobe, eTa boR proSn. sovay mUl probondhe esiai limiTeDer nirrwahI poricalok mOyallem cOUdhurI boleno, korrmoghoNTa hisab korole coTTogram bondore Sulkayon kaj hoy ekhon bochore mOT 87 din. baki 278 din kaj hoy na. tini boleno, zodi 365 dinoi karrykrom cole, tahole Sudhu coTTogram bondor 
thekei poNy OThanO-onamanO O jahaj nONgor kora babod sorokarer otirikt ay hobe 71 kOTi 50 lakh Taka. ete ekhonokar ceye ek hajar 117Ti jahaj bondore nONgor kora, Trak theke ek kOTi 57 lakh tin hajar 148Ti karrgO OThanO-onamanO ar jahaj theke pa^c lakh 98 hajar 333Ti konoTeinar OThanO-onamanO somvob hobe. efobisisiaiyer jyeShTh sohosovapoti josim uddino, sohosovapoti mOstofa ajad cOUdhurI, coTTogram kasTomer otirikt komiSonar motiur rohoman promukh boktoby den. satoTi bidyut''kendrer prostab kroy komiTite onumOdon 570 megaOyaT kShomotasomponn satoTi bidyut''kendr nirrmaNer sponsor nirrwaconer doroprostab onumOdon koreche sorokari kroyosongkrant montrisova komiTi. bidyut''kendrogulOr beSir vagoi sthapit hobe nirrmaNo, poricalona O malikana (obiOO) vittite.

oyelovittik tinoTi bidyut''kendr sthapon korobe zOUthovabe konosOrrTiyam ob paOyar ob samuda O eesoem kemikyal. esob kendre proti kilOOyaT bidyut'' ut''padone khoroc poRobe 6 doSomik 98 theke 7 doSomik 18 Taka. keranIgoNGje Duyel fuyelovittik bidyut''kendr nirrmaN korobe mOtiyara paOyar pyak konosOrrTiyam limiTeD. e kendre proti kilOOyaT bidyut'' ut''padone khoroc hobe 8 doSomik 98 Taka. misorer miDol isT oyel rifainari theke tin lakh 30 hajar meTrik Ton gyas oyel (oDijelo)o, kuyet peTrOliyam koropOreSon theke pa^c lakh 70 hajar Ton gyas oyel O 90 hajar Ton jeT oyel amodanir primiyam nirrdharit hoy. proti byarele primiyam dhora hoyeche 4 doSomik 5 Dolar. songzukt arob 
amirat theke ek lakh 50 hajar Ton gyas oyel amodani kora hobe. proti byareler primiyam dhora hoyeche 3 doSomik 27 Dolar. filipain theke dui lakh 28 hajar Ton gyas oyel O 10 hajar Ton jeT fuyelo, maloyeSiyar peTrOnas theke tin lakh Ton gyas oyelo, 30 hajar Ton jeT fuyelo, 30 hajar Ton kerOsin amodanir doroprostab onumOdon koreche montrisova komiTi. e chaRa 168 kOTi Taka byye riya inTaronyaSonaler madhyme amodani kora hobe 25 hajar Ton cini. proti Ton cinir mUly 570 Dolar. esokeef egrOveTer barrShik sommelon esokeef egrOveT DiviSoner barrShik sommelone kOmpanir ceyaromyan lotifur rohomanosoh onyra esokeef egrOveT DiviSoner barrShik sommelono-o20o11 
got Sonibar rajodhanIr ekoTi konovenoSon senTare onuShThit hoy. kOmpanir ceyaromyan lotifur rohoman sommeloner udwOdhon koren. ete kOmpanir prodhan nirrwahI korrmokorrta simIn hOseno, poricalok saifur rohomano, atikur rohoman O aroSad Oyaliur rohoman uposthit chilen. sommelone aroO uposthit chilen esokeef egrOveT DiviSoner upodeShTa iyan hofoTaijaro, mohabybosthapok e ar sorodar O jatIy bikroy bybosthapok mohidul isolam cOUdhurI. bijNGopti. coTTograme briTiS haikomiSonar dwipokShIy baNijy 4 bochore Sot kOTi paunDe unnIt hobe agamI car bochore zuktorajy O bangladeSer dwipakShik baNijy 10o0 kOTi paunDe unnIt hobe bole mone koren Dhakay nizukt briTiS haikomiSonar robarrT Dobliu giboson. coTTogram cemware bybosayI netader soNgge gotokal rObobar ek motobinimoy sovay 
tini e aSabad bykt koren. e somoy sthanIy sangsod O coTTogram cemwarer sabek sovapoti em e lotifo, borrtoman sovapoti mOroSed murad ibrahimo, jyeShTh sohosovapoti mahobubul alomo, poricalok em e chalam promukh uposthit chilen. briTiS haikomiSonar boleno, dui deSer modhye somporrk obyahot thakay baNijyik lenoden baRoche. se onuzayI 20o0o5 theke 20o10 sale dui deSer modhye baNijyik lenoden beReche pray 42 SotangS. fole zuktorajy ekhon bangladeSer trritIy brrihottom roptani bajar. er age sokale briTiS haikomiSonar bondor vobone bondorer ceyaromyan komODor em anoOyarul isolamer soNgge sakShat'' koren. e somoy bondorer sodosy (oprokOUSolo) kyapTen anoOyarul hok cOUdhurI, sodosy (oharobar O merino) kyapTen em Sahojahan 
ebong socib sOIyod forohad uddin ahomed uposthit chilen. jIbon bima kOmpanigulOke somorUp OyebosaiT tOIri korote hobe jIbon bima kOmpanigulOke nijeder jony somorUp (oiuniforrmo) OyebosaiT tOIri korote boleche bima unnoyon O niyontroN korrtrripokSh (oaiDiaroe). borrtomaner OyebosaiTogulOy kOmpanir proyOjonIy tothy khu^je paOya zay na bole songsthaTi e tagid diyeche. aiDiaroe chaRa kOmpanigulOke uccomanosomponn somorUp (oiuniforrmo) sofoToOyyar tOIri koroteO nirrdeS diyeche. tobe nijera tOIri korote na parole ony deS theke ta songgroh korote parobe kOmpanigulO. ullekhy, somorUp OyebosaiT bolote OyebosaiTer dhoron O tothybinyaser prokrriti ekoi rokom bOjhanO hoyeche. e chaRa songsthaTi komiSon O komiSonovittik jonoboler storer ovinn podobi nirrdharoN O oyakocuyariyal sTuDenT korrmosUcir 
nItimala tOIri koraroO tagid diyeche. e biShoye 12 januyari jari kora projNGapon bastobayon korote 25 januyari aiDiaroe karryaloye ekoTi motobinimoy sova onuShThit hoy. sovay sorrwsommotite Oi projNGapon bastobayon korote progresiv laif inosyurens kOmpanir bybosthapona poricalok (oemoDi) em e korimoke ahwayok kore ekoTi komiTi goThon kora hoyeche. komiTir ony sodosyra holeno: jIbon bima koropOreSoner bybosthapona poricalok porIkShit'' dotto, popular laif inosyurenser emoDi biem iusuf alI, sondhanI laif inosyurenser emoDi ahosanul isolamo, nyaSonal laif inosyurenser otirikt emoDi jamal abodul naser ebong meTolaif alikOr rijiunal siniyor vais presiDenT nUrul isolam. komiTi aj sOmobarer modhye ovinn podobi nirrdharoNobiShoyok protibedon dakhil korobe aiDiaroer kache. e 
chaRa komiTike oyakocuyariyal nItimalabiShoyok protibedon agamI 29 februyari, OyebosaiT 15 marrc O uccomanosomponn somorUp sofoToOyyar tOIrir protibedon 30 marrcer modhye aiDiaroer kache dakhil korote hobe. jana geche, jIbon bima kOmpanigulOte borrtoman protinidhider pa^c theke 10oTi kore stor royeche. ta dui theke tin store rakhar kotha bola hoyeche. e chaRa jIbon bima kOmpanigulOte ekhon theke oyakocuyariyal bivag thaka badhytamUlok kora hoyeche. e bivager dayitw dite hobe oyakocuyariyal kaje dharoNasomponn chatrochatrIder. ta^der ontot oyakocuyariyal bijNGaner ekoTi ongS (oparrTo) somponn kora thakote hobe. sUtr janayo, aiDiaroer udyOgoke sucaruvabe somponn korote aj sOmobar komiTir sodosyder soNgge ekoTi bOIThoke bosoche songsthaTi. borrtomane ekek jIbon bima 
kOmpanir OyebosaiT ekek rokom hoOyay kOnO grahok ThikomotO tothy khu^je pan na. onek kOmpanir tothyO Thik thake na. e niye onek ovizOg ase aiDiaroer kache. zOgazOg korole aiDiaroer ceyaromyan em Sefak ahomed prothom alOke boleno, protinidhi stor meTolaif alikOr motO korar cinta royeche. udahoroN diye tini boleno, stor hote pare tinoTi: ejensi myanejaro, iuniT myanejar O ejenT. OyebosaiT biShoye Sefak ahomed boleno, âouccomanosomponn OyebosaiT na thakay onek kOmpanir kache tothy ceyeO paOya zacche na. ta chaRa valO sofoToOyyar jalo-ojaliyati rOdhe sohayok hobe.â korrmokShetre narIder ongSogrohoNe boR dhoroner ogrogoti korrmosongsthan baRoleO bekarotw komeni got koyek bochore deSe korrmosongsthan baRoleO bekar manuSher 
songkhyaO beReche. fole bekarotwer har beReche. 20o0o6 theke 20o10 sal porrynt deSe 67 lakh manuSher korrmosongsthan hoyeche. kintu e somoyer SeShe, orrthat'' 20o10 sale deSe bekarotwer har beRe saRe 4 SotangSe unnIt hoyeche. 20o0o6 sale e har chil 4 doSomik 30 SotangS. tobe ei somoyokale korrmokShetre puruSher ceye narIr ongSogrohoNer haroTiO beReche. orrthat'' SromoSoktite niyOjit narIder modhye bekarotw kichuTa komeche. bangladeS porisongkhyan byurO poricalit 20o10 saler SromoSokti somIkShar prathomik folafole emon citr uThe eseche. 20o0o6 sal porrynt korrmorot narI chilen ek kOTi 13 lakh. 20o10 sale ese ta beRe da^Riyeche ek kOTi 62 lakh. car bochorer bybodhane pray orrdhokOTi narI korrmokShetre probeS korechen. tobe se tulonay puruSher korrmokShetre probeSer har beS kom. 20o10 sal porrynt pray tin kOTi 79 lakh puruSh korrmokShetre royechen. 20o0o6 sal porrynt tin kOTi 60 lakh puruSh korrmokShetre chilen. car bochore matr 18 lakh puruSh notun kore korrmokShetre probeS korechen. zOgazOg kora hole porisongkhyan bivager socib rIti ibrahIm prothom alOke boleno, âosomIkShaTi cURant kora hoyeche. eroi modhye ta prokaSer bybostha neOya hoyeche.â tini aroO boleno, got koyek bochore orrthonOItik korrmokaND 
baRay notun korrmosongsthan hoyeche. tobe bekarotwer haroO beReche. SromoSoktir bivajon SromoSokti somIkShar somoy swniyOjit korrmI, cakoridata, cakorijIbI, mojuribihIn grrihokorrmI, dinomojur provrriti SreNIte vag kora hoyeche. ete dekha zayo, 20o10 sal nagad deSe dui kOTi 20 lakh swniyOjit korrmI royechen. orrthat'' e^ra nijerai nijeder SromokShetr tOIri korechen. 20o0o6 sal porrynt emon korrmIr songkhya chil ek kOTi 99 lakh. ar deSer cakoridata, orrthat'' udyOkta royechen ek lakho, za^ra nijera kaj korar paSapaSi korrmosongsthan korechen. 20o0o6 saleO emon udyOktar songkhya ek lakh chil. se hisebe notun cakoridata zOg hoyoni. alOcy somoye 28 lakh bykti cakori peyechen. 20o10 sal porrynt sorokari-obesorokari cakori koreno, emon 
bykti royechen 94 lakh. 20o0o6 sale e songkhya chil 66 lakh. ar ekhon ek kOTi choy lakh dinomojurivittik Sromik royechen. 20o0o6 sale emon dinomojurer songkhya chil 86 lakh. got car bochore 20 lakh notun dinomojur peSay esechen. grrihosthalir korrmokaND somIkSha onusare, sara deSe ek kOTi 18 lakh narI-opuruSh grrihosthalir kaj koren. er modhye gramIN elakay pray 97 lakh narI-opuruSh emon kaj kore thaken. Sromer mojuri na deOyay ta^der SromoSokti hisebe bibecona kora zacche na. e deSer proti poribarer narIra mojuri chaRai grrihosthalir kaj kore thaken. samajik prekShapoTer karoNe ta^der Sromer mojuri deOya hoy na. ta^der anuShThanik kOnO swIkrritoO nei. somIkSha 
onuzayI, emon korrmokaNDe pray 91 lakh narI joRit. ar puruSh royechen 27 lakh. zotharIti gramaNGcole pray bina mojurite 74 lakh narI grrihosthalir kaj koren. e prosoNgge porisongkhyan bivager socib rIti ibrahIm boleno, grrihosthalir kaj koreno, emon byktike SromoSoktir bibeconay ana hoy na. zuboSokti deSer korrmokShetre mUl Sokti hisebe kaj koroche biSal toruN projonm. mOT SromoSoktir pray orrdhek holO 15 theke 29 bochor boyosI toruN projonm. kajer modhye royechen dui kOTi noy lakho, emon toruNo-otoruNI. 20o10 sal porrynt got car bochore notun SromoSoktite zOg hoyeche 31 lakh toruNo-otoruNI. tobe aSoNgkar biShoyo, ei boyosovittik zuboSoktite puruSher ongSogrohoN komeche. 20o0o6 sal porrynt ek 
kOTi 32 lakh toruN Sromobajare chil. 20o10 sale ese Sromobajare toruNer songkhya kome ek kOTi 31 lakhe nemeche. tobe toruNIder korrmokShetre ongSogrohoN beReche. 20o0o6 sal porrynt 46 lakh toruNI Sromobajare chil. ar 20o10 sale ta beRe da^Riyeche 78 lakh. alOcy somoye toruNIder korrmokShetre probeSer har pray 70 SotangS beReche. onydike, deSer mOT jonogOShThIr pray tin kOTi 89 lakh bykti ekhonO SromoSoktir baire roye gechen. ager somIkShay dekha geche, e SromoSoktir baire tin kOTi 51 lakh bykti chil. saptahik porryalOcona mUly-oay onupat saRe pa^c bochorer modhye sorrwnimn deSer prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGje (oDiesoi) Seyarer goR mUly-oay onupat (opii reSiO) saRe 
pa^c bochorer modhye sorrwnimn porryaye neme eseche. got soptah SeShe Diesoite pii reSiOr goR (ovarito) da^Riyeche 11 doSomik 81-oe. er age 20o0o6 saler julai mas SeShe Diesoir ei onupat chil 11 doSomik 37. Diesoi sUtre e tothy jana geche. bajar biSleShokera janano, ze bajarer pii onupat zot kom sei bajar biniyOger jony totoTai uttom. ekoi soNgge ta biniyOgokarIder jony kom jhu^kipUrrN. sei bibeconay deSer Seyarobajare biniyOger khuboi valO somoy par hocche. emotabosthay bajare niyomit doropotoner jony biniyOgokarIder asthar songkoTo, pu^jibajar somporrke somyk bOjhapoRar ghaToti O ozacit hostokShepoke dayI korochen ta^ra. talikavukt kOmpanigulOr Seyaroproti ay (oipieso) O bajaromUly bibeconay pii onupat 
nirrdharoN kora hoy. zOgazOg kora hole Diesoir sovapoti Sakil rijovI prothom alOke boleno, âoamader Seyarobajarer borrtoman pii onupat aSopaSer deSogulOr ceye onek kom. bajare za^ra notun biniyOge asoben ta^der jony eTi khuboi valO khobor. tobe se kShetre biniyOgokarIder TreDing (odOInik kenabecaro) manosikota porihar kore valO Seyar bachai korote hobe.â Sakil rijovI aroO boleno, âobajarer goR pii onupat 11 doSomik 81 holeO emon onek kOmpani ache, zader pii onupat ek oNgker ghore royeche, za got koyek bochorer modhye sorrwnimn.â Diesoi sUtr janiyeche, 20o10 saler februyari mas SeShe Dhakar bajare Seyarer mUly-oayer onupat beRe sorrwOcc 31-oe uThechil. ar dui bochorer bybodhane seTi 
ekhon 11 doSomik 81-ote neme eseche. edike deSer Seyarobajar doropotoner arekoTi soptah par korol. got soptaher pa^c karrydiboser modhye car dinoi bajare doropoton ghoTeche. er fole soptah SeShe prodhan Seyarobajar Dhaka sTok eksoceNGjer (oDiesoi) sadharoN mUlysUcok neme eseche saRe car hajar poyenTer nice. eTi got pray dui bochorer modhye sorrwnimn. Seyarobajare oprodorrSit orrth ba kalOTaka biniyOg niye jari hoOya jatIy rajosw bOrrDer (oenobiaro) notun projNGapon O sorokari korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIder biniyOgoke ghire coloti maser majhamajhi Seyarobajare notun kore osthirota tOIri hoy. taroi dharabahikotay bajare Tana doropoton coloche. mudranItike ghireO kichuTa osthirota dekha dey . tobe Diesoi sovapoti Sakil rijovI boleno, âoghOShit notun 
mudranItite pu^jibajarer jony itibacoko-onetibacok kOnO kichui nei. borong Seyarobajaroke ut''padonoSIl khat hisebe bibeconay neOya hoyeche. sutorang notun mudranItir karoNe biniyOgokarIder vIt hoOyar kOnO karoN nei.â soptah SeShe Dhakar bajare dOInik goR lenodener porimaN aRai S kOTi Takar nice neme eseche. ager soptaheO ei porimaN chil 30o0 kOTi Takay. sei hisebe ek soptaher bybodhane Diesoite dOInik goR lenoden pray 20 SotangS kome geche. korrmokShetre narIder ongSogrohoNe boR dhoroner ogrogoti korrmosongsthan baRoleO bekarotw komeni got koyek bochore deSe korrmosongsthan baRoleO bekar manuSher songkhyaO beReche. fole bekarotwer har beReche. 20o0o6 theke 20o10 sal porrynt deSe 67 lakh manuSher korrmosongsthan hoyeche. kintu e somoyer 
SeShe, orrthat'' 20o10 sale deSe bekarotwer har beRe saRe 4 SotangSe unnIt hoyeche. 20o0o6 sale e har chil 4 doSomik 30 SotangS. tobe ei somoyokale korrmokShetre puruSher ceye narIr ongSogrohoNer haroTiO beReche. orrthat'' SromoSoktite niyOjit narIder modhye bekarotw kichuTa komeche. bangladeS porisongkhyan byurO poricalit 20o10 saler SromoSokti somIkShar prathomik folafole emon citr uThe eseche. Sigogiroi somIkShaTi anuShThanikovabe prokaS kora hobe. SromoSokti somIkSha 20o0o5-o0o6 onuzayI, se somoy deSe bekar lOker songkhya chil 21 lakh. ar 20o10 saler somIkShay ta beRe da^Riyeche 26 lakhe. orrthat'' alOcy somoye notunovabe pa^c lakh manuSh bekar hoyeche. tobe ei somoyokale narI bekarotwer har 7 SotangS theke 
neme eseche 5 doSomik 80 SotangSe. ar puruShoder modhye bekarotwer har 3 doSomik 40 SotangS theke beRe hoyeche 4 doSomik 10 SotangS. 20o10 sal porrynt bivinnovabe kajer modhye royeche ba korrmorot ache pa^c kOTi 41 lakh lOk. ar 20o0o6 sal porrynt ei songkhya chil car kOTi 74 lakh. pa^c bochore notun korrmosongsthan hoyeche 67 lakh. tobe orrthonOItikovabe sokriy ache, emon lOker songkhya 20o10 sal nagad pa^c kOTi 67 lakh. deSer SromoSoktir kShetre itibacok ekoTi ogrogoti holO korrmokShetre narIr ongSogrohoN brriddhi. 20o0o6 sal porrynt korrmorot narI chilen ek kOTi 13 lakh. 20o10 sale ese ta beRe da^Riyeche ek kOTi 62 lakh. 
car bochorer bybodhane pray orrdhokOTi narI korrmokShetre probeS korechen. tobe se tulonay puruSher korrmokShetre probeSer har beS kom. 20o10 sal porrynt pray tin kOTi 79 lakh puruSh korrmokShetre royechen. 20o0o6 sal porrynt tin kOTi 60 lakh puruSh korrmokShetre chilen. car bochore matr 18 lakh puruSh notun kore korrmokShetre probeS korechen. zOgazOg kora hole porisongkhyan bivager socib rIti ibrahIm prothom alOke boleno, âosomIkShaTi cURant kora hoyeche. eroi modhye ta prokaSer bybostha neOya hoyeche.â tini aroO boleno, got koyek bochore orrthonOItik korrmokaND baRay notun korrmosongsthan hoyeche. tobe bekarotwer haroO beReche. SromoSoktir bivajon SromoSokti somIkShar somoy swniyOjit korrmI, cakoridata, cakorijIbI, mojuribihIn grrihokorrmI, dinomojur 
provrriti SreNIte vag kora hoyeche. ete dekha zayo, 20o10 sal nagad deSe dui kOTi 20 lakh swniyOjit korrmI royechen. orrthat'' e^ra nijerai nijeder SromokShetr tOIri korechen. 20o0o6 sal porrynt emon korrmIr songkhya chil ek kOTi 99 lakh. ar deSer cakoridata, orrthat'' udyOkta royechen ek lakho, za^ra nijera kaj korar paSapaSi korrmosongsthan korechen. 20o0o6 saleO emon udyOktar songkhya ek lakh chil. se hisebe notun cakoridata zOg hoyoni. alOcy somoye 28 lakh bykti cakori peyechen. 20o10 sal porrynt sorokari-obesorokari cakori koreno, emon bykti royechen 94 lakh. 20o0o6 sale e songkhya chil 66 lakh. ar ekhon ek kOTi choy lakh dinomojurivittik Sromik royechen. 
20o0o6 sale emon dinomojurer songkhya chil 86 lakh. got car bochore 20 lakh notun dinomojur peSay esechen. grrihosthalir korrmokaND somIkSha onusare, sara deSe ek kOTi 18 lakh narI-opuruSh grrihosthalir kaj koren. er modhye gramIN elakay pray 97 lakh narI-opuruSh emon kaj kore thaken. Sromer mojuri na deOyay ta^der SromoSokti hisebe bibecona kora zacche na. e deSer proti poribarer narIra mojuri chaRai grrihosthalir kaj kore thaken. samajik prekShapoTer karoNe ta^der Sromer mojuri deOya hoy na. ta^der anuShThanik kOnO swIkrritoO nei. somIkSha onuzayI, emon korrmokaNDe pray 91 lakh narI joRit. ar puruSh royechen 27 lakh. zotharIti gramaNGcole pray bina mojurite 74 lakh 
narI grrihosthalir kaj koren. e prosoNgge porisongkhyan bivager socib rIti ibrahIm boleno, grrihosthalir kaj koreno, emon byktike SromoSoktir bibeconay ana hoy na. zuboSokti deSer korrmokShetre mUl Sokti hisebe kaj koroche biSal toruN projonm. mOT SromoSoktir pray orrdhek holO 15 theke 29 bochor boyosI toruN projonm. kajer modhye royechen dui kOTi noy lakho, emon toruNo-otoruNI. 20o10 sal porrynt got car bochore notun SromoSoktite zOg hoyeche 31 lakh toruNo-otoruNI. tobe aSoNgkar biShoyo, ei boyosovittik zuboSoktite puruSher ongSogrohoN komeche. 20o0o6 sal porrynt ek kOTi 32 lakh toruN Sromobajare chil. 20o10 sale ese Sromobajare toruNer songkhya kome ek kOTi 31 lakhe nemeche. tobe toruNIder 
korrmokShetre ongSogrohoN beReche. 20o0o6 sal porrynt 46 lakh toruNI Sromobajare chil. ar 20o10 sale ta beRe da^Riyeche 78 lakh. alOcy somoye toruNIder korrmokShetre probeSer har pray 70 SotangS beReche. onydike, deSer mOT jonogOShThIr pray tin kOTi 89 lakh bykti ekhonO SromoSoktir baire roye gechen. ager somIkShay dekha geche, e SromoSoktir baire tin kOTi 51 lakh bykti chil. bajare komeche khOla soyabin teler dam vOjytel amodanir rriNopotr beReche abul hasonat vOjytel amodanir jony rriNopotr (oelosi) khOlar porimaN beReche. sarrwikovabe coloti orrthobochorer prothom choy mase ager bochorer ceye vOjytel amodanir rriNopotr khOlar porimaN kom chil. tobe Disemwre e obosthar poriborrton hoyeche. ager 
bochorer ceye beSi rriNopotr khOla hoyeche. bybosayIra bole asochileno, byangker rriNer sudohar beRe zaOya O Dolarer binimoy mUlyer osthitiSIlotay got koyek mase vOjytel amodani kome ase, zodiO antorrjatik bajare soyabin teler dam kromagot komotir dike chil. edike deSer bajare khOla soyabin teler damoO komote Suru koreche. khucora bajare ekhon proti liTar khOla soyabin tel paOya zacche 120 theke 122 Takay. eko-odeR mas dhore ei teler dam 128 Takar aSopaSe OThanama korochil. antorrjatik bajare beS koyek mas dhorei soyabin teler dam komoleO deSer tel poriSOdhonokarI bybosayIra vOjytel amodanite khub ekoTa agroh dekhanoni. nitypoNyer bajarodor porrybekShoN kore emon ekoTi antorrjatik protiShThan inoDeks 
munDi boloche, soyabin teler masik goR dam chil me mase Tonoproti ek hajar 255 doSomik 67 Dolaro, jun mase ek hajar 250 doSomik 0o6, julai mase ek hajar 242 doSomik 10o, agosT mase ek hajar 225 doSomik 21, sepTemwr mase ek hajar 218 doSomik 86, okTObor mase ek hajar 126 doSomik 77, novemwr mase ek hajar 118 doSomik 32 O Disemwr mase ek hajar 10o3 doSomik 0o4 Dolar. bybosayIder hisab onuzayI, deSe bochore 14 theke 15 lakh Ton vOjyteler cahida royeche. 17 januyari bangladeS byangker OyebosaiTe deOya choyoTi nitypoNyer amodanir jony rriNopotr khOlar porisongkhyan theke dekha zayo, julai theke Disemwr 
porrynt choy lakh 14 hajar Ton oporiSOdhit vOjytel amodanir jony rriNopotr khOla hoyeche. ager bochor ekoi somoye rriNopotr khOlar porimaN chil sat lakh 38 hajar Ton. samogrikovabe zodiO rriNopotr khOlar porimaN ager bochorer tulonay komeche, tobe Sudhu Disemwr maser hisabe er porimaN beReche. bangladeS byangker tothyanuzayI, coloti orrthobochorer prothom pa^c mase (ojulai theke novemwro) rriNopotr khOla hoyechil pa^c lakh 57 Ton. ager bochor ekoi somoye rriNopotr khOlar porimaN chil choy lakh 91 hajar Ton. kintu Disemwr mase ese rriNopotr khOlar porimaN beRe zay. Disemwre 57 hajar Ton tel amodanir jony rriNopotr khOla hoyo, za ager bochorer ekoi somoyer tulonay doSomik 
12 SotangS beSi. rriNopotr khOlar porimaN ken baRoche janote caile es alom gruper ceyaromyan saiful alom prothom alOke boleno, SIte soyabin teler cahida beSi thake. se karoNe amodanir jony rriNopotrer porimaNoO beReche. siTi gruper mohabybosthapok biSwjit'' ghOSh boleno, soyabin tel amodanir Opor age 15 SotangS hare kor chil. ta komiye sorokar 10 SotangS kore. prothom dike ei korosubidhar meyad nirrdharoN kora hoy 31 Disemwr porrynt. sorokar er meyad baRiyeche. hoyotO e karoNei rriNopotr khOlar porimaN beReche. komoche soyabin teler damo: SIt Surur por Disemwrer prothom soptahe hoThat'' kore liTaroproti khOla soyabin teler dam 110o-o112 theke beRe da^Ray 123-o125 Taka. majhamajhi giye dam OThe 124-o128 Takay. bOtolojat soyabiner damoO beRe zay. bOtolojat soyabin teler dam liTaroproti car Taka baRay tel poriSOdhonokarI protiShThanogulO. tobe dui-otin din dhore vOjyteler paikari bajare soyabin teler dam komeche. ekhon khOla tel bikri hocche 110o-o112 Takay. soptah khanek ageO paikari bajare khOla soyabin teler dam chil 118-o122 Taka. ekhon milogeTe khOla tel bikri hocche 10o8 Takay. er provab poReche rajodhanIr khucora bajareO. khOla soyabin tel ekhon bikri hocche 120o-o122 Takay. tobe bOtolojat soyabin teler dam komeni. SeSh chuTir dine upoce poRa viR baNijy melar ekoTi sTole poNy dekhochen kretara Dhaka antorrjatik baNijy mela SeSh hote ar 
matr tin din baki. tai SeSh muhUrrte proyOjonIy poNyTi kinote sob boyoser kretar podocaroNe mukhor ekhon mela praNggoN. gotokal Sonibar mela SeSh hoOyar age SeSh chuTir dine viR chil koyek guN beSi. procur lOkosomagom hoOyay melar aSopaSer soRoke gotokal sara dinoi zanojoT lege chil. bijoy soroNi mOR O agaroga^O mORoâodui prant theke melay asote onekeroi ghoNTa khanek somoy legeche. e chaRa mela praNggoNer Thik samoner soRokeO zanobahoner dIrrgh joT lokSh kora geche. âoaj melay kot dorrSonarrthI esechenoâoâoemon proSner uttore baNijy mela ayOjok komiTir sodosysocib sOIyod belal hOsen gotokal bikele prothom alOke boleno, âoonyany chuTir diner ceye onek beSi kreta-odorrSonarrthI melay 
esechen. ekhon porrynt mone hocche, ei songkhya pray car lakh hobe. tobe aSa korochi, rate viR aroO baRobe.â edike, melay ongS neOya onek protiShThanoi mela borrdhit korar dabi janiyechen. tobe melar ayOjok komiTi sei somvabona nakoc kore diyeche. komiTir sodosysocib biShoyoTi niScit kore boleno, âomelar somoy baRanOr kOnO porikolpona nei.â melar SeSh muhUrrte bivinn dhoroner chaRer subidha diye kretader akrriShT korar ceShTa koroche onek protiShThan. oneke abar ager soNgge notun kore âobiSeSh chaRoâ zOg koreche. zemono: melay brryanDobihIn bivinn blejar bikreta protiShThan et din ek hajar 60o0 theke ek hajar 80o0 Takay blejar bikri korechen. kintu gotokal pray sob protiShThanokei 
ek hajar 50o0 Takay blejar bikri korote dekha zay. krOkarij bikreta onek protiShThan ekoTi Oven kinole 20oTi akorrShoNIy puroskar deOyar nOTiS TaNgiye rekheche nijeder sTole. age esob protiShThan dit 10oTi puroskar. mela praNggoN ghure dekha geche, narI O toruNIrai beSi kenakaTa korochen. zesob pyaviliyon O sTole imiTeSoner goyona, meyeder pOSako, kaSmIri Sal O cadoro, prosadhon samogrI, plasTikopoNy, grrihosthalir bivinn samogrI prodorrSit hoccheâosesob sTole viR chil beS. ilekoTronikos poNyer sTologulOteO kretader byapok viR lokSh kora zay. deSi-obideSi esob sTol theke Oveno, Tivi, frijosoh nityproyOjonIy onek jinis kinochen ta^ra. TransoTek bivinn moDeler frije pa^c hajar 40o0 Taka porrynt chaR dicche. OyaloTon mela 
upolokShe sat SotangS mUlochaRosoh skrryac karrDer madhyme akorrShoNIy upohar dicche. melar ayOjok komiTi janayo, vOkta odhikar songrokShoN odhidoptor Sukrobar oswasthykor poribeSer ovizOge tinoTi khabarer dOkanoke 11 hajar Taka jorimana koreche. e chaRa beainivabe bybosa korar daye 20 jonoke aTok kora hoy. gotokaloO ekoivabe vejalobirOdhI ovizan cole. rajodhanIr Serebangla nogore baNijy montroNaloy O ipibi zOUthovabe masobyapI 17tom baNijy melar ayOjon koreche. moNggolobar melar SeSh din. e soptaher sakShat''kar bekarotwer cap mOkabilay Silp khater probrriddhi oporiharry jatIy O bOISwik korrmosongsthan niye prothom alOr soNgge kotha bolechen bangladeS emoployarrs feDareSoner sovapoti fojolul hok prothom alO: bangladeSe bekarotw baRoche. ei cap mOkabilay besorokari khater 
koroNIy kI? fojolul hoko: bekarotw mOkabilay besorokari khater ze ekoTi sorrwatmok porikolpona royeche, ta bola zabe na. tobe Silpo-obybosar unnoyon O somprosaroNer madhyme besorokari khat korrmosongsthan srriShTite totha bekarotw mOkabilay vUmika rakhoche. zokhon bybosa-obaNijyer prosar ghoTe, zokhon Silpokarokhana tOIri hoyo, tokhon Sromiker proyOjon hoyo, manobosompoder proyOjon hoy. ar sei proyOjon meTanOr madhyme kajer suzOg tOIri hoy. bangladeSe ekhon besorokari khatoi kintu korrmosongsthane boR vUmika rakhoche. vobiShyte ta aroO baRobe. prothom alO: sorokari porisongkhyan onusare, got tin bochore deSe bekarer songkhya ontot pa^c lakh beReche. tahole ki besorokari khat kaj dite paroche na? fojolul hoko: asole besorokari khat bohu kShetrei tader 
cahida O proyOjon onusare SromoSokti pacche na. ajoke amora zokhon biSwayoner zuge sara duniyar soNgge tal rekhe bybosa-obaNijy korochi, tokhon SromoSoktir guNogot manoTa khub gurutwpUrrN hoye uTheche. e jony dokSh O kuSolI hote hobe. amader ekhane ei jayogaTite boR dhoroner ghaToti dekha diyeche. eTa Thik ze, kaj kore ovijNGota O korrmo-oproSikShoNer madhyme dokShota-okuSolota baRe. kintu ekoTa valO vitti chaRa Suru korole beSi dUr ogrosor hoOya koThin. biSeSh kore karigori jNGan O kuSolotar ovab prokoT. prothom alO: eTa ken hocche? ar e theke uttoroNeroi ba upay kI? fojolul hoko: er mUle royeche amader SikShabybosthay golod. onek kShetrei paThykromogulO zugOpozOgI noy. SikSharrthIra 
manosomponn SikSha pacche na. uccoSikShar kShetre guNomane valOâoemon protiShThaner songkhya sImit. ar tai biSwbidyaloyer ba uccoSikShar Digri niye hajar hajar chelemeye kaj pay na. karigori SikShar obostha aroO kharap. karigori O brrittimUlok SikShaprotiShThanogulO ekhonO pray purOTai sorokarivabe poricalit. tobe man unnoyoner dike nojor khub kom. e obosthay amader SikShabybosthake ut''padonomukhI kora chaRa bikolp nei. sorokaroke ei kajoTi drut korote hobe. besorokari khat e jony sohozOgita debe. asole sorokari-obesorokari zOUth proceShTatei kaj korote hobe. prothom alO: DisenT Oyarrk ba SOvon kajer biShoye antorrjatik Srom songstha (oaieloO) onek din dhorei bole asoche. niyOgodata hisebe aponara e biShoye kotoTa soceShT O socetono? fojolul 
hoko: DisenT Oyarrker mUl biShoyoTi holO ekoTi susth O suuShThu kajer poribeS niScit kora. bangladeSe amora e biShoye antorrjatik Srom songsthar (oaieloO) soNgge kaj korochi. bivinn khate socetonota tOIrir ceShTa kora hocche. kenona, kajer poribeS valO hole kajoTaO valO hoyo, Sromiko-okorrmI valOvabe kaj korote pare. eTa gOTa ut''padono-oprokriyay itibacok provab fele. tobe bangladeSer arrthosamajik bastobotay Sotovag DisenT Oyarrk protyaSa kora zay na. amora e biShoye protiSrutiboddh. tobe ratarati hobe na. prothom alO: aieloO boleche, agamI ek doSoke 60 kOTi lOker korrmosongsthan korote hobe. bOISwik korrmosongsthaner ei cyaleNGj amader Opor kIvabe provab felote pare? fojolul hoko: asole bangladeSer jonyO notun korrmosongsthan 
srriShTi ekoTa biraT cyaleNGj. vobiShyte eTa aroO baRobe. kenona, prozuktigot bikaSer provabe krriShite ut''padon beReche, korrmosongsthan songkucit hoyeche. mane, krriShi khate korrmosongsthan khub ekoTa baRar suzOg kom. se kShetre seba khate kajer suzOg tOIrir cap baRobe. kintu protibochor goRe 22 lakh manuSher kajer suzOg srriShTir ze cap ekhon bangladeSe royeche, ta mOkabila korote hole Silp khater probrriddhir dikei soboceye beSi jOr dite hobe. durrvagyjonokovabe gyaso-obidyut'', zOgazOgosoh obokaThamOgot songkoT Silp khater bikaSe boR badha hoye uTheche. sorokarer edike nojor dite hobe. ta na hole korrmohIn manuSher songkhya beRe samajik osthirota O oporadhoproboNota beRe zabe, samajik bOIShomy beRe zabe. [osakShat''kar niyechen asojadul 
kiboriya] sunamogoNGje masobyapI baNijy mela Suru sunamogoNGj Sohorer ShOloghor khelar maThe gotokal Sonibar theke masobyapI baNijy mela Suru hoyeche. melaTir ayOjon koreche sunamogoNGj cemwar ob komarrs oyanD inDasTri. relomontrI suroNGjit senogupt prodhan otithi hisebe e melar udwOdhon koren. cemwarer sovapoti khayorul huda copoler sovapotitwe onuShThane aroO boktoby den aOyamI lIger kendrIy sanggoThonik sompadok misobahouddin sirajo, sunamogoNGjo-o4 asoner sangsod motiur rohoman. seminare boktara Seyarobajar byangk khatonirrvor hoOya ucit noy coTTograme bangladeS orrthonIti somitir seminare prodhan otithir boktoby den SilpomontrI dilIp deSer Seyarobajaroke ekokovabe byangking khater Opor nirrvoroSIl kore tOlar somalOcona korechen orrthonItibidera. ta^ra boleno, ekoTi arrthik khat ekokovabe arekoTi arrthik khater 
Opor nirrvoroSIl hote pare na. ete samogrik orrthonIti jhu^kir modhye poRe zay. bangladeS orrthonIti somitir coTTogram odhyay ayOjit ek aNGcolik seminare boktara esob kotha bolen. ete bola hoyo, byangkogulO Seyarobajare biniyOger jony goNohare rriN diye geche. e jony deSer Silposoh nana khate biniyOg kichuTa holeO badhagrost hoyeche. coTTogramer thiyeTar inosTiTiuT milonayotone gotokal Sonibar seminaroTi onuShThit hoy. seminarer udwOdhonI odhibeSone prodhan otithi chilen SilpomontrI dilIp boRuya. ete sovapotitw koren orrthonIti somitir coTTogram odhyayer sovapoti jyOtiprokaS dott. dilIp boRuya boleno, âodeSer orrthonIti voNggur obosthay potit hoyeche bole zevabe carodike alOcona-osomalOcona hocche, ta adOU Thik noy. ut''padonoSIl khatosoh nana khate dokShota orrjoner madhyme 
amora onek dUr egiyechi.â isT DelTa iunivarrsiTir upacarry sikandar khan boleno, kShudrorriNer madhyme deSer orrthonItite ze ogrogoti hoyeche, ta bibeconay ana ucit. karoNo, kShudrorriNer probahoke egiye neOyar madhyme deSer orrthonItike aroO egiye neOya somvob. dinobyapI e seminarer duTi odhibeSone aToTi probondh uposthapon hoy. egulOr Opor imeriTas odhyapok Do. jamal nojorul isolamosoh onyra alOcona koren. seminare âobangladeS byangk ebong arrthik khater bybosthaponaâ SIrrShok prothom odhibeSone caroTi probondh uposthapon koren zothakrome bangladeS byangker nirrwahI poricalok mO. noOSad alI cOUdhurI, coTTogram biSwbidyaloyer SikShok mO. saiful isolamo, fenI garrlos kyaDeT kolejer SikShok muhammod josIm uddin O coTTogram biSwbidyaloyer SikSharrthI sanojida aktar. alOcona koren mO. 
alI aSoraf O abul kalam ajad. orrthonIti somitir sadharoN sompadok tOUfik ahomod cOUdhUrIr sovapotitwe dwitIy odhibeSone biSwmonda ebong bangladeSer bOIdeSik baNijy biShoye caroTi probondh uposthapon koren zothakrome rajoSahI biSwbidyaloyer odhyapok mO. abodul Oyadud O provaShok mO. selim reja, iunivarrsiTi ob lonDon skul ob ikOnomikos oyanD finyanser SikSharrthI rumman korim cOUdhurI, primiyar biSwbidyaloyer fatema jOhora ebong coTTogram biSwbidyaloyer mO. fosiul alom. er arek uddeSy hocche, Dolarer dor ar baRote na deOya. mUlot orrthonOItik songkoT theke ba^cote orrthonItir goti komiye deOya hocche. komanO hocche deSer samogrik cahida. sorokar mone koroche, ete mUlysfIti kichu komobe. tobe er fole mOT deSoj ut''padone (ojiDipi) probrriddhir haroO komobe bole aSoNgka kora hocche. orrthomontrI abul mal abodul muhit nijeO gotokal budhobar efobisisi-oaiyer onuShThane bolecheno, deSer samoShTik orrthonItir sthitiSIlotar jony proyOjone orrthonOItik probrriddhike jolaNGjoli diteO tini raji achen. borrtoman sorokarer somoye 20o0o9-o10 orrthobochore jiDipi probrriddhir har chil 6 doSomik 1 SotangS. 20o10o-o11 orrthobochore probrriddhi hoy 6 doSomik 7 SotangS. ar coloti orrthobochorer jony lokShymatra 7 SotangS. biSwbyangkosoh bivinn

aiemoefo: orrthonItike SItol kore songkoT komanOr dharoNa mUlot antorrjatik mudra tohobil (oaiemoefo) theke paOya. sorokar bOIdeSik mudrar mojud baRate aiemoef theke 10o0 kOTi Dolar rriN nite alOcona koroche. paSapaSi sarrwvOUm rriN neOyaroO porikolpona coloche. e niye sorokarer modhyeO dui dhoroner motamot ache. orrth montroNaloyosongkrant songsodIy sthayI komiTi got mase orrthonOItik poristhiti niye ekoTi bOIThok koreche. ei bOIThoke aiemoef theke rriN na niye sarrwvOUm rriN neOyar supariS kora hoy. kenona, aiemoefer rriNer Sorrt koThin. ete orrthonItir goti kome zay. kintu SeSh porrynt aiemoefokei adorrS manoche sorokar. bidyut'' kom bybohar korole bile subidha beSi paben grahok nimn O modhym SreNIr zesob abasik

fole grahokera bidyut'' bybohare areO saSroyI hoben. bitoroNokarI songsthagulOroO ay baRobe. biiarosir got Disemwr maser ghOShoNa onuzayI, 1 februyari theke dwitIy dofay sara deSe sob SreNIr grahoker bidyuter dam beReche. er fole ekhon theke proti iuniT (okilOOyaTo-oghoNTa) bidyuter goR khucora mUly da^Riyeche pa^c Taka dui poyosa. got Disemwre prothom dofay dam baRar por eTa hoyechil car Taka 71 poyosa. e chaRa biiarosir got 24 novemwrer arek adeS anuzayI, e mas theke bidyuter paikari damoO baRoche. fole bidyut'' bitoroNokarI songsthagulOke piDibir kach theke proti iuniT bidyut'' kinote hobe goRe tin Taka 74 poyosay. grahokovede damo: notun mUlyhar onuzayI piDibi, DipiDisi, DesokO 
ebong OjOpaDikOr abasik grahokoder kShetre 10o0 iuniT porrynt proti iuniTer dam hocche dui Taka 87 poyosa. 10o1 theke 40o0 iuniT porrynt car Taka car poyosa ebong 40o0 iuniTer beSi bybohar korole proti iuniTer dam poRobe sat Taka 43 poyosa. krriShite proti iuniT poRobe dui Taka 13 poyosa. kShudr Silpe pa^c Taka 67 poyosa (oflaT reTo). baNijyik byboharer kShetre sat Taka 33 poyosa (oflaT reTo). pollI bidyuter dam somitivede abasik grahokoder kShetre 10o0 iuniT porrynt dui Taka 90 poyosa theke tin Taka 34 poyosa. 10o1 theke 30o0 iuniT porrynt tin Taka 45 poyosa theke tin Taka 95 poyosa. 30o1 theke 50o0

biSwbyangke dudoker onusondhan protibedoner sarosongkShep jananO hoyeche. kI prokriyay ei onusondhan kora hoyeche, ta-oO biSwbyangk korrtrripokShoke jananO hoyeche. aj brrihospotibar bikele nij karryaloye sangbadikoder esob tothy diyechen dudoker ceyaromyan gOlam rohoman. gOlam rohoman boleno, dudoker ei onusondhan prokriyay durrnItir ovizOger kOnO promaN meleni. tobe zodi keu ei ovizOgo-osomporrkit dalilik promaN uposthapon korote pareno, tahole abaroO onusondhan kora hobe. tini boleno, dudok aine vuya ovizOgokarIr biruddhe bybostha neOyar kOnO upay nei. tobe sorokar caile dudok vuya ovizOgokarIr biruddhe bybostha grohoN korote pare. haikOrrTer ray jOr kore lOna pani tule cingRi caSh obOIdh khulona, satokShIra, bagerohaTo, nOyakhalI, koksobajarosoh upokUlIy jelar krriShi O 
bonovUmite jOr kore lOna pani tule cingRi caSh obOIdh ghOShoNa korechen haikOrrT. gotokal budhobar bicaropoti e eic em Samosuddin cOUdhurI O bicaropoti jahaNggIr hOsener somonwye goThit haikOrrT beNGc e ray den. ekoi soNgge cingRi caShe karoO icchar biruddhe jOr kore lOna pani uttOlon bondhe karrykor podokShep nite songSliShT byktider proti nirrdeS deOya hoy. jana zayo, upokUlIy jelagulOte lOna pani Dhukiye krriShi O bonovUmite cingRi caSher biruddhe proyOjonIy nirrdeSona ceye 20o10 saler 10 januyari bangladeS poribeS ainobid somiti (obela) O besorokari unnoyon songstha âonijera koriâ haikOrrTe riT abedon kore. abedone bola hoyo, Oi pa^c jelar krriShivUmite (odeSer mOT vUmir Sotokora 17 
vago) jOr kore lOna pani probeS koranOy krriShivUmi O gachopala kome zacche. prathomik Sunanir por Oi din adalot rul jari koren. rule upokUlIy jelar krriShi O bonovUmite jOr kore lOna pani probeS koriye cingRi caSh ken obOIdh O jonoswarrthobirOdhI ghOShoNa kora hobe na, ta janote caOya hoy. pore 20o10 saler 15 februyari upokUlIy jelagulOte jOr kore lOna pani probeS koriye baNijyik cingRi caSh theke birot thakar nirrdeS deOya hoy. eropor ruler Opor cURant Sunani SeShe gotokal adalot ray den. adalote riT abedoner pokShe ainojIbI sOIyoda rijoOyana hasan O ikobal kobir Sunani koren. vUmi montroNaloyer pokShe ainojIbI monojil mOrosed O pani 
unnoyon bOrrDer pokShe ainojIbI delOyar hOsen somaddar mamola poricalona koren. mot''sy montroNaloyer pokShe chilen DepuTi oyaTorrni jenarel e bi em alotaf hOsen. pore ikobal kobir prothom alOke boleno, upokUlIy jelagulOy krriShi O bonovUmite jOr kore lOna pani tule cingRir caSh obOIdh ghOShoNa korechen adalot. paSapaSi adalot upokUlIy jelagulOr krriShi O bonovUmite jOr kore lOna pani probeS koriye cingRi caSh bondhe karrykor podokShep nite songSliShT korrtrripokShoke nirrdeS diyechen. aj nyazymUlyer cal fer bikri nimnomaner cal soroboraher ovizOge gotokal budhobar nyazymUlyer cal bikri bondh rekhechil Trakosel feyar prais O Oemoes Dilar somiti. tobe khady bivager aSwaser poriprekShite aj theke abaroO cal bikri 
Suru korote zacchen Dilarora. gotokal khady bivager otirikt mohaporicalok enayet hOsenosoh koyekojon korrmokorrtar soNgge Dilarora bOIThok koren. bOIThoke khady bivag theke aSwas deOya hoyo, ekhon theke nimnomaner cal soroborah kora hobe na. Dilarora bolecheno, 12 februyarir modhye unnotomaner cal soroborah Suru na korole 13 februyari theke onirrdiShTokaler jony cal bikri bondh rakhoben ta^ra. cal bikri bondh rakha korrmosUcir prothom dine gotokal sokal 10oTay Dilar somitir pokSh theke rajodhanIr tejoga^O kendrIy khady songrokShoNagare ek somabeSer ayOjon kora hoy. somitir sovapoti alomogIr sOIkoter sovapotitwe ony Dilarora somabeSe boktoby den. somitir sadharoN sompadok haruN or roSid e byapare prothom alOke boleno, nimnomaner cal 
kretara nite caichen na. ek diner cal dui din ghureO bikri kora zacche na. fole badhy hoye Dilarora cal bikri bondh rekhechen. khady bivager otirikt mohaporicalok enayet hOsen e byapare prothom alOke boleno, sadharoN bajare caler dam kome zaOyay emonitei nyazymUlyer caler cahida kome geche. taroporoO Dilaroder dabir kotha bibecona kore unnotomaner cal soroboraher ceShTa kora hobe. narayoNogoNGje bipul porimaN cOrai tel uddharo, aTok 3 narayoNogoNGj sodor upojelar fotullay gotokal budhobar cOrai teler bivinn astanay ovizan caliye tin hajar 30o0 liTar tel uddhar koreche roâyab. aTok kora hoyeche tinojonoke. aTok byktira holeno: abodus salam (o50o)o, ibrahim kholil (o43) O rajIb

Diesoite brrihospotibar 260oTi kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer lenoden hoy. er modhye 170oTiroi dam komeche, beReche 78Tir ar oporiborrtit chil 12Tir kOmpanir Seyarer dam. coTTogram sTok eksoceNGjer (osiesoi) sarrwik mUlysUcok pray 224 poyenT kome gotokal din SeShe neme eseche 11 hajar 353 poyenTe. siesoite lenoden hoOya 183Ti kOmpani O miucuyal fanDer modhye 152Tiroi dam komeche, beReche 24Tir ar oporiborrtit chil satoTi kOmpanir Seyarer dam. Oi din coTTogramer bajare 31 kOTi Taka lenoden hoyo, za ager diner ceye sat kOTi Taka kom. sOIyodopure notun relokOc karokhana sthaponer udyOg 
sOIyodopure dwitIy reloOye karokhana nirrmaNer udyOg neOya hoyeche. e lokShye dui diner prathomik somIkSha gotokal brrihospotibar SeSh hoyeche. somIkShaTi calay varotIy reloOyer oNggoprotiShThan raiTos limiTeD O inDiyar grup jenarel myanejar punit kumarer netrritwe dui sodosyer ekoTi protinidhidol. punit kumar boleno, âosOIyodopure zehetu reloOyer ekoTi meramot karokhana royeche, sehetu ekhane onukUl poribeS O onek suzOgo-osubidha royeche. amora kebol ekoTi notun karokhana sthapone sarrwik poristhiti porrybekShoN O meSin sthaponer dikogulO bibeconay rekhechi.â punit kumar aroO janano, agamI dui soptaher modhye uccoporryayer aroO ekoTi varotIy protinidhidol sOIyodopur sofore asobe. tara obokaThamO nirrmaN O karigori dik niye somvabyta zacai kore bangladeS reloOyer kache ekoTi 
protibedon joma debe. jana geche, varotIy orrthayone sOIyodopure ei notun relokOc (obogi) nirrmaN karokhana hobe. bangladeS reloOyer otirikt mohaporicalok kholilur rohoman prothom alOke janano, somproti prodhanomontrI sOIyodopure aroO ekoTi rel karokhana sthaponer nirrdeSona den. e chaRa 22 januyari relomontrI suroNGjit senoguptoO ekhane arekoTi karokhana sthaponer ghOShoNa den. se onuzayIi bangladeS reloOye ekoTi rUporekha tOIri koreche ebong varotIy protinidhidol somIkSha calacche. kholilur rohoman janano, 1870 sale tot''kalIn asamo-obeNggol reloOyer brrihottom karokhanaTi sthapon kora hoy sOIyodopure. otIte ekhane notun kOcoO nirrmaN kora holeO borrtomane kebol reloOye kOc O Oyagon meramot kora hoy. deR bochor por bieefoefoer komiTi ghOShoNa mamolar karoNe pray deR 
bochor jhule thakar por bangladeS freiT foroOyarrDos oyasOsiyeSoner (obieefoefoe) nirrwaconer fol budhobar ghOShoNa kora hoyeche. nirrwacon komiSoner ceyaromyan em tanovIr madarer soi kora bijNGoptir madhyme nirrwacit poricalona porrShoder sodosyder talika songSliShT sobar kache paThanO hoyeche. nirrwacit poricalokera holeno: mahobubul anamo, e bi em rofikujjamano, omiy Songkor borrmoNo, amirul isolam cOUdhurI, ariful ahosano, asif e cOUdhurI, johir uddIn ahomedo, bodorul hok cOUdhurI, em e sObohano, jahid hOseno, sOIyod mO. bokhotiyaro, sOIyod gOlam moOla, helalouddIn akoboro, khayorul alom sujono, belalo-oi-obakI idrisI, mO. mofijul isolamo, josim iu ahomedo, nasir ahomed khan O es e jaman. prosoNggoto, 20o10 saler 10 agosT ei nirrwacon onuShThit 
hoy. tobe adaloter mamolar karoNe fol prokaS korote pareni nirrwacon komiSon. e niye riT abedon O konoTemoT abedoner madhyme nirrwaconer fol prokaSer badha dUr hoy. varot ebar tripuray khadySosy nite cay abaroO aSugoNGj nOUbondor bybohar kore bohumatrik TranojiTo-osubidha ceyeche varot. pray 35 hajar Ton khadySosy kolokata theke aSugoNGj bondor porrynt nOUpothe, ar bakiTa soRokopothe tripurar rajodhanI agorotolay neOyar suzOg dite bangladeS sorokaroke onurOdh koreche varot. dui deSer bidyman TranojiTo-osongkrant nOU-oproTOkoler aOtay ei poNy zabe. got 30 januyari Dhakay varotIy haikomiSon theke e-osongkrant ekoTi ciThi pororaShTr montroNaloye paThanO hoyeche. ei ciThir onulipi nOU montroNaloyo, jatIy rajosw bOrrD (oenobiaro) ebong bangladeS ovyntorIN 
nOUporibohon korrtrripokSher (obiaiDobliuTie) kache paThiyeche varotIy haikomiSon. varotIy haikomiSoner ciThite bola hoyeche, nOU-oproTOkoler aOtay varot aSugoNGj bondoroke TranoSipomenT poyenT hisebe bybohar kore 35 hajar Ton khadySosy tripuray paThate cay varot. er modhye 10 hajar Ton khadySosy jorurivittite paThanO proyOjon. 10 hajar Toner calanoTi prostutoO ache. e chaRa aSugoNGj bondore ei poNy drut OThanamar jony jhu^ki bonD isyusoh onyany anuShThanikota somponn na koraroO onurOdh janiyeche varot. bangladeSer pokShe nOU-oproTOkoloTi karrykorer mUl dayitw nOU montroNaloyer. zOgazOg kora hole nOU montroNaloyer zugm socib mOhammod alauddin janano, ekhonO nOU montroNaloyer kache anuShThanikovabe prostaboTi aseni. ei dhoroner prostab ele songSliShT sob pokShogulOr motamot niye siddhant

kore fele! porerobar abaroO miShTi moric caSh korote gele gramer lOkojon hasahasi Suru koren. emonoki nijer bouO ragaragi koren. jhogoRa hoy. bou rag kore vatoO khete denoni. kintu zokhon e moric caSh kore safoly peleno, tokhon sobai proSongsa Suru koren. khuSi hon bouO. golper SuruTa 12 bochor ager. nayok boguRar SibogoNGj upojelar daRidoh iuniyoner bujoruk SOkora gramer anochar alI. ta^r sei somoy ar ei somoyer parrthoky onek. ovabI manuShoTi aj sofol caShi. miShTi moric diye Surur por bideSi soboji caSh kore ovab joy korechen. ta^r kache poramorrS niye sekhanokar onekei bideSi soboji caSher dike jhu^kochen. anocharer grame ek dino: upojela

tin din ekoivabe Oi byangk korrmokorrta sob moric kine niye zan. anochar khO^j niye janote pareno, Oi byangk korrmokorrta esob moric beSi dame Dhakay bikri koren. tai er dike jhu^ke poRa.â bolen anochar. nijer goRa khamaro: ekhon bivinn sthan theke lOkojon bideSi soboji, bIj O cara kinote anochar alIr grame asen. tai tini âoOyesTarrn vejiTebol proDakoSon krriShi farrmoâ namer ekoTi khamar goRe tulechen. ekhon soboji kenar jony Dhaka theke e Thikanay ogrim Taka paThiye deOya hocche. cahida onuzayI soboji kokhonO nijei pOU^che deno, kokhonO DhakagamI poribohone tule den. sofol manuSho: bideSi soboji caSh kore paOya Taka diye cheleke bideSe paThiyechen anochar. dui meyeke biye diyechen. e porrynt 13 bigha jomir malik hoyechen. ku^Reghor theke hoyeche paka baRi. tobe eka unnotite biSwasI non sofol e manuShoTi. tini

chaRa nityproyOjonIy gomo, cini, vOjytelo, Dalosoh beSir vag vOgypoNy amodaninirrvor. esob poNyer dam nirrvor kore antorrjatik bajarodor ebong amodani ba soroboraher Opor. bangladeS byangk coTTogram oNGcoler dayitwSIl ekoTi sUtr janayo, gomo, cini, vOjytelo, Dalosoh sat dhoroner vOgypoNy amodanir jony coTTogram oNGcole got okTObore 11 kOTi 17 lakh 45 hajar 884 Dolarer rriNopotr khOlen sthanIy bybosayIra. porer mase rriNopotr khOla hoy aT kOTi 14 lakh 31 hajar 570 Dolarer. 16 hajar Ton ebong Disemwre ek lakh 10 hajar Ton gom amodanir rriNopotr khOla hoy. coTTogram siTi koropOreSon boR bajeTer kaj hocche somojhOtar madhyme! coTTogram siTi koropOreSoner boR bajeTer unnoyonokajogulO somojhOtar madhyme coRa dame koyekojon Thikadar niye nicchen bole ovizOg paOya geche. got car mase pray 29 kOTi Takar caroTi kaje somojhOta hoOyar khobor paOya geche. got budhobaroO e dhoroner ekoTi kajer somojhOta hoyeche bole jana geche. jana zayo, coTTogram siTi koropOreSon nijosw orrthayone nogorer baTali pahaRer kache nimn ayer lOkoder jony 70o0 flyaT nirrmaN korobe. got budhobar ei kaj peyechen coTTogram siTi koropOreSon Thikadar somitir sovapoti moNGjurul alom. ta^r 
protiShThan mesarrs moNGjurul alom cOUdhurI pa^c kOTi 59 lakh Takar kajoTir jony pa^c kOTi 99 lakh Takay doropotr joma dey. got okTOboreO tini choy kOTi Takar ekoTi kaj somojhOtar madhyme pan prakkolit byyer 5 SotangS beSite. goN khate kroyobidhi onuzayI, prakkolit byyer ceye kom kingba beSite doropotr joma deOya zay. tobe protizOgitar madhyme e dhoroner kaj hole sorokari orrther saSroy hoy. siTi koropOreSone tin maser caroTi kaj somojhOtar madhyme deOyar karoNe ontot choy kOTi Takar kShoti hoyeche bole dharoNa korochen ekadhik Thikadar. othoc protizOgitar madhyme zesob doropotrer karryadeS deOya hoyeche, segulO 5 theke 15 SotangS porrynt kom Takay karryadeS deOya

ceye beSi dore kichutei doropotr deOya ucit noy. jana zayo, sorrwSeSh kajoTir jony 57Ti doropotr kena holeO joma poRe matr caroTi. somojhOtar karoNe ony doropotrogulO ar joma poReni. tobe mesarrs moNGjurul isolam cOUdhurI chaRa ar ze tinoTi doropotr joma poReche, segulOte nirapotta jamanotosoh onek proyOjonIy kagojoi joma deOya hoyoni. Thikadaroder soNgge kotha bole jana zayo, ager din rate ei niye Oi Thikadarera bOIThok koren. eropor lOk dekhanO doropotr joma deOya hoy. moNGjurul alomer doropotrer paSapaSi ony doropotrogulOte prakkolit byyer ceye aroO beSi mUly dekhanO hoy. somojhOtar madhyme kaj paOyar kotha swIkar korechen moNGjurul alom. tini prothom alOke boleno, Thikadarera sobai

tini boleno, kShomotasIn doler kichu Thikadar onekoTa jOr kore esob kaje ony Thikadaroder somojhOtay asote badhy korochen. fole boR kaje ovijNG O peSadar Thikadarera protizOgitay ongS nite parochen na. proSasonoO biShoyoTi jene na janar van koroche. jana geche, sorokarer kach theke thOk boradd orrdhek kome zaOya ebong lokShymatra onuzayI pOUrokor aday na hoOyay coTTogram siTi koropOreSon borrtomane maratmok orrthokoShTer modhye royeche. got orrthobochore sorokar coTTogram siTi koropOreSonoke thOk boradd diyechil 17 kOTi Taka. ebar dicche matr sat kOTi Taka. er modhye paOya geche matr ek kOTi Taka. fole nijosw tohobil theke korrmokorrta-okorrmocarIder betono-ovata poriSOdher por khub olp Takaroi unnoyonokaj korote
